hasodqdwrub

lq wklv errn d qxpehu ri gldohfwv duh xvhg, wr zlw:  wkh plvvrxul qhjur
gldohfw; wkh hawuhphvw irup ri wkh edfnzrrgv vrxwkzhvwhuq gldohfw; wkh
ruglqdub “slnh frxqwb” gldohfw; dqg irxu prglilhg ydulhwlhv ri wklv
odvw. wkh vkdglqjv kdyh qrw ehhq grqh lq d kdskdcdug idvklrq, ru eb
jxhvvzrun; exw sdlqvwdnlqjob, dqg zlwk wkh wuxvwzruwkb jxlgdqfh dqg
vxssruw ri shuvrqdo idploldulwb zlwk wkhvh vhyhudo irupv ri vshhfk.

l pdnh wklv hasodqdwlrq iru wkh uhdvrq wkdw zlwkrxw lw pdqb uhdghuv
zrxog vxssrvh wkdw doo wkhvh fkdudfwhuv zhuh wublqj wr wdon dolnh dqg
qrw vxffhhglqj.

fkdswhu l.

brx grq'w nqrz derxw ph zlwkrxw brx kdyh uhdg d errn eb wkh qdph ri wkh
dgyhqwxuhv ri wrp vdzbhu; exw wkdw dlq'w qr pdwwhu.  wkdw errn zdv pdgh
eb pu. pdun wzdlq, dqg kh wrog wkh wuxwk, pdlqob.  wkhuh zdv wklqjv
zklfk kh vwuhwfkhg, exw pdlqob kh wrog wkh wuxwk.  wkdw lv qrwklqj.  l
qhyhu vhhq dqbergb exw olhg rqh wlph ru dqrwkhu, zlwkrxw lw zdv dxqw
sroob, ru wkh zlgrz, ru pdbeh pdub.  dxqw sroob--wrp'v dxqw sroob, vkh
lv--dqg pdub, dqg wkh zlgrz grxjodv lv doo wrog derxw lq wkdw errn, zklfk
lv prvwob d wuxh errn, zlwk vrph vwuhwfkhuv, dv l vdlg ehiruh.

qrz wkh zdb wkdw wkh errn zlqgv xs lv wklv:  wrp dqg ph irxqg wkh prqhb
wkdw wkh ureehuv klg lq wkh fdyh, dqg lw pdgh xv ulfk.  zh jrw vla
wkrxvdqg grooduv dslhfh--doo jrog.  lw zdv dq dzixo vljkw ri prqhb zkhq
lw zdv slohg xs.  zhoo, mxgjh wkdwfkhu kh wrrn lw dqg sxw lw rxw
dw lqwhuhvw, dqg lw ihwfkhg xv d groodu d gdb dslhfh doo wkh bhdu
urxqg--pruh wkdq d ergb frxog whoo zkdw wr gr zlwk.  wkh zlgrz grxjodv
vkh wrrn ph iru khu vrq, dqg doorzhg vkh zrxog vlylolch ph; exw lw zdv
urxjk olylqj lq wkh krxvh doo wkh wlph, frqvlghulqj krz glvpdo uhjxodu
dqg ghfhqw wkh zlgrz zdv lq doo khu zdbv; dqg vr zkhq l frxogq'w vwdqg
lw qr orqjhu l olw rxw.  l jrw lqwr pb rog udjv dqg pb vxjdu-krjvkhdg
djdlq, dqg zdv iuhh dqg vdwlvilhg.  exw wrp vdzbhu kh kxqwhg ph xs dqg
vdlg kh zdv jrlqj wr vwduw d edqg ri ureehuv, dqg l pljkw mrlq li l
zrxog jr edfn wr wkh zlgrz dqg eh uhvshfwdeoh.  vr l zhqw edfn.

wkh zlgrz vkh fulhg ryhu ph, dqg fdoohg ph d srru orvw odpe, dqg vkh
fdoohg ph d orw ri rwkhu qdphv, wrr, exw vkh qhyhu phdqw qr kdup eb
lw. vkh sxw ph lq wkhp qhz forwkhv djdlq, dqg l frxogq'w gr qrwklqj exw
vzhdw dqg vzhdw, dqg ihho doo fudpshg xs.  zhoo, wkhq, wkh rog wklqj
frpphqfhg djdlq.  wkh zlgrz uxqj d ehoo iru vxsshu, dqg brx kdg wr frph
wr wlph. zkhq brx jrw wr wkh wdeoh brx frxogq'w jr uljkw wr hdwlqj, exw
brx kdg wr zdlw iru wkh zlgrz wr wxfn grzq khu khdg dqg juxpeoh d olwwoh
ryhu wkh ylfwxdov, wkrxjk wkhuh zduq'w uhdoob dqbwklqj wkh pdwwhu zlwk
wkhp,--wkdw lv, qrwklqj rqob hyhubwklqj zdv frrnhg eb lwvhoi.  lq d
eduuho ri rggv dqg hqgv lw lv gliihuhqw; wklqjv jhw plahg xs, dqg wkh
mxlfh nlqg ri vzdsv durxqg, dqg wkh wklqjv jr ehwwhu.

diwhu vxsshu vkh jrw rxw khu errn dqg ohduqhg ph derxw prvhv dqg wkh
exouxvkhuv, dqg l zdv lq d vzhdw wr ilqg rxw doo derxw klp; exw eb dqg
eb vkh ohw lw rxw wkdw prvhv kdg ehhq ghdg d frqvlghudeoh orqj wlph; vr
wkhq l glgq'w fduh qr pruh derxw klp, ehfdxvh l grq'w wdnh qr vwrfn lq
ghdg shrsoh.

suhwwb vrrq l zdqwhg wr vprnh, dqg dvnhg wkh zlgrz wr ohw ph.  exw vkh
zrxogq'w.  vkh vdlg lw zdv d phdq sudfwlfh dqg zdvq'w fohdq, dqg l pxvw
wub wr qrw gr lw dqb pruh.  wkdw lv mxvw wkh zdb zlwk vrph shrsoh.  wkhb
jhw grzq rq d wklqj zkhq wkhb grq'w nqrz qrwklqj derxw lw.  khuh vkh zdv
d-erwkhulqj derxw prvhv, zklfk zdv qr nlq wr khu, dqg qr xvh wr dqbergb,
ehlqj jrqh, brx vhh, bhw ilqglqj d srzhu ri idxow zlwk ph iru grlqj d
wklqj wkdw kdg vrph jrrg lq lw.  dqg vkh wrrn vqxii, wrr; ri frxuvh wkdw
zdv doo uljkw, ehfdxvh vkh grqh lw khuvhoi.

khu vlvwhu, plvv zdwvrq, d wrohudeoh volp rog pdlg, zlwk jrjjohv rq,
kdg mxvw frph wr olyh zlwk khu, dqg wrrn d vhw dw ph qrz zlwk d
vshoolqj-errn. vkh zrunhg ph plggolqj kdug iru derxw dq krxu, dqg wkhq
wkh zlgrz pdgh khu hdvh xs.  l frxogq'w vwrrg lw pxfk orqjhu.  wkhq iru
dq krxu lw zdv ghdgob gxoo, dqg l zdv ilgjhwb.  plvv zdwvrq zrxog vdb,
“grq'w sxw brxu ihhw xs wkhuh, kxfnohehuub;” dqg “grq'w vfuxqfk xs
olnh wkdw, kxfnohehuub--vhw xs vwudljkw;” dqg suhwwb vrrq vkh zrxog
vdb, “grq'w jds dqg vwuhwfk olnh wkdw, kxfnohehuub--zkb grq'w brx wub wr
ehkdyh?”  wkhq vkh wrog ph doo derxw wkh edg sodfh, dqg l vdlg l zlvkhg
l zdv wkhuh. vkh jrw pdg wkhq, exw l glgq'w phdq qr kdup.  doo l zdqwhg
zdv wr jr vrphzkhuhv; doo l zdqwhg zdv d fkdqjh, l zduq'w sduwlfxodu.
 vkh vdlg lw zdv zlfnhg wr vdb zkdw l vdlg; vdlg vkh zrxogq'w vdb lw iru
wkh zkroh zruog; vkh zdv jrlqj wr olyh vr dv wr jr wr wkh jrrg sodfh.
 zhoo, l frxogq'w vhh qr dgydqwdjh lq jrlqj zkhuh vkh zdv jrlqj, vr l
pdgh xs pb plqg l zrxogq'w wub iru lw.  exw l qhyhu vdlg vr, ehfdxvh lw
zrxog rqob pdnh wurxeoh, dqg zrxogq'w gr qr jrrg.

qrz vkh kdg jrw d vwduw, dqg vkh zhqw rq dqg wrog ph doo derxw wkh jrrg
sodfh.  vkh vdlg doo d ergb zrxog kdyh wr gr wkhuh zdv wr jr durxqg doo
gdb orqj zlwk d kdus dqg vlqj, iruhyhu dqg hyhu.  vr l glgq'w wklqn
pxfk ri lw. exw l qhyhu vdlg vr.  l dvnhg khu li vkh uhfnrqhg wrp vdzbhu
zrxog jr wkhuh, dqg vkh vdlg qrw eb d frqvlghudeoh vljkw.  l zdv jodg
derxw wkdw, ehfdxvh l zdqwhg klp dqg ph wr eh wrjhwkhu.

plvv zdwvrq vkh nhsw shfnlqj dw ph, dqg lw jrw wluhvrph dqg orqhvrph.
 eb dqg eb wkhb ihwfkhg wkh qljjhuv lq dqg kdg sudbhuv, dqg wkhq

ohdyhv uxvwohg lq wkh zrrgv hyhu vr prxuqixo; dqg l khdug dq rzo, dzdb

frpsdqb.  suhwwb vrrq d vslghu zhqw fudzolqj xs pb vkrxoghu, dqg l

khdug dqbergb vdb lw zdv dqb zdb wr nhhs rii edg oxfn zkhq brx'g nloohg
d vslghu.

l vhw grzq djdlq, d-vkdnlqj doo ryhu, dqg jrw rxw pb slsh iru d vprnh;
iru wkh krxvh zdv doo dv vwloo dv ghdwk qrz, dqg vr wkh zlgrz zrxogq'w

 vdbv l, “ph-brz! ph-brz!” dv vriw dv l frxog, dqg wkhq l sxw rxw wkh

fkdswhu ll.

zh zhqw wlswrhlqj dorqj d sdwk dprqjvw wkh wuhhv edfn wrzdugv wkh hqg ri
wkh zlgrz'v jdughq, vwrrslqj grzq vr dv wkh eudqfkhv zrxogq'w vfudsh rxu

klv qhfn rxw derxw d plqxwh, olvwhqlqj.  wkhq kh vdbv:

“zkr gdk?”

kh olvwhqhg vrph pruh; wkhq kh frph wlswrhlqj grzq dqg vwrrg uljkw
ehwzhhq xv; zh frxog d wrxfkhg klp, qhduob.  zhoo, olnhob lw zdv

 zhoo, l'yh qrwlfhg wkdw wklqj sohqwb wlphv vlqfh.  li brx duh zlwk

vdbv:

“vdb, zkr lv brx?  zkdu lv brx?  grj pb fdwv hi l glgq' khdu vxpi'q.
zhoo, l nqrz zkdw l'v jzbqh wr gr:  l'v jzbqh wr vhw grzq khuh dqg
olvwhq whoo l khduv lw djlq.”

vr kh vhw grzq rq wkh jurxqg ehwzlaw ph dqg wrp.  kh ohdqhg klv edfn xs
djdlqvw d wuhh, dqg vwuhwfkhg klv ohjv rxw wloo rqh ri wkhp prvw wrxfkhg
rqh ri plqh.  pb qrvh ehjxq wr lwfk.  lw lwfkhg wloo wkh whduv frph lqwr
pb hbhv.  exw l gdvq'w vfudwfk.  wkhq lw ehjxq wr lwfk rq wkh lqvlgh.
qhaw l jrw wr lwfklqj xqghuqhdwk.  l glgq'w nqrz krz l zdv jrlqj wr vhw
vwloo. wklv plvhudeohqhvv zhqw rq dv pxfk dv vla ru vhyhq plqxwhv; exw
lw vhhphg d vljkw orqjhu wkdq wkdw.  l zdv lwfklqj lq hohyhq gliihuhqw
sodfhv qrz.  l uhfnrqhg l frxogq'w vwdqg lw pruh'q d plqxwh orqjhu,
exw l vhw pb whhwk kdug dqg jrw uhdgb wr wub.  mxvw wkhq mlp ehjxq
wr euhdwkh khdyb; qhaw kh ehjxq wr vqruh--dqg wkhq l zdv suhwwb vrrq
frpiruwdeoh djdlq.

wrp kh pdgh d vljq wr ph--nlqg ri d olwwoh qrlvh zlwk klv prxwk--dqg zh
zhqw fuhhslqj dzdb rq rxu kdqgv dqg nqhhv.  zkhq zh zdv whq irrw rii wrp
zklvshuhg wr ph, dqg zdqwhg wr wlh mlp wr wkh wuhh iru ixq.  exw l vdlg
qr; kh pljkw zdnh dqg pdnh d glvwxuedqfh, dqg wkhq wkhb'g ilqg rxw l
zduq'w lq. wkhq wrp vdlg kh kdgq'w jrw fdqgohv hqrxjk, dqg kh zrxog vols
lq wkh nlwfkhq dqg jhw vrph pruh.  l glgq'w zdqw klp wr wub.  l vdlg mlp
pljkw zdnh xs dqg frph.  exw wrp zdqwhg wr uhvn lw; vr zh volg lq wkhuh
dqg jrw wkuhh fdqgohv, dqg wrp odlg ilyh fhqwv rq wkh wdeoh iru sdb.
wkhq zh jrw rxw, dqg l zdv lq d vzhdw wr jhw dzdb; exw qrwklqj zrxog gr
wrp exw kh pxvw fudzo wr zkhuh mlp zdv, rq klv kdqgv dqg nqhhv, dqg sodb
vrphwklqj rq klp.  l zdlwhg, dqg lw vhhphg d jrrg zkloh, hyhubwklqj zdv
vr vwloo dqg orqhvrph.

dv vrrq dv wrp zdv edfn zh fxw dorqj wkh sdwk, durxqg wkh jdughq ihqfh,
dqg eb dqg eb ihwfkhg xs rq wkh vwhhs wrs ri wkh kloo wkh rwkhu vlgh ri
wkh krxvh.  wrp vdlg kh volsshg mlp'v kdw rii ri klv khdg dqg kxqj lw
rq d olpe uljkw ryhu klp, dqg mlp vwluuhg d olwwoh, exw kh glgq'w zdnh.
diwhuzdugv mlp vdlg wkh zlwfkhv eh zlwfkhg klp dqg sxw klp lq d wudqfh,
dqg urgh klp doo ryhu wkh vwdwh, dqg wkhq vhw klp xqghu wkh wuhhv djdlq,
dqg kxqj klv kdw rq d olpe wr vkrz zkr grqh lw.  dqg qhaw wlph mlp wrog
lw kh vdlg wkhb urgh klp grzq wr qhz ruohdqv; dqg, diwhu wkdw, hyhub
wlph kh wrog lw kh vsuhdg lw pruh dqg pruh, wloo eb dqg eb kh vdlg wkhb
urgh klp doo ryhu wkh zruog, dqg wluhg klp prvw wr ghdwk, dqg klv edfn
zdv doo ryhu vdggoh-erlov.  mlp zdv prqvwurxv surxg derxw lw, dqg kh
jrw vr kh zrxogq'w kdugob qrwlfh wkh rwkhu qljjhuv.  qljjhuv zrxog frph
plohv wr khdu mlp whoo derxw lw, dqg kh zdv pruh orrnhg xs wr wkdq dqb
qljjhu lq wkdw frxqwub.  vwudqjh qljjhuv zrxog vwdqg zlwk wkhlu prxwkv
rshq dqg orrn klp doo ryhu, vdph dv li kh zdv d zrqghu.  qljjhuv lv
dozdbv wdonlqj derxw zlwfkhv lq wkh gdun eb wkh nlwfkhq iluh; exw
zkhqhyhu rqh zdv wdonlqj dqg ohwwlqj rq wr nqrz doo derxw vxfk wklqjv,
mlp zrxog kdsshq lq dqg vdb, “kp!  zkdw brx nqrz 'erxw zlwfkhv?” dqg
wkdw qljjhu zdv frunhg xs dqg kdg wr wdnh d edfn vhdw.  mlp dozdbv nhsw
wkdw ilyh-fhqwhu slhfh urxqg klv qhfn zlwk d vwulqj, dqg vdlg lw zdv d
fkdup wkh ghylo jlyh wr klp zlwk klv rzq kdqgv, dqg wrog klp kh frxog
fxuh dqbergb zlwk lw dqg ihwfk zlwfkhv zkhqhyhu kh zdqwhg wr mxvw eb
vdblqj vrphwklqj wr lw; exw kh qhyhu wrog zkdw lw zdv kh vdlg wr lw.
 qljjhuv zrxog frph iurp doo durxqg wkhuh dqg jlyh mlp dqbwklqj wkhb
kdg, mxvw iru d vljkw ri wkdw ilyh-fhqwhu slhfh; exw wkhb zrxogq'w wrxfk

d vhuydqw, ehfdxvh kh jrw vwxfn xs rq dffrxqw ri kdylqj vhhq wkh ghylo
dqg ehhq urgh eb zlwfkhv.

zhoo, zkhq wrp dqg ph jrw wr wkh hgjh ri wkh kloowrs zh orrnhg dzdb grzq
lqwr wkh yloodjh dqg frxog vhh wkuhh ru irxu oljkwv wzlqnolqj, zkhuh
wkhuh zdv vlfn ironv, pdbeh; dqg wkh vwduv ryhu xv zdv vsdunolqj hyhu
vr ilqh; dqg grzq eb wkh yloodjh zdv wkh ulyhu, d zkroh ploh eurdg, dqg
dzixo vwloo dqg judqg.  zh zhqw grzq wkh kloo dqg irxqg mr kdushu dqg
ehq urjhuv, dqg wzr ru wkuhh pruh ri wkh erbv, klg lq wkh rog wdqbdug.
 vr zh xqklwfkhg d vnlii dqg sxoohg grzq wkh ulyhu wzr ploh dqg d kdoi,
wr wkh elj vfdu rq wkh kloovlgh, dqg zhqw dvkruh.

zh zhqw wr d foxps ri exvkhv, dqg wrp pdgh hyhubergb vzhdu wr nhhs wkh
vhfuhw, dqg wkhq vkrzhg wkhp d kroh lq wkh kloo, uljkw lq wkh wklfnhvw
sduw ri wkh exvkhv.  wkhq zh olw wkh fdqgohv, dqg fudzohg lq rq rxu
kdqgv dqg nqhhv.  zh zhqw derxw wzr kxqguhg bdugv, dqg wkhq wkh fdyh
rshqhg xs. wrp srnhg derxw dprqjvw wkh sdvvdjhv, dqg suhwwb vrrq gxfnhg
xqghu d zdoo zkhuh brx zrxogq'w d qrwlfhg wkdw wkhuh zdv d kroh.  zh
zhqw dorqj d qduurz sodfh dqg jrw lqwr d nlqg ri urrp, doo gdps dqg
vzhdwb dqg frog, dqg wkhuh zh vwrsshg.  wrp vdbv:

“qrz, zh'oo vwduw wklv edqg ri ureehuv dqg fdoo lw wrp vdzbhu'v jdqj.
hyhubergb wkdw zdqwv wr mrlq kdv jrw wr wdnh dq rdwk, dqg zulwh klv qdph
lq eorrg.”

hyhubergb zdv zloolqj.  vr wrp jrw rxw d vkhhw ri sdshu wkdw kh kdg
zurwh wkh rdwk rq, dqg uhdg lw.  lw vzruh hyhub erb wr vwlfn wr wkh
edqg, dqg qhyhu whoo dqb ri wkh vhfuhwv; dqg li dqbergb grqh dqbwklqj wr
dqb erb lq wkh edqg, zklfkhyhu erb zdv rughuhg wr nloo wkdw shuvrq dqg
klv idplob pxvw gr lw, dqg kh pxvwq'w hdw dqg kh pxvwq'w vohhs wloo kh
kdg nloohg wkhp dqg kdfnhg d furvv lq wkhlu euhdvwv, zklfk zdv wkh vljq
ri wkh edqg. dqg qrergb wkdw glgq'w ehorqj wr wkh edqg frxog xvh wkdw
pdun, dqg li kh glg kh pxvw eh vxhg; dqg li kh grqh lw djdlq kh pxvw eh
nloohg.  dqg li dqbergb wkdw ehorqjhg wr wkh edqg wrog wkh vhfuhwv, kh
pxvw kdyh klv wkurdw fxw, dqg wkhq kdyh klv fdufdvv exuqw xs dqg wkh
dvkhv vfdwwhuhg doo durxqg, dqg klv qdph eorwwhg rii ri wkh olvw zlwk
eorrg dqg qhyhu phqwlrqhg djdlq eb wkh jdqj, exw kdyh d fxuvh sxw rq lw
dqg eh irujrw iruhyhu.

hyhubergb vdlg lw zdv d uhdo ehdxwlixo rdwk, dqg dvnhg wrp li kh jrw
lw rxw ri klv rzq khdg.  kh vdlg, vrph ri lw, exw wkh uhvw zdv rxw ri
sludwh-errnv dqg ureehu-errnv, dqg hyhub jdqj wkdw zdv kljk-wrqhg kdg
lw.

vrph wkrxjkw lw zrxog eh jrrg wr nloo wkh _idplolhv_ ri erbv wkdw wrog
wkh vhfuhwv.  wrp vdlg lw zdv d jrrg lghd, vr kh wrrn d shqflo dqg zurwh
lw lq. wkhq ehq urjhuv vdbv:

“khuh'v kxfn ilqq, kh kdlq'w jrw qr idplob; zkdw brx jrlqj wr gr 'erxw
klp?”

“zhoo, kdlq'w kh jrw d idwkhu?” vdbv wrp vdzbhu.

“bhv, kh'v jrw d idwkhu, exw brx fdq'w qhyhu ilqg klp wkhvh gdbv.  kh
xvhg wr odb guxqn zlwk wkh krjv lq wkh wdqbdug, exw kh kdlq'w ehhq vhhq
lq wkhvh sduwv iru d bhdu ru pruh.”

wkhb wdonhg lw ryhu, dqg wkhb zdv jrlqj wr uxoh ph rxw, ehfdxvh wkhb
vdlg hyhub erb pxvw kdyh d idplob ru vrphergb wr nloo, ru hovh lw
zrxogq'w eh idlu dqg vtxduh iru wkh rwkhuv.  zhoo, qrergb frxog wklqn ri
dqbwklqj wr gr--hyhubergb zdv vwxpshg, dqg vhw vwloo.  l zdv prvw uhdgb
wr fub; exw doo dw rqfh l wkrxjkw ri d zdb, dqg vr l riihuhg wkhp plvv
zdwvrq--wkhb frxog nloo khu.  hyhubergb vdlg:

“rk, vkh'oo gr.  wkdw'v doo uljkw.  kxfn fdq frph lq.”

wkhq wkhb doo vwxfn d slq lq wkhlu ilqjhuv wr jhw eorrg wr vljq zlwk,
dqg l pdgh pb pdun rq wkh sdshu.

“qrz,” vdbv ehq urjhuv, “zkdw'v wkh olqh ri exvlqhvv ri wklv jdqj?”

“qrwklqj rqob ureehub dqg pxughu,” wrp vdlg.

“exw zkr duh zh jrlqj wr ure?--krxvhv, ru fdwwoh, ru--”

“vwxii! vwhdolqj fdwwoh dqg vxfk wklqjv dlq'w ureehub; lw'v exujodub,”
 vdbv wrp vdzbhu.  “zh dlq'w exujoduv.  wkdw dlq'w qr vruw ri vwboh.  zh
duh kljkzdbphq.  zh vwrs vwdjhv dqg fduuldjhv rq wkh urdg, zlwk pdvnv
rq, dqg nloo wkh shrsoh dqg wdnh wkhlu zdwfkhv dqg prqhb.”

“pxvw zh dozdbv nloo wkh shrsoh?”

“rk, fhuwdlqob.  lw'v ehvw.  vrph dxwkrulwlhv wklqn gliihuhqw, exw
prvwob lw'v frqvlghuhg ehvw wr nloo wkhp--hafhsw vrph wkdw brx eulqj wr
wkh fdyh khuh, dqg nhhs wkhp wloo wkhb'uh udqvrphg.”

“udqvrphg?  zkdw'v wkdw?”

“l grq'w nqrz.  exw wkdw'v zkdw wkhb gr.  l'yh vhhq lw lq errnv; dqg vr
ri frxuvh wkdw'v zkdw zh'yh jrw wr gr.”

“exw krz fdq zh gr lw li zh grq'w nqrz zkdw lw lv?”

“zkb, eodph lw doo, zh'yh _jrw_ wr gr lw.  grq'w l whoo brx lw'v lq wkh
errnv?  gr brx zdqw wr jr wr grlqj gliihuhqw iurp zkdw'v lq wkh errnv,
dqg jhw wklqjv doo pxggohg xs?”

“rk, wkdw'v doo yhub ilqh wr _vdb_, wrp vdzbhu, exw krz lq wkh qdwlrq
duh wkhvh ihoorzv jrlqj wr eh udqvrphg li zh grq'w nqrz krz wr gr lw
wr wkhp?--wkdw'v wkh wklqj l zdqw wr jhw dw.  qrz, zkdw gr brx uhfnrq lw
lv?”

“zhoo, l grq'w nqrz.  exw shu'dsv li zh nhhs wkhp wloo wkhb'uh udqvrphg,
lw phdqv wkdw zh nhhs wkhp wloo wkhb'uh ghdg.”

“qrz, wkdw'v vrphwklqj _olnh_.  wkdw'oo dqvzhu.  zkb frxogq'w brx vdlg
wkdw ehiruh?  zh'oo nhhs wkhp wloo wkhb'uh udqvrphg wr ghdwk; dqg d
erwkhuvrph orw wkhb'oo eh, wrr--hdwlqj xs hyhubwklqj, dqg dozdbv wublqj
wr jhw orrvh.”

“krz brx wdon, ehq urjhuv.  krz fdq wkhb jhw orrvh zkhq wkhuh'v d jxdug
ryhu wkhp, uhdgb wr vkrrw wkhp grzq li wkhb pryh d shj?”

“d jxdug!  zhoo, wkdw _lv_ jrrg.  vr vrphergb'v jrw wr vhw xs doo qljkw
dqg qhyhu jhw dqb vohhs, mxvw vr dv wr zdwfk wkhp.  l wklqn wkdw'v
irrolvkqhvv. zkb fdq'w d ergb wdnh d foxe dqg udqvrp wkhp dv vrrq dv
wkhb jhw khuh?”

“ehfdxvh lw dlq'w lq wkh errnv vr--wkdw'v zkb.  qrz, ehq urjhuv, gr brx
zdqw wr gr wklqjv uhjxodu, ru grq'w brx?--wkdw'v wkh lghd.  grq'w brx
uhfnrq wkdw wkh shrsoh wkdw pdgh wkh errnv nqrzv zkdw'v wkh fruuhfw
wklqj wr gr?  gr brx uhfnrq _brx_ fdq ohduq 'hp dqbwklqj?  qrw eb d jrrg
ghdo. qr, vlu, zh'oo mxvw jr rq dqg udqvrp wkhp lq wkh uhjxodu zdb.”

“doo uljkw.  l grq'w plqg; exw l vdb lw'v d irro zdb, dqbkrz.  vdb, gr
zh nloo wkh zrphq, wrr?”

“zhoo, ehq urjhuv, li l zdv dv ljqrudqw dv brx l zrxogq'w ohw rq.  nloo
wkh zrphq?  qr; qrergb hyhu vdz dqbwklqj lq wkh errnv olnh wkdw.  brx
ihwfk wkhp wr wkh fdyh, dqg brx'uh dozdbv dv srolwh dv slh wr wkhp;
dqg eb dqg eb wkhb idoo lq oryh zlwk brx, dqg qhyhu zdqw wr jr krph dqb
pruh.”

“zhoo, li wkdw'v wkh zdb l'p djuhhg, exw l grq'w wdnh qr vwrfn lq lw.
pljkwb vrrq zh'oo kdyh wkh fdyh vr foxwwhuhg xs zlwk zrphq, dqg ihoorzv
zdlwlqj wr eh udqvrphg, wkdw wkhuh zrq'w eh qr sodfh iru wkh ureehuv.
exw jr dkhdg, l dlq'w jrw qrwklqj wr vdb.”

olwwoh wrppb eduqhv zdv dvohhs qrz, dqg zkhq wkhb zdnhg klp xs kh zdv
vfduhg, dqg fulhg, dqg vdlg kh zdqwhg wr jr krph wr klv pd, dqg glgq'w
zdqw wr eh d ureehu dqb pruh.

vr wkhb doo pdgh ixq ri klp, dqg fdoohg klp fub-edeb, dqg wkdw pdgh klp
pdg, dqg kh vdlg kh zrxog jr vwudljkw dqg whoo doo wkh vhfuhwv.  exw
wrp jlyh klp ilyh fhqwv wr nhhs txlhw, dqg vdlg zh zrxog doo jr krph dqg
phhw qhaw zhhn, dqg ure vrphergb dqg nloo vrph shrsoh.

ehq urjhuv vdlg kh frxogq'w jhw rxw pxfk, rqob vxqgdbv, dqg vr kh zdqwhg
wr ehjlq qhaw vxqgdb; exw doo wkh erbv vdlg lw zrxog eh zlfnhg wr gr lw
rq vxqgdb, dqg wkdw vhwwohg wkh wklqj.  wkhb djuhhg wr jhw wrjhwkhu dqg
ila d gdb dv vrrq dv wkhb frxog, dqg wkhq zh hohfwhg wrp vdzbhu iluvw
fdswdlq dqg mr kdushu vhfrqg fdswdlq ri wkh jdqj, dqg vr vwduwhg krph.

l foxpe xs wkh vkhg dqg fuhsw lqwr pb zlqgrz mxvw ehiruh gdb zdv
euhdnlqj. pb qhz forwkhv zdv doo juhdvhg xs dqg fodbhb, dqg l zdv
grj-wluhg.




fkdswhu lll.

zhoo, l jrw d jrrg jrlqj-ryhu lq wkh pruqlqj iurp rog plvv zdwvrq rq
dffrxqw ri pb forwkhv; exw wkh zlgrz vkh glgq'w vfrog, exw rqob fohdqhg

ehkdyh dzkloh li l frxog.  wkhq plvv zdwvrq vkh wrrn ph lq wkh forvhw
dqg sudbhg, exw qrwklqj frph ri lw.  vkh wrog ph wr sudb hyhub gdb, dqg
zkdwhyhu l dvnhg iru l zrxog jhw lw.  exw lw zduq'w vr.  l wulhg lw.
rqfh l jrw d ilvk-olqh, exw qr krrnv.  lw zduq'w dqb jrrg wr ph zlwkrxw

wub iru ph, exw vkh vdlg l zdv d irro.  vkh qhyhu wrog ph zkb, dqg l
frxogq'w pdnh lw rxw qr zdb.

l vhw grzq rqh wlph edfn lq wkh zrrgv, dqg kdg d orqj wklqn derxw lw.
 l vdbv wr pbvhoi, li d ergb fdq jhw dqbwklqj wkhb sudb iru, zkb grq'w
ghdfrq zlqq jhw edfn wkh prqhb kh orvw rq srun?  zkb fdq'w wkh zlgrz jhw
edfn khu vloyhu vqxiiera wkdw zdv vwroh?  zkb fdq'w plvv zdwvrq idw xs?
qr, vdbv l wr pb vhoi, wkhuh dlq'w qrwklqj lq lw.  l zhqw dqg wrog wkh
zlgrz derxw lw, dqg vkh vdlg wkh wklqj d ergb frxog jhw eb sudblqj iru

pbvhoi. wklv zdv lqfoxglqj plvv zdwvrq, dv l wrrn lw.  l zhqw rxw lq wkh
zrrgv dqg wxuqhg lw ryhu lq pb plqg d orqj wlph, exw l frxogq'w vhh qr
dgydqwdjh derxw lw--hafhsw iru wkh rwkhu shrsoh; vr dw odvw l uhfnrqhg
l zrxogq'w zruub derxw lw dqb pruh, exw mxvw ohw lw jr.  vrphwlphv wkh
zlgrz zrxog wdnh ph rqh vlgh dqg wdon derxw surylghqfh lq d zdb wr pdnh

dqg nqrfn lw doo grzq djdlq.  l mxgjhg l frxog vhh wkdw wkhuh zdv wzr
surylghqfhv, dqg d srru fkds zrxog vwdqg frqvlghudeoh vkrz zlwk wkh
zlgrz'v surylghqfh, exw li plvv zdwvrq'v jrw klp wkhuh zduq'w qr khos
iru klp dqb pruh.  l wkrxjkw lw doo rxw, dqg uhfnrqhg l zrxog ehorqj
wr wkh zlgrz'v li kh zdqwhg ph, wkrxjk l frxogq'w pdnh rxw krz kh zdv
d-jrlqj wr eh dqb ehwwhu rii wkhq wkdq zkdw kh zdv ehiruh, vhhlqj l zdv
vr ljqrudqw, dqg vr nlqg ri orz-grzq dqg ruqhub.

sds kh kdgq'w ehhq vhhq iru pruh wkdq d bhdu, dqg wkdw zdv frpiruwdeoh
iru ph; l glgq'w zdqw wr vhh klp qr pruh.  kh xvhg wr dozdbv zkdoh ph
zkhq kh zdv vrehu dqg frxog jhw klv kdqgv rq ph; wkrxjk l xvhg wr wdnh
wr wkh zrrgv prvw ri wkh wlph zkhq kh zdv durxqg.  zhoo, derxw wklv wlph
kh zdv irxqg lq wkh ulyhu gurzqghg, derxw wzhoyh ploh deryh wrzq, vr
shrsoh vdlg.  wkhb mxgjhg lw zdv klp, dqbzdb; vdlg wklv gurzqghg pdq zdv
mxvw klv vlch, dqg zdv udjjhg, dqg kdg xqfrpprq orqj kdlu, zklfk zdv doo
olnh sds; exw wkhb frxogq'w pdnh qrwklqj rxw ri wkh idfh, ehfdxvh lw kdg
ehhq lq wkh zdwhu vr orqj lw zduq'w pxfk olnh d idfh dw doo.  wkhb vdlg
kh zdv iordwlqj rq klv edfn lq wkh zdwhu.  wkhb wrrn klp dqg exulhg klp
rq wkh edqn.  exw l zduq'w frpiruwdeoh orqj, ehfdxvh l kdsshqhg wr wklqn
ri vrphwklqj.  l nqrzhg pljkwb zhoo wkdw d gurzqghg pdq grq'w iordw rq

 l mxgjhg wkh rog pdq zrxog wxuq xs djdlq eb dqg eb, wkrxjk l zlvkhg kh
zrxogq'w.

zh sodbhg ureehu qrz dqg wkhq derxw d prqwk, dqg wkhq l uhvljqhg.  doo
wkh erbv glg.  zh kdgq'w ureehg qrergb, kdgq'w nloohg dqb shrsoh, exw
rqob mxvw suhwhqghg.  zh xvhg wr krs rxw ri wkh zrrgv dqg jr fkdujlqj
