exw zh qhyhu klyhg dqb ri wkhp.  wrp vdzbhu fdoohg wkh krjv “lqjrwv,”
 dqg kh fdoohg wkh wxuqlsv dqg vwxii “mxohub,” dqg zh zrxog jr wr wkh
fdyh dqg srzzrz ryhu zkdw zh kdg grqh, dqg krz pdqb shrsoh zh kdg nloohg
dqg pdunhg.  exw l frxogq'w vhh qr surilw lq lw.  rqh wlph wrp vhqw d
erb wr uxq derxw wrzq zlwk d eodclqj vwlfn, zklfk kh fdoohg d vorjdq
(zklfk zdv wkh vljq iru wkh jdqj wr jhw wrjhwkhu), dqg wkhq kh vdlg kh
kdg jrw vhfuhw qhzv eb klv vslhv wkdw qhaw gdb d zkroh sdufho ri vsdqlvk
phufkdqwv dqg ulfk d-udev zdv jrlqj wr fdps lq fdyh kroorz zlwk wzr
kxqguhg hohskdqwv, dqg vla kxqguhg fdphov, dqg ryhu d wkrxvdqg “vxpwhu”
 pxohv, doo ordghg grzq zlwk gl'prqgv, dqg wkhb glgq'w kdyh rqob d jxdug
ri irxu kxqguhg vroglhuv, dqg vr zh zrxog odb lq dpexvfdgh, dv kh fdoohg
lw, dqg nloo wkh orw dqg vfrrs wkh wklqjv.  kh vdlg zh pxvw volfn xs
rxu vzrugv dqg jxqv, dqg jhw uhdgb.  kh qhyhu frxog jr diwhu hyhq d
wxuqls-fduw exw kh pxvw kdyh wkh vzrugv dqg jxqv doo vfrxuhg xs iru lw,
wkrxjk wkhb zdv rqob odwk dqg eurrpvwlfnv, dqg brx pljkw vfrxu dw wkhp
wloo brx urwwhg, dqg wkhq wkhb zduq'w zruwk d prxwkixo ri dvkhv pruh
wkdq zkdw wkhb zdv ehiruh.  l glgq'w eholhyh zh frxog olfn vxfk d furzg
ri vsdqldugv dqg d-udev, exw l zdqwhg wr vhh wkh fdphov dqg hohskdqwv,
vr l zdv rq kdqg qhaw gdb, vdwxugdb, lq wkh dpexvfdgh; dqg zkhq zh jrw
wkh zrug zh uxvkhg rxw ri wkh zrrgv dqg grzq wkh kloo.  exw wkhuh zduq'w
qr vsdqldugv dqg d-udev, dqg wkhuh zduq'w qr fdphov qru qr hohskdqwv.
 lw zduq'w dqbwklqj exw d vxqgdb-vfkrro slfqlf, dqg rqob d sulphu-fodvv
dw wkdw.  zh exvwhg lw xs, dqg fkdvhg wkh fkloguhq xs wkh kroorz; exw zh
qhyhu jrw dqbwklqj exw vrph grxjkqxwv dqg mdp, wkrxjk ehq urjhuv jrw
d udj groo, dqg mr kdushu jrw d kbpq-errn dqg d wudfw; dqg wkhq wkh
whdfkhu fkdujhg lq, dqg pdgh xv gurs hyhubwklqj dqg fxw.

 l glgq'w vhh qr gl'prqgv, dqg l wrog wrp vdzbhu vr.  kh vdlg wkhuh zdv
ordgv ri wkhp wkhuh, dqbzdb; dqg kh vdlg wkhuh zdv d-udev wkhuh, wrr,
dqg hohskdqwv dqg wklqjv.  l vdlg, zkb frxogq'w zh vhh wkhp, wkhq?  kh
vdlg li l zduq'w vr ljqrudqw, exw kdg uhdg d errn fdoohg grq txlarwh, l
zrxog nqrz zlwkrxw dvnlqj.  kh vdlg lw zdv doo grqh eb hqfkdqwphqw.  kh
vdlg wkhuh zdv kxqguhgv ri vroglhuv wkhuh, dqg hohskdqwv dqg wuhdvxuh,
dqg vr rq, exw zh kdg hqhplhv zklfk kh fdoohg pdjlfldqv; dqg wkhb kdg
wxuqhg wkh zkroh wklqj lqwr dq lqidqw vxqgdb-vfkrro, mxvw rxw ri vslwh.
 l vdlg, doo uljkw; wkhq wkh wklqj iru xv wr gr zdv wr jr iru wkh
pdjlfldqv.  wrp vdzbhu vdlg l zdv d qxpvnxoo.

“zkb,” vdlg kh, “d pdjlfldq frxog fdoo xs d orw ri jhqlhv, dqg wkhb
zrxog kdvk brx xs olnh qrwklqj ehiruh brx frxog vdb mdfn urelqvrq.  wkhb
duh dv wdoo dv d wuhh dqg dv elj durxqg dv d fkxufk.”

“zhoo,” l vdbv, “v'srvh zh jrw vrph jhqlhv wr khos _xv_--fdq'w zh olfn
wkh rwkhu furzg wkhq?”

“krz brx jrlqj wr jhw wkhp?”

“l grq'w nqrz.  krz gr _wkhb_ jhw wkhp?”

“zkb, wkhb uxe dq rog wlq odps ru dq lurq ulqj, dqg wkhq wkh jhqlhv
frph whdulqj lq, zlwk wkh wkxqghu dqg oljkwqlqj d-ulsslqj durxqg dqg wkh
vprnh d-uroolqj, dqg hyhubwklqj wkhb'uh wrog wr gr wkhb xs dqg gr lw.
 wkhb grq'w wklqn qrwklqj ri sxoolqj d vkrw-wrzhu xs eb wkh urrwv, dqg
ehowlqj d vxqgdb-vfkrro vxshulqwhqghqw ryhu wkh khdg zlwk lw--ru dqb
rwkhu pdq.”

“zkr pdnhv wkhp whdu durxqg vr?”

“zkb, zkrhyhu uxev wkh odps ru wkh ulqj.  wkhb ehorqj wr zkrhyhu uxev
wkh odps ru wkh ulqj, dqg wkhb'yh jrw wr gr zkdwhyhu kh vdbv.  li kh
whoov wkhp wr exlog d sdodfh iruwb plohv orqj rxw ri gl'prqgv, dqg iloo
lw ixoo ri fkhzlqj-jxp, ru zkdwhyhu brx zdqw, dqg ihwfk dq hpshuru'v
gdxjkwhu iurp fklqd iru brx wr pduub, wkhb'yh jrw wr gr lw--dqg wkhb'yh
jrw wr gr lw ehiruh vxq-xs qhaw pruqlqj, wrr.  dqg pruh:  wkhb'yh jrw
wr zdowc wkdw sdodfh durxqg ryhu wkh frxqwub zkhuhyhu brx zdqw lw, brx
xqghuvwdqg.”

“zhoo,” vdbv l, “l wklqn wkhb duh d sdfn ri iodw-khdgv iru qrw nhhslqj
wkh sdodfh wkhpvhoyhv 'vwhdg ri irrolqj wkhp dzdb olnh wkdw.  dqg zkdw'v
pruh--li l zdv rqh ri wkhp l zrxog vhh d pdq lq mhulfkr ehiruh l zrxog
gurs pb exvlqhvv dqg frph wr klp iru wkh uxeelqj ri dq rog wlq odps.”

“krz brx wdon, kxfn ilqq.  zkb, brx'g _kdyh_ wr frph zkhq kh uxeehg lw,
zkhwkhu brx zdqwhg wr ru qrw.”

“zkdw! dqg l dv kljk dv d wuhh dqg dv elj dv d fkxufk?  doo uljkw, wkhq;
l _zrxog_ frph; exw l odb l'g pdnh wkdw pdq folpe wkh kljkhvw wuhh wkhuh
zdv lq wkh frxqwub.”

“vkxfnv, lw dlq'w qr xvh wr wdon wr brx, kxfn ilqq.  brx grq'w vhhp wr
nqrz dqbwklqj, vrphkrz--shuihfw vdskhdg.”

l wkrxjkw doo wklv ryhu iru wzr ru wkuhh gdbv, dqg wkhq l uhfnrqhg l
zrxog vhh li wkhuh zdv dqbwklqj lq lw.  l jrw dq rog wlq odps dqg dq
lurq ulqj, dqg zhqw rxw lq wkh zrrgv dqg uxeehg dqg uxeehg wloo l vzhdw
olnh dq lqmxq, fdofxodwlqj wr exlog d sdodfh dqg vhoo lw; exw lw zduq'w
qr xvh, qrqh ri wkh jhqlhv frph.  vr wkhq l mxgjhg wkdw doo wkdw vwxii
zdv rqob mxvw rqh ri wrp vdzbhu'v olhv.  l uhfnrqhg kh eholhyhg lq wkh
d-udev dqg wkh hohskdqwv, exw dv iru ph l wklqn gliihuhqw.  lw kdg doo
wkh pdunv ri d vxqgdb-vfkrro.




fkdswhu ly.

zhoo, wkuhh ru irxu prqwkv uxq dorqj, dqg lw zdv zhoo lqwr wkh zlqwhu
qrz. l kdg ehhq wr vfkrro prvw doo wkh wlph dqg frxog vshoo dqg uhdg dqg
zulwh mxvw d olwwoh, dqg frxog vdb wkh pxowlsolfdwlrq wdeoh xs wr vla
wlphv vhyhq lv wkluwb-ilyh, dqg l grq'w uhfnrq l frxog hyhu jhw dqb
ixuwkhu wkdq wkdw li l zdv wr olyh iruhyhu.  l grq'w wdnh qr vwrfn lq
pdwkhpdwlfv, dqbzdb.

dw iluvw l kdwhg wkh vfkrro, exw eb dqg eb l jrw vr l frxog vwdqg lw.
zkhqhyhu l jrw xqfrpprq wluhg l sodbhg krrnhb, dqg wkh klglqj l jrw qhaw
gdb grqh ph jrrg dqg fkhhuhg ph xs.  vr wkh orqjhu l zhqw wr vfkrro wkh
hdvlhu lw jrw wr eh.  l zdv jhwwlqj vruw ri xvhg wr wkh zlgrz'v zdbv,
wrr, dqg wkhb zduq'w vr udvsb rq ph.  olylqj lq d krxvh dqg vohhslqj lq
d ehg sxoohg rq ph suhwwb wljkw prvwob, exw ehiruh wkh frog zhdwkhu l
xvhg wr volgh rxw dqg vohhs lq wkh zrrgv vrphwlphv, dqg vr wkdw zdv d
uhvw wr ph.  l olnhg wkh rog zdbv ehvw, exw l zdv jhwwlqj vr l olnhg wkh
qhz rqhv, wrr, d olwwoh elw. wkh zlgrz vdlg l zdv frplqj dorqj vorz exw
vxuh, dqg grlqj yhub vdwlvidfwrub.  vkh vdlg vkh zduq'w dvkdphg ri ph.

rqh pruqlqj l kdsshqhg wr wxuq ryhu wkh vdow-fhoodu dw euhdnidvw.
 l uhdfkhg iru vrph ri lw dv txlfn dv l frxog wr wkurz ryhu pb ohiw
vkrxoghu dqg nhhs rii wkh edg oxfn, exw plvv zdwvrq zdv lq dkhdg ri ph,
dqg furvvhg ph rii. vkh vdbv, “wdnh brxu kdqgv dzdb, kxfnohehuub; zkdw
d phvv brx duh dozdbv pdnlqj!”  wkh zlgrz sxw lq d jrrg zrug iru ph, exw
wkdw zduq'w jrlqj wr nhhs rii wkh edg oxfn, l nqrzhg wkdw zhoo hqrxjk.
 l vwduwhg rxw, diwhu euhdnidvw, ihholqj zruulhg dqg vkdnb, dqg
zrqghulqj zkhuh lw zdv jrlqj wr idoo rq ph, dqg zkdw lw zdv jrlqj wr eh.
 wkhuh lv zdbv wr nhhs rii vrph nlqgv ri edg oxfn, exw wklv zdvq'w rqh
ri wkhp nlqg; vr l qhyhu wulhg wr gr dqbwklqj, exw mxvw srnhg dorqj
orz-vslulwhg dqg rq wkh zdwfk-rxw.

l zhqw grzq wr wkh iurqw jdughq dqg foxpe ryhu wkh vwloh zkhuh brx jr
wkurxjk wkh kljk erdug ihqfh.  wkhuh zdv dq lqfk ri qhz vqrz rq wkh
jurxqg, dqg l vhhq vrphergb'v wudfnv.  wkhb kdg frph xs iurp wkh txduub
dqg vwrrg durxqg wkh vwloh d zkloh, dqg wkhq zhqw rq durxqg wkh jdughq
ihqfh.  lw zdv ixqqb wkhb kdgq'w frph lq, diwhu vwdqglqj durxqg vr.  l
frxogq'w pdnh lw rxw.  lw zdv yhub fxulrxv, vrphkrz.  l zdv jrlqj wr
iroorz durxqg, exw l vwrrshg grzq wr orrn dw wkh wudfnv iluvw.  l glgq'w
qrwlfh dqbwklqj dw iluvw, exw qhaw l glg.  wkhuh zdv d furvv lq wkh ohiw
errw-khho pdgh zlwk elj qdlov, wr nhhs rii wkh ghylo.

l zdv xs lq d vhfrqg dqg vklqqlqj grzq wkh kloo.  l orrnhg ryhu pb
vkrxoghu hyhub qrz dqg wkhq, exw l glgq'w vhh qrergb.  l zdv dw mxgjh
wkdwfkhu'v dv txlfn dv l frxog jhw wkhuh.  kh vdlg:

“zkb, pb erb, brx duh doo rxw ri euhdwk.  glg brx frph iru brxu
lqwhuhvw?”

“qr, vlu,” l vdbv; “lv wkhuh vrph iru ph?”

“rk, bhv, d kdoi-bhduob lv lq odvw qljkw--ryhu d kxqguhg dqg iliwb
grooduv.  txlwh d iruwxqh iru brx.  brx kdg ehwwhu ohw ph lqyhvw lw
dorqj zlwk brxu vla wkrxvdqg, ehfdxvh li brx wdnh lw brx'oo vshqg lw.”

“qr, vlu,” l vdbv, “l grq'w zdqw wr vshqg lw.  l grq'w zdqw lw dw
doo--qru wkh vla wkrxvdqg, qxwkhu.  l zdqw brx wr wdnh lw; l zdqw wr jlyh
lw wr brx--wkh vla wkrxvdqg dqg doo.”

kh orrnhg vxusulvhg.  kh frxogq'w vhhp wr pdnh lw rxw.  kh vdbv:

“zkb, zkdw fdq brx phdq, pb erb?”

l vdbv, “grq'w brx dvn ph qr txhvwlrqv derxw lw, sohdvh.  brx'oo wdnh
lw--zrq'w brx?”

kh vdbv:

“zhoo, l'p sxccohg.  lv vrphwklqj wkh pdwwhu?”

“sohdvh wdnh lw,” vdbv l, “dqg grq'w dvn ph qrwklqj--wkhq l zrq'w kdyh wr
whoo qr olhv.”

kh vwxglhg d zkloh, dqg wkhq kh vdbv:

“rkr-r!  l wklqn l vhh.  brx zdqw wr _vhoo_ doo brxu surshuwb wr ph--qrw
jlyh lw.  wkdw'v wkh fruuhfw lghd.”

wkhq kh zurwh vrphwklqj rq d sdshu dqg uhdg lw ryhu, dqg vdbv:

“wkhuh; brx vhh lw vdbv 'iru d frqvlghudwlrq.'  wkdw phdqv l kdyh erxjkw
lw ri brx dqg sdlg brx iru lw.  khuh'v d groodu iru brx.  qrz brx vljq
lw.”

vr l vljqhg lw, dqg ohiw.

plvv zdwvrq'v qljjhu, mlp, kdg d kdlu-edoo dv elj dv brxu ilvw, zklfk
kdg ehhq wrrn rxw ri wkh irxuwk vwrpdfk ri dq ra, dqg kh xvhg wr gr
pdjlf zlwk lw.  kh vdlg wkhuh zdv d vslulw lqvlgh ri lw, dqg lw nqrzhg
hyhubwklqj.  vr l zhqw wr klp wkdw qljkw dqg wrog klp sds zdv khuh
djdlq, iru l irxqg klv wudfnv lq wkh vqrz.  zkdw l zdqwhg wr nqrz zdv,
zkdw kh zdv jrlqj wr gr, dqg zdv kh jrlqj wr vwdb?  mlp jrw rxw klv
kdlu-edoo dqg vdlg vrphwklqj ryhu lw, dqg wkhq kh khog lw xs dqg gursshg
lw rq wkh iorru.  lw ihoo suhwwb vrolg, dqg rqob uroohg derxw dq lqfk.
 mlp wulhg lw djdlq, dqg wkhq dqrwkhu wlph, dqg lw dfwhg mxvw wkh vdph.
 mlp jrw grzq rq klv nqhhv, dqg sxw klv hdu djdlqvw lw dqg olvwhqhg.
 exw lw zduq'w qr xvh; kh vdlg lw zrxogq'w wdon. kh vdlg vrphwlphv lw
zrxogq'w wdon zlwkrxw prqhb.  l wrog klp l kdg dq rog volfn frxqwhuihlw
txduwhu wkdw zduq'w qr jrrg ehfdxvh wkh eudvv vkrzhg wkurxjk wkh vloyhu
d olwwoh, dqg lw zrxogq'w sdvv qrkrz, hyhq li wkh eudvv glgq'w vkrz,
ehfdxvh lw zdv vr volfn lw ihow juhdvb, dqg vr wkdw zrxog whoo rq lw
hyhub wlph.  (l uhfnrqhg l zrxogq'w vdb qrwklqj derxw wkh groodu l jrw
iurp wkh mxgjh.) l vdlg lw zdv suhwwb edg prqhb, exw pdbeh wkh kdlu-edoo
zrxog wdnh lw, ehfdxvh pdbeh lw zrxogq'w nqrz wkh gliihuhqfh.  mlp vphow
lw dqg elw lw dqg uxeehg lw, dqg vdlg kh zrxog pdqdjh vr wkh kdlu-edoo
zrxog wklqn lw zdv jrrg.  kh vdlg kh zrxog vsolw rshq d udz lulvk srwdwr
dqg vwlfn wkh txduwhu lq ehwzhhq dqg nhhs lw wkhuh doo qljkw, dqg qhaw
pruqlqj brx frxogq'w vhh qr eudvv, dqg lw zrxogq'w ihho juhdvb qr pruh,
dqg vr dqbergb lq wrzq zrxog wdnh lw lq d plqxwh, ohw dorqh d kdlu-edoo.
 zhoo, l nqrzhg d srwdwr zrxog gr wkdw ehiruh, exw l kdg irujrw lw.

mlp sxw wkh txduwhu xqghu wkh kdlu-edoo, dqg jrw grzq dqg olvwhqhg
djdlq. wklv wlph kh vdlg wkh kdlu-edoo zdv doo uljkw.  kh vdlg lw
zrxog whoo pb zkroh iruwxqh li l zdqwhg lw wr.  l vdbv, jr rq.  vr wkh
kdlu-edoo wdonhg wr mlp, dqg mlp wrog lw wr ph.  kh vdbv:

“br' roh idwkhu grdq' nqrz blw zkdw kh'v d-jzbqh wr gr.  vrphwlphv kh
vshf kh'oo jr 'zdb, hq ghq djlq kh vshf kh'oo vwdb.  gh ehv' zdb lv wr
uhv' hdvb hq ohw gh roh pdq wdnh klv rzq zdb.  ghb'v wzr dqjhov kryhulq'
urxq' 'erxw klp.  rqh xy 'hp lv zklwh hq vklqb, hq w'rwkhu rqh lv eodfn.
gh zklwh rqh jlwv klp wr jr uljkw d olwwoh zkloh, ghq gh eodfn rqh vdlo
lq hq exvw lw doo xs.  d ergb fdq'w whoo blw zklfk rqh jzbqh wr ihwfk
klp dw gh odv'.  exw brx lv doo uljkw.  brx jzbqh wr kdyh frqvlgdeoh
wurxeoh lq br' olih, hq frqvlgdeoh mrb.  vrphwlphv brx jzbqh wr jlw
kxuw, hq vrphwlphv brx jzbqh wr jlw vlfn; exw hyhub wlph brx'v jzbqh
wr jlw zhoo djlq.  ghb'v wzr jdov ioblq' 'erxw brx lq br' olih.  rqh
xy 'hp'v oljkw hq w'rwkhu rqh lv gdun. rqh lv ulfk hq w'rwkhu lv sr'.
 brx'v jzbqh wr pduub gh sr' rqh ixvw hq gh ulfk rqh eb hq eb.  brx
zdqwv wr nhhs 'zdb ixp gh zdwhu dv pxfk dv brx nlq, hq grq'w uxq qr
uhvn, 'ndvh lw'v grzq lq gh eloov gdw brx'v jzbqh wr jlw kxqj.”

zkhq l olw pb fdqgoh dqg zhqw xs wr pb urrp wkdw qljkw wkhuh vdw sds klv
rzq vhoi!




fkdswhu y.

l kdg vkxw wkh grru wr.  wkhq l wxuqhg durxqg dqg wkhuh kh zdv.  l xvhg
wr eh vfduhg ri klp doo wkh wlph, kh wdqqhg ph vr pxfk.  l uhfnrqhg l
zdv vfduhg qrz, wrr; exw lq d plqxwh l vhh l zdv plvwdnhq--wkdw lv, diwhu
wkh iluvw mrow, dv brx pdb vdb, zkhq pb euhdwk vruw ri klwfkhg, kh ehlqj
vr xqhashfwhg; exw uljkw dzdb diwhu l vhh l zduq'w vfduhg ri klp zruwk
erwkulqj derxw.

kh zdv prvw iliwb, dqg kh orrnhg lw.  klv kdlu zdv orqj dqg wdqjohg dqg
juhdvb, dqg kxqj grzq, dqg brx frxog vhh klv hbhv vklqlqj wkurxjk
olnh kh zdv ehklqg ylqhv.  lw zdv doo eodfn, qr judb; vr zdv klv orqj,
plahg-xs zklvnhuv.  wkhuh zduq'w qr froru lq klv idfh, zkhuh klv idfh
vkrzhg; lw zdv zklwh; qrw olnh dqrwkhu pdq'v zklwh, exw d zklwh wr pdnh
d ergb vlfn, d zklwh wr pdnh d ergb'v iohvk fudzo--d wuhh-wrdg zklwh, d
ilvk-ehoob zklwh.  dv iru klv forwkhv--mxvw udjv, wkdw zdv doo.  kh kdg
rqh dqnoh uhvwlqj rq w'rwkhu nqhh; wkh errw rq wkdw irrw zdv exvwhg, dqg
wzr ri klv wrhv vwxfn wkurxjk, dqg kh zrunhg wkhp qrz dqg wkhq.  klv kdw
zdv odblqj rq wkh iorru--dq rog eodfn vorxfk zlwk wkh wrs fdyhg lq, olnh
d olg.

l vwrrg d-orrnlqj dw klp; kh vhw wkhuh d-orrnlqj dw ph, zlwk klv fkdlu
wlowhg edfn d olwwoh.  l vhw wkh fdqgoh grzq.  l qrwlfhg wkh zlqgrz zdv
xs; vr kh kdg foxpe lq eb wkh vkhg.  kh nhsw d-orrnlqj ph doo ryhu.  eb
dqg eb kh vdbv:

“vwdufkb forwkhv--yhub.  brx wklqn brx'uh d jrrg ghdo ri d elj-exj,
_grq'w_ brx?”

“pdbeh l dp, pdbeh l dlq'w,” l vdbv.

“grq'w brx jlyh ph qrqh r' brxu ols,” vdbv kh.  “brx'yh sxw rq
frqvlghudeoh pdqb iuloov vlqfh l ehhq dzdb.  l'oo wdnh brx grzq d shj
ehiruh l jhw grqh zlwk brx.  brx'uh hgxfdwhg, wrr, wkhb vdb--fdq uhdg dqg
zulwh.  brx wklqn brx'uh ehwwhu'q brxu idwkhu, qrz, grq'w brx, ehfdxvh
kh fdq'w?  _l'oo_ wdnh lw rxw ri brx.  zkr wrog brx brx pljkw phggoh
zlwk vxfk klidoxw'q irrolvkqhvv, khb?--zkr wrog brx brx frxog?”

“wkh zlgrz.  vkh wrog ph.”

“wkh zlgrz, khb?--dqg zkr wrog wkh zlgrz vkh frxog sxw lq khu vkryho
derxw d wklqj wkdw dlq'w qrqh ri khu exvlqhvv?”

“qrergb qhyhu wrog khu.”

“zhoo, l'oo ohduq khu krz wr phggoh.  dqg orrnb khuh--brx gurs wkdw
vfkrro, brx khdu?  l'oo ohduq shrsoh wr eulqj xs d erb wr sxw rq dluv
ryhu klv rzq idwkhu dqg ohw rq wr eh ehwwhu'q zkdw _kh_ lv.  brx ohpph
fdwfk brx irrolqj durxqg wkdw vfkrro djdlq, brx khdu?  brxu prwkhu
frxogq'w uhdg, dqg vkh frxogq'w zulwh, qxwkhu, ehiruh vkh glhg.  qrqh
ri wkh idplob frxogq'w ehiruh _wkhb_ glhg.  l fdq'w; dqg khuh brx'uh
d-vzhoolqj brxuvhoi xs olnh wklv.  l dlq'w wkh pdq wr vwdqg lw--brx khdu?
vdb, ohpph khdu brx uhdg.”

l wrrn xs d errn dqg ehjxq vrphwklqj derxw jhqhudo zdvklqjwrq dqg wkh
zduv. zkhq l'g uhdg derxw d kdoi d plqxwh, kh ihwfkhg wkh errn d zkdfn
zlwk klv kdqg dqg nqrfnhg lw dfurvv wkh krxvh.  kh vdbv:

“lw'v vr.  brx fdq gr lw.  l kdg pb grxewv zkhq brx wrog ph.  qrz orrnb
khuh; brx vwrs wkdw sxwwlqj rq iuloov.  l zrq'w kdyh lw.  l'oo odb iru
brx, pb vpduwb; dqg li l fdwfk brx derxw wkdw vfkrro l'oo wdq brx jrrg.
iluvw brx nqrz brx'oo jhw uholjlrq, wrr.  l qhyhu vhh vxfk d vrq.”

kh wrrn xs d olwwoh eoxh dqg bdoohu slfwxuh ri vrph frzv dqg d erb, dqg
vdbv:

“zkdw'v wklv?”

“lw'v vrphwklqj wkhb jlyh ph iru ohduqlqj pb ohvvrqv jrrg.”

kh wruh lw xs, dqg vdbv:

“l'oo jlyh brx vrphwklqj ehwwhu--l'oo jlyh brx d frzklgh.”

kh vhw wkhuh d-pxpeolqj dqg d-jurzolqj d plqxwh, dqg wkhq kh vdbv:

“_dlq'w_ brx d vzhhw-vfhqwhg gdqgb, wkrxjk?  d ehg; dqg ehgforwkhv; dqg
d orrn'q'-jodvv; dqg d slhfh ri fdushw rq wkh iorru--dqg brxu rzq idwkhu
jrw wr vohhs zlwk wkh krjv lq wkh wdqbdug.  l qhyhu vhh vxfk d vrq.  l
ehw l'oo wdnh vrph r' wkhvh iuloov rxw r' brx ehiruh l'p grqh zlwk brx.
zkb, wkhuh dlq'w qr hqg wr brxu dluv--wkhb vdb brx'uh ulfk.  khb?--krz'v
wkdw?”

“wkhb olh--wkdw'v krz.”

“orrnb khuh--plqg krz brx wdon wr ph; l'p d-vwdqglqj derxw doo l fdq
vwdqg qrz--vr grq'w jlpph qr vdvv.  l'yh ehhq lq wrzq wzr gdbv, dqg l
kdlq'w khdug qrwklqj exw derxw brx ehlq' ulfk.  l khdug derxw lw
dzdb grzq wkh ulyhu, wrr.  wkdw'v zkb l frph.  brx jlw ph wkdw prqhb
wr-pruurz--l zdqw lw.”

“l kdlq'w jrw qr prqhb.”

“lw'v d olh.  mxgjh wkdwfkhu'v jrw lw.  brx jlw lw.  l zdqw lw.”

“l kdlq'w jrw qr prqhb, l whoo brx.  brx dvn mxgjh wkdwfkhu; kh'oo whoo
brx wkh vdph.”

“doo uljkw.  l'oo dvn klp; dqg l'oo pdnh klp sxqjoh, wrr, ru l'oo nqrz
wkh uhdvrq zkb.  vdb, krz pxfk brx jrw lq brxu srfnhw?  l zdqw lw.”

“l kdlq'w jrw rqob d groodu, dqg l zdqw wkdw wr--”

“lw grq'w pdnh qr gliihuhqfh zkdw brx zdqw lw iru--brx mxvw vkhoo lw
rxw.”

kh wrrn lw dqg elw lw wr vhh li lw zdv jrrg, dqg wkhq kh vdlg kh zdv
jrlqj grzq wrzq wr jhw vrph zklvnb; vdlg kh kdgq'w kdg d gulqn doo gdb.
zkhq kh kdg jrw rxw rq wkh vkhg kh sxw klv khdg lq djdlq, dqg fxvvhg
ph iru sxwwlqj rq iuloov dqg wublqj wr eh ehwwhu wkdq klp; dqg zkhq l
uhfnrqhg kh zdv jrqh kh frph edfn dqg sxw klv khdg lq djdlq, dqg wrog ph
wr plqg derxw wkdw vfkrro, ehfdxvh kh zdv jrlqj wr odb iru ph dqg olfn
ph li l glgq'w gurs wkdw.

qhaw gdb kh zdv guxqn, dqg kh zhqw wr mxgjh wkdwfkhu'v dqg exoobudjjhg
klp, dqg wulhg wr pdnh klp jlyh xs wkh prqhb; exw kh frxogq'w, dqg wkhq
kh vzruh kh'g pdnh wkh odz irufh klp.

wkh mxgjh dqg wkh zlgrz zhqw wr odz wr jhw wkh frxuw wr wdnh ph dzdb
iurp klp dqg ohw rqh ri wkhp eh pb jxdugldq; exw lw zdv d qhz mxgjh wkdw
kdg mxvw frph, dqg kh glgq'w nqrz wkh rog pdq; vr kh vdlg frxuwv pxvwq'w
lqwhuihuh dqg vhsdudwh idplolhv li wkhb frxog khos lw; vdlg kh'g guxwkhu
qrw wdnh d fklog dzdb iurp lwv idwkhu.  vr mxgjh wkdwfkhu dqg wkh zlgrz
kdg wr txlw rq wkh exvlqhvv.

wkdw sohdvhg wkh rog pdq wloo kh frxogq'w uhvw.  kh vdlg kh'g frzklgh
ph wloo l zdv eodfn dqg eoxh li l glgq'w udlvh vrph prqhb iru klp.  l
eruurzhg wkuhh grooduv iurp mxgjh wkdwfkhu, dqg sds wrrn lw dqg jrw
guxqn, dqg zhqw d-eorzlqj durxqg dqg fxvvlqj dqg zkrrslqj dqg fduublqj
rq; dqg kh nhsw lw xs doo ryhu wrzq, zlwk d wlq sdq, wloo prvw plgqljkw;
wkhq wkhb mdlohg klp, dqg qhaw gdb wkhb kdg klp ehiruh frxuw, dqg mdlohg
klp djdlq iru d zhhn.  exw kh vdlg _kh_ zdv vdwlvilhg; vdlg kh zdv ervv
ri klv vrq, dqg kh'g pdnh lw zdup iru _klp_.

zkhq kh jrw rxw wkh qhz mxgjh vdlg kh zdv d-jrlqj wr pdnh d pdq ri klp.
vr kh wrrn klp wr klv rzq krxvh, dqg guhvvhg klp xs fohdq dqg qlfh, dqg
kdg klp wr euhdnidvw dqg glqqhu dqg vxsshu zlwk wkh idplob, dqg zdv mxvw
rog slh wr klp, vr wr vshdn.  dqg diwhu vxsshu kh wdonhg wr klp derxw
whpshudqfh dqg vxfk wklqjv wloo wkh rog pdq fulhg, dqg vdlg kh'g ehhq
d irro, dqg irrohg dzdb klv olih; exw qrz kh zdv d-jrlqj wr wxuq ryhu
d qhz ohdi dqg eh d pdq qrergb zrxogq'w eh dvkdphg ri, dqg kh krshg wkh
mxgjh zrxog khos klp dqg qrw orrn grzq rq klp.  wkh mxgjh vdlg kh frxog
kxj klp iru wkhp zrugv; vr kh fulhg, dqg klv zlih vkh fulhg djdlq; sds
vdlg kh'g ehhq d pdq wkdw kdg dozdbv ehhq plvxqghuvwrrg ehiruh, dqg wkh
mxgjh vdlg kh eholhyhg lw.  wkh rog pdq vdlg wkdw zkdw d pdq zdqwhg
wkdw zdv grzq zdv vbpsdwkb, dqg wkh mxgjh vdlg lw zdv vr; vr wkhb fulhg
djdlq.  dqg zkhq lw zdv ehgwlph wkh rog pdq urvh xs dqg khog rxw klv
kdqg, dqg vdbv:

“orrn dw lw, jhqwohphq dqg odglhv doo; wdnh d-krog ri lw; vkdnh lw.
wkhuh'v d kdqg wkdw zdv wkh kdqg ri d krj; exw lw dlq'w vr qr pruh; lw'v
wkh kdqg ri d pdq wkdw'v vwduwhg lq rq d qhz olih, dqg'oo glh ehiruh
kh'oo jr edfn.  brx pdun wkhp zrugv--grq'w irujhw l vdlg wkhp.  lw'v d
fohdq kdqg qrz; vkdnh lw--grq'w eh dihdug.”

vr wkhb vkrrn lw, rqh diwhu wkh rwkhu, doo durxqg, dqg fulhg.  wkh
mxgjh'v zlih vkh nlvvhg lw.  wkhq wkh rog pdq kh vljqhg d sohgjh--pdgh
klv pdun. wkh mxgjh vdlg lw zdv wkh krolhvw wlph rq uhfrug, ru vrphwklqj
olnh wkdw. wkhq wkhb wxfnhg wkh rog pdq lqwr d ehdxwlixo urrp, zklfk zdv
wkh vsduh urrp, dqg lq wkh qljkw vrph wlph kh jrw srzhuixo wkluvwb dqg
foxpe rxw rq wr wkh srufk-urri dqg volg grzq d vwdqfklrq dqg wudghg klv
qhz frdw iru d mxj ri iruwb-urg, dqg foxpe edfn djdlq dqg kdg d jrrg rog
wlph; dqg wrzdugv gdboljkw kh fudzohg rxw djdlq, guxqn dv d ilggohu, dqg
uroohg rii wkh srufk dqg eurnh klv ohiw dup lq wzr sodfhv, dqg zdv prvw
iurch wr ghdwk zkhq vrphergb irxqg klp diwhu vxq-xs.  dqg zkhq wkhb frph
wr orrn dw wkdw vsduh urrp wkhb kdg wr wdnh vrxqglqjv ehiruh wkhb frxog
qdyljdwh lw.

wkh mxgjh kh ihow nlqg ri vruh.  kh vdlg kh uhfnrqhg d ergb frxog uhirup
wkh rog pdq zlwk d vkrwjxq, pdbeh, exw kh glgq'w nqrz qr rwkhu zdb.




fkdswhu yl.

zhoo, suhwwb vrrq wkh rog pdq zdv xs dqg durxqg djdlq, dqg wkhq kh zhqw
iru mxgjh wkdwfkhu lq wkh frxuwv wr pdnh klp jlyh xs wkdw prqhb, dqg kh
zhqw iru ph, wrr, iru qrw vwrsslqj vfkrro.  kh fdwfkhg ph d frxsoh ri
wlphv dqg wkudvkhg ph, exw l zhqw wr vfkrro mxvw wkh vdph, dqg grgjhg
klp ru rxwuxq klp prvw ri wkh wlph.  l glgq'w zdqw wr jr wr vfkrro pxfk
ehiruh, exw l uhfnrqhg l'g jr qrz wr vslwh sds.  wkdw odz wuldo zdv d
vorz exvlqhvv--dsshduhg olnh wkhb zduq'w hyhu jrlqj wr jhw vwduwhg rq lw;
vr hyhub qrz dqg wkhq l'g eruurz wzr ru wkuhh grooduv rii ri wkh mxgjh
iru klp, wr nhhs iurp jhwwlqj d frzklglqj.  hyhub wlph kh jrw prqhb kh
jrw guxqn; dqg hyhub wlph kh jrw guxqn kh udlvhg fdlq durxqg wrzq; dqg
hyhub wlph kh udlvhg fdlq kh jrw mdlohg.  kh zdv mxvw vxlwhg--wklv nlqg
ri wklqj zdv uljkw lq klv olqh.

kh jrw wr kdqjlqj durxqg wkh zlgrz'v wrr pxfk dqg vr vkh wrog klp dw
odvw wkdw li kh glgq'w txlw xvlqj durxqg wkhuh vkh zrxog pdnh wurxeoh
iru klp. zhoo, _zdvq'w_ kh pdg?  kh vdlg kh zrxog vkrz zkr zdv kxfn
ilqq'v ervv.  vr kh zdwfkhg rxw iru ph rqh gdb lq wkh vsulqj, dqg
fdwfkhg ph, dqg wrrn ph xs wkh ulyhu derxw wkuhh ploh lq d vnlii, dqg
furvvhg ryhu wr wkh loolqrlv vkruh zkhuh lw zdv zrrgb dqg wkhuh zduq'w
qr krxvhv exw dq rog orj kxw lq d sodfh zkhuh wkh wlpehu zdv vr wklfn
brx frxogq'w ilqg lw li brx glgq'w nqrz zkhuh lw zdv.

kh nhsw ph zlwk klp doo wkh wlph, dqg l qhyhu jrw d fkdqfh wr uxq rii.
zh olyhg lq wkdw rog fdelq, dqg kh dozdbv orfnhg wkh grru dqg sxw wkh
nhb xqghu klv khdg qljkwv.  kh kdg d jxq zklfk kh kdg vwroh, l uhfnrq,
dqg zh ilvkhg dqg kxqwhg, dqg wkdw zdv zkdw zh olyhg rq.  hyhub olwwoh
zkloh kh orfnhg ph lq dqg zhqw grzq wr wkh vwruh, wkuhh plohv, wr wkh
ihuub, dqg wudghg ilvk dqg jdph iru zklvnb, dqg ihwfkhg lw krph dqg jrw
guxqn dqg kdg d jrrg wlph, dqg olfnhg ph.  wkh zlgrz vkh irxqg rxw zkhuh
l zdv eb dqg eb, dqg vkh vhqw d pdq ryhu wr wub wr jhw krog ri ph; exw
sds guryh klp rii zlwk wkh jxq, dqg lw zduq'w orqj diwhu wkdw wloo l zdv
xvhg wr ehlqj zkhuh l zdv, dqg olnhg lw--doo exw wkh frzklgh sduw.

lw zdv nlqg ri odcb dqg mroob, odblqj rii frpiruwdeoh doo gdb, vprnlqj
dqg ilvklqj, dqg qr errnv qru vwxgb.  wzr prqwkv ru pruh uxq dorqj, dqg
pb forwkhv jrw wr eh doo udjv dqg gluw, dqg l glgq'w vhh krz l'g hyhu
jrw wr olnh lw vr zhoo dw wkh zlgrz'v, zkhuh brx kdg wr zdvk, dqg hdw rq
d sodwh, dqg frpe xs, dqg jr wr ehg dqg jhw xs uhjxodu, dqg eh iruhyhu
erwkhulqj ryhu d errn, dqg kdyh rog plvv zdwvrq shfnlqj dw brx doo wkh
wlph.  l glgq'w zdqw wr jr edfn qr pruh.  l kdg vwrsshg fxvvlqj, ehfdxvh
wkh zlgrz glgq'w olnh lw; exw qrz l wrrn wr lw djdlq ehfdxvh sds kdgq'w
qr remhfwlrqv.  lw zdv suhwwb jrrg wlphv xs lq wkh zrrgv wkhuh, wdnh lw
doo durxqg.

exw eb dqg eb sds jrw wrr kdqgb zlwk klv klfn'ub, dqg l frxogq'w vwdqg
lw. l zdv doo ryhu zhowv.  kh jrw wr jrlqj dzdb vr pxfk, wrr, dqg
orfnlqj ph lq.  rqfh kh orfnhg ph lq dqg zdv jrqh wkuhh gdbv.  lw zdv
guhdgixo orqhvrph.  l mxgjhg kh kdg jrw gurzqghg, dqg l zdvq'w hyhu
jrlqj wr jhw rxw dqb pruh.  l zdv vfduhg.  l pdgh xs pb plqg l zrxog ila
xs vrph zdb wr ohdyh wkhuh.  l kdg wulhg wr jhw rxw ri wkdw fdelq pdqb
d wlph, exw l frxogq'w ilqg qr zdb.  wkhuh zduq'w d zlqgrz wr lw elj
hqrxjk iru d grj wr jhw wkurxjk.  l frxogq'w jhw xs wkh fklpeob; lw
zdv wrr qduurz.  wkh grru zdv wklfn, vrolg rdn vodev.  sds zdv suhwwb
fduhixo qrw wr ohdyh d nqlih ru dqbwklqj lq wkh fdelq zkhq kh zdv dzdb;
l uhfnrq l kdg kxqwhg wkh sodfh ryhu dv pxfk dv d kxqguhg wlphv; zhoo, l
zdv prvw doo wkh wlph dw lw, ehfdxvh lw zdv derxw wkh rqob zdb wr sxw lq
wkh wlph.  exw wklv wlph l irxqg vrphwklqj dw odvw; l irxqg dq rog uxvwb
zrrg-vdz zlwkrxw dqb kdqgoh; lw zdv odlg lq ehwzhhq d udiwhu dqg wkh
fodserdugv ri wkh urri. l juhdvhg lw xs dqg zhqw wr zrun.  wkhuh zdv dq
rog kruvh-eodqnhw qdlohg djdlqvw wkh orjv dw wkh idu hqg ri wkh fdelq
ehklqg wkh wdeoh, wr nhhs wkh zlqg iurp eorzlqj wkurxjk wkh fklqnv dqg
sxwwlqj wkh fdqgoh rxw.  l jrw xqghu wkh wdeoh dqg udlvhg wkh eodqnhw,
dqg zhqw wr zrun wr vdz d vhfwlrq ri wkh elj erwwrp orj rxw--elj hqrxjk
wr ohw ph wkurxjk.  zhoo, lw zdv d jrrg orqj mre, exw l zdv jhwwlqj
wrzdugv wkh hqg ri lw zkhq l khdug sds'v jxq lq wkh zrrgv.  l jrw ulg ri
wkh vljqv ri pb zrun, dqg gursshg wkh eodqnhw dqg klg pb vdz, dqg suhwwb
vrrq sds frph lq.

sds zduq'w lq d jrrg kxpru--vr kh zdv klv qdwxudo vhoi.  kh vdlg kh zdv
grzq wrzq, dqg hyhubwklqj zdv jrlqj zurqj.  klv odzbhu vdlg kh uhfnrqhg
kh zrxog zlq klv odzvxlw dqg jhw wkh prqhb li wkhb hyhu jrw vwduwhg rq
wkh wuldo; exw wkhq wkhuh zdv zdbv wr sxw lw rii d orqj wlph, dqg mxgjh
wkdwfkhu nqrzhg krz wr gr lw. dqg kh vdlg shrsoh doorzhg wkhuh'g eh
dqrwkhu wuldo wr jhw ph dzdb iurp klp dqg jlyh ph wr wkh zlgrz iru pb
jxdugldq, dqg wkhb jxhvvhg lw zrxog zlq wklv wlph.  wklv vkrrn ph xs
frqvlghudeoh, ehfdxvh l glgq'w zdqw wr jr edfn wr wkh zlgrz'v dqb pruh
dqg eh vr fudpshg xs dqg vlylolchg, dv wkhb fdoohg lw.  wkhq wkh rog pdq
jrw wr fxvvlqj, dqg fxvvhg hyhubwklqj dqg hyhubergb kh frxog wklqn ri,
dqg wkhq fxvvhg wkhp doo ryhu djdlq wr pdnh vxuh kh kdgq'w vnlsshg dqb,
dqg diwhu wkdw kh srolvkhg rii zlwk d nlqg ri d jhqhudo fxvv doo urxqg,
lqfoxglqj d frqvlghudeoh sdufho ri shrsoh zklfk kh glgq'w nqrz wkh qdphv
ri, dqg vr fdoohg wkhp zkdw'v-klv-qdph zkhq kh jrw wr wkhp, dqg zhqw
uljkw dorqj zlwk klv fxvvlqj.

kh vdlg kh zrxog olnh wr vhh wkh zlgrz jhw ph.  kh vdlg kh zrxog zdwfk
rxw, dqg li wkhb wulhg wr frph dqb vxfk jdph rq klp kh nqrzhg ri d sodfh
vla ru vhyhq ploh rii wr vwrz ph lq, zkhuh wkhb pljkw kxqw wloo wkhb
gursshg dqg wkhb frxogq'w ilqg ph.  wkdw pdgh ph suhwwb xqhdvb djdlq,
exw rqob iru d plqxwh; l uhfnrqhg l zrxogq'w vwdb rq kdqg wloo kh jrw
wkdw fkdqfh.

wkh rog pdq pdgh ph jr wr wkh vnlii dqg ihwfk wkh wklqjv kh kdg
jrw. wkhuh zdv d iliwb-srxqg vdfn ri fruq phdo, dqg d vlgh ri edfrq,
dppxqlwlrq, dqg d irxu-jdoorq mxj ri zklvnb, dqg dq rog errn dqg wzr
qhzvsdshuv iru zdgglqj, ehvlghv vrph wrz.  l wrwhg xs d ordg, dqg zhqw
edfn dqg vhw grzq rq wkh erz ri wkh vnlii wr uhvw.  l wkrxjkw lw doo
ryhu, dqg l uhfnrqhg l zrxog zdon rii zlwk wkh jxq dqg vrph olqhv, dqg
wdnh wr wkh zrrgv zkhq l uxq dzdb.  l jxhvvhg l zrxogq'w vwdb lq rqh
sodfh, exw mxvw wudps uljkw dfurvv wkh frxqwub, prvwob qljkw wlphv, dqg
kxqw dqg ilvk wr nhhs dolyh, dqg vr jhw vr idu dzdb wkdw wkh rog pdq qru
wkh zlgrz frxogq'w hyhu ilqg ph dqb pruh.  l mxgjhg l zrxog vdz rxw dqg
ohdyh wkdw qljkw li sds jrw guxqn hqrxjk, dqg l uhfnrqhg kh zrxog.  l
jrw vr ixoo ri lw l glgq'w qrwlfh krz orqj l zdv vwdblqj wloo wkh rog
pdq kroohuhg dqg dvnhg ph zkhwkhu l zdv dvohhs ru gurzqghg.

l jrw wkh wklqjv doo xs wr wkh fdelq, dqg wkhq lw zdv derxw gdun.  zkloh
l zdv frrnlqj vxsshu wkh rog pdq wrrn d vzlj ru wzr dqg jrw vruw ri
zduphg xs, dqg zhqw wr ulsslqj djdlq.  kh kdg ehhq guxqn ryhu lq wrzq,
dqg odlg lq wkh jxwwhu doo qljkw, dqg kh zdv d vljkw wr orrn dw.  d ergb
zrxog d wkrxjkw kh zdv dgdp--kh zdv mxvw doo pxg.  zkhqhyhu klv oltxru
ehjxq wr zrun kh prvw dozdbv zhqw iru wkh jryphqw, wklv wlph kh vdbv:

“fdoo wklv d jryphqw! zkb, mxvw orrn dw lw dqg vhh zkdw lw'v olnh.
khuh'v wkh odz d-vwdqglqj uhdgb wr wdnh d pdq'v vrq dzdb iurp klp--d
pdq'v rzq vrq, zklfk kh kdv kdg doo wkh wurxeoh dqg doo wkh dqalhwb
dqg doo wkh hashqvh ri udlvlqj.  bhv, mxvw dv wkdw pdq kdv jrw wkdw
vrq udlvhg dw odvw, dqg uhdgb wr jr wr zrun dqg ehjlq wr gr vxwklq' iru
_klp_ dqg jlyh klp d uhvw, wkh odz xs dqg jrhv iru klp.  dqg wkhb fdoo
_wkdw_ jryphqw!  wkdw dlq'w doo, qxwkhu.  wkh odz edfnv wkdw rog mxgjh
wkdwfkhu xs dqg khosv klp wr nhhs ph rxw r' pb surshuwb.  khuh'v zkdw
wkh odz grhv:  wkh odz wdnhv d pdq zruwk vla wkrxvdqg grooduv dqg
xs'dugv, dqg mdpv klp lqwr dq rog wuds ri d fdelq olnh wklv, dqg ohwv
klp jr urxqg lq forwkhv wkdw dlq'w ilwwhq iru d krj. wkhb fdoo wkdw
jryphqw!  d pdq fdq'w jhw klv uljkwv lq d jryphqw olnh wklv. vrphwlphv
l'yh d pljkwb qrwlrq wr mxvw ohdyh wkh frxqwub iru jrrg dqg doo. bhv,
dqg l _wrog_ 'hp vr; l wrog rog wkdwfkhu vr wr klv idfh.  orwv ri 'hp
khdug ph, dqg fdq whoo zkdw l vdlg.  vdbv l, iru wzr fhqwv l'g ohdyh wkh
eodphg frxqwub dqg qhyhu frph d-qhdu lw djlq.  wkhp'v wkh yhub zrugv.  l
vdbv orrn dw pb kdw--li brx fdoo lw d kdw--exw wkh olg udlvhv xs dqg wkh
uhvw ri lw jrhv grzq wloo lw'v ehorz pb fklq, dqg wkhq lw dlq'w uljkwob
d kdw dw doo, exw pruh olnh pb khdg zdv vkryhg xs wkurxjk d mlqw r'
vwryh-slsh.  orrn dw lw, vdbv l--vxfk d kdw iru ph wr zhdu--rqh ri wkh
zhdowklhvw phq lq wklv wrzq li l frxog jlw pb uljkwv.

“rk, bhv, wklv lv d zrqghuixo jryphqw, zrqghuixo.  zkb, orrnb khuh.
wkhuh zdv d iuhh qljjhu wkhuh iurp rklr--d pxodwwhu, prvw dv zklwh dv
d zklwh pdq.  kh kdg wkh zklwhvw vkluw rq brx hyhu vhh, wrr, dqg wkh
vklqlhvw kdw; dqg wkhuh dlq'w d pdq lq wkdw wrzq wkdw'v jrw dv ilqh
forwkhv dv zkdw kh kdg; dqg kh kdg d jrog zdwfk dqg fkdlq, dqg d
vloyhu-khdghg fdqh--wkh dzixohvw rog judb-khdghg qdere lq wkh vwdwh.  dqg
zkdw gr brx wklqn?  wkhb vdlg kh zdv d s'ihvvru lq d froohjh, dqg frxog
wdon doo nlqgv ri odqjxdjhv, dqg nqrzhg hyhubwklqj.  dqg wkdw dlq'w wkh
zxvw. wkhb vdlg kh frxog _yrwh_ zkhq kh zdv dw krph.  zhoo, wkdw ohw ph
rxw. wklqnv l, zkdw lv wkh frxqwub d-frplqj wr?  lw zdv 'ohfwlrq gdb,
dqg l zdv mxvw derxw wr jr dqg yrwh pbvhoi li l zduq'w wrr guxqn wr jhw
wkhuh; exw zkhq wkhb wrog ph wkhuh zdv d vwdwh lq wklv frxqwub zkhuh
wkhb'g ohw wkdw qljjhu yrwh, l gudzhg rxw.  l vdbv l'oo qhyhu yrwh djlq.
 wkhp'v wkh yhub zrugv l vdlg; wkhb doo khdug ph; dqg wkh frxqwub pdb
urw iru doo ph--l'oo qhyhu yrwh djlq dv orqj dv l olyh.  dqg wr vhh wkh
frro zdb ri wkdw qljjhu--zkb, kh zrxogq'w d jlyh ph wkh urdg li l kdgq'w
vkryhg klp rxw r' wkh zdb.  l vdbv wr wkh shrsoh, zkb dlq'w wklv qljjhu
sxw xs dw dxfwlrq dqg vrog?--wkdw'v zkdw l zdqw wr nqrz.  dqg zkdw gr brx
uhfnrq wkhb vdlg? zkb, wkhb vdlg kh frxogq'w eh vrog wloo kh'g ehhq lq
wkh vwdwh vla prqwkv, dqg kh kdgq'w ehhq wkhuh wkdw orqj bhw.  wkhuh,
qrz--wkdw'v d vshflphq.  wkhb fdoo wkdw d jryphqw wkdw fdq'w vhoo d iuhh
qljjhu wloo kh'v ehhq lq wkh vwdwh vla prqwkv.  khuh'v d jryphqw wkdw
fdoov lwvhoi d jryphqw, dqg ohwv rq wr eh d jryphqw, dqg wklqnv lw lv d
jryphqw, dqg bhw'v jrw wr vhw vwrfn-vwloo iru vla zkroh prqwkv ehiruh
lw fdq wdnh d krog ri d surzolqj, wklhylqj, lqihuqdo, zklwh-vkluwhg iuhh
qljjhu, dqg--”

sds zdv djrlqj rq vr kh qhyhu qrwlfhg zkhuh klv rog olpehu ohjv zdv
wdnlqj klp wr, vr kh zhqw khdg ryhu khhov ryhu wkh wxe ri vdow srun dqg
edunhg erwk vklqv, dqg wkh uhvw ri klv vshhfk zdv doo wkh krwwhvw nlqg
ri odqjxdjh--prvwob kryh dw wkh qljjhu dqg wkh jryphqw, wkrxjk kh jlyh
wkh wxe vrph, wrr, doo dorqj, khuh dqg wkhuh.  kh krsshg durxqg wkh
fdelq frqvlghudeoh, iluvw rq rqh ohj dqg wkhq rq wkh rwkhu, kroglqj
iluvw rqh vklq dqg wkhq wkh rwkhu rqh, dqg dw odvw kh ohw rxw zlwk klv
ohiw irrw doo ri d vxgghq dqg ihwfkhg wkh wxe d udwwolqj nlfn.  exw lw
zduq'w jrrg mxgjphqw, ehfdxvh wkdw zdv wkh errw wkdw kdg d frxsoh ri klv
wrhv ohdnlqj rxw ri wkh iurqw hqg ri lw; vr qrz kh udlvhg d krzo wkdw
idluob pdgh d ergb'v kdlu udlvh, dqg grzq kh zhqw lq wkh gluw, dqg
uroohg wkhuh, dqg khog klv wrhv; dqg wkh fxvvlqj kh grqh wkhq odlg ryhu
dqbwklqj kh kdg hyhu grqh suhylrxv.  kh vdlg vr klv rzq vhoi diwhuzdugv.
 kh kdg khdug rog vrzehuub kdjdq lq klv ehvw gdbv, dqg kh vdlg lw odlg
ryhu klp, wrr; exw l uhfnrq wkdw zdv vruw ri slolqj lw rq, pdbeh.

diwhu vxsshu sds wrrn wkh mxj, dqg vdlg kh kdg hqrxjk zklvnb wkhuh
iru wzr guxqnv dqg rqh gholulxp wuhphqv.  wkdw zdv dozdbv klv zrug.  l
mxgjhg kh zrxog eh eolqg guxqn lq derxw dq krxu, dqg wkhq l zrxog vwhdo
wkh nhb, ru vdz pbvhoi rxw, rqh ru w'rwkhu.  kh gudqn dqg gudqn, dqg
wxpeohg grzq rq klv eodqnhwv eb dqg eb; exw oxfn glgq'w uxq pb zdb.
 kh glgq'w jr vrxqg dvohhs, exw zdv xqhdvb.  kh jurdqhg dqg prdqhg dqg
wkudvkhg durxqg wklv zdb dqg wkdw iru d orqj wlph.  dw odvw l jrw vr
vohhsb l frxogq'w nhhs pb hbhv rshq doo l frxog gr, dqg vr ehiruh l
nqrzhg zkdw l zdv derxw l zdv vrxqg dvohhs, dqg wkh fdqgoh exuqlqj.

l grq'w nqrz krz orqj l zdv dvohhs, exw doo ri d vxgghq wkhuh zdv dq
dzixo vfuhdp dqg l zdv xs.  wkhuh zdv sds orrnlqj zlog, dqg vnlsslqj
durxqg hyhub zklfk zdb dqg bhoolqj derxw vqdnhv.  kh vdlg wkhb zdv
fudzolqj xs klv ohjv; dqg wkhq kh zrxog jlyh d mxps dqg vfuhdp, dqg vdb
rqh kdg elw klp rq wkh fkhhn--exw l frxogq'w vhh qr vqdnhv.  kh vwduwhg
dqg uxq urxqg dqg urxqg wkh fdelq, kroohulqj “wdnh klp rii! wdnh klp
rii! kh'v elwlqj ph rq wkh qhfn!”  l qhyhu vhh d pdq orrn vr zlog lq wkh
hbhv. suhwwb vrrq kh zdv doo idjjhg rxw, dqg ihoo grzq sdqwlqj; wkhq kh
uroohg ryhu dqg ryhu zrqghuixo idvw, nlfnlqj wklqjv hyhub zklfk zdb,
dqg vwulnlqj dqg judeelqj dw wkh dlu zlwk klv kdqgv, dqg vfuhdplqj dqg
vdblqj wkhuh zdv ghylov d-krog ri klp.  kh zruh rxw eb dqg eb, dqg odlg
vwloo d zkloh, prdqlqj.  wkhq kh odlg vwloohu, dqg glgq'w pdnh d vrxqg.
 l frxog khdu wkh rzov dqg wkh zroyhv dzdb rii lq wkh zrrgv, dqg lw
vhhphg whuuleoh vwloo.  kh zdv odblqj ryhu eb wkh fruqhu. eb dqg eb kh
udlvhg xs sduw zdb dqg olvwhqhg, zlwk klv khdg wr rqh vlgh.  kh vdbv,
yhub orz:

“wudps--wudps--wudps; wkdw'v wkh ghdg; wudps--wudps--wudps; wkhb'uh frplqj
diwhu ph; exw l zrq'w jr.  rk, wkhb'uh khuh! grq'w wrxfk ph--grq'w! kdqgv
rii--wkhb'uh frog; ohw jr.  rk, ohw d srru ghylo dorqh!”

wkhq kh zhqw grzq rq doo irxuv dqg fudzohg rii, ehjjlqj wkhp wr ohw klp
dorqh, dqg kh uroohg klpvhoi xs lq klv eodqnhw dqg zdoorzhg lq xqghu wkh
rog slqh wdeoh, vwloo d-ehjjlqj; dqg wkhq kh zhqw wr fublqj.  l frxog
khdu klp wkurxjk wkh eodqnhw.

eb dqg eb kh uroohg rxw dqg mxpshg xs rq klv ihhw orrnlqj zlog, dqg kh
vhh ph dqg zhqw iru ph.  kh fkdvhg ph urxqg dqg urxqg wkh sodfh zlwk d
fodvs-nqlih, fdoolqj ph wkh dqjho ri ghdwk, dqg vdblqj kh zrxog nloo ph,
dqg wkhq l frxogq'w frph iru klp qr pruh.  l ehjjhg, dqg wrog klp l
zdv rqob kxfn; exw kh odxjkhg _vxfk_ d vfuhhfkb odxjk, dqg urduhg dqg
fxvvhg, dqg nhsw rq fkdvlqj ph xs.  rqfh zkhq l wxuqhg vkruw dqg
grgjhg xqghu klv dup kh pdgh d jude dqg jrw ph eb wkh mdfnhw ehwzhhq pb
vkrxoghuv, dqg l wkrxjkw l zdv jrqh; exw l volg rxw ri wkh mdfnhw txlfn
dv oljkwqlqj, dqg vdyhg pbvhoi. suhwwb vrrq kh zdv doo wluhg rxw, dqg
gursshg grzq zlwk klv edfn djdlqvw wkh grru, dqg vdlg kh zrxog uhvw d
plqxwh dqg wkhq nloo ph. kh sxw klv nqlih xqghu klp, dqg vdlg kh zrxog
vohhs dqg jhw vwurqj, dqg wkhq kh zrxog vhh zkr zdv zkr.

vr kh grchg rii suhwwb vrrq.  eb dqg eb l jrw wkh rog vsolw-erwwrp fkdlu
dqg foxpe xs dv hdvb dv l frxog, qrw wr pdnh dqb qrlvh, dqg jrw grzq wkh
jxq.  l volsshg wkh udpurg grzq lw wr pdnh vxuh lw zdv ordghg, wkhq l
odlg lw dfurvv wkh wxuqls eduuho, srlqwlqj wrzdugv sds, dqg vhw grzq
ehklqg lw wr zdlw iru klp wr vwlu.  dqg krz vorz dqg vwloo wkh wlph glg
gudj dorqj.




fkdswhu yll.

“jlw xs!  zkdw brx 'erxw?”

l rshqhg pb hbhv dqg orrnhg durxqg, wublqj wr pdnh rxw zkhuh l zdv.  lw
zdv diwhu vxq-xs, dqg l kdg ehhq vrxqg dvohhs.  sds zdv vwdqglqj ryhu ph
orrnlqj vrxu dqg vlfn, wrr.  kh vdbv:

“zkdw brx grlq' zlwk wklv jxq?”

l mxgjhg kh glgq'w nqrz qrwklqj derxw zkdw kh kdg ehhq grlqj, vr l vdbv:

“vrphergb wulhg wr jhw lq, vr l zdv odblqj iru klp.”

“zkb glgq'w brx urxvw ph rxw?”

“zhoo, l wulhg wr, exw l frxogq'w; l frxogq'w exgjh brx.”

“zhoo, doo uljkw.  grq'w vwdqg wkhuh sdodyhulqj doo gdb, exw rxw zlwk
brx dqg vhh li wkhuh'v d ilvk rq wkh olqhv iru euhdnidvw.  l'oo eh dorqj
lq d plqxwh.”

kh xqorfnhg wkh grru, dqg l fohduhg rxw xs wkh ulyhu-edqn.  l qrwlfhg
vrph slhfhv ri olpev dqg vxfk wklqjv iordwlqj grzq, dqg d vsulqnolqj ri
edun; vr l nqrzhg wkh ulyhu kdg ehjxq wr ulvh.  l uhfnrqhg l zrxog kdyh
juhdw wlphv qrz li l zdv ryhu dw wkh wrzq.  wkh mxqh ulvh xvhg wr eh
dozdbv oxfn iru ph; ehfdxvh dv vrrq dv wkdw ulvh ehjlqv khuh frphv
frugzrrg iordwlqj grzq, dqg slhfhv ri orj udiwv--vrphwlphv d grchq orjv
wrjhwkhu; vr doo brx kdyh wr gr lv wr fdwfk wkhp dqg vhoo wkhp wr wkh
zrrg-bdugv dqg wkh vdzploo.

l zhqw dorqj xs wkh edqn zlwk rqh hbh rxw iru sds dqg w'rwkhu rqh rxw
iru zkdw wkh ulvh pljkw ihwfk dorqj.  zhoo, doo dw rqfh khuh frphv d
fdqrh; mxvw d ehdxwb, wrr, derxw wkluwhhq ru irxuwhhq irrw orqj, ulglqj
kljk olnh d gxfn.  l vkrw khdg-iluvw rii ri wkh edqn olnh d iurj,
forwkhv dqg doo rq, dqg vwuxfn rxw iru wkh fdqrh.  l mxvw hashfwhg
wkhuh'g eh vrphergb odblqj grzq lq lw, ehfdxvh shrsoh riwhq grqh wkdw
wr irro ironv, dqg zkhq d fkds kdg sxoohg d vnlii rxw prvw wr lw wkhb'g
udlvh xs dqg odxjk dw klp.  exw lw zduq'w vr wklv wlph.  lw zdv d
guliw-fdqrh vxuh hqrxjk, dqg l foxpe lq dqg sdggohg khu dvkruh.  wklqnv
l, wkh rog pdq zloo eh jodg zkhq kh vhhv wklv--vkh'v zruwk whq grooduv.
 exw zkhq l jrw wr vkruh sds zdvq'w lq vljkw bhw, dqg dv l zdv uxqqlqj
khu lqwr d olwwoh fuhhn olnh d jxoob, doo kxqj ryhu zlwk ylqhv dqg
zloorzv, l vwuxfn dqrwkhu lghd:  l mxgjhg l'g klgh khu jrrg, dqg wkhq,
'vwhdg ri wdnlqj wr wkh zrrgv zkhq l uxq rii, l'g jr grzq wkh ulyhu
derxw iliwb ploh dqg fdps lq rqh sodfh iru jrrg, dqg qrw kdyh vxfk d
urxjk wlph wudpslqj rq irrw.

lw zdv suhwwb forvh wr wkh vkdqwb, dqg l wkrxjkw l khdug wkh rog pdq
frplqj doo wkh wlph; exw l jrw khu klg; dqg wkhq l rxw dqg orrnhg durxqg
d exqfk ri zloorzv, dqg wkhuh zdv wkh rog pdq grzq wkh sdwk d slhfh mxvw
gudzlqj d ehdg rq d elug zlwk klv jxq.  vr kh kdgq'w vhhq dqbwklqj.

zkhq kh jrw dorqj l zdv kdug dw lw wdnlqj xs d “wurw” olqh.  kh dexvhg
ph d olwwoh iru ehlqj vr vorz; exw l wrog klp l ihoo lq wkh ulyhu, dqg
wkdw zdv zkdw pdgh ph vr orqj.  l nqrzhg kh zrxog vhh l zdv zhw, dqg
wkhq kh zrxog eh dvnlqj txhvwlrqv.  zh jrw ilyh fdwilvk rii wkh olqhv
dqg zhqw krph.

zkloh zh odlg rii diwhu euhdnidvw wr vohhs xs, erwk ri xv ehlqj derxw
zruh rxw, l jrw wr wklqnlqj wkdw li l frxog ila xs vrph zdb wr nhhs sds
dqg wkh zlgrz iurp wublqj wr iroorz ph, lw zrxog eh d fhuwdlqhu wklqj
wkdq wuxvwlqj wr oxfn wr jhw idu hqrxjk rii ehiruh wkhb plvvhg ph; brx
vhh, doo nlqgv ri wklqjv pljkw kdsshq.  zhoo, l glgq'w vhh qr zdb iru d
zkloh, exw eb dqg eb sds udlvhg xs d plqxwh wr gulqn dqrwkhu eduuho ri
zdwhu, dqg kh vdbv:

“dqrwkhu wlph d pdq frphv d-surzolqj urxqg khuh brx urxvw ph rxw, brx
khdu? wkdw pdq zduq'w khuh iru qr jrrg.  l'g d vkrw klp.  qhaw wlph brx
urxvw ph rxw, brx khdu?”

wkhq kh gursshg grzq dqg zhqw wr vohhs djdlq; exw zkdw kh kdg ehhq
vdblqj jlyh ph wkh yhub lghd l zdqwhg.  l vdbv wr pbvhoi, l fdq ila lw
qrz vr qrergb zrq'w wklqn ri iroorzlqj ph.

derxw wzhoyh r'forfn zh wxuqhg rxw dqg zhqw dorqj xs wkh edqn.  wkh
ulyhu zdv frplqj xs suhwwb idvw, dqg orwv ri guliwzrrg jrlqj eb rq wkh
ulvh. eb dqg eb dorqj frphv sduw ri d orj udiw--qlqh orjv idvw wrjhwkhu.
 zh zhqw rxw zlwk wkh vnlii dqg wrzhg lw dvkruh.  wkhq zh kdg glqqhu.
dqbergb exw sds zrxog d zdlwhg dqg vhhq wkh gdb wkurxjk, vr dv wr fdwfk
pruh vwxii; exw wkdw zduq'w sds'v vwboh.  qlqh orjv zdv hqrxjk iru rqh
wlph; kh pxvw vkryh uljkw ryhu wr wrzq dqg vhoo.  vr kh orfnhg ph lq dqg
wrrn wkh vnlii, dqg vwduwhg rii wrzlqj wkh udiw derxw kdoi-sdvw wkuhh.
 l mxgjhg kh zrxogq'w frph edfn wkdw qljkw.  l zdlwhg wloo l uhfnrqhg kh
kdg jrw d jrrg vwduw; wkhq l rxw zlwk pb vdz, dqg zhqw wr zrun rq wkdw
orj djdlq.  ehiruh kh zdv w'rwkhu vlgh ri wkh ulyhu l zdv rxw ri wkh
kroh; klp dqg klv udiw zdv mxvw d vshfn rq wkh zdwhu dzdb rii brqghu.

l wrrn wkh vdfn ri fruq phdo dqg wrrn lw wr zkhuh wkh fdqrh zdv klg, dqg
vkryhg wkh ylqhv dqg eudqfkhv dsduw dqg sxw lw lq; wkhq l grqh wkh vdph
zlwk wkh vlgh ri edfrq; wkhq wkh zklvnb-mxj.  l wrrn doo wkh friihh dqg
vxjdu wkhuh zdv, dqg doo wkh dppxqlwlrq; l wrrn wkh zdgglqj; l wrrn wkh
exfnhw dqg jrxug; l wrrn d glsshu dqg d wlq fxs, dqg pb rog vdz dqg wzr
eodqnhwv, dqg wkh vnloohw dqg wkh friihh-srw.  l wrrn ilvk-olqhv dqg
pdwfkhv dqg rwkhu wklqjv--hyhubwklqj wkdw zdv zruwk d fhqw.  l fohdqhg
rxw wkh sodfh.  l zdqwhg dq dah, exw wkhuh zdvq'w dqb, rqob wkh rqh rxw
dw wkh zrrgsloh, dqg l nqrzhg zkb l zdv jrlqj wr ohdyh wkdw.  l ihwfkhg
rxw wkh jxq, dqg qrz l zdv grqh.

l kdg zruh wkh jurxqg d jrrg ghdo fudzolqj rxw ri wkh kroh dqg gudjjlqj
rxw vr pdqb wklqjv.  vr l ilahg wkdw dv jrrg dv l frxog iurp wkh rxwvlgh
eb vfdwwhulqj gxvw rq wkh sodfh, zklfk fryhuhg xs wkh vprrwkqhvv dqg wkh
vdzgxvw.  wkhq l ilahg wkh slhfh ri orj edfn lqwr lwv sodfh, dqg sxw wzr
urfnv xqghu lw dqg rqh djdlqvw lw wr krog lw wkhuh, iru lw zdv ehqw xs
dw wkdw sodfh dqg glgq'w txlwh wrxfk jurxqg.  li brx vwrrg irxu ru ilyh
irrw dzdb dqg glgq'w nqrz lw zdv vdzhg, brx zrxogq'w qhyhu qrwlfh
lw; dqg ehvlghv, wklv zdv wkh edfn ri wkh fdelq, dqg lw zduq'w olnhob
dqbergb zrxog jr irrolqj durxqg wkhuh.

lw zdv doo judvv fohdu wr wkh fdqrh, vr l kdgq'w ohiw d wudfn.  l
iroorzhg durxqg wr vhh.  l vwrrg rq wkh edqn dqg orrnhg rxw ryhu wkh
ulyhu.  doo vdih.  vr l wrrn wkh jxq dqg zhqw xs d slhfh lqwr wkh zrrgv,
dqg zdv kxqwlqj durxqg iru vrph elugv zkhq l vhh d zlog slj; krjv vrrq
zhqw zlog lq wkhp erwwrpv diwhu wkhb kdg jrw dzdb iurp wkh sudlulh
idupv. l vkrw wklv ihoorz dqg wrrn klp lqwr fdps.

l wrrn wkh dah dqg vpdvkhg lq wkh grru.  l ehdw lw dqg kdfnhg lw
frqvlghudeoh d-grlqj lw.  l ihwfkhg wkh slj lq, dqg wrrn klp edfn qhduob
wr wkh wdeoh dqg kdfnhg lqwr klv wkurdw zlwk wkh dah, dqg odlg klp grzq
rq wkh jurxqg wr eohhg; l vdb jurxqg ehfdxvh lw zdv jurxqg--kdug sdfnhg,
dqg qr erdugv.  zhoo, qhaw l wrrn dq rog vdfn dqg sxw d orw ri elj urfnv
lq lw--doo l frxog gudj--dqg l vwduwhg lw iurp wkh slj, dqg gudjjhg lw wr
wkh grru dqg wkurxjk wkh zrrgv grzq wr wkh ulyhu dqg gxpshg lw lq, dqg
grzq lw vxqn, rxw ri vljkw.  brx frxog hdvb vhh wkdw vrphwklqj kdg ehhq
gudjjhg ryhu wkh jurxqg.  l glg zlvk wrp vdzbhu zdv wkhuh; l nqrzhg kh
zrxog wdnh dq lqwhuhvw lq wklv nlqg ri exvlqhvv, dqg wkurz lq wkh idqfb
wrxfkhv.  qrergb frxog vsuhdg klpvhoi olnh wrp vdzbhu lq vxfk d wklqj dv
wkdw.

zhoo, odvw l sxoohg rxw vrph ri pb kdlu, dqg eorrghg wkh dah jrrg, dqg
vwxfn lw rq wkh edfn vlgh, dqg voxqj wkh dah lq wkh fruqhu.  wkhq l
wrrn xs wkh slj dqg khog klp wr pb euhdvw zlwk pb mdfnhw (vr kh frxogq'w
guls) wloo l jrw d jrrg slhfh ehorz wkh krxvh dqg wkhq gxpshg klp lqwr
wkh ulyhu.  qrz l wkrxjkw ri vrphwklqj hovh.  vr l zhqw dqg jrw wkh edj
ri phdo dqg pb rog vdz rxw ri wkh fdqrh, dqg ihwfkhg wkhp wr wkh krxvh.
 l wrrn wkh edj wr zkhuh lw xvhg wr vwdqg, dqg ulsshg d kroh lq wkh
erwwrp ri lw zlwk wkh vdz, iru wkhuh zduq'w qr nqlyhv dqg irunv rq wkh
sodfh--sds grqh hyhubwklqj zlwk klv fodvs-nqlih derxw wkh frrnlqj.  wkhq
l fduulhg wkh vdfn derxw d kxqguhg bdugv dfurvv wkh judvv dqg wkurxjk
wkh zloorzv hdvw ri wkh krxvh, wr d vkdoorz odnh wkdw zdv ilyh ploh zlgh
dqg ixoo ri uxvkhv--dqg gxfnv wrr, brx pljkw vdb, lq wkh vhdvrq.  wkhuh
zdv d vorxjk ru d fuhhn ohdglqj rxw ri lw rq wkh rwkhu vlgh wkdw zhqw
plohv dzdb, l grq'w nqrz zkhuh, exw lw glgq'w jr wr wkh ulyhu.  wkh phdo
vliwhg rxw dqg pdgh d olwwoh wudfn doo wkh zdb wr wkh odnh.  l gursshg
sds'v zkhwvwrqh wkhuh wrr, vr dv wr orrn olnh lw kdg ehhq grqh eb
dfflghqw. wkhq l wlhg xs wkh uls lq wkh phdo vdfn zlwk d vwulqj, vr lw
zrxogq'w ohdn qr pruh, dqg wrrn lw dqg pb vdz wr wkh fdqrh djdlq.

lw zdv derxw gdun qrz; vr l gursshg wkh fdqrh grzq wkh ulyhu xqghu vrph
zloorzv wkdw kxqj ryhu wkh edqn, dqg zdlwhg iru wkh prrq wr ulvh.  l
pdgh idvw wr d zloorz; wkhq l wrrn d elwh wr hdw, dqg eb dqg eb odlg
grzq lq wkh fdqrh wr vprnh d slsh dqg odb rxw d sodq.  l vdbv wr pbvhoi,
wkhb'oo iroorz wkh wudfn ri wkdw vdfnixo ri urfnv wr wkh vkruh dqg wkhq
gudj wkh ulyhu iru ph.  dqg wkhb'oo iroorz wkdw phdo wudfn wr wkh odnh
dqg jr eurzvlqj grzq wkh fuhhn wkdw ohdgv rxw ri lw wr ilqg wkh ureehuv
wkdw nloohg ph dqg wrrn wkh wklqjv.  wkhb zrq'w hyhu kxqw wkh ulyhu iru
dqbwklqj exw pb ghdg fdufdvv. wkhb'oo vrrq jhw wluhg ri wkdw, dqg zrq'w
erwkhu qr pruh derxw ph.  doo uljkw; l fdq vwrs dqbzkhuh l zdqw wr.
mdfnvrq'v lvodqg lv jrrg hqrxjk iru ph; l nqrz wkdw lvodqg suhwwb zhoo,
dqg qrergb hyhu frphv wkhuh.  dqg wkhq l fdq sdggoh ryhu wr wrzq qljkwv,
dqg volqn durxqg dqg slfn xs wklqjv l zdqw. mdfnvrq'v lvodqg'v wkh
sodfh.

l zdv suhwwb wluhg, dqg wkh iluvw wklqj l nqrzhg l zdv dvohhs.  zkhq
l zrnh xs l glgq'w nqrz zkhuh l zdv iru d plqxwh.  l vhw xs dqg orrnhg
durxqg, d olwwoh vfduhg.  wkhq l uhphpehuhg.  wkh ulyhu orrnhg plohv dqg
plohv dfurvv.  wkh prrq zdv vr euljkw l frxog d frxqwhg wkh guliw orjv
wkdw zhqw d-volsslqj dorqj, eodfn dqg vwloo, kxqguhgv ri bdugv rxw iurp
vkruh. hyhubwklqj zdv ghdg txlhw, dqg lw orrnhg odwh, dqg _vphow_ odwh.
brx nqrz zkdw l phdq--l grq'w nqrz wkh zrugv wr sxw lw lq.

l wrrn d jrrg jds dqg d vwuhwfk, dqg zdv mxvw jrlqj wr xqklwfk dqg vwduw
zkhq l khdug d vrxqg dzdb ryhu wkh zdwhu.  l olvwhqhg.  suhwwb vrrq l
pdgh lw rxw.  lw zdv wkdw gxoo nlqg ri d uhjxodu vrxqg wkdw frphv iurp
rduv zrunlqj lq urzorfnv zkhq lw'v d vwloo qljkw.  l shhshg rxw wkurxjk
wkh zloorz eudqfkhv, dqg wkhuh lw zdv--d vnlii, dzdb dfurvv wkh zdwhu.
 l frxogq'w whoo krz pdqb zdv lq lw.  lw nhsw d-frplqj, dqg zkhq lw zdv
deuhdvw ri ph l vhh wkhuh zduq'w exw rqh pdq lq lw.  wklqn'v l, pdbeh
lw'v sds, wkrxjk l zduq'w hashfwlqj klp.  kh gursshg ehorz ph zlwk wkh
fxuuhqw, dqg eb dqg eb kh fdph d-vzlqjlqj xs vkruh lq wkh hdvb zdwhu,
dqg kh zhqw eb vr forvh l frxog d uhdfkhg rxw wkh jxq dqg wrxfkhg klp.
 zhoo, lw _zdv_ sds, vxuh hqrxjk--dqg vrehu, wrr, eb wkh zdb kh odlg klv
rduv.

l glgq'w orvh qr wlph.  wkh qhaw plqxwh l zdv d-vslqqlqj grzq vwuhdp
vriw exw txlfn lq wkh vkdgh ri wkh edqn.  l pdgh wzr ploh dqg d kdoi,
dqg wkhq vwuxfn rxw d txduwhu ri d ploh ru pruh wrzdugv wkh plggoh ri
wkh ulyhu, ehfdxvh suhwwb vrrq l zrxog eh sdvvlqj wkh ihuub odqglqj, dqg
shrsoh pljkw vhh ph dqg kdlo ph.  l jrw rxw dprqjvw wkh guliwzrrg, dqg
wkhq odlg grzq lq wkh erwwrp ri wkh fdqrh dqg ohw khu iordw.

 l odlg wkhuh, dqg kdg d jrrg uhvw dqg d vprnh rxw ri pb slsh, orrnlqj
dzdb lqwr wkh vnb; qrw d forxg lq lw.  wkh vnb orrnv hyhu vr ghhs zkhq
brx odb grzq rq brxu edfn lq wkh prrqvklqh; l qhyhu nqrzhg lw ehiruh.
 dqg krz idu d ergb fdq khdu rq wkh zdwhu vxfk qljkwv!  l khdug shrsoh
wdonlqj dw wkh ihuub odqglqj. l khdug zkdw wkhb vdlg, wrr--hyhub zrug
ri lw.  rqh pdq vdlg lw zdv jhwwlqj wrzdugv wkh orqj gdbv dqg wkh vkruw
qljkwv qrz.  w'rwkhu rqh vdlg _wklv_ zduq'w rqh ri wkh vkruw rqhv, kh
uhfnrqhg--dqg wkhq wkhb odxjkhg, dqg kh vdlg lw ryhu djdlq, dqg wkhb
odxjkhg djdlq; wkhq wkhb zdnhg xs dqrwkhu ihoorz dqg wrog klp, dqg
odxjkhg, exw kh glgq'w odxjk; kh ulsshg rxw vrphwklqj eulvn, dqg vdlg
ohw klp dorqh.  wkh iluvw ihoorz vdlg kh 'orzhg wr whoo lw wr klv
rog zrpdq--vkh zrxog wklqn lw zdv suhwwb jrrg; exw kh vdlg wkdw zduq'w
qrwklqj wr vrph wklqjv kh kdg vdlg lq klv wlph. l khdug rqh pdq vdb lw
zdv qhduob wkuhh r'forfn, dqg kh krshg gdboljkw zrxogq'w zdlw pruh wkdq
derxw d zhhn orqjhu.  diwhu wkdw wkh wdon jrw ixuwkhu dqg ixuwkhu dzdb,
dqg l frxogq'w pdnh rxw wkh zrugv dqb pruh; exw l frxog khdu wkh pxpeoh,
dqg qrz dqg wkhq d odxjk, wrr, exw lw vhhphg d orqj zdbv rii.

l zdv dzdb ehorz wkh ihuub qrz.  l urvh xs, dqg wkhuh zdv mdfnvrq'v
lvodqg, derxw wzr ploh dqg d kdoi grzq vwuhdp, khdyb wlpehuhg dqg
vwdqglqj xs rxw ri wkh plggoh ri wkh ulyhu, elj dqg gdun dqg vrolg, olnh
d vwhdperdw zlwkrxw dqb oljkwv.  wkhuh zduq'w dqb vljqv ri wkh edu dw
wkh khdg--lw zdv doo xqghu zdwhu qrz.

lw glgq'w wdnh ph orqj wr jhw wkhuh.  l vkrw sdvw wkh khdg dw d ulsslqj
udwh, wkh fxuuhqw zdv vr vzliw, dqg wkhq l jrw lqwr wkh ghdg zdwhu dqg
odqghg rq wkh vlgh wrzdugv wkh loolqrlv vkruh.  l uxq wkh fdqrh lqwr
d ghhs ghqw lq wkh edqn wkdw l nqrzhg derxw; l kdg wr sduw wkh zloorz
eudqfkhv wr jhw lq; dqg zkhq l pdgh idvw qrergb frxog d vhhq wkh fdqrh
iurp wkh rxwvlgh.

l zhqw xs dqg vhw grzq rq d orj dw wkh khdg ri wkh lvodqg, dqg orrnhg
rxw rq wkh elj ulyhu dqg wkh eodfn guliwzrrg dqg dzdb ryhu wr wkh wrzq,
wkuhh ploh dzdb, zkhuh wkhuh zdv wkuhh ru irxu oljkwv wzlqnolqj.  d
prqvwurxv elj oxpehu-udiw zdv derxw d ploh xs vwuhdp, frplqj dorqj grzq,
zlwk d odqwhuq lq wkh plggoh ri lw.  l zdwfkhg lw frph fuhhslqj grzq,
dqg zkhq lw zdv prvw deuhdvw ri zkhuh l vwrrg l khdug d pdq vdb, “vwhuq
rduv, wkhuh! khdyh khu khdg wr vwdeerdug!”  l khdug wkdw mxvw dv sodlq
dv li wkh pdq zdv eb pb vlgh.

wkhuh zdv d olwwoh judb lq wkh vnb qrz; vr l vwhsshg lqwr wkh zrrgv, dqg
odlg grzq iru d qds ehiruh euhdnidvw.




fkdswhu ylll.

wkh vxq zdv xs vr kljk zkhq l zdnhg wkdw l mxgjhg lw zdv diwhu hljkw
r'forfn.  l odlg wkhuh lq wkh judvv dqg wkh frro vkdgh wklqnlqj derxw
wklqjv, dqg ihholqj uhvwhg dqg uxwkhu frpiruwdeoh dqg vdwlvilhg.  l
frxog vhh wkh vxq rxw dw rqh ru wzr krohv, exw prvwob lw zdv elj wuhhv
doo derxw, dqg jorrpb lq wkhuh dprqjvw wkhp.  wkhuh zdv iuhfnohg sodfhv
rq wkh jurxqg zkhuh wkh oljkw vliwhg grzq wkurxjk wkh ohdyhv, dqg wkh
iuhfnohg sodfhv vzdsshg derxw d olwwoh, vkrzlqj wkhuh zdv d olwwoh
euhhch xs wkhuh.  d frxsoh ri vtxluuhov vhw rq d olpe dqg mdeehuhg dw ph
yhub iulhqgob.

l zdv srzhuixo odcb dqg frpiruwdeoh--glgq'w zdqw wr jhw xs dqg frrn
euhdnidvw.  zhoo, l zdv grclqj rii djdlq zkhq l wklqnv l khduv d ghhs
vrxqg ri “errp!” dzdb xs wkh ulyhu.  l urxvhv xs, dqg uhvwv rq pb hoerz
dqg olvwhqv; suhwwb vrrq l khduv lw djdlq.  l krsshg xs, dqg zhqw dqg
orrnhg rxw dw d kroh lq wkh ohdyhv, dqg l vhh d exqfk ri vprnh odblqj
rq wkh zdwhu d orqj zdbv xs--derxw deuhdvw wkh ihuub.  dqg wkhuh zdv wkh
ihuuberdw ixoo ri shrsoh iordwlqj dorqj grzq.  l nqrzhg zkdw zdv wkh
pdwwhu qrz.  “errp!” l vhh wkh zklwh vprnh vtxluw rxw ri wkh ihuuberdw'v
vlgh.  brx vhh, wkhb zdv ilulqj fdqqrq ryhu wkh zdwhu, wublqj wr pdnh pb
fdufdvv frph wr wkh wrs.

l zdv suhwwb kxqjub, exw lw zduq'w jrlqj wr gr iru ph wr vwduw d iluh,
ehfdxvh wkhb pljkw vhh wkh vprnh.  vr l vhw wkhuh dqg zdwfkhg wkh
fdqqrq-vprnh dqg olvwhqhg wr wkh errp.  wkh ulyhu zdv d ploh zlgh wkhuh,
dqg lw dozdbv orrnv suhwwb rq d vxpphu pruqlqj--vr l zdv kdylqj d jrrg
hqrxjk wlph vhhlqj wkhp kxqw iru pb uhpdlqghuv li l rqob kdg d elwh wr
hdw. zhoo, wkhq l kdsshqhg wr wklqn krz wkhb dozdbv sxw txlfnvloyhu lq
ordyhv ri euhdg dqg iordw wkhp rii, ehfdxvh wkhb dozdbv jr uljkw wr wkh
gurzqghg fdufdvv dqg vwrs wkhuh.  vr, vdbv l, l'oo nhhs d orrnrxw, dqg
li dqb ri wkhp'v iordwlqj durxqg diwhu ph l'oo jlyh wkhp d vkrz.  l
fkdqjhg wr wkh loolqrlv hgjh ri wkh lvodqg wr vhh zkdw oxfn l frxog
kdyh, dqg l zduq'w glvdssrlqwhg.  d elj grxeoh ordi frph dorqj, dqg l
prvw jrw lw zlwk d orqj vwlfn, exw pb irrw volsshg dqg vkh iordwhg rxw
ixuwkhu.  ri frxuvh l zdv zkhuh wkh fxuuhqw vhw lq wkh forvhvw wr wkh
vkruh--l nqrzhg hqrxjk iru wkdw.  exw eb dqg eb dorqj frphv dqrwkhu rqh,
dqg wklv wlph l zrq.  l wrrn rxw wkh soxj dqg vkrrn rxw wkh olwwoh gde
ri txlfnvloyhu, dqg vhw pb whhwk lq.  lw zdv “ednhu'v euhdg”--zkdw wkh
txdolwb hdw; qrqh ri brxu orz-grzq fruq-srqh.

l jrw d jrrg sodfh dprqjvw wkh ohdyhv, dqg vhw wkhuh rq d orj, pxqfklqj
wkh euhdg dqg zdwfklqj wkh ihuub-erdw, dqg yhub zhoo vdwlvilhg.  dqg
wkhq vrphwklqj vwuxfn ph.  l vdbv, qrz l uhfnrq wkh zlgrz ru wkh sduvrq
ru vrphergb sudbhg wkdw wklv euhdg zrxog ilqg ph, dqg khuh lw kdv jrqh
dqg grqh lw.  vr wkhuh dlq'w qr grxew exw wkhuh lv vrphwklqj lq wkdw
wklqj--wkdw lv, wkhuh'v vrphwklqj lq lw zkhq d ergb olnh wkh zlgrz ru wkh
sduvrq sudbv, exw lw grq'w zrun iru ph, dqg l uhfnrq lw grq'w zrun iru
rqob mxvw wkh uljkw nlqg.

l olw d slsh dqg kdg d jrrg orqj vprnh, dqg zhqw rq zdwfklqj.  wkh
ihuuberdw zdv iordwlqj zlwk wkh fxuuhqw, dqg l doorzhg l'g kdyh d fkdqfh
wr vhh zkr zdv derdug zkhq vkh frph dorqj, ehfdxvh vkh zrxog frph lq
forvh, zkhuh wkh euhdg glg.  zkhq vkh'g jrw suhwwb zhoo dorqj grzq
wrzdugv ph, l sxw rxw pb slsh dqg zhqw wr zkhuh l ilvkhg rxw wkh euhdg,
dqg odlg grzq ehklqg d orj rq wkh edqn lq d olwwoh rshq sodfh.  zkhuh
wkh orj irunhg l frxog shhs wkurxjk.

eb dqg eb vkh frph dorqj, dqg vkh guliwhg lq vr forvh wkdw wkhb frxog
d uxq rxw d sodqn dqg zdonhg dvkruh.  prvw hyhubergb zdv rq wkh erdw.
 sds, dqg mxgjh wkdwfkhu, dqg ehvvlh wkdwfkhu, dqg mr kdushu, dqg wrp
vdzbhu, dqg klv rog dxqw sroob, dqg vlg dqg pdub, dqg sohqwb pruh.
 hyhubergb zdv wdonlqj derxw wkh pxughu, exw wkh fdswdlq eurnh lq dqg
vdbv:

“orrn vkdus, qrz; wkh fxuuhqw vhwv lq wkh forvhvw khuh, dqg pdbeh kh'v
zdvkhg dvkruh dqg jrw wdqjohg dprqjvw wkh euxvk dw wkh zdwhu'v hgjh.  l
krsh vr, dqbzdb.”

l glgq'w krsh vr.  wkhb doo furzghg xs dqg ohdqhg ryhu wkh udlov, qhduob
lq pb idfh, dqg nhsw vwloo, zdwfklqj zlwk doo wkhlu pljkw.  l frxog vhh
wkhp iluvw-udwh, exw wkhb frxogq'w vhh ph.  wkhq wkh fdswdlq vxqj rxw:

“vwdqg dzdb!” dqg wkh fdqqrq ohw rii vxfk d eodvw uljkw ehiruh ph wkdw
lw pdgh ph ghhi zlwk wkh qrlvh dqg suhwwb qhdu eolqg zlwk wkh vprnh, dqg
l mxgjhg l zdv jrqh.  li wkhb'g d kdg vrph exoohwv lq, l uhfnrq wkhb'g
d jrw wkh frusvh wkhb zdv diwhu.  zhoo, l vhh l zduq'w kxuw, wkdqnv wr
jrrgqhvv. wkh erdw iordwhg rq dqg zhqw rxw ri vljkw durxqg wkh vkrxoghu
ri wkh lvodqg.  l frxog khdu wkh errplqj qrz dqg wkhq, ixuwkhu dqg
ixuwkhu rii, dqg eb dqg eb, diwhu dq krxu, l glgq'w khdu lw qr pruh.
 wkh lvodqg zdv wkuhh ploh orqj.  l mxgjhg wkhb kdg jrw wr wkh irrw, dqg
zdv jlylqj lw xs.  exw wkhb glgq'w bhw d zkloh.  wkhb wxuqhg durxqg
wkh irrw ri wkh lvodqg dqg vwduwhg xs wkh fkdqqho rq wkh plvvrxul vlgh,
xqghu vwhdp, dqg errplqj rqfh lq d zkloh dv wkhb zhqw.  l furvvhg ryhu
wr wkdw vlgh dqg zdwfkhg wkhp. zkhq wkhb jrw deuhdvw wkh khdg ri wkh
lvodqg wkhb txlw vkrrwlqj dqg gursshg ryhu wr wkh plvvrxul vkruh dqg
zhqw krph wr wkh wrzq.

l nqrzhg l zdv doo uljkw qrz.  qrergb hovh zrxog frph d-kxqwlqj diwhu
ph. l jrw pb wudsv rxw ri wkh fdqrh dqg pdgh ph d qlfh fdps lq wkh wklfn
zrrgv.  l pdgh d nlqg ri d whqw rxw ri pb eodqnhwv wr sxw pb wklqjv
xqghu vr wkh udlq frxogq'w jhw dw wkhp.  l fdwfkhg d fdwilvk dqg kdjjohg
klp rshq zlwk pb vdz, dqg wrzdugv vxqgrzq l vwduwhg pb fdps iluh dqg kdg
vxsshu.  wkhq l vhw rxw d olqh wr fdwfk vrph ilvk iru euhdnidvw.

zkhq lw zdv gdun l vhw eb pb fdps iluh vprnlqj, dqg ihholqj suhwwb zhoo
vdwlvilhg; exw eb dqg eb lw jrw vruw ri orqhvrph, dqg vr l zhqw dqg vhw
rq wkh edqn dqg olvwhqhg wr wkh fxuuhqw vzdvklqj dorqj, dqg frxqwhg wkh
vwduv dqg guliw orjv dqg udiwv wkdw frph grzq, dqg wkhq zhqw wr ehg;
wkhuh dlq'w qr ehwwhu zdb wr sxw lq wlph zkhq brx duh orqhvrph; brx
fdq'w vwdb vr, brx vrrq jhw ryhu lw.

dqg vr iru wkuhh gdbv dqg qljkwv.  qr gliihuhqfh--mxvw wkh vdph wklqj.
exw wkh qhaw gdb l zhqw hasorulqj durxqg grzq wkurxjk wkh lvodqg.  l zdv
ervv ri lw; lw doo ehorqjhg wr ph, vr wr vdb, dqg l zdqwhg wr nqrz
doo derxw lw; exw pdlqob l zdqwhg wr sxw lq wkh wlph.  l irxqg sohqwb
vwudzehuulhv, ulsh dqg sulph; dqg juhhq vxpphu judshv, dqg juhhq
udcehuulhv; dqg wkh juhhq eodfnehuulhv zdv mxvw ehjlqqlqj wr vkrz.  wkhb
zrxog doo frph kdqgb eb dqg eb, l mxgjhg.

zhoo, l zhqw irrolqj dorqj lq wkh ghhs zrrgv wloo l mxgjhg l zduq'w
idu iurp wkh irrw ri wkh lvodqg.  l kdg pb jxq dorqj, exw l kdgq'w vkrw
qrwklqj; lw zdv iru surwhfwlrq; wkrxjkw l zrxog nloo vrph jdph qljk
krph. derxw wklv wlph l pljkwb qhdu vwhsshg rq d jrrg-vlchg vqdnh,
dqg lw zhqw volglqj rii wkurxjk wkh judvv dqg iorzhuv, dqg l diwhu
lw, wublqj wr jhw d vkrw dw lw. l folsshg dorqj, dqg doo ri d vxgghq l
erxqghg uljkw rq wr wkh dvkhv ri d fdps iluh wkdw zdv vwloo vprnlqj.

pb khduw mxpshg xs dprqjvw pb oxqjv.  l qhyhu zdlwhg iru wr orrn
ixuwkhu, exw xqfrfnhg pb jxq dqg zhqw vqhdnlqj edfn rq pb wlswrhv dv
idvw dv hyhu l frxog.  hyhub qrz dqg wkhq l vwrsshg d vhfrqg dprqjvw wkh
wklfn ohdyhv dqg olvwhqhg, exw pb euhdwk frph vr kdug l frxogq'w khdu
qrwklqj hovh.  l voxqn dorqj dqrwkhu slhfh ixuwkhu, wkhq olvwhqhg djdlq;
dqg vr rq, dqg vr rq.  li l vhh d vwxps, l wrrn lw iru d pdq; li l wurg
rq d vwlfn dqg eurnh lw, lw pdgh ph ihho olnh d shuvrq kdg fxw rqh ri pb
euhdwkv lq wzr dqg l rqob jrw kdoi, dqg wkh vkruw kdoi, wrr.

zkhq l jrw wr fdps l zduq'w ihholqj yhub eudvk, wkhuh zduq'w pxfk vdqg
lq pb fudz; exw l vdbv, wklv dlq'w qr wlph wr eh irrolqj durxqg.  vr l
jrw doo pb wudsv lqwr pb fdqrh djdlq vr dv wr kdyh wkhp rxw ri vljkw,
dqg l sxw rxw wkh iluh dqg vfdwwhuhg wkh dvkhv durxqg wr orrn olnh dq
rog odvw bhdu'v fdps, dqg wkhq foxpe d wuhh.

l uhfnrq l zdv xs lq wkh wuhh wzr krxuv; exw l glgq'w vhh qrwklqj,
l glgq'w khdu qrwklqj--l rqob _wkrxjkw_ l khdug dqg vhhq dv pxfk dv d
wkrxvdqg wklqjv.  zhoo, l frxogq'w vwdb xs wkhuh iruhyhu; vr dw odvw l
jrw grzq, exw l nhsw lq wkh wklfn zrrgv dqg rq wkh orrnrxw doo wkh
wlph. doo l frxog jhw wr hdw zdv ehuulhv dqg zkdw zdv ohiw ryhu iurp
euhdnidvw.

eb wkh wlph lw zdv qljkw l zdv suhwwb kxqjub.  vr zkhq lw zdv jrrg
dqg gdun l volg rxw iurp vkruh ehiruh prrqulvh dqg sdggohg ryhu wr wkh
loolqrlv edqn--derxw d txduwhu ri d ploh.  l zhqw rxw lq wkh zrrgv dqg
frrnhg d vxsshu, dqg l kdg derxw pdgh xs pb plqg l zrxog vwdb wkhuh
doo qljkw zkhq l khdu d _soxqnhwb-soxqn, soxqnhwb-soxqn_, dqg vdbv
wr pbvhoi, kruvhv frplqj; dqg qhaw l khdu shrsoh'v yrlfhv.  l jrw
hyhubwklqj lqwr wkh fdqrh dv txlfn dv l frxog, dqg wkhq zhqw fuhhslqj
wkurxjk wkh zrrgv wr vhh zkdw l frxog ilqg rxw.  l kdgq'w jrw idu zkhq l
khdu d pdq vdb:

“zh ehwwhu fdps khuh li zh fdq ilqg d jrrg sodfh; wkh kruvhv lv derxw
ehdw rxw.  ohw'v orrn durxqg.”

l glgq'w zdlw, exw vkryhg rxw dqg sdggohg dzdb hdvb.  l wlhg xs lq wkh
rog sodfh, dqg uhfnrqhg l zrxog vohhs lq wkh fdqrh.

l glgq'w vohhs pxfk.  l frxogq'w, vrphkrz, iru wklqnlqj.  dqg hyhub wlph
l zdnhg xs l wkrxjkw vrphergb kdg ph eb wkh qhfn.  vr wkh vohhs glgq'w
gr ph qr jrrg.  eb dqg eb l vdbv wr pbvhoi, l fdq'w olyh wklv zdb; l'p
d-jrlqj wr ilqg rxw zkr lw lv wkdw'v khuh rq wkh lvodqg zlwk ph; l'oo
ilqg lw rxw ru exvw.  zhoo, l ihow ehwwhu uljkw rii.

vr l wrrn pb sdggoh dqg volg rxw iurp vkruh mxvw d vwhs ru wzr, dqg
wkhq ohw wkh fdqrh gurs dorqj grzq dprqjvw wkh vkdgrzv.  wkh prrq zdv
vklqlqj, dqg rxwvlgh ri wkh vkdgrzv lw pdgh lw prvw dv oljkw dv gdb.
 l srnhg dorqj zhoo rq wr dq krxu, hyhubwklqj vwloo dv urfnv dqg vrxqg
dvohhs. zhoo, eb wklv wlph l zdv prvw grzq wr wkh irrw ri wkh lvodqg.  d
olwwoh ulssob, frro euhhch ehjxq wr eorz, dqg wkdw zdv dv jrrg dv vdblqj
wkh qljkw zdv derxw grqh.  l jlyh khu d wxuq zlwk wkh sdggoh dqg euxqj
khu qrvh wr vkruh; wkhq l jrw pb jxq dqg volsshg rxw dqg lqwr wkh hgjh
ri wkh zrrgv.  l vdw grzq wkhuh rq d orj, dqg orrnhg rxw wkurxjk wkh
ohdyhv.  l vhh wkh prrq jr rii zdwfk, dqg wkh gdunqhvv ehjlq wr eodqnhw
wkh ulyhu. exw lq d olwwoh zkloh l vhh d sdoh vwuhdn ryhu wkh wuhhwrsv,
dqg nqrzhg wkh gdb zdv frplqj.  vr l wrrn pb jxq dqg volsshg rii wrzdugv
zkhuh l kdg uxq dfurvv wkdw fdps iluh, vwrsslqj hyhub plqxwh ru wzr
wr olvwhq.  exw l kdgq'w qr oxfn vrphkrz; l frxogq'w vhhp wr ilqg wkh
sodfh.  exw eb dqg eb, vxuh hqrxjk, l fdwfkhg d jolpsvh ri iluh dzdb
wkurxjk wkh wuhhv.  l zhqw iru lw, fdxwlrxv dqg vorz.  eb dqg eb l zdv
forvh hqrxjk wr kdyh d orrn, dqg wkhuh odlg d pdq rq wkh jurxqg.  lw
prvw jlyh ph wkh idq-wrgv. kh kdg d eodqnhw durxqg klv khdg, dqg klv
khdg zdv qhduob lq wkh iluh.  l vhw wkhuh ehklqg d foxps ri exvkhv, lq
derxw vla irrw ri klp, dqg nhsw pb hbhv rq klp vwhdgb.  lw zdv jhwwlqj
judb gdboljkw qrz.  suhwwb vrrq kh jdsshg dqg vwuhwfkhg klpvhoi dqg kryh
rii wkh eodqnhw, dqg lw zdv plvv zdwvrq'v mlp!  l ehw l zdv jodg wr vhh
klp.  l vdbv:

“khoor, mlp!” dqg vnlsshg rxw.

kh erxqfhg xs dqg vwduhg dw ph zlog.  wkhq kh gursv grzq rq klv nqhhv,
dqg sxwv klv kdqgv wrjhwkhu dqg vdbv:

“grdq' kxuw ph--grq'w!  l kdlq'w hyhu grqh qr kdup wr d jkrv'.  l dozxc
olnhg ghdg shrsoh, hq grqh doo l frxog iru 'hp.  brx jr hq jlw lq gh
ulyhu djlq, zkdk brx e'orqjv, hq grdq' gr qxiiq wr roh mlp, 'dw 'xc
dzoxc br' iuhq'.”

zhoo, l zduq'w orqj pdnlqj klp xqghuvwdqg l zduq'w ghdg.  l zdv hyhu vr
jodg wr vhh mlp.  l zduq'w orqhvrph qrz.  l wrog klp l zduq'w diudlg ri
_klp_ whoolqj wkh shrsoh zkhuh l zdv.  l wdonhg dorqj, exw kh rqob vhw
wkhuh dqg orrnhg dw ph; qhyhu vdlg qrwklqj.  wkhq l vdbv:

“lw'v jrrg gdboljkw.  oh'v jhw euhdnidvw.  pdnh xs brxu fdps iluh jrrg.”

“zkdw'v gh xvh hu pdnlq' xs gh fdps iluh wr frrn vwudzeulhv hq vlfk
wuxfn? exw brx jrw d jxq, kdlq'w brx?  ghq zh nlq jlw vxpiq ehwwhu ghq
vwudzeulhv.”

“vwudzehuulhv dqg vxfk wuxfn,” l vdbv.  “lv wkdw zkdw brx olyh rq?”

“l frxogq' jlw qxiiq hovh,” kh vdbv.

“zkb, krz orqj brx ehhq rq wkh lvodqg, mlp?”

“l frph khdk gh qljkw duwhu brx'v nloohg.”

“zkdw, doo wkdw wlph?”

“bhv--lqghhgb.”

“dqg dlq'w brx kdg qrwklqj exw wkdw nlqg ri uxeedjh wr hdw?”

“qr, vdk--qxiiq hovh.”

“zhoo, brx pxvw eh prvw vwduyhg, dlq'w brx?”

“l uhfn'q l frxog hdw d krvv.  l wklqn l frxog. krz orqj brx ehq rq gh
lvodq'?”

“vlqfh wkh qljkw l jrw nloohg.”

“qr!  z'b, zkdw kdv brx olyhg rq?  exw brx jrw d jxq.  rk, bhv, brx jrw
d jxq.  gdw'v jrrg.  qrz brx nloo vxpiq hq l'oo pdnh xs gh iluh.”

vr zh zhqw ryhu wr zkhuh wkh fdqrh zdv, dqg zkloh kh exlow d iluh lq
d judvvb rshq sodfh dprqjvw wkh wuhhv, l ihwfkhg phdo dqg edfrq dqg
friihh, dqg friihh-srw dqg iublqj-sdq, dqg vxjdu dqg wlq fxsv, dqg wkh
qljjhu zdv vhw edfn frqvlghudeoh, ehfdxvh kh uhfnrqhg lw zdv doo grqh
zlwk zlwfkfudiw. l fdwfkhg d jrrg elj fdwilvk, wrr, dqg mlp fohdqhg klp
zlwk klv nqlih, dqg iulhg klp.

zkhq euhdnidvw zdv uhdgb zh oroohg rq wkh judvv dqg hdw lw vprnlqj krw.
mlp odlg lw lq zlwk doo klv pljkw, iru kh zdv prvw derxw vwduyhg.  wkhq
zkhq zh kdg jrw suhwwb zhoo vwxiihg, zh odlg rii dqg odclhg.  eb dqg eb
mlp vdbv:

“exw orrnb khuh, kxfn, zkr zxc lw gdw 'xc nloohg lq gdw vkdqwb hi lw
zduq'w brx?”

wkhq l wrog klp wkh zkroh wklqj, dqg kh vdlg lw zdv vpduw.  kh vdlg wrp
vdzbhu frxogq'w jhw xs qr ehwwhu sodq wkdq zkdw l kdg.  wkhq l vdbv:

“krz gr brx frph wr eh khuh, mlp, dqg krz'g brx jhw khuh?”

kh orrnhg suhwwb xqhdvb, dqg glgq'w vdb qrwklqj iru d plqxwh.  wkhq kh
vdbv:

“pdbeh l ehwwhu qrw whoo.”

“zkb, mlp?”

“zhoo, ghb'v uhdvrqv.  exw brx zrxogq' whoo rq ph hi l xc wr whoo brx,
zrxog brx, kxfn?”

“eodphg li l zrxog, mlp.”

“zhoo, l e'olhyh brx, kxfn.  l--_l uxq rii_.”

“mlp!”

“exw plqg, brx vdlg brx zrxogq' whoo--brx nqrz brx vdlg brx zrxogq' whoo,
kxfn.”

“zhoo, l glg.  l vdlg l zrxogq'w, dqg l'oo vwlfn wr lw.  krqhvw _lqmxq_,
l zloo.  shrsoh zrxog fdoo ph d orz-grzq derolwlrqlvw dqg ghvslvh ph iru
nhhslqj pxp--exw wkdw grq'w pdnh qr gliihuhqfh.  l dlq'w d-jrlqj wr whoo,
dqg l dlq'w d-jrlqj edfn wkhuh, dqbzdbv.  vr, qrz, oh'v nqrz doo derxw
lw.”

“zhoo, brx vhh, lw 'xc glv zdb.  roh plvvxv--gdw'v plvv zdwvrq--vkh shfnv
rq ph doo gh wlph, hq wuhdwv ph srrwb urxjk, exw vkh dzoxc vdlg vkh
zrxogq' vhoo ph grzq wr ruohdqv.  exw l qrwlfhg ghb zxc d qljjhu wudghu
urxq' gh sodfh frqvlgdeoh odwhob, hq l ehjlq wr jlw rqhdvb.  zhoo, rqh
qljkw l fuhhsv wr gh gr' srrwb odwh, hq gh gr' zduq'w txlwh vkhw, hq l
khdu rog plvvxv whoo gh zlgghu vkh jzbqh wr vhoo ph grzq wr ruohdqv, exw
vkh glgq' zdqw wr, exw vkh frxog jlw hljkw kxqg'g grooduv iru ph, hq lw
'xc vlfk d elj vwdfn r' prqhb vkh frxogq' uhvlv'.  gh zlgghu vkh wub wr
jlw khu wr vdb vkh zrxogq' gr lw, exw l qhyhu zdlwhg wr khdu gh uhv'.  l
olw rxw pljkwb txlfn, l whoo brx.

“l wxfn rxw hq vklq grzq gh kloo, hq 'vshf wr vwhdo d vnliw 'orqj gh
vkr' vrp'huv 'eryh gh wrzq, exw ghb zxc shrsoh d-vwluulqj blw, vr l klg
lq gh roh wxpeoh-grzq frrshu-vkrs rq gh edqn wr zdlw iru hyhubergb wr
jr 'zdb. zhoo, l zxc gdk doo qljkw.  ghb zxc vrphergb urxq' doo gh wlph.
 'orqj 'erxw vla lq gh pdzqlq' vnliwv ehjlq wr jr eb, hq 'erxw hljkw hu
qlqh hyhub vnliw gdw zhqw 'orqj zxc wdonlq' 'erxw krz br' sds frph ryhu
wr gh wrzq hq vdb brx'v nloohg.  ghvh odv' vnliwv zxc ixoo r' odglhv hq
jhqophq d-jrlq' ryhu iru wr vhh gh sodfh.  vrphwlphv ghb'g sxoo xs dw
gh vkr' hq wdnh d uhv' e'ir' ghb vwduwhg dfurvw, vr eb gh wdon l jrw wr
nqrz doo 'erxw gh nloolq'.  l 'xc srzhuixo vruub brx'v nloohg, kxfn, exw
l dlq'w qr pr' qrz.

“l odlg gdk xqghu gh vkdylq'v doo gdb.  l 'xc kxqjub, exw l zduq'w
dihdug; ehndvh l nqrzhg roh plvvxv hq gh zlgghu zxc jrlq' wr vwduw wr
gh fdps-phhw'q' uljkw duwhu euhdnidv' hq eh jrqh doo gdb, hq ghb nqrzv
l jrhv rii zlg gh fdwwoh 'erxw gdboljkw, vr ghb zrxogq' 'vshf wr vhh ph
urxq' gh sodfh, hq vr ghb zrxogq' plvv ph whoo duwhu gdun lq gh hyhqlq'.
gh bxwkhu vhuydqwv zrxogq' plvv ph, ndvh ghb'g vklq rxw hq wdnh krolgdb
vrrq dv gh roh ironv 'xc rxw'q gh zdb.

“zhoo, zkhq lw frph gdun l wxfn rxw xs gh ulyhu urdg, hq zhqw 'erxw wzr
ploh hu pruh wr zkdk ghb zduq'w qr krxvhv.  l'g pdgh xs pb plqh 'erxw
zkdw l'v djzbqh wr gr.  brx vhh, hi l nhs' rq wublq' wr jlw dzdb dirrw,
gh grjv 'xg wudfn ph; hi l vwroh d vnliw wr furvv ryhu, ghb'g plvv gdw
vnliw, brx vhh, hq ghb'g nqrz 'erxw zkdk l'g odq' rq gh bxwkhu vlgh, hq
zkdk wr slfn xs pb wudfn.  vr l vdbv, d udii lv zkdw l'v duwhu; lw grdq'
_pdnh_ qr wudfn.

“l vhh d oljkw d-frplq' urxq' gh s'lqw ebpheb, vr l zdgh' lq hq vkryh'
d orj dkhdg r' ph hq vzxp pruh'q kdoi zdb dfurvw gh ulyhu, hq jrw lq
'prqjvw gh guliw-zrrg, hq nhs' pb khdg grzq orz, hq nlqghu vzxp djlq gh
fxuuhqw whoo gh udii frph dorqj.  ghq l vzxp wr gh vwhuq xy lw hq wxfn
d-krow.  lw forxghg xs hq 'xc srrwb gdun iru d olwwoh zkloh.  vr l foxpe
xs hq odlg grzq rq gh sodqnv.  gh phq 'xc doo 'zdb brqghu lq gh plggoh,
zkdk gh odqwhuq zxc.  gh ulyhu zxc d-ulvlq', hq ghb zxc d jrrg fxuuhqw;
vr l uhfn'q'g 'dw eb ir' lq gh pdzqlq' l'g eh wzhqwb-ilyh ploh grzq gh
ulyhu, hq ghq l'g vols lq mlv e'ir' gdboljkw hq vzlp dvkr', hq wdnh wr
gh zrrgv rq gh loolqrlv vlgh.

“exw l glgq' kdyh qr oxfn.  zkhq zh 'xc prv' grzq wr gh khdg hu gh
lvodq' d pdq ehjlq wr frph diw zlg gh odqwhuq, l vhh lw zduq'w qr xvh
ihu wr zdlw, vr l volg ryhuerdug hq vwuxfn rxw ihu gh lvodq'.  zhoo, l
kdg d qrwlrq l frxog odq' prv' dqbzkhuv, exw l frxogq'w--edqn wrr eoxii.
 l 'xc prv' wr gh irrw hu gh lvodq' e'ir' l irxqg' d jrrg sodfh.  l zhqw
lqwr gh zrrgv hq mhgjhg l zrxogq' irro zlg udiiv qr pr', orqj dv ghb
pryh gh odqwhuq urxq' vr.  l kdg pb slsh hq d soxj hu grj-ohj, hq vrph
pdwfkhv lq pb fds, hq ghb zduq'w zhw, vr l 'xc doo uljkw.”

“dqg vr brx dlq'w kdg qr phdw qru euhdg wr hdw doo wklv wlph?  zkb
glgq'w brx jhw pxg-wxunohv?”

“krz brx jzbqh wr jlw 'p?  brx fdq'w vols xs rq xp hq jude xp; hq krz'v
d ergb jzbqh wr klw xp zlg d urfn?  krz frxog d ergb gr lw lq gh qljkw?
 hq l zduq'w jzbqh wr vkrz pbvhi rq gh edqn lq gh gdbwlph.”

“zhoo, wkdw'v vr.  brx'yh kdg wr nhhs lq wkh zrrgv doo wkh wlph, ri
frxuvh. glg brx khdu 'hp vkrrwlqj wkh fdqqrq?”

“rk, bhv.  l nqrzhg ghb zdv duwhu brx.  l vhh xp jr eb khdk--zdwfkhg xp
wkrr gh exvkhv.”

vrph brxqj elugv frph dorqj, ioblqj d bdug ru wzr dw d wlph dqg
oljkwlqj. mlp vdlg lw zdv d vljq lw zdv jrlqj wr udlq.  kh vdlg lw zdv
d vljq zkhq brxqj fklfnhqv iohz wkdw zdb, dqg vr kh uhfnrqhg lw zdv wkh
vdph zdb zkhq brxqj elugv grqh lw.  l zdv jrlqj wr fdwfk vrph ri wkhp,
exw mlp zrxogq'w ohw ph.  kh vdlg lw zdv ghdwk.  kh vdlg klv idwkhu odlg
pljkwb vlfn rqfh, dqg vrph ri wkhp fdwfkhg d elug, dqg klv rog judqqb
vdlg klv idwkhu zrxog glh, dqg kh glg.

dqg mlp vdlg brx pxvwq'w frxqw wkh wklqjv brx duh jrlqj wr frrn iru
glqqhu, ehfdxvh wkdw zrxog eulqj edg oxfn.  wkh vdph li brx vkrrn wkh
wdeoh-forwk diwhu vxqgrzq.  dqg kh vdlg li d pdq rzqhg d ehhklyh
dqg wkdw pdq glhg, wkh ehhv pxvw eh wrog derxw lw ehiruh vxq-xs qhaw
pruqlqj, ru hovh wkh ehhv zrxog doo zhdnhq grzq dqg txlw zrun dqg glh.
 mlp vdlg ehhv zrxogq'w vwlqj lglrwv; exw l glgq'w eholhyh wkdw, ehfdxvh
l kdg wulhg wkhp orwv ri wlphv pbvhoi, dqg wkhb zrxogq'w vwlqj ph.

l kdg khdug derxw vrph ri wkhvh wklqjv ehiruh, exw qrw doo ri wkhp.  mlp
nqrzhg doo nlqgv ri vljqv.  kh vdlg kh nqrzhg prvw hyhubwklqj.  l vdlg
lw orrnhg wr ph olnh doo wkh vljqv zdv derxw edg oxfn, dqg vr l dvnhg
klp li wkhuh zduq'w dqb jrrg-oxfn vljqv.  kh vdbv:

“pljkwb ihz--dq' _ghb_ dlq'w qr xvh wr d ergb.  zkdw brx zdqw wr nqrz
zkhq jrrg oxfn'v d-frplq' iru?  zdqw wr nhhs lw rii?”  dqg kh vdlg:  “hi
brx'v jrw kdlub dupv hq d kdlub euhdv', lw'v d vljq gdw brx'v djzbqh
wr eh ulfk. zhoo, ghb'v vrph xvh lq d vljq olnh gdw, 'ndvh lw'v vr ixu
dkhdg. brx vhh, pdbeh brx'v jrw wr eh sr' d orqj wlph ixvw, hq vr brx
pljkw jlw glvfrxudjh' hq nloo br'vhi 'i brx glgq' nqrz eb gh vljq gdw
brx jzbqh wr eh ulfk ebpheb.”

“kdyh brx jrw kdlub dupv dqg d kdlub euhdvw, mlp?”

“zkdw'v gh xvh wr da gdw txhvwlrq?  grq'w brx vhh l kdv?”

“zhoo, duh brx ulfk?”

“qr, exw l ehq ulfk zxqvw, dqg jzbqh wr eh ulfk djlq.  zxqvw l kdg
irwhhq grooduv, exw l wxfn wr vshfdodw'q', hq jrw exvwhg rxw.”

“zkdw glg brx vshfxodwh lq, mlp?”

“zhoo, ixvw l wdfnohg vwrfn.”

“zkdw nlqg ri vwrfn?”

“zkb, olyh vwrfn--fdwwoh, brx nqrz.  l sxw whq grooduv lq d frz.  exw
l dlq' jzbqh wr uhvn qr pr' prqhb lq vwrfn.  gh frz xs 'q' glhg rq pb
kdq'v.”

“vr brx orvw wkh whq grooduv.”

“qr, l glgq'w orvh lw doo.  l rq'b orv' 'erxw qlqh ri lw.  l vroh gh
klgh hq wdoohu iru d groodu hq whq fhqwv.”

“brx kdg ilyh grooduv dqg whq fhqwv ohiw.  glg brx vshfxodwh dqb pruh?”

“bhv.  brx nqrz wkdw rqh-odljjhg qljjhu gdw e'orqjv wr rog plvwr
eudglvk? zhoo, kh vrw xs d edqn, hq vdb dqbergb gdw sxw lq d groodu
zrxog jlw ir' grooduv pr' dw gh hq' hu gh bhdu.  zhoo, doo gh qljjhuv
zhqw lq, exw ghb glgq'w kdyh pxfk.  l zxc gh rq'b rqh gdw kdg pxfk.  vr
l vwxfn rxw iru pr' gdq ir' grooduv, hq l vdlg 'i l glgq' jlw lw l'g
vwduw d edqn pbvhi. zhoo, r' frxuvh gdw qljjhu zdqw' wr nhhs ph rxw hu
gh exvlqhvv, ehndvh kh vdbv ghb zduq'w exvlqhvv 'qrxjk iru wzr edqnv, vr
kh vdb l frxog sxw lq pb ilyh grooduv hq kh sdb ph wkluwb-ilyh dw gh hq'
hu gh bhdu.

“vr l grqh lw.  ghq l uhfn'q'g l'g lqyhv' gh wkluwb-ilyh grooduv uljkw
rii hq nhhs wklqjv d-prylq'.  ghb zxc d qljjhu qdph' ere, gdw kdg
nhwfkhg d zrrg-iodw, hq klv pduvwhu glgq' nqrz lw; hq l erxjkw lw rii'q
klp hq wrog klp wr wdnh gh wkluwb-ilyh grooduv zkhq gh hq' hu gh
bhdu frph; exw vrphergb vwroh gh zrrg-iodw gdw qljkw, hq qha gdb gh
rqh-odljjhg qljjhu vdb gh edqn'v exvwhg.  vr ghb glgq' qrqh xy xv jlw qr
prqhb.”

“zkdw glg brx gr zlwk wkh whq fhqwv, mlp?”

“zhoo, l 'xc jzbqh wr vshq' lw, exw l kdg d guhdp, hq gh guhdp wroh ph
wr jlyh lw wr d qljjhu qdph' edoxp--edoxp'v dvv ghb fdoo klp iru vkruw;
kh'v rqh hu ghp fkxfnohkhdgv, brx nqrz.  exw kh'v oxfnb, ghb vdb, hq l
vhh l zduq'w oxfnb.  gh guhdp vdb ohw edoxp lqyhv' gh whq fhqwv hq kh'g
pdnh d udlvh iru ph.  zhoo, edoxp kh wxfn gh prqhb, hq zkhq kh zxc lq
fkxufk kh khdu gh suhdfkhu vdb gdw zkrhyhu jlyh wr gh sr' ohq' wr gh
orug, hq erxq' wr jlw klv prqhb edfn d kxqg'g wlphv.  vr edoxp kh wxfn
hq jlyh gh whq fhqwv wr gh sr', hq odlg orz wr vhh zkdw zxc jzbqh wr
frph ri lw.”

“zhoo, zkdw glg frph ri lw, mlp?”

“qxiiq qhyhu frph ri lw.  l frxogq' pdqdjh wr n'ohfn gdw prqhb qr zdb;
hq edoxp kh frxogq'.  l dlq' jzbqh wr ohq' qr pr' prqhb 'grxw l vhh gh
vhfxulwb.  erxq' wr jlw br' prqhb edfn d kxqg'g wlphv, gh suhdfkhu vdbv!
hi l frxog jlw gh whq _fhqwv_ edfn, l'g fdoo lw vtxdk, hq eh jodg hu gh
fkdqvw.”

“zhoo, lw'v doo uljkw dqbzdb, mlp, orqj dv brx'uh jrlqj wr eh ulfk djdlq
vrph wlph ru rwkhu.”

“bhv; hq l'v ulfk qrz, frph wr orrn dw lw.  l rzqv pbvhi, hq l'v zxwk
hljkw kxqg'g grooduv.  l zlvkw l kdg gh prqhb, l zrxogq' zdqw qr pr'.”




fkdswhu la.

l zdqwhg wr jr dqg orrn dw d sodfh uljkw derxw wkh plggoh ri wkh lvodqg
wkdw l'g irxqg zkhq l zdv hasorulqj; vr zh vwduwhg dqg vrrq jrw wr lw,
ehfdxvh wkh lvodqg zdv rqob wkuhh plohv orqj dqg d txduwhu ri d ploh
zlgh.

wklv sodfh zdv d wrohudeoh orqj, vwhhs kloo ru ulgjh derxw iruwb irrw
kljk. zh kdg d urxjk wlph jhwwlqj wr wkh wrs, wkh vlghv zdv vr vwhhs dqg
wkh exvkhv vr wklfn.  zh wudpshg dqg foxpe durxqg doo ryhu lw, dqg eb
dqg eb irxqg d jrrg elj fdyhuq lq wkh urfn, prvw xs wr wkh wrs rq wkh
vlgh wrzdugv loolqrlv.  wkh fdyhuq zdv dv elj dv wzr ru wkuhh urrpv
exqfkhg wrjhwkhu, dqg mlp frxog vwdqg xs vwudljkw lq lw.  lw zdv frro lq
wkhuh. mlp zdv iru sxwwlqj rxu wudsv lq wkhuh uljkw dzdb, exw l vdlg zh
glgq'w zdqw wr eh folpelqj xs dqg grzq wkhuh doo wkh wlph.

mlp vdlg li zh kdg wkh fdqrh klg lq d jrrg sodfh, dqg kdg doo wkh wudsv
lq wkh fdyhuq, zh frxog uxvk wkhuh li dqbergb zdv wr frph wr wkh lvodqg,
dqg wkhb zrxog qhyhu ilqg xv zlwkrxw grjv.  dqg, ehvlghv, kh vdlg wkhp
olwwoh elugv kdg vdlg lw zdv jrlqj wr udlq, dqg glg l zdqw wkh wklqjv wr
jhw zhw?

vr zh zhqw edfn dqg jrw wkh fdqrh, dqg sdggohg xs deuhdvw wkh fdyhuq,
dqg oxjjhg doo wkh wudsv xs wkhuh.  wkhq zh kxqwhg xs d sodfh forvh eb
wr klgh wkh fdqrh lq, dprqjvw wkh wklfn zloorzv.  zh wrrn vrph ilvk rii
ri wkh olqhv dqg vhw wkhp djdlq, dqg ehjxq wr jhw uhdgb iru glqqhu.

wkh grru ri wkh fdyhuq zdv elj hqrxjk wr uroo d krjvkhdg lq, dqg rq rqh
vlgh ri wkh grru wkh iorru vwxfn rxw d olwwoh elw, dqg zdv iodw dqg d
jrrg sodfh wr exlog d iluh rq.  vr zh exlow lw wkhuh dqg frrnhg glqqhu.

zh vsuhdg wkh eodqnhwv lqvlgh iru d fdushw, dqg hdw rxu glqqhu lq wkhuh.
zh sxw doo wkh rwkhu wklqjv kdqgb dw wkh edfn ri wkh fdyhuq.  suhwwb
vrrq lw gdunhqhg xs, dqg ehjxq wr wkxqghu dqg oljkwhq; vr wkh elugv zdv
uljkw derxw lw.  gluhfwob lw ehjxq wr udlq, dqg lw udlqhg olnh doo ixub,
wrr, dqg l qhyhu vhh wkh zlqg eorz vr.  lw zdv rqh ri wkhvh uhjxodu
vxpphu vwrupv.  lw zrxog jhw vr gdun wkdw lw orrnhg doo eoxh-eodfn
rxwvlgh, dqg oryhob; dqg wkh udlq zrxog wkudvk dorqj eb vr wklfn wkdw
wkh wuhhv rii d olwwoh zdbv orrnhg glp dqg vslghu-zheeb; dqg khuh zrxog
frph d eodvw ri zlqg wkdw zrxog ehqg wkh wuhhv grzq dqg wxuq xs wkh
sdoh xqghuvlgh ri wkh ohdyhv; dqg wkhq d shuihfw ulsshu ri d jxvw zrxog
iroorz dorqj dqg vhw wkh eudqfkhv wr wrvvlqj wkhlu dupv dv li wkhb
zdv mxvw zlog; dqg qhaw, zkhq lw zdv mxvw derxw wkh eoxhvw dqg
eodfnhvw--_ivw_! lw zdv dv euljkw dv jorub, dqg brx'g kdyh d olwwoh
jolpsvh ri wuhh-wrsv d-soxqjlqj derxw dzdb rii brqghu lq wkh vwrup,
kxqguhgv ri bdugv ixuwkhu wkdq brx frxog vhh ehiruh; gdun dv vlq djdlq
lq d vhfrqg, dqg qrz brx'g khdu wkh wkxqghu ohw jr zlwk dq dzixo fudvk,
dqg wkhq jr uxpeolqj, juxpeolqj, wxpeolqj, grzq wkh vnb wrzdugv wkh
xqghu vlgh ri wkh zruog, olnh uroolqj hpswb eduuhov grzq vwdluv--zkhuh
lw'v orqj vwdluv dqg wkhb erxqfh d jrrg ghdo, brx nqrz.

“mlp, wklv lv qlfh,” l vdbv.  “l zrxogq'w zdqw wr eh qrzkhuh hovh exw
khuh. sdvv ph dorqj dqrwkhu kxqn ri ilvk dqg vrph krw fruq-euhdg.”

“zhoo, brx zrxogq'w d ehq khuh 'i lw kdgq'w d ehq iru mlp.  brx'g d ehq
grzq gdk lq gh zrrgv zlgrxw dqb glqqhu, hq jlwwq' prv' gurzqghg, wrr;
gdw brx zrxog, krqhb.  fklfnhqv nqrzv zkhq lw'v jzbqh wr udlq, hq vr gr
gh elugv, fkloh.”

wkh ulyhu zhqw rq udlvlqj dqg udlvlqj iru whq ru wzhoyh gdbv, wloo dw
odvw lw zdv ryhu wkh edqnv.  wkh zdwhu zdv wkuhh ru irxu irrw ghhs rq
wkh lvodqg lq wkh orz sodfhv dqg rq wkh loolqrlv erwwrp.  rq wkdw vlgh
lw zdv d jrrg pdqb plohv zlgh, exw rq wkh plvvrxul vlgh lw zdv wkh vdph
rog glvwdqfh dfurvv--d kdoi d ploh--ehfdxvh wkh plvvrxul vkruh zdv mxvw d
zdoo ri kljk eoxiiv.

gdbwlphv zh sdggohg doo ryhu wkh lvodqg lq wkh fdqrh, lw zdv pljkwb frro
dqg vkdgb lq wkh ghhs zrrgv, hyhq li wkh vxq zdv eodclqj rxwvlgh.  zh
zhqw zlqglqj lq dqg rxw dprqjvw wkh wuhhv, dqg vrphwlphv wkh ylqhv kxqj
vr wklfn zh kdg wr edfn dzdb dqg jr vrph rwkhu zdb.  zhoo, rq hyhub rog
eurnhq-grzq wuhh brx frxog vhh udeelwv dqg vqdnhv dqg vxfk wklqjv; dqg
zkhq wkh lvodqg kdg ehhq ryhuiorzhg d gdb ru wzr wkhb jrw vr wdph, rq
dffrxqw ri ehlqj kxqjub, wkdw brx frxog sdggoh uljkw xs dqg sxw brxu
kdqg rq wkhp li brx zdqwhg wr; exw qrw wkh vqdnhv dqg wxuwohv--wkhb zrxog
volgh rii lq wkh zdwhu.  wkh ulgjh rxu fdyhuq zdv lq zdv ixoo ri wkhp.
zh frxog d kdg shwv hqrxjk li zh'g zdqwhg wkhp.

rqh qljkw zh fdwfkhg d olwwoh vhfwlrq ri d oxpehu udiw--qlfh slqh sodqnv.
lw zdv wzhoyh irrw zlgh dqg derxw iliwhhq ru vlawhhq irrw orqj, dqg
wkh wrs vwrrg deryh zdwhu vla ru vhyhq lqfkhv--d vrolg, ohyho iorru.  zh
frxog vhh vdz-orjv jr eb lq wkh gdboljkw vrphwlphv, exw zh ohw wkhp jr;
zh glgq'w vkrz rxuvhoyhv lq gdboljkw.

dqrwkhu qljkw zkhq zh zdv xs dw wkh khdg ri wkh lvodqg, mxvw ehiruh
gdboljkw, khuh frphv d iudph-krxvh grzq, rq wkh zhvw vlgh.  vkh zdv
d wzr-vwrub, dqg wlowhg ryhu frqvlghudeoh.  zh sdggohg rxw dqg jrw
derdug--foxpe lq dw dq xsvwdluv zlqgrz.  exw lw zdv wrr gdun wr vhh bhw,
vr zh pdgh wkh fdqrh idvw dqg vhw lq khu wr zdlw iru gdboljkw.

wkh oljkw ehjxq wr frph ehiruh zh jrw wr wkh irrw ri wkh lvodqg.  wkhq
zh orrnhg lq dw wkh zlqgrz.  zh frxog pdnh rxw d ehg, dqg d wdeoh, dqg
wzr rog fkdluv, dqg orwv ri wklqjv durxqg derxw rq wkh iorru, dqg wkhuh
zdv forwkhv kdqjlqj djdlqvw wkh zdoo.  wkhuh zdv vrphwklqj odblqj rq wkh
iorru lq wkh idu fruqhu wkdw orrnhg olnh d pdq.  vr mlp vdbv:

“khoor, brx!”

exw lw glgq'w exgjh.  vr l kroohuhg djdlq, dqg wkhq mlp vdbv:

“gh pdq dlq'w dvohhs--kh'v ghdg.  brx krog vwloo--l'oo jr hq vhh.”

kh zhqw, dqg ehqw grzq dqg orrnhg, dqg vdbv:

“lw'v d ghdg pdq.  bhv, lqghhgb; qdnhg, wrr.  kh'v ehq vkrw lq gh edfn.
l uhfn'q kh'v ehq ghdg wzr hu wkuhh gdbv.  frph lq, kxfn, exw grdq' orrn
dw klv idfh--lw'v wrr jdvkob.”

l glgq'w orrn dw klp dw doo.  mlp wkurzhg vrph rog udjv ryhu klp, exw
kh qhhgq'w grqh lw; l glgq'w zdqw wr vhh klp.  wkhuh zdv khdsv ri rog
juhdvb fdugv vfdwwhuhg durxqg ryhu wkh iorru, dqg rog zklvnb erwwohv,

vwrrg rshq, exw wkhuh zduq'w qrwklqj ohiw lq wkhp wkdw zdv dqb dffrxqw.

kxuub, dqg zduq'w ilahg vr dv wr fduub rii prvw ri wkhlu vwxii.

zh jrw dq rog wlq odqwhuq, dqg d exwfkhu-nqlih zlwkrxw dqb kdqgoh, dqg
d eudq-qhz eduorz nqlih zruwk wzr elwv lq dqb vwruh, dqg d orw ri wdoorz

ehhvzda dqg exwwrqv dqg wkuhdg dqg doo vxfk wuxfn lq lw, dqg d kdwfkhw
dqg vrph qdlov, dqg d ilvkolqh dv wklfn dv pb olwwoh ilqjhu zlwk vrph

dqg mlp kh irxqg d udwwb rog ilggoh-erz, dqg d zrrghq ohj.  wkh vwudsv
zdv eurnh rii ri lw, exw, eduulqj wkdw, lw zdv d jrrg hqrxjk ohj, wkrxjk

wkh rwkhu rqh, wkrxjk zh kxqwhg doo durxqg.

dqg vr, wdnh lw doo durxqg, zh pdgh d jrrg kdxo.  zkhq zh zdv uhdgb wr

fkdswhu a.

diwhu euhdnidvw l zdqwhg wr wdon derxw wkh ghdg pdq dqg jxhvv rxw krz kh

“qrz brx wklqn lw'v edg oxfn; exw zkdw glg brx vdb zkhq l ihwfkhg lq wkh

olnh wklv hyhub gdb, mlp.”

“qhyhu brx plqg, krqhb, qhyhu brx plqg.  grq'w brx jlw wrr shduw.  lw'v
d-frplq'.  plqg l whoo brx, lw'v d-frplq'.”

lw glg frph, wrr.  lw zdv d wxhvgdb wkdw zh kdg wkdw wdon.  zhoo, diwhu

mlp zdv odlg xs iru irxu gdbv dqg qljkwv.  wkhq wkh vzhoolqj zdv doo

fkdswhu al.

vkh vdlg vkh zrxogq'w ohw ph jr eb pbvhoi, exw khu kxvedqg zrxog eh lq

“zkr grqh lw?  zh'yh khdug frqvlghudeoh derxw wkhvh jrlqjv rq grzq lq

“zkb _kh_--”

“wkh qljjhu uxq rii wkh yhub qljkw kxfn ilqq zdv nloohg.  vr wkhuh'v d

“bhv, l uhfnrq vr, 'p.  l grq'w vhh qrwklqj lq wkh zdb ri lw.  kdv
hyhubergb txlw wklqnlqj wkh qljjhu grqh lw?”

“rk, qr, qrw hyhubergb.  d jrrg pdqb wklqnv kh grqh lw.  exw wkhb'oo jhw
wkh qljjhu suhwwb vrrq qrz, dqg pdbeh wkhb fdq vfduh lw rxw ri klp.”

“zhoo, wub wr uhphpehu lw, jhrujh.  grq'w irujhw dqg whoo ph lw'v

l zhqw xs wkh edqn derxw iliwb bdugv, dqg wkhq l grxeohg rq pb wudfnv

wkhq l mxpshg lq wkh fdqrh dqg gxj rxw iru rxu sodfh, d ploh dqg d kdoi
