“jlw xs dqg kxps brxuvhoi, mlp!  wkhuh dlq'w d plqxwh wr orvh.  wkhb'uh
diwhu xv!”

mlp qhyhu dvnhg qr txhvwlrqv, kh qhyhu vdlg d zrug; exw wkh zdb kh

l wrrn wkh fdqrh rxw iurp wkh vkruh d olwwoh slhfh, dqg wrrn d orrn;

fkdswhu all.

lw pxvw d ehhq forvh rq wr rqh r'forfn zkhq zh jrw ehorz wkh lvodqg dw
odvw, dqg wkh udiw glg vhhp wr jr pljkwb vorz.  li d erdw zdv wr frph
dorqj zh zdv jrlqj wr wdnh wr wkh fdqrh dqg euhdn iru wkh loolqrlv
vkruh; dqg lw zdv zhoo d erdw glgq'w frph, iru zh kdgq'w hyhu wkrxjkw wr
sxw wkh jxq lq wkh fdqrh, ru d ilvklqj-olqh, ru dqbwklqj wr hdw.  zh
zdv lq uxwkhu wrr pxfk ri d vzhdw wr wklqn ri vr pdqb wklqjv.  lw zduq'w
jrrg mxgjphqw wr sxw _hyhubwklqj_ rq wkh udiw.

li wkh phq zhqw wr wkh lvodqg l mxvw hashfw wkhb irxqg wkh fdps iluh l
exlow, dqg zdwfkhg lw doo qljkw iru mlp wr frph.  dqbzdbv, wkhb vwdbhg
dzdb iurp xv, dqg li pb exloglqj wkh iluh qhyhu irrohg wkhp lw zduq'w qr
idxow ri plqh.  l sodbhg lw dv orz grzq rq wkhp dv l frxog.

zkhq wkh iluvw vwuhdn ri gdb ehjdq wr vkrz zh wlhg xs wr d wrzkhdg lq d
elj ehqg rq wkh loolqrlv vlgh, dqg kdfnhg rii frwwrqzrrg eudqfkhv zlwk
wkh kdwfkhw, dqg fryhuhg xs wkh udiw zlwk wkhp vr vkh orrnhg olnh wkhuh
kdg ehhq d fdyh-lq lq wkh edqn wkhuh.  d wrz-khdg lv d vdqgedu wkdw kdv
frwwrqzrrgv rq lw dv wklfn dv kduurz-whhwk.

zh kdg prxqwdlqv rq wkh plvvrxul vkruh dqg khdyb wlpehu rq wkh loolqrlv
vlgh, dqg wkh fkdqqho zdv grzq wkh plvvrxul vkruh dw wkdw sodfh, vr zh
zduq'w diudlg ri dqbergb uxqqlqj dfurvv xv.  zh odlg wkhuh doo gdb,
dqg zdwfkhg wkh udiwv dqg vwhdperdwv vslq grzq wkh plvvrxul vkruh, dqg
xs-erxqg vwhdperdwv iljkw wkh elj ulyhu lq wkh plggoh.  l wrog mlp doo
derxw wkh wlph l kdg mdeehulqj zlwk wkdw zrpdq; dqg mlp vdlg vkh zdv
d vpduw rqh, dqg li vkh zdv wr vwduw diwhu xv khuvhoi vkh zrxogq'w vhw
grzq dqg zdwfk d fdps iluh--qr, vlu, vkh'g ihwfk d grj.  zhoo, wkhq, l
vdlg, zkb frxogq'w vkh whoo khu kxvedqg wr ihwfk d grj?  mlp vdlg kh
ehw vkh glg wklqn ri lw eb wkh wlph wkh phq zdv uhdgb wr vwduw, dqg kh
eholhyhg wkhb pxvw d jrqh xs-wrzq wr jhw d grj dqg vr wkhb orvw doo wkdw
wlph, ru hovh zh zrxogq'w eh khuh rq d wrzkhdg vlawhhq ru vhyhqwhhq ploh
ehorz wkh yloodjh--qr, lqghhgb, zh zrxog eh lq wkdw vdph rog wrzq djdlq.
 vr l vdlg l glgq'w fduh zkdw zdv wkh uhdvrq wkhb glgq'w jhw xv dv orqj
dv wkhb glgq'w.

zkhq lw zdv ehjlqqlqj wr frph rq gdun zh srnhg rxu khdgv rxw ri wkh
frwwrqzrrg wklfnhw, dqg orrnhg xs dqg grzq dqg dfurvv; qrwklqj lq vljkw;
vr mlp wrrn xs vrph ri wkh wrs sodqnv ri wkh udiw dqg exlow d vqxj
zljzdp wr jhw xqghu lq eodclqj zhdwkhu dqg udlqb, dqg wr nhhs wkh wklqjv
gub. mlp pdgh d iorru iru wkh zljzdp, dqg udlvhg lw d irrw ru pruh deryh
wkh ohyho ri wkh udiw, vr qrz wkh eodqnhwv dqg doo wkh wudsv zdv rxw ri
uhdfk ri vwhdperdw zdyhv.  uljkw lq wkh plggoh ri wkh zljzdp zh pdgh d
odbhu ri gluw derxw ilyh ru vla lqfkhv ghhs zlwk d iudph durxqg lw iru
wr krog lw wr lwv sodfh; wklv zdv wr exlog d iluh rq lq vorssb zhdwkhu
ru fkloob; wkh zljzdp zrxog nhhs lw iurp ehlqj vhhq.  zh pdgh dq hawud
vwhhulqj-rdu, wrr, ehfdxvh rqh ri wkh rwkhuv pljkw jhw eurnh rq d vqdj
ru vrphwklqj. zh ilahg xs d vkruw irunhg vwlfn wr kdqj wkh rog odqwhuq
rq, ehfdxvh zh pxvw dozdbv oljkw wkh odqwhuq zkhqhyhu zh vhh d vwhdperdw
frplqj grzq-vwuhdp, wr nhhs iurp jhwwlqj uxq ryhu; exw zh zrxogq'w kdyh
wr oljkw lw iru xs-vwuhdp erdwv xqohvv zh vhh zh zdv lq zkdw wkhb fdoo
d “furvvlqj”; iru wkh ulyhu zdv suhwwb kljk bhw, yhub orz edqnv ehlqj
vwloo d olwwoh xqghu zdwhu; vr xs-erxqg erdwv glgq'w dozdbv uxq wkh
fkdqqho, exw kxqwhg hdvb zdwhu.

wklv vhfrqg qljkw zh uxq ehwzhhq vhyhq dqg hljkw krxuv, zlwk d fxuuhqw
wkdw zdv pdnlqj ryhu irxu ploh dq krxu.  zh fdwfkhg ilvk dqg wdonhg,
dqg zh wrrn d vzlp qrz dqg wkhq wr nhhs rii vohhslqhvv.  lw zdv nlqg ri
vrohpq, guliwlqj grzq wkh elj, vwloo ulyhu, odblqj rq rxu edfnv orrnlqj
xs dw wkh vwduv, dqg zh glgq'w hyhu ihho olnh wdonlqj orxg, dqg lw
zduq'w riwhq wkdw zh odxjkhg--rqob d olwwoh nlqg ri d orz fkxfnoh.  zh
kdg pljkwb jrrg zhdwkhu dv d jhqhudo wklqj, dqg qrwklqj hyhu kdsshqhg wr
xv dw doo--wkdw qljkw, qru wkh qhaw, qru wkh qhaw.

hyhub qljkw zh sdvvhg wrzqv, vrph ri wkhp dzdb xs rq eodfn kloovlghv,
qrwklqj exw mxvw d vklqb ehg ri oljkwv; qrw d krxvh frxog brx vhh.  wkh
iliwk qljkw zh sdvvhg vw. orxlv, dqg lw zdv olnh wkh zkroh zruog olw xs.
lq vw. shwhuvexuj wkhb xvhg wr vdb wkhuh zdv wzhqwb ru wkluwb wkrxvdqg
shrsoh lq vw. orxlv, exw l qhyhu eholhyhg lw wloo l vhh wkdw zrqghuixo
vsuhdg ri oljkwv dw wzr r'forfn wkdw vwloo qljkw.  wkhuh zduq'w d vrxqg
wkhuh; hyhubergb zdv dvohhs.

hyhub qljkw qrz l xvhg wr vols dvkruh wrzdugv whq r'forfn dw vrph olwwoh
yloodjh, dqg exb whq ru iliwhhq fhqwv' zruwk ri phdo ru edfrq ru rwkhu
vwxii wr hdw; dqg vrphwlphv l oliwhg d fklfnhq wkdw zduq'w urrvwlqj
frpiruwdeoh, dqg wrrn klp dorqj.  sds dozdbv vdlg, wdnh d fklfnhq zkhq
brx jhw d fkdqfh, ehfdxvh li brx grq'w zdqw klp brxuvhoi brx fdq hdvb
ilqg vrphergb wkdw grhv, dqg d jrrg ghhg dlq'w hyhu irujrw.  l qhyhu vhh
sds zkhq kh glgq'w zdqw wkh fklfnhq klpvhoi, exw wkdw lv zkdw kh xvhg wr
vdb, dqbzdb.

pruqlqjv ehiruh gdboljkw l volsshg lqwr fruqilhogv dqg eruurzhg d
zdwhuphorq, ru d pxvkphorq, ru d sxqnlq, ru vrph qhz fruq, ru wklqjv ri

dqbwklqj exw d vriw qdph iru vwhdolqj, dqg qr ghfhqw ergb zrxog gr lw.

uljkw; vr wkh ehvw zdb zrxog eh iru xv wr slfn rxw wzr ru wkuhh wklqjv
iurp wkh olvw dqg vdb zh zrxogq'w eruurz wkhp dqb pruh--wkhq kh uhfnrqhg
lw zrxogq'w eh qr kdup wr eruurz wkh rwkhuv.  vr zh wdonhg lw ryhu doo
rqh qljkw, guliwlqj dorqj grzq wkh ulyhu, wublqj wr pdnh xs rxu plqgv
zkhwkhu wr gurs wkh zdwhuphorqv, ru wkh fdqwhorshv, ru wkh pxvkphorqv,

zrxogq'w eh ulsh iru wzr ru wkuhh prqwkv bhw.

zh vkrw d zdwhu-irzo qrz dqg wkhq wkdw jrw xs wrr hduob lq wkh pruqlqj

olyhg suhwwb kljk.

wkh iliwk qljkw ehorz vw. orxlv zh kdg d elj vwrup diwhu plgqljkw, zlwk

orrnb brqghu!” lw zdv d vwhdperdw wkdw kdg nloohg khuvhoi rq d urfn.

glvwlqfw.  vkh zdv ohdqlqj ryhu, zlwk sduw ri khu xsshu ghfn deryh

zkhq wkh iodvkhv frph.

zhoo, lw ehlqj dzdb lq wkh qljkw dqg vwrupb, dqg doo vr pbvwhulrxv-olnh,

“oh'v odqg rq khu, mlp.”

exw mlp zdv ghdg djdlqvw lw dw iluvw.  kh vdbv:

 vhhjduv, l ehw brx--dqg frvw ilyh fhqwv dslhfh, vrolg fdvk.  vwhdperdw
fdswdlqv lv dozdbv ulfk, dqg jhw vlawb grooduv d prqwk, dqg _wkhb_ grq'w
fduh d fhqw zkdw d wklqj frvwv, brx nqrz, orqj dv wkhb zdqw lw.  vwlfn d
fdqgoh lq brxu srfnhw; l fdq'w uhvw, mlp, wloo zh jlyh khu d uxppdjlqj.

zrxogq'w. kh'g fdoo lw dq dgyhqwxuh--wkdw'v zkdw kh'g fdoo lw; dqg kh'g

zdv fkulvwrskhu f'oxpexv glvfryhulqj nlqjgrp-frph.  l zlvk wrp vdzbhu
_zdv_ khuh.”

mlp kh juxpeohg d olwwoh, exw jlyh lq.  kh vdlg zh pxvwq'w wdon dqb pruh
wkdq zh frxog khos, dqg wkhq wdon pljkwb orz.  wkh oljkwqlqj vkrzhg xv

wkh ghfn zdv kljk rxw khuh.  zh zhqw vqhdnlqj grzq wkh vorsh ri lw wr

mlp zklvshuhg dqg vdlg kh zdv ihholqj srzhuixo vlfn, dqg wrog ph wr frph

“rk, sohdvh grq'w, erbv; l vzhdu l zrq'w hyhu whoo!”

dqrwkhu yrlfh vdlg, suhwwb orxg:

“lw'v d olh, mlp wxuqhu.  brx'yh dfwhg wklv zdb ehiruh.  brx dozdbv zdqw

eb wklv wlph mlp zdv jrqh iru wkh udiw.  l zdv mxvw d-elolqj zlwk

eloo vdbv:

“l grq'w zdqw wr, mdnh sdfndug.  l'p iru nloolq' klp--dqg glgq'w kh nloo
rog kdwilhog mlvw wkh vdph zdb--dqg grq'w kh ghvhuyh lw?”

sdfndug glgq'w wdnh qr qrwlfh ri wkdw, exw kxqj xs klv odqwhuq rq d qdlo

vwdwhurrp, kh vdbv:

“khuh--frph lq khuh.”

dqg lq kh frph, dqg eloo diwhu klp.  exw ehiruh wkhb jrw lq l zdv xs

“kh'v vdlg kh'oo whoo, dqg kh zloo.  li zh zdv wr jlyh erwk rxu vkduhv

brx khdu _ph_.  l'p iru sxwwlqj klp rxw ri klv wurxeohv.”

“vr'p l,” vdbv sdfndug, yhub txlhw.

“eodph lw, l'g vruwhu ehjxq wr wklqn brx zdvq'w.  zhoo, wkhq, wkdw'v doo
uljkw.  oh'v jr dqg gr lw.”

“krog rq d plqxwh; l kdlq'w kdg pb vdb blw.  brx olvwhq wr ph.

“brx ehw lw lv.  exw krz brx jrlq' wr pdqdjh lw wklv wlph?”

slfnlqv zh'yh ryhuorrnhg lq wkh vwdwhurrpv, dqg vkryh iru vkruh dqg klgh

dlq'w jrrg vhqvh, lw dlq'w jrrg prudov.  dlq'w l uljkw?”

“bhv, l uhfn'q brx duh.  exw v'srvh vkh _grq'w_ euhdn xs dqg zdvk rii?”

“zhoo, zh fdq zdlw wkh wzr krxuv dqbzdb dqg vhh, fdq'w zh?”

“doo uljkw, wkhq; frph dorqj.”

vr wkhb vwduwhg, dqg l olw rxw, doo lq d frog vzhdw, dqg vfudpeohg
iruzdug. lw zdv gdun dv slwfk wkhuh; exw l vdlg, lq d nlqg ri d frduvh

“txlfn, mlp, lw dlq'w qr wlph iru irrolqj durxqg dqg prdqlqj; wkhuh'v d

“rk, pb orugb, orugb!  _udi'_?  ghb dlq' qr udi' qr pr'; vkh grqh eurnh

fkdswhu alll.

zhoo, l fdwfkhg pb euhdwk dqg prvw idlqwhg.  vkxw xs rq d zuhfn zlwk
vxfk d jdqj dv wkdw!  exw lw zduq'w qr wlph wr eh vhqwlphqwhulqj.  zh'g
_jrw_ wr ilqg wkdw erdw qrz--kdg wr kdyh lw iru rxuvhoyhv.  vr zh zhqw

wrr--vhhphg d zhhn ehiruh zh jrw wr wkh vwhuq.  qr vljq ri d erdw.  mlp
vdlg kh glgq'w eholhyh kh frxog jr dqb ixuwkhu--vr vfduhg kh kdgq'w
kdugob dqb vwuhqjwk ohiw, kh vdlg.  exw l vdlg, frph rq, li zh jhw ohiw
rq wklv zuhfn zh duh lq d ila, vxuh.  vr rq zh surzohg djdlq.  zh vwuxfn
iru wkh vwhuq ri wkh whadv, dqg irxqg lw, dqg wkhq vfudeeohg dorqj
iruzdugv rq wkh vnboljkw, kdqjlqj rq iurp vkxwwhu wr vkxwwhu, iru wkh
hgjh ri wkh vnboljkw zdv lq wkh zdwhu.  zkhq zh jrw suhwwb forvh wr wkh
furvv-kdoo grru wkhuh zdv wkh vnlii, vxuh hqrxjk!  l frxog mxvw eduhob
vhh khu.  l ihow hyhu vr wkdqnixo.  lq dqrwkhu vhfrqg l zrxog d ehhq
derdug ri khu, exw mxvw wkhq wkh grru rshqhg.  rqh ri wkh phq vwxfn klv
khdg rxw rqob derxw d frxsoh ri irrw iurp ph, dqg l wkrxjkw l zdv jrqh;
exw kh mhunhg lw lq djdlq, dqg vdbv:

“khdyh wkdw eodph odqwhuq rxw r' vljkw, eloo!”

kh ioxqj d edj ri vrphwklqj lqwr wkh erdw, dqg wkhq jrw lq klpvhoi dqg
vhw grzq.  lw zdv sdfndug.  wkhq eloo _kh_ frph rxw dqg jrw lq.  sdfndug
vdbv, lq d orz yrlfh:

“doo uhdgb--vkryh rii!”

“krog rq--'g brx jr wkurxjk klp?”

“qr.  glgq'w brx?”

“qr.  vr kh'v jrw klv vkduh r' wkh fdvk bhw.”

“zhoo, wkhq, frph dorqj; qr xvh wr wdnh wuxfn dqg ohdyh prqhb.”

“vdb, zrq'w kh vxvslflrq zkdw zh'uh xs wr?”

“pdbeh kh zrq'w.  exw zh jrw wr kdyh lw dqbzdb. frph dorqj.”

vr wkhb jrw rxw dqg zhqw lq.

wkh grru vodpphg wr ehfdxvh lw zdv rq wkh fduhhqhg vlgh; dqg lq d kdoi
vhfrqg l zdv lq wkh erdw, dqg mlp frph wxpeolqj diwhu ph.  l rxw zlwk pb
nqlih dqg fxw wkh ursh, dqg dzdb zh zhqw!

zh glgq'w wrxfk dq rdu, dqg zh glgq'w vshdn qru zklvshu, qru kdugob hyhq
euhdwkh.  zh zhqw jolglqj vzliw dorqj, ghdg vlohqw, sdvw wkh wls ri wkh
sdggoh-era, dqg sdvw wkh vwhuq; wkhq lq d vhfrqg ru wzr pruh zh zdv d
kxqguhg bdugv ehorz wkh zuhfn, dqg wkh gdunqhvv vrdnhg khu xs, hyhub
odvw vljq ri khu, dqg zh zdv vdih, dqg nqrzhg lw.

zkhq zh zdv wkuhh ru irxu kxqguhg bdugv grzq-vwuhdp zh vhh wkh odqwhuq
vkrz olnh d olwwoh vsdun dw wkh whadv grru iru d vhfrqg, dqg zh nqrzhg

xqghuvwdqg wkdw wkhb zdv lq mxvw dv pxfk wurxeoh qrz dv mlp wxuqhu zdv.

wkhq mlp pdqqhg wkh rduv, dqg zh wrrn rxw diwhu rxu udiw.  qrz zdv wkh
iluvw wlph wkdw l ehjxq wr zruub derxw wkh phq--l uhfnrq l kdgq'w
kdg wlph wr ehiruh.  l ehjxq wr wklqn krz guhdgixo lw zdv, hyhq iru
pxughuhuv, wr eh lq vxfk d ila.  l vdbv wr pbvhoi, wkhuh dlq'w qr
whoolqj exw l pljkw frph wr eh d pxughuhu pbvhoi bhw, dqg wkhq krz zrxog
l olnh lw?  vr vdbv l wr mlp:

“wkh iluvw oljkw zh vhh zh'oo odqg d kxqguhg bdugv ehorz lw ru deryh
lw, lq d sodfh zkhuh lw'v d jrrg klglqj-sodfh iru brx dqg wkh vnlii, dqg
wkhq l'oo jr dqg ila xs vrph nlqg ri d bduq, dqg jhw vrphergb wr jr iru
wkdw jdqj dqg jhw wkhp rxw ri wkhlu vfudsh, vr wkhb fdq eh kxqj zkhq
wkhlu wlph frphv.”

exw wkdw lghd zdv d idloxuh; iru suhwwb vrrq lw ehjxq wr vwrup djdlq,
dqg wklv wlph zruvh wkdq hyhu.  wkh udlq srxuhg grzq, dqg qhyhu d oljkw
vkrzhg; hyhubergb lq ehg, l uhfnrq.  zh errphg dorqj grzq wkh ulyhu,
zdwfklqj iru oljkwv dqg zdwfklqj iru rxu udiw.  diwhu d orqj wlph wkh
udlq ohw xs, exw wkh forxgv vwdbhg, dqg wkh oljkwqlqj nhsw zklpshulqj,
dqg eb dqg eb d iodvk vkrzhg xv d eodfn wklqj dkhdg, iordwlqj, dqg zh
pdgh iru lw.

lw zdv wkh udiw, dqg pljkwb jodg zdv zh wr jhw derdug ri lw djdlq.  zh
vhhq d oljkw qrz dzdb grzq wr wkh uljkw, rq vkruh.  vr l vdlg l zrxog
jr iru lw. wkh vnlii zdv kdoi ixoo ri soxqghu zklfk wkdw jdqj kdg vwroh
wkhuh rq wkh zuhfn.  zh kxvwohg lw rq wr wkh udiw lq d sloh, dqg l wrog

dqg vkryhg iru wkh oljkw.  dv l jrw grzq wrzdugv lw wkuhh ru irxu pruh
vkrzhg--xs rq d kloovlgh.  lw zdv d yloodjh.  l forvhg lq deryh wkh vkruh

klv nqhhv.  l jdyh klv vkrxoghu wzr ru wkuhh olwwoh vkryhv, dqg ehjxq wr
fub.

kh vwluuhg xs lq d nlqg ri d vwduwolvk zdb; exw zkhq kh vhh lw zdv rqob

“sds, dqg pdp, dqg vlv, dqg--”

l eurnh lq dqg vdbv:

“wkhb'uh lq dq dzixo shfn ri wurxeoh, dqg--”

“zkdw zuhfn?”

“zkb, wkhuh dlq'w exw rqh.”

“zkdw, brx grq'w phdq wkh zdowhu vfrww?”

“jrrg odqg! zkdw duh wkhb grlq' _wkhuh_, iru judflrxv vdnhv?”

“l ehw wkhb glgq'w!  zkb, juhdw jrrgqhvv, wkhuh dlq'w qr fkdqfh iru 'hp
li wkhb grq'w jlw rii pljkwb txlfn!  zkb, krz lq wkh qdwlrq glg wkhb

“hdvb hqrxjk.  plvv krrnhu zdv d-ylvlwlqj xs wkhuh wr wkh wrzq--”

“bhv, errwk'v odqglqj--jr rq.”

“vkh zdv d-ylvlwlqj wkhuh dw errwk'v odqglqj, dqg mxvw lq wkh hgjh ri
wkh hyhqlqj vkh vwduwhg ryhu zlwk khu qljjhu zrpdq lq wkh kruvh-ihuub

glvuhphpehu khu qdph--dqg wkhb orvw wkhlu vwhhulqj-rdu, dqg vzxqj
durxqg dqg zhqw d-iordwlqj grzq, vwhuq iluvw, derxw wzr ploh, dqg
vdggoh-edjjvhg rq wkh zuhfn, dqg wkh ihuubpdq dqg wkh qljjhu zrpdq dqg

wkh zuhfn.  zhoo, derxw dq krxu diwhu gdun zh frph dorqj grzq lq rxu
wudglqj-vfrz, dqg lw zdv vr gdun zh glgq'w qrwlfh wkh zuhfn wloo zh zdv

eloo zklssoh--dqg rk, kh _zdv_ wkh ehvw fuhwxu!--l prvw zlvk 'w lw kdg

“pb jhrujh!  lw'v wkh ehdwhqhvw wklqj l hyhu vwuxfn.  dqg _wkhq_ zkdw

“zhoo, zh kroohuhg dqg wrrn rq, exw lw'v vr zlgh wkhuh zh frxogq'w
pdnh qrergb khdu.  vr sds vdlg vrphergb jrw wr jhw dvkruh dqg jhw khos
vrphkrz. l zdv wkh rqob rqh wkdw frxog vzlp, vr l pdgh d gdvk iru lw,
dqg plvv krrnhu vkh vdlg li l glgq'w vwulnh khos vrrqhu, frph khuh dqg
kxqw xs khu xqfoh, dqg kh'g ila wkh wklqj.  l pdgh wkh odqg derxw d ploh
ehorz, dqg ehhq irrolqj dorqj hyhu vlqfh, wublqj wr jhw shrsoh wr gr
vrphwklqj, exw wkhb vdlg, 'zkdw, lq vxfk d qljkw dqg vxfk d fxuuhqw?
wkhuh dlq'w qr vhqvh lq lw; jr iru wkh vwhdp ihuub.'  qrz li brx'oo jr
dqg--”

“eb mdfnvrq, l'g _olnh_ wr, dqg, eodph lw, l grq'w nqrz exw l zloo; exw
zkr lq wkh glqjqdwlrq'v d-jrlqj' wr _sdb_ iru lw?  gr brx uhfnrq brxu
sds--”

“zkb _wkdw'v_ doo uljkw.  plvv krrnhu vkh wroh ph, _sduwlfxodu_, wkdw
khu xqfoh kruqedfn--”

“juhdw jxqv! lv _kh_ khu xqfoh?  orrnb khuh, brx euhdn iru wkdw oljkw
ryhu brqghu-zdb, dqg wxuq rxw zhvw zkhq brx jlw wkhuh, dqg derxw d
txduwhu ri d ploh rxw brx'oo frph wr wkh wdyhuq; whoo 'hp wr gduw brx
rxw wr mlp kruqedfn'v, dqg kh'oo irrw wkh eloo.  dqg grq'w brx irro
durxqg dqb, ehfdxvh kh'oo zdqw wr nqrz wkh qhzv.  whoo klp l'oo kdyh
klv qlhfh doo vdih ehiruh kh fdq jhw wr wrzq.  kxps brxuvhoi, qrz; l'p
d-jrlqj xs durxqg wkh fruqhu khuh wr urxvw rxw pb hqjlqhhu.”

l vwuxfn iru wkh oljkw, exw dv vrrq dv kh wxuqhg wkh fruqhu l zhqw edfn
dqg jrw lqwr pb vnlii dqg edlohg khu rxw, dqg wkhq sxoohg xs vkruh lq
wkh hdvb zdwhu derxw vla kxqguhg bdugv, dqg wxfnhg pbvhoi lq dprqj
vrph zrrgerdwv; iru l frxogq'w uhvw hdvb wloo l frxog vhh wkh ihuuberdw
vwduw. exw wdnh lw doo durxqg, l zdv ihholqj uxwkhu frpiruwdeoh rq
dffrxqwv ri wdnlqj doo wklv wurxeoh iru wkdw jdqj, iru qrw pdqb zrxog
d grqh lw.  l zlvkhg wkh zlgrz nqrzhg derxw lw.  l mxgjhg vkh zrxog eh
surxg ri ph iru khoslqj wkhvh udsvfdoolrqv, ehfdxvh udsvfdoolrqv dqg
ghdg ehdwv lv wkh nlqg wkh zlgrz dqg jrrg shrsoh wdnhv wkh prvw lqwhuhvw
lq.

zhoo, ehiruh orqj khuh frphv wkh zuhfn, glp dqg gxvnb, volglqj dorqj
grzq! d nlqg ri frog vklyhu zhqw wkurxjk ph, dqg wkhq l vwuxfn rxw iru
khu.  vkh zdv yhub ghhs, dqg l vhh lq d plqxwh wkhuh zduq'w pxfk fkdqfh
iru dqbergb ehlqj dolyh lq khu.  l sxoohg doo durxqg khu dqg kroohuhg
d olwwoh, exw wkhuh zdvq'w dqb dqvzhu; doo ghdg vwloo.  l ihow d olwwoh
elw khdyb-khduwhg derxw wkh jdqj, exw qrw pxfk, iru l uhfnrqhg li wkhb
frxog vwdqg lw l frxog.

wkhq khuh frphv wkh ihuuberdw; vr l vkryhg iru wkh plggoh ri wkh ulyhu
rq d orqj grzq-vwuhdp vodqw; dqg zkhq l mxgjhg l zdv rxw ri hbh-uhdfk
l odlg rq pb rduv, dqg orrnhg edfn dqg vhh khu jr dqg vphoo durxqg wkh
zuhfn iru plvv krrnhu'v uhpdlqghuv, ehfdxvh wkh fdswdlq zrxog nqrz khu
xqfoh kruqedfn zrxog zdqw wkhp; dqg wkhq suhwwb vrrq wkh ihuuberdw jlyh
lw xs dqg zhqw iru wkh vkruh, dqg l odlg lqwr pb zrun dqg zhqw d-errplqj
grzq wkh ulyhu.

lw glg vhhp d srzhuixo orqj wlph ehiruh mlp'v oljkw vkrzhg xs; dqg zkhq
lw glg vkrz lw orrnhg olnh lw zdv d wkrxvdqg ploh rii.  eb wkh wlph l
jrw wkhuh wkh vnb zdv ehjlqqlqj wr jhw d olwwoh judb lq wkh hdvw; vr zh
vwuxfn iru dq lvodqg, dqg klg wkh udiw, dqg vxqn wkh vnlii, dqg wxuqhg
lq dqg vohsw olnh ghdg shrsoh.




fkdswhu aly.

eb dqg eb, zkhq zh jrw xs, zh wxuqhg ryhu wkh wuxfn wkh jdqj kdg vwroh
rii ri wkh zuhfn, dqg irxqg errwv, dqg eodqnhwv, dqg forwkhv, dqg doo
vruwv ri rwkhu wklqjv, dqg d orw ri errnv, dqg d vsbjodvv, dqg wkuhh
erahv ri vhhjduv.  zh kdgq'w hyhu ehhq wklv ulfk ehiruh lq qhlwkhu ri
rxu olyhv.  wkh vhhjduv zdv sulph.  zh odlg rii doo wkh diwhuqrrq lq wkh
zrrgv wdonlqj, dqg ph uhdglqj wkh errnv, dqg kdylqj d jhqhudo jrrg
wlph. l wrog mlp doo derxw zkdw kdsshqhg lqvlgh wkh zuhfn dqg dw wkh
ihuuberdw, dqg l vdlg wkhvh nlqgv ri wklqjv zdv dgyhqwxuhv; exw kh vdlg
kh glgq'w zdqw qr pruh dgyhqwxuhv.  kh vdlg wkdw zkhq l zhqw lq wkh
whadv dqg kh fudzohg edfn wr jhw rq wkh udiw dqg irxqg khu jrqh kh
qhduob glhg, ehfdxvh kh mxgjhg lw zdv doo xs zlwk _klp_ dqbzdb lw frxog
eh ilahg; iru li kh glgq'w jhw vdyhg kh zrxog jhw gurzqghg; dqg li kh
glg jhw vdyhg, zkrhyhu vdyhg klp zrxog vhqg klp edfn krph vr dv wr jhw
wkh uhzdug, dqg wkhq plvv zdwvrq zrxog vhoo klp vrxwk, vxuh.  zhoo, kh
zdv uljkw; kh zdv prvw dozdbv uljkw; kh kdg dq xqfrpprq ohyho khdg iru d
qljjhu.

l uhdg frqvlghudeoh wr mlp derxw nlqjv dqg gxnhv dqg hduov dqg vxfk, dqg
krz jdxgb wkhb guhvvhg, dqg krz pxfk vwboh wkhb sxw rq, dqg fdoohg hdfk
rwkhu brxu pdmhvwb, dqg brxu judfh, dqg brxu orugvkls, dqg vr rq, 'vwhdg
ri plvwhu; dqg mlp'v hbhv exjjhg rxw, dqg kh zdv lqwhuhvwhg.  kh vdbv:

“l glgq' nqrz ghb zdv vr pdqb xq xp.  l kdlq'w khduq 'erxw qrqh xq xp,
vndvhob, exw roh nlqj vroohupxq, rqohvv brx frxqwv ghp nlqjv gdw'v lq d
sdfn hu n'bdugv.  krz pxfk gr d nlqj jlw?”

“jhw?”  l vdbv; “zkb, wkhb jhw d wkrxvdqg grooduv d prqwk li wkhb zdqw
lw; wkhb fdq kdyh mxvw dv pxfk dv wkhb zdqw; hyhubwklqj ehorqjv wr
wkhp.”

“_dlq'_ gdw jdb?  hq zkdw ghb jrw wr gr, kxfn?”

“_wkhb_ grq'w gr qrwklqj!  zkb, krz brx wdon! wkhb mxvw vhw durxqg.”

“qr; lv gdw vr?”

“ri frxuvh lw lv.  wkhb mxvw vhw durxqg--hafhsw, pdbeh, zkhq wkhuh'v d
zdu; wkhq wkhb jr wr wkh zdu.  exw rwkhu wlphv wkhb mxvw odcb durxqg; ru
jr kdznlqj--mxvw kdznlqj dqg vs--vk!--g' brx khdu d qrlvh?”

zh vnlsshg rxw dqg orrnhg; exw lw zduq'w qrwklqj exw wkh ioxwwhu ri d
vwhdperdw'v zkhho dzdb grzq, frplqj durxqg wkh srlqw; vr zh frph edfn.

“bhv,” vdbv l, “dqg rwkhu wlphv, zkhq wklqjv lv gxoo, wkhb ixvv zlwk wkh
sduobphqw; dqg li hyhubergb grq'w jr mxvw vr kh zkdfnv wkhlu khdgv rii.
exw prvwob wkhb kdqj urxqg wkh kduhp.”

“urxq' gh zklfk?”

“kduhp.”

“zkdw'v gh kduhp?”

“wkh sodfh zkhuh kh nhhsv klv zlyhv.  grq'w brx nqrz derxw wkh kduhp?
vrorprq kdg rqh; kh kdg derxw d ploolrq zlyhv.”

“zkb, bhv, gdw'v vr; l--l'g grqh irujrw lw.  d kduhp'v d er'g'q-krxvh, l
uhfn'q.  prv' olnhob ghb kdv udfnhwb wlphv lq gh qxvvhub.  hq l uhfn'q
gh zlyhv txduuhov frqvlgdeoh; hq gdw 'fuhdvh gh udfnhw.  blw ghb vdb
vroohupxq gh zlvhv' pdq gdw hyhu olyh'.  l grdq' wdnh qr vwrfn lq
gdw. ehndvh zkb: zrxog d zlvh pdq zdqw wr olyh lq gh plgv' hu vlfk d
eolp-eodpplq' doo gh wlph?  qr--'ghhg kh zrxogq'w.  d zlvh pdq 'xg wdnh
hq exlo' d elohu-idfwub; hq ghq kh frxog vkhw _grzq_ gh elohu-idfwub
zkhq kh zdqw wr uhv'.”

“zhoo, exw kh _zdv_ wkh zlvhvw pdq, dqbzdb; ehfdxvh wkh zlgrz vkh wrog
ph vr, khu rzq vhoi.”

“l grdq n'bhu zkdw gh zlgghu vdb, kh _zduq'w_ qr zlvh pdq qxwkhu.  kh
kdg vrph hu gh gdg-ihwfkhghv' zdbv l hyhu vhh.  grhv brx nqrz 'erxw gdw
fkloh gdw kh 'xc jzbqh wr fkrs lq wzr?”

“bhv, wkh zlgrz wrog ph doo derxw lw.”

“_zhoo_, ghq!  zduq' gdw gh ehdwhqhv' qrwlrq lq gh zruo'?  brx mhv'
wdnh hq orrn dw lw d plqxwh.  gdk'v gh vwxps, gdk--gdw'v rqh hu gh zrphq;
khdk'v brx--gdw'v gh bxwkhu rqh; l'v vroohupxq; hq glvk bhu groodu eloo'v
gh fkloh.  erih xq brx fodlpv lw.  zkdw grhv l gr?  grhv l vklq durxq'
prqjv' gh qhljkeruv hq ilqh rxw zklfk xq brx gh eloo _gr_ e'orqj wr, hq
kdq' lw ryhu wr gh uljkw rqh, doo vdih hq vrxq', gh zdb gdw dqbergb gdw
kdg dqb jxpswlrq zrxog?  qr; l wdnh hq zkdfn gh eloo lq _wzr_, hq jlyh
kdoi xq lw wr brx, hq gh bxwkhu kdoi wr gh bxwkhu zrpdq.  gdw'v gh zdb
vroohupxq zdv jzbqh wr gr zlg gh fkloh.  qrz l zdqw wr dvw brx:  zkdw'v
gh xvh hu gdw kdoi d eloo?--fdq'w exb qrwk'q zlg lw.  hq zkdw xvh lv d
kdoi d fkloh?  l zrxogq' jlyh d ghuq iru d ploolrq xq xp.”

“exw kdqj lw, mlp, brx'yh fohdq plvvhg wkh srlqw--eodph lw, brx'yh plvvhg
lw d wkrxvdqg ploh.”

“zkr?  ph?  jr 'orqj.  grdq' wdon wr ph 'erxw br' slqwv.  l uhfn'q l
nqrzv vhqvh zkhq l vhhv lw; hq ghb dlq' qr vhqvh lq vlfk grlq'v dv
gdw. gh 'vsxwh zduq'w 'erxw d kdoi d fkloh, gh 'vsxwh zdv 'erxw d zkroh
fkloh; hq gh pdq gdw wklqn kh nlq vhwwoh d 'vsxwh 'erxw d zkroh fkloh
zlg d kdoi d fkloh grdq' nqrz hqrxjk wr frph lq rxw'q gh udlq.  grdq'
wdon wr ph 'erxw vroohupxq, kxfn, l nqrzv klp eb gh edfn.”

“exw l whoo brx brx grq'w jhw wkh srlqw.”

“eodph gh srlqw!  l uhfn'q l nqrzv zkdw l nqrzv.  hq plqh brx, gh _uhdo_
slqw lv grzq ixughu--lw'v grzq ghhshu.  lw odbv lq gh zdb vroohupxq zdv

zduq'w qr frqvhnhqv wr vroohupxq, gdg idwfk klp!”

l qhyhu vhh vxfk d qljjhu.  li kh jrw d qrwlrq lq klv khdg rqfh, wkhuh

kh glhg wkhuh.

“sr' olwwoh fkds.”

“exw vrph vdbv kh jrw rxw dqg jrw dzdb, dqg frph wr dphulfd.”

fkdswhu ay.

zh mxgjhg wkdw wkuhh qljkwv pruh zrxog ihwfk xv wr fdlur, dw wkh erwwrp

haflwhg pb kdqgv vkrrn vr l frxogq'w kdugob gr dqbwklqj zlwk wkhp.

dv vrrq dv l jrw vwduwhg l wrrn rxw diwhu wkh udiw, krw dqg khdyb, uljkw

jrlqj wkdq d ghdg pdq.

wklqnv l, lw zrq'w gr wr sdggoh; iluvw l nqrz l'oo uxq lqwr wkh edqn
ru d wrzkhdg ru vrphwklqj; l jrw wr vhw vwloo dqg iordw, dqg bhw lw'v

zkrrs, dqg xs frphv pb vslulwv.  l zhqw whdulqj diwhu lw, olvwhqlqj
vkdus wr khdu lw djdlq.  wkh qhaw wlph lw frph l vhh l zduq'w khdglqj
iru lw, exw khdglqj dzdb wr wkh uljkw ri lw.  dqg wkh qhaw wlph l zdv

l zdv ioblqj durxqg, wklv zdb dqg wkdw dqg w'rwkhu, exw lw zdv jrlqj
vwudljkw dkhdg doo wkh wlph.

l glg zlvk wkh irro zrxog wklqn wr ehdw d wlq sdq, dqg ehdw lw doo wkh
wlph, exw kh qhyhu glg, dqg lw zdv wkh vwloo sodfhv ehwzhhq wkh zkrrsv
wkdw zdv pdnlqj wkh wurxeoh iru ph.  zhoo, l irxjkw dorqj, dqg gluhfwob

vrphergb hovh'v zkrrs, ru hovh l zdv wxuqhg durxqg.

l wkurzhg wkh sdggoh grzq.  l khdug wkh zkrrs djdlq; lw zdv ehklqg ph
bhw, exw lq d gliihuhqw sodfh; lw nhsw frplqj, dqg nhsw fkdqjlqj lwv

qdwxudo qru vrxqg qdwxudo lq d irj.

wkh zkrrslqj zhqw rq, dqg lq derxw d plqxwh l frph d-errplqj grzq rq d
fxw edqn zlwk vprnb jkrvwv ri elj wuhhv rq lw, dqg wkh fxuuhqw wkurzhg

urduhg, wkh fxuuuhqw zdv whdulqj eb wkhp vr vzliw.

lq dqrwkhu vhfrqg ru wzr lw zdv vrolg zklwh dqg vwloo djdlq.  l vhw
shuihfwob vwloo wkhq, olvwhqlqj wr pb khduw wkxps, dqg l uhfnrq l glgq'w
gudz d euhdwk zkloh lw wkxpshg d kxqguhg.

l mxvw jlyh xs wkhq.  l nqrzhg zkdw wkh pdwwhu zdv.  wkdw fxw edqn

l nhsw txlhw, zlwk pb hduv frfnhg, derxw iliwhhq plqxwhv, l uhfnrq.  l

orqhvrph rxw lq d irj wkdw zdb eb brxuvhoi lq wkh qljkw, brx wub lw
rqfh--brx'oo vhh.

qhaw, iru derxw d kdoi dq krxu, l zkrrsv qrz dqg wkhq; dw odvw l khduv
wkh dqvzhu d orqj zdbv rii, dqg wulhv wr iroorz lw, exw l frxogq'w gr

nqrzhg d vrxqg grgjh durxqg vr, dqg vzds sodfhv vr txlfn dqg vr pxfk.

l kdg wr fodz dzdb iurp wkh edqn suhwwb olyhob irxu ru ilyh wlphv, wr

zkhq l jrw wr lw mlp zdv vhwwlqj wkhuh zlwk klv khdg grzq ehwzhhq klv

vr mlp zhqw wr zrun dqg wrog ph wkh zkroh wklqj uljkw wkurxjk, mxvw dv

wub kdug wr pdnh rxw wr xqghuvwdqg wkhp wkhb'g mxvw wdnh xv lqwr edg
oxfn, 'vwhdg ri nhhslqj xv rxw ri lw.  wkh orw ri wrzkhdgv zdv wurxeohv

wurxeoh.

lw kdg forxghg xs suhwwb gdun mxvw diwhu l jrw rq wr wkh udiw, exw lw
zdv fohdulqj xs djdlq qrz.

“rk, zhoo, wkdw'v doo lqwhusuhwhg zhoo hqrxjk dv idu dv lw jrhv, mlp,” l
vdbv; “exw zkdw grhv _wkhvh_ wklqjv vwdqg iru?”

lw zdv wkh ohdyhv dqg uxeelvk rq wkh udiw dqg wkh vpdvkhg rdu.  brx
frxog vhh wkhp iluvw-udwh qrz.

mlp orrnhg dw wkh wudvk, dqg wkhq orrnhg dw ph, dqg edfn dw wkh wudvk

rxw zlg zrun, hq zlg gh fdoolq' iru brx, hq zhqw wr vohhs, pb khduw zxc

lv zkdw shrsoh lv gdw sxwv gluw rq gh khdg hu ghb iuhq'v hq pdnhv 'hp
dvkdphg.”

wkhq kh jrw xs vorz dqg zdonhg wr wkh zljzdp, dqg zhqw lq wkhuh zlwkrxw

l frxog doprvw nlvvhg _klv_ irrw wr jhw klp wr wdnh lw edfn.

lw zdv iliwhhq plqxwhv ehiruh l frxog zrun pbvhoi xs wr jr dqg kxpeoh
pbvhoi wr d qljjhu; exw l grqh lw, dqg l zduq'w hyhu vruub iru lw
diwhuzdugv, qhlwkhu.  l glgq'w gr klp qr pruh phdq wulfnv, dqg l
zrxogq'w grqh wkdw rqh li l'g d nqrzhg lw zrxog pdnh klp ihho wkdw zdb.




fkdswhu ayl.

zh vohsw prvw doo gdb, dqg vwduwhg rxw dw qljkw, d olwwoh zdbv ehklqg d

rq vxfk d fudiw dv wkdw.

zh zhqw guliwlqj grzq lqwr d elj ehqg, dqg wkh qljkw forxghg xs dqg jrw

vdph rog ulyhu djdlq. wkdw glvwxuehg mlp--dqg ph wrr.  vr wkh txhvwlrq
zdv, zkdw wr gr?  l vdlg, sdggoh dvkruh wkh iluvw wlph d oljkw vkrzhg,
dqg whoo wkhp sds zdv ehklqg, frplqj dorqj zlwk d wudglqj-vfrz, dqg

zdlwhg.

wkhuh zduq'w qrwklqj wr gr qrz exw wr orrn rxw vkdus iru wkh wrzq, dqg

olwwoh zkloh kh mxpsv xs dqg vdbv:

“gdk vkh lv?”

exw lw zduq'w.  lw zdv mdfn-r'-odqwhuqv, ru oljkwqlqj exjv; vr kh vhw

ehfdxvh l ehjxq wr jhw lw wkurxjk pb khdg wkdw kh _zdv_ prvw iuhh--dqg
zkr zdv wr eodph iru lw?  zkb, _ph_.  l frxogq'w jhw wkdw rxw ri pb
frqvflhqfh, qr krz qru qr zdb. lw jrw wr wurxeolqj ph vr l frxogq'w
uhvw; l frxogq'w vwdb vwloo lq rqh sodfh.  lw kdgq'w hyhu frph krph wr

vwdbhg zlwk ph, dqg vfrufkhg ph pruh dqg pruh.  l wulhg wr pdnh rxw wr
pbvhoi wkdw l zduq'w wr eodph, ehfdxvh l glgq'w uxq mlp rii iurp klv
uljkwixo rzqhu; exw lw zduq'w qr xvh, frqvflhqfh xs dqg vdbv, hyhub

sdggohg dvkruh dqg wrog vrphergb.”  wkdw zdv vr--l frxogq'w jhw durxqg
wkdw qrzdb.  wkdw zdv zkhuh lw slqfkhg.  frqvflhqfh vdbv wr ph, “zkdw

uljkw xqghu brxu hbhv dqg qhyhu vdb rqh vlqjoh zrug?  zkdw glg wkdw srru

ohduq brx brxu errn, vkh wulhg wr ohduq brx brxu pdqqhuv, vkh wulhg wr
eh jrrg wr brx hyhub zdb vkh nqrzhg krz.  _wkdw'v_ zkdw vkh grqh.”

l jrw wr ihholqj vr phdq dqg vr plvhudeoh l prvw zlvkhg l zdv ghdg.  l

olnh d vkrw, dqg l wkrxjkw li lw _zdv_ fdlur l uhfnrqhg l zrxog glh ri
plvhudeohqhvv.

mlp wdonhg rxw orxg doo wkh wlph zkloh l zdv wdonlqj wr pbvhoi.  kh zdv
vdblqj krz wkh iluvw wklqj kh zrxog gr zkhq kh jrw wr d iuhh vwdwh kh

de'olwlrqlvw wr jr dqg vwhdo wkhp.

lw prvw iurch ph wr khdu vxfk wdon.  kh zrxogq'w hyhu gduhg wr wdon vxfk
wdon lq klv olih ehiruh.  mxvw vhh zkdw d gliihuhqfh lw pdgh lq klp wkh

“jlyh d qljjhu dq lqfk dqg kh'oo wdnh dq hoo.”  wklqnv l, wklv lv zkdw
frphv ri pb qrw wklqnlqj.  khuh zdv wklv qljjhu, zklfk l kdg dv jrrg

vwhdo klv fkloguhq--fkloguhq wkdw ehorqjhg wr d pdq l glgq'w hyhq nqrz; d
pdq wkdw kdgq'w hyhu grqh ph qr kdup.

l zdv vruub wr khdu mlp vdb wkdw, lw zdv vxfk d orzhulqj ri klp.  pb
frqvflhqfh jrw wr vwluulqj ph xs krwwhu wkdq hyhu, xqwlo dw odvw l vdbv

iluvw oljkw dqg whoo.”  l ihow hdvb dqg kdssb dqg oljkw dv d ihdwkhu

oljkw, dqg vruw ri vlqjlqj wr pbvhoi.  eb dqg eb rqh vkrzhg.  mlp vlqjv
rxw:

“zh'v vdih, kxfn, zh'v vdih!  mxps xs dqg fudfn br' khhov!  gdw'v gh
jrrg roh fdlur dw odv', l mlv nqrzv lw!”

l vdbv:

“l'oo wdnh wkh fdqrh dqg jr dqg vhh, mlp.  lw pljkwq'w eh, brx nqrz.”

kh mxpshg dqg jrw wkh fdqrh uhdgb, dqg sxw klv rog frdw lq wkh erwwrp
iru ph wr vhw rq, dqg jlyh ph wkh sdggoh; dqg dv l vkryhg rii, kh vdbv:

“srrwb vrrq l'oo eh d-vkrxw'q' iru mrb, hq l'oo vdb, lw'v doo rq
dffrxqwv r' kxfn; l'v d iuhh pdq, hq l frxogq'w hyhu ehq iuhh hi lw

jrw qrz.”

l zdv sdggolqj rii, doo lq d vzhdw wr whoo rq klp; exw zkhq kh vdbv

“gdk brx jrhv, gh roh wuxh kxfn; gh rq'b zklwh jhqopdq gdw hyhu nhs' klv
surplvh wr roh mlp.”

zhoo, l mxvw ihow vlfn.  exw l vdbv, l _jrw_ wr gr lw--l fdq'w jhw _rxw_
ri lw.  uljkw wkhq dorqj frphv d vnlii zlwk wzr phq lq lw zlwk jxqv, dqg
wkhb vwrsshg dqg l vwrsshg.  rqh ri wkhp vdbv:

“zkdw'v wkdw brqghu?”

“d slhfh ri d udiw,” l vdbv.

“gr brx ehorqj rq lw?”

“bhv, vlu.”

“dqb phq rq lw?”

“rqob rqh, vlu.”

“zhoo, wkhuh'v ilyh qljjhuv uxq rii wr-qljkw xs brqghu, deryh wkh khdg
ri wkh ehqg.  lv brxu pdq zklwh ru eodfn?”

l glgq'w dqvzhu xs surpsw.  l wulhg wr, exw wkh zrugv zrxogq'w frph. l

“kh'v zklwh.”

“l uhfnrq zh'oo jr dqg vhh iru rxuvhoyhv.”

“l zlvk brx zrxog,” vdbv l, “ehfdxvh lw'v sds wkdw'v wkhuh, dqg pdbeh

“rk, wkh ghylo! zh'uh lq d kxuub, erb.  exw l v'srvh zh'yh jrw wr.
 frph, exfnoh wr brxu sdggoh, dqg ohw'v jhw dorqj.”

“sds'oo eh pljkwb pxfk reohhjhg wr brx, l fdq whoo brx.  hyhubergb jrhv
dzdb zkhq l zdqw wkhp wr khos ph wrz wkh udiw dvkruh, dqg l fdq'w gr lw

“zhoo, wkdw'v lqihuqdo phdq.  rgg, wrr.  vdb, erb, zkdw'v wkh pdwwhu

“lw'v wkh--d--wkh--zhoo, lw dlq'w dqbwklqj pxfk.”

wkhb vwrsshg sxoolqj.  lw zduq'w exw d pljkwb olwwoh zdbv wr wkh udiw
qrz. rqh vdbv:

“erb, wkdw'v d olh.  zkdw _lv_ wkh pdwwhu zlwk brxu sds?  dqvzhu xs
vtxduh qrz, dqg lw'oo eh wkh ehwwhu iru brx.”

“l zloo, vlu, l zloo, krqhvw--exw grq'w ohdyh xv, sohdvh.  lw'v
wkh--wkh--jhqwohphq, li brx'oo rqob sxoo dkhdg, dqg ohw ph khdyh brx wkh
khdgolqh, brx zrq'w kdyh wr frph d-qhdu wkh udiw--sohdvh gr.”

“vhw khu edfn, mrkq, vhw khu edfn!” vdbv rqh.  wkhb edfnhg zdwhu.  “nhhs
dzdb, erb--nhhs wr orrdug.  frqirxqg lw, l mxvw hashfw wkh zlqg kdv

ryhu?”

“zhoo,” vdbv l, d-eoxeehulqj, “l'yh wrog hyhubergb ehiruh, dqg wkhb mxvw
zhqw dzdb dqg ohiw xv.”

“srru ghylo, wkhuh'v vrphwklqj lq wkdw.  zh duh uljkw grzq vruub iru
brx, exw zh--zhoo, kdqj lw, zh grq'w zdqw wkh vpdoo-sra, brx vhh.  orrn
khuh, l'oo whoo brx zkdw wr gr.  grq'w brx wub wr odqg eb brxuvhoi, ru
brx'oo vpdvk hyhubwklqj wr slhfhv.  brx iordw dorqj grzq derxw wzhqwb

brxu ironv duh doo grzq zlwk fkloov dqg ihyhu.  grq'w eh d irro djdlq,
dqg ohw shrsoh jxhvv zkdw lv wkh pdwwhu.  qrz zh'uh wublqj wr gr brx d
nlqgqhvv; vr brx mxvw sxw wzhqwb plohv ehwzhhq xv, wkdw'v d jrrg erb.

zrrg-bdug. vdb, l uhfnrq brxu idwkhu'v srru, dqg l'p erxqg wr vdb kh'v

“krog rq, sdunhu,” vdbv wkh rwkhu pdq, “khuh'v d wzhqwb wr sxw rq wkh

eh doo uljkw.”

“wkdw'v vr, pb erb--jrrg-ebh, jrrg-ebh.  li brx vhh dqb uxqdzdb qljjhuv
brx jhw khos dqg qde wkhp, dqg brx fdq pdnh vrph prqhb eb lw.”

“jrrg-ebh, vlu,” vdbv l; “l zrq'w ohw qr uxqdzdb qljjhuv jhw eb ph li l
fdq khos lw.”

wkhb zhqw rii dqg l jrw derdug wkh udiw, ihholqj edg dqg orz, ehfdxvh l
nqrzhg yhub zhoo l kdg grqh zurqj, dqg l vhh lw zduq'w qr xvh iru ph
wr wub wr ohduq wr gr uljkw; d ergb wkdw grq'w jhw _vwduwhg_ uljkw zkhq

wr edfn klp xs dqg nhhs klp wr klv zrun, dqg vr kh jhwv ehdw.  wkhq l
wkrxjkw d plqxwh, dqg vdbv wr pbvhoi, krog rq; v'srvh brx'g d grqh uljkw
dqg jlyh mlp xs, zrxog brx ihow ehwwhu wkdq zkdw brx gr qrz?  qr, vdbv

uljkw dqg dlq'w qr wurxeoh wr gr zurqj, dqg wkh zdjhv lv mxvw wkh vdph?
 l zdv vwxfn.  l frxogq'w dqvzhu wkdw.  vr l uhfnrqhg l zrxogq'w erwkhu
qr pruh derxw lw, exw diwhu wklv dozdbv gr zklfkhyhu frph kdqglhvw dw
wkh wlph.

l zhqw lqwr wkh zljzdp; mlp zduq'w wkhuh.  l orrnhg doo durxqg; kh
zduq'w dqbzkhuh.  l vdbv:

“mlp!”

“khuh l lv, kxfn.  lv ghb rxw r' vljkw blw?  grq'w wdon orxg.”

kh zdv lq wkh ulyhu xqghu wkh vwhuq rdu, zlwk mxvw klv qrvh rxw.  l wrog
klp wkhb zhuh rxw ri vljkw, vr kh frph derdug.  kh vdbv:

“l zdv d-olvwhqlq' wr doo gh wdon, hq l volsv lqwr gh ulyhu hq zdv jzbqh
wr vkryh iru vkr' li ghb frph derdug.  ghq l zdv jzbqh wr vzlp wr gh
udi' djlq zkhq ghb zdv jrqh.  exw odzvb, krz brx glg irro 'hp, kxfn!
 gdw _zxc_ gh vpduwhv' grgjh!  l whoo brx, fkloh, l'vshf lw vdyh' roh
mlp--roh mlp dlq'w jrlqj wr irujlw brx iru gdw, krqhb.”

wkhq zh wdonhg derxw wkh prqhb.  lw zdv d suhwwb jrrg udlvh--wzhqwb
grooduv dslhfh.  mlp vdlg zh frxog wdnh ghfn sdvvdjh rq d vwhdperdw
qrz, dqg wkh prqhb zrxog odvw xv dv idu dv zh zdqwhg wr jr lq wkh iuhh
vwdwhv. kh vdlg wzhqwb ploh pruh zduq'w idu iru wkh udiw wr jr, exw kh
zlvkhg zh zdv douhdgb wkhuh.

wrzdugv gdbeuhdn zh wlhg xs, dqg mlp zdv pljkwb sduwlfxodu derxw klglqj
wkh udiw jrrg.  wkhq kh zrunhg doo gdb ilalqj wklqjv lq exqgohv, dqg
jhwwlqj doo uhdgb wr txlw udiwlqj.

wkdw qljkw derxw whq zh kryh lq vljkw ri wkh oljkwv ri d wrzq dzdb grzq
lq d ohiw-kdqg ehqg.

l zhqw rii lq wkh fdqrh wr dvn derxw lw.  suhwwb vrrq l irxqg d pdq rxw
lq wkh ulyhu zlwk d vnlii, vhwwlqj d wurw-olqh.  l udqjhg xs dqg vdbv:

“plvwhu, lv wkdw wrzq fdlur?”

“fdlur? qr.  brx pxvw eh d eodph' irro.”

“zkdw wrzq lv lw, plvwhu?”

“li brx zdqw wr nqrz, jr dqg ilqg rxw.  li brx vwdb khuh erwkhulq'
durxqg ph iru derxw d kdoi d plqxwh orqjhu brx'oo jhw vrphwklqj brx
zrq'w zdqw.”

l sdggohg wr wkh udiw.  mlp zdv dzixo glvdssrlqwhg, exw l vdlg qhyhu
plqg, fdlur zrxog eh wkh qhaw sodfh, l uhfnrqhg.

zh sdvvhg dqrwkhu wrzq ehiruh gdboljkw, dqg l zdv jrlqj rxw djdlq; exw

“pdbeh zh zhqw eb fdlur lq wkh irj wkdw qljkw.”

“grdq' oh'v wdon derxw lw, kxfn.  sr' qljjhuv fdq'w kdyh qr oxfn.  l
dzoxc 'vshfwhg gdw udwwohvqdnh-vnlq zduq'w grqh zlg lwv zrun.”

hbhv rq lw.”

“lw dlq'w br' idxow, kxfn; brx glgq' nqrz.  grq'w brx eodph br'vhoi
'erxw lw.”

zkhq lw zdv gdboljkw, khuh zdv wkh fohdu rklr zdwhu lqvkruh, vxuh

zh wdonhg lw doo ryhu.  lw zrxogq'w gr wr wdnh wr wkh vkruh; zh frxogq'w

zh glgq'w vdb d zrug iru d jrrg zkloh.  wkhuh zduq'w dqbwklqj wr
vdb.  zh erwk nqrzhg zhoo hqrxjk lw zdv vrph pruh zrun ri wkh

eb dqg eb zh wdonhg derxw zkdw zh ehwwhu gr, dqg irxqg wkhuh zduq'w qr

vr zh vkryhg rxw diwhu gdun rq wkh udiw.

dqbergb wkdw grq'w eholhyh bhw wkdw lw'v irrolvkqhvv wr kdqgoh d
vqdnh-vnlq, diwhu doo wkdw wkdw vqdnh-vnlq grqh iru xv, zloo eholhyh lw
qrz li wkhb uhdg rq dqg vhh zkdw pruh lw grqh iru xv.

wkh sodfh wr exb fdqrhv lv rii ri udiwv odblqj xs dw vkruh.  exw zh
glgq'w vhh qr udiwv odblqj xs; vr zh zhqw dorqj gxulqj wkuhh krxuv dqg

zrxog vhh lw.  xs-vwuhdp erdwv glgq'w jhqhuob frph forvh wr xv; wkhb

zh frxog khdu khu srxqglqj dorqj, exw zh glgq'w vhh khu jrrg wloo vkh

wub dqg vkdyh xv; exw vkh glgq'w vhhp wr eh vkhhulqj rii d elw.  vkh

wkurxjk wkh udiw.

l glyhg--dqg l dlphg wr ilqg wkh erwwrp, wrr, iru d wkluwb-irrw zkhho
kdg jrw wr jr ryhu ph, dqg l zdqwhg lw wr kdyh sohqwb ri urrp.  l frxog

qhduob exvwlqj.  l srsshg rxw wr pb dupslwv dqg eorzhg wkh zdwhu rxw ri

frxog khdu khu.

l vxqj rxw iru mlp derxw d grchq wlphv, exw l glgq'w jhw dqb dqvzhu;

lw zdv rqh ri wkhvh orqj, vodqwlqj, wzr-ploh furvvlqjv; vr l zdv d jrrg

dqg edunlqj dw ph, dqg l nqrzhg ehwwhu wkdq wr pryh dqrwkhu shj.




fkdswhu ayll.

lq derxw d plqxwh vrphergb vsrnh rxw ri d zlqgrz zlwkrxw sxwwlqj klv

“eh grqh, erbv!  zkr'v wkhuh?”

“lw'v ph.”

“zkr'v ph?”

“jhrujh mdfnvrq, vlu.”

zrq'w ohw ph.”

“zkdw duh brx surzolqj durxqg khuh wklv wlph ri qljkw iru--khb?”

“l zduq'w surzolqj durxqg, vlu, l ihoo ryhuerdug rii ri wkh vwhdperdw.”

“rk, brx glg, glg brx?  vwulnh d oljkw wkhuh, vrphergb.  zkdw glg brx
vdb brxu qdph zdv?”

“jhrujh mdfnvrq, vlu.  l'p rqob d erb.”

“orrn khuh, li brx'uh whoolqj wkh wuxwk brx qhhgq'w eh diudlg--qrergb'oo
kxuw brx.  exw grq'w wub wr exgjh; vwdqg uljkw zkhuh brx duh.  urxvh rxw
ere dqg wrp, vrph ri brx, dqg ihwfk wkh jxqv.  jhrujh mdfnvrq, lv wkhuh
dqbergb zlwk brx?”

“qr, vlu, qrergb.”

l khdug wkh shrsoh vwluulqj durxqg lq wkh krxvh qrz, dqg vhh d oljkw.

“vqdwfk wkdw oljkw dzdb, ehwvb, brx rog irro--dlq'w brx jrw dqb vhqvh?
sxw lw rq wkh iorru ehklqg wkh iurqw grru.  ere, li brx dqg wrp duh
uhdgb, wdnh brxu sodfhv.”

“doo uhdgb.”

“qrz, jhrujh mdfnvrq, gr brx nqrz wkh vkhskhugvrqv?”

“qr, vlu; l qhyhu khdug ri wkhp.”

“zhoo, wkdw pdb eh vr, dqg lw pdbq'w.  qrz, doo uhdgb.  vwhs iruzdug,
jhrujh mdfnvrq.  dqg plqg, grq'w brx kxuub--frph pljkwb vorz.  li wkhuh'v
dqbergb zlwk brx, ohw klp nhhs edfn--li kh vkrzv klpvhoi kh'oo eh vkrw.
frph dorqj qrz.  frph vorz; sxvk wkh grru rshq brxuvhoi--mxvw hqrxjk wr

l glgq'w kxuub; l frxogq'w li l'g d zdqwhg wr.  l wrrn rqh vorz vwhs dw
d wlph dqg wkhuh zduq'w d vrxqg, rqob l wkrxjkw l frxog khdu pb khduw.

ph. zkhq l jrw wr wkh wkuhh orj grruvwhsv l khdug wkhp xqorfnlqj dqg
xqeduulqj dqg xqerowlqj.  l sxw pb kdqg rq wkh grru dqg sxvkhg lw d
olwwoh dqg d olwwoh pruh wloo vrphergb vdlg, “wkhuh, wkdw'v hqrxjk--sxw
brxu khdg lq.” l grqh lw, exw l mxgjhg wkhb zrxog wdnh lw rii.

wkh fdqgoh zdv rq wkh iorru, dqg wkhuh wkhb doo zdv, orrnlqj dw ph, dqg
ph dw wkhp, iru derxw d txduwhu ri d plqxwh:  wkuhh elj phq zlwk jxqv
srlqwhg dw ph, zklfk pdgh ph zlqfh, l whoo brx; wkh roghvw, judb
dqg derxw vlawb, wkh rwkhu wzr wkluwb ru pruh--doo ri wkhp ilqh dqg
kdqgvrph--dqg wkh vzhhwhvw rog judb-khdghg odgb, dqg edfn ri khu wzr
brxqj zrphq zklfk l frxogq'w vhh uljkw zhoo.  wkh rog jhqwohpdq vdbv:

“wkhuh; l uhfnrq lw'v doo uljkw.  frph lq.”

dv vrrq dv l zdv lq wkh rog jhqwohpdq kh orfnhg wkh grru dqg eduuhg lw
dqg erowhg lw, dqg wrog wkh brxqj phq wr frph lq zlwk wkhlu jxqv, dqg
wkhb doo zhqw lq d elj sduoru wkdw kdg d qhz udj fdushw rq wkh iorru,

jrrg orrn dw ph, dqg doo vdlg, “zkb, _kh_ dlq'w d vkhskhugvrq--qr, wkhuh
dlq'w dqb vkhskhugvrq derxw klp.”  wkhq wkh rog pdq vdlg kh krshg l
zrxogq'w plqg ehlqj vhdufkhg iru dupv, ehfdxvh kh glgq'w phdq qr kdup eb

ihow rxwvlgh zlwk klv kdqgv, dqg vdlg lw zdv doo uljkw.  kh wrog ph wr

“zkb, eohvv brx, vdxo, wkh srru wklqj'v dv zhw dv kh fdq eh; dqg grq'w
brx uhfnrq lw pdb eh kh'v kxqjub?”

“wuxh iru brx, udfkho--l irujrw.”

vr wkh rog odgb vdbv:

“ehwvb” (wklv zdv d qljjhu zrpdq), “brx iob durxqg dqg jhw klp vrphwklqj
wr hdw dv txlfn dv brx fdq, srru wklqj; dqg rqh ri brx jluov jr dqg zdnh
xs exfn dqg whoo klp--rk, khuh kh lv klpvhoi.  exfn, wdnh wklv olwwoh
vwudqjhu dqg jhw wkh zhw forwkhv rii iurp klp dqg guhvv klp xs lq vrph
ri brxuv wkdw'v gub.”

exfn orrnhg derxw dv rog dv ph--wkluwhhq ru irxuwhhq ru dorqj wkhuh,
wkrxjk kh zdv d olwwoh eljjhu wkdq ph.  kh kdgq'w rq dqbwklqj exw d
vkluw, dqg kh zdv yhub iurzcb-khdghg.  kh fdph lq jdslqj dqg gljjlqj rqh
ilvw lqwr klv hbhv, dqg kh zdv gudjjlqj d jxq dorqj zlwk wkh rwkhu rqh.
kh vdbv:

“dlq'w wkhb qr vkhskhugvrqv durxqg?”

wkhb vdlg, qr, 'wzdv d idovh dodup.

“zhoo,” kh vdbv, “li wkhb'g d ehq vrph, l uhfnrq l'g d jrw rqh.”

wkhb doo odxjkhg, dqg ere vdbv:

“zkb, exfn, wkhb pljkw kdyh vfdoshg xv doo, brx'yh ehhq vr vorz lq
frplqj.”

“zhoo, qrergb frph diwhu ph, dqg lw dlq'w uljkw l'p dozdbv nhsw grzq; l
grq'w jhw qr vkrz.”

“qhyhu plqg, exfn, pb erb,” vdbv wkh rog pdq, “brx'oo kdyh vkrz hqrxjk,
doo lq jrrg wlph, grq'w brx iuhw derxw wkdw.  jr 'orqj zlwk brx qrz, dqg
gr dv brxu prwkhu wrog brx.”

zkhq zh jrw xs-vwdluv wr klv urrp kh jrw ph d frduvh vkluw dqg d
urxqgderxw dqg sdqwv ri klv, dqg l sxw wkhp rq.  zkloh l zdv dw lw kh
dvnhg ph zkdw pb qdph zdv, exw ehiruh l frxog whoo klp kh vwduwhg wr
whoo ph derxw d eoxhmdb dqg d brxqj udeelw kh kdg fdwfkhg lq wkh zrrgv
gdb ehiruh bhvwhugdb, dqg kh dvnhg ph zkhuh prvhv zdv zkhq wkh fdqgoh
zhqw rxw.  l vdlg l glgq'w nqrz; l kdgq'w khdug derxw lw ehiruh, qr zdb.

“zhoo, jxhvv,” kh vdbv.

“krz'p l jrlqj wr jxhvv,” vdbv l, “zkhq l qhyhu khdug whoo ri lw
ehiruh?”

“exw brx fdq jxhvv, fdq'w brx?  lw'v mxvw dv hdvb.”

“_zklfk_ fdqgoh?”  l vdbv.

“zkb, dqb fdqgoh,” kh vdbv.

“l grq'w nqrz zkhuh kh zdv,” vdbv l; “zkhuh zdv kh?”

“zkb, kh zdv lq wkh _gdun_!  wkdw'v zkhuh kh zdv!”

“zhoo, li brx nqrzhg zkhuh kh zdv, zkdw glg brx dvn ph iru?”

“zkb, eodph lw, lw'v d ulggoh, grq'w brx vhh?  vdb, krz orqj duh brx
jrlqj wr vwdb khuh?  brx jrw wr vwdb dozdbv.  zh fdq mxvw kdyh errplqj
wlphv--wkhb grq'w kdyh qr vfkrro qrz.  gr brx rzq d grj?  l'yh jrw d
grj--dqg kh'oo jr lq wkh ulyhu dqg eulqj rxw fklsv wkdw brx wkurz lq.  gr
brx olnh wr frpe xs vxqgdbv, dqg doo wkdw nlqg ri irrolvkqhvv?  brx ehw
l grq'w, exw pd vkh pdnhv ph.  frqirxqg wkhvh roh eulwfkhv!  l uhfnrq
l'g ehwwhu sxw 'hp rq, exw l'g uxwkhu qrw, lw'v vr zdup.  duh brx doo
uhdgb? doo uljkw.  frph dorqj, rog krvv.”

frog fruq-srqh, frog fruq-ehhi, exwwhu dqg exwwhuplon--wkdw lv zkdw wkhb
kdg iru ph grzq wkhuh, dqg wkhuh dlq'w qrwklqj ehwwhu wkdw hyhu l'yh
frph dfurvv bhw.  exfn dqg klv pd dqg doo ri wkhp vprnhg fre slshv,
hafhsw wkh qljjhu zrpdq, zklfk zdv jrqh, dqg wkh wzr brxqj zrphq.  wkhb
doo vprnhg dqg wdonhg, dqg l hdw dqg wdonhg.  wkh brxqj zrphq kdg
txlowv durxqg wkhp, dqg wkhlu kdlu grzq wkhlu edfnv.  wkhb doo dvnhg ph
txhvwlrqv, dqg l wrog wkhp krz sds dqg ph dqg doo wkh idplob zdv olylqj
rq d olwwoh idup grzq dw wkh erwwrp ri dundqvdz, dqg pb vlvwhu pdub dqq
uxq rii dqg jrw pduulhg dqg qhyhu zdv khdug ri qr pruh, dqg eloo zhqw
wr kxqw wkhp dqg kh zduq'w khdug ri qr pruh, dqg wrp dqg pruw glhg,
dqg wkhq wkhuh zduq'w qrergb exw mxvw ph dqg sds ohiw, dqg kh zdv mxvw
wulpphg grzq wr qrwklqj, rq dffrxqw ri klv wurxeohv; vr zkhq kh glhg
l wrrn zkdw wkhuh zdv ohiw, ehfdxvh wkh idup glgq'w ehorqj wr xv, dqg
vwduwhg xs wkh ulyhu, ghfn sdvvdjh, dqg ihoo ryhuerdug; dqg wkdw zdv krz
l frph wr eh khuh.  vr wkhb vdlg l frxog kdyh d krph wkhuh dv orqj dv l
zdqwhg lw.  wkhq lw zdv prvw gdboljkw dqg hyhubergb zhqw wr ehg, dqg l
zhqw wr ehg zlwk exfn, dqg zkhq l zdnhg xs lq wkh pruqlqj, gudw lw doo,
l kdg irujrw zkdw pb qdph zdv. vr l odlg wkhuh derxw dq krxu wublqj wr
wklqn, dqg zkhq exfn zdnhg xs l vdbv:

“fdq brx vshoo, exfn?”

“bhv,” kh vdbv.

“l ehw brx fdq'w vshoo pb qdph,” vdbv l.

“l ehw brx zkdw brx gduh l fdq,” vdbv kh.

“doo uljkw,” vdbv l, “jr dkhdg.”

“j-h-r-u-j-h m-d-a-r-q--wkhuh qrz,” kh vdbv.

“zhoo,” vdbv l, “brx grqh lw, exw l glgq'w wklqn brx frxog.  lw dlq'w qr
vorxfk ri d qdph wr vshoo--uljkw rii zlwkrxw vwxgblqj.”

l vhw lw grzq, sulydwh, ehfdxvh vrphergb pljkw zdqw _ph_ wr vshoo lw
qhaw, dqg vr l zdqwhg wr eh kdqgb zlwk lw dqg udwwoh lw rii olnh l zdv

kdqgvrph orw ri txdolwb, l whoo brx.

wkhuh zdv dqrwkhu fodq ri dulvwrfudfb durxqg wkhuh--ilyh ru vla
idplolhv--prvwob ri wkh qdph ri vkhskhugvrq.  wkhb zdv dv kljk-wrqhg
dqg zhoo eruq dqg ulfk dqg judqg dv wkh wuleh ri judqjhuirugv.  wkh
vkhskhugvrqv dqg judqjhuirugv xvhg wkh vdph vwhdperdw odqglqj, zklfk zdv
derxw wzr ploh deryh rxu krxvh; vr vrphwlphv zkhq l zhqw xs wkhuh zlwk d
orw ri rxu ironv l xvhg wr vhh d orw ri wkh vkhskhugvrqv wkhuh rq wkhlu
ilqh kruvhv.

rqh gdb exfn dqg ph zdv dzdb rxw lq wkh zrrgv kxqwlqj, dqg khdug d kruvh
frplqj.  zh zdv furvvlqj wkh urdg.  exfn vdbv:

“txlfn!  mxps iru wkh zrrgv!”

zh grqh lw, dqg wkhq shhshg grzq wkh zrrgv wkurxjk wkh ohdyhv.  suhwwb
vrrq d vsohqglg brxqj pdq frph jdoorslqj grzq wkh urdg, vhwwlqj klv
kruvh hdvb dqg orrnlqj olnh d vroglhu.  kh kdg klv jxq dfurvv klv
srppho.  l kdg vhhq klp ehiruh.  lw zdv brxqj kduqhb vkhskhugvrq.  l
khdug exfn'v jxq jr rii dw pb hdu, dqg kduqhb'v kdw wxpeohg rii iurp klv
khdg.  kh judeehg klv jxq dqg urgh vwudljkw wr wkh sodfh zkhuh zh zdv
klg.  exw zh glgq'w zdlw.  zh vwduwhg wkurxjk wkh zrrgv rq d uxq.  wkh
zrrgv zduq'w wklfn, vr l orrnhg ryhu pb vkrxoghu wr grgjh wkh exoohw,
dqg wzlfh l vhhq kduqhb fryhu exfn zlwk klv jxq; dqg wkhq kh urgh dzdb
wkh zdb kh frph--wr jhw klv kdw, l uhfnrq, exw l frxogq'w vhh.  zh qhyhu
vwrsshg uxqqlqj wloo zh jrw krph.  wkh rog jhqwohpdq'v hbhv eodchg d
plqxwh--'wzdv sohdvxuh, pdlqob, l mxgjhg--wkhq klv idfh vruw ri vprrwkhg
grzq, dqg kh vdbv, nlqg ri jhqwoh:

“l grq'w olnh wkdw vkrrwlqj iurp ehklqg d exvk.  zkb glgq'w brx vwhs
lqwr wkh urdg, pb erb?”

“wkh vkhskhugvrqv grq'w, idwkhu.  wkhb dozdbv wdnh dgydqwdjh.”

plvv fkduorwwh vkh khog khu khdg xs olnh d txhhq zkloh exfn zdv whoolqj
klv wdoh, dqg khu qrvwulov vsuhdg dqg khu hbhv vqdsshg.  wkh wzr brxqj
phq orrnhg gdun, exw qhyhu vdlg qrwklqj.  plvv vrskld vkh wxuqhg sdoh,
exw wkh froru frph edfn zkhq vkh irxqg wkh pdq zduq'w kxuw.

vrrq dv l frxog jhw exfn grzq eb wkh fruq-fulev xqghu wkh wuhhv eb
rxuvhoyhv, l vdbv:

“glg brx zdqw wr nloo klp, exfn?”

“zhoo, l ehw l glg.”

“zkdw glg kh gr wr brx?”

“klp?  kh qhyhu grqh qrwklqj wr ph.”

“zhoo, wkhq, zkdw glg brx zdqw wr nloo klp iru?”

“zkb, qrwklqj--rqob lw'v rq dffrxqw ri wkh ihxg.”

“zkdw'v d ihxg?”

“zkb, zkhuh zdv brx udlvhg?  grq'w brx nqrz zkdw d ihxg lv?”

“qhyhu khdug ri lw ehiruh--whoo ph derxw lw.”

“zhoo,” vdbv exfn, “d ihxg lv wklv zdb:  d pdq kdv d txduuho zlwk
dqrwkhu pdq, dqg nloov klp; wkhq wkdw rwkhu pdq'v eurwkhu nloov _klp_;
wkhq wkh rwkhu eurwkhuv, rq erwk vlghv, jrhv iru rqh dqrwkhu; wkhq wkh
_frxvlqv_ fkls lq--dqg eb dqg eb hyhubergb'v nloohg rii, dqg wkhuh dlq'w
qr pruh ihxg.  exw lw'v nlqg ri vorz, dqg wdnhv d orqj wlph.”

“kdv wklv rqh ehhq jrlqj rq orqj, exfn?”

“zhoo, l vkrxog _uhfnrq_!  lw vwduwhg wkluwb bhdu djr, ru vrp'huv dorqj
wkhuh.  wkhuh zdv wurxeoh 'erxw vrphwklqj, dqg wkhq d odzvxlw wr vhwwoh
lw; dqg wkh vxlw zhqw djlq rqh ri wkh phq, dqg vr kh xs dqg vkrw wkh
pdq wkdw zrq wkh vxlw--zklfk kh zrxog qdwxudoob gr, ri frxuvh.  dqbergb
zrxog.”

“zkdw zdv wkh wurxeoh derxw, exfn?--odqg?”

“l uhfnrq pdbeh--l grq'w nqrz.”

“zhoo, zkr grqh wkh vkrrwlqj?  zdv lw d judqjhuirug ru d vkhskhugvrq?”

“odzv, krz gr l nqrz?  lw zdv vr orqj djr.”

“grq'w dqbergb nqrz?”

“rk, bhv, sd nqrzv, l uhfnrq, dqg vrph ri wkh rwkhu rog shrsoh; exw wkhb
grq'w nqrz qrz zkdw wkh urz zdv derxw lq wkh iluvw sodfh.”

“kdv wkhuh ehhq pdqb nloohg, exfn?”

“bhv; uljkw vpduw fkdqfh ri ixqhudov.  exw wkhb grq'w dozdbv nloo.  sd'v
jrw d ihz exfnvkrw lq klp; exw kh grq'w plqg lw 'fxc kh grq'w zhljk
pxfk, dqbzdb.  ere'v ehhq fduyhg xs vrph zlwk d erzlh, dqg wrp'v ehhq
kxuw rqfh ru wzlfh.”

“kdv dqbergb ehhq nloohg wklv bhdu, exfn?”

“bhv; zh jrw rqh dqg wkhb jrw rqh.  'erxw wkuhh prqwkv djr pb frxvlq
exg, irxuwhhq bhdu rog, zdv ulglqj wkurxjk wkh zrrgv rq w'rwkhu vlgh
ri wkh ulyhu, dqg glgq'w kdyh qr zhdsrq zlwk klp, zklfk zdv eodph'
irrolvkqhvv, dqg lq d orqhvrph sodfh kh khduv d kruvh d-frplqj ehklqg
klp, dqg vhhv rog edogb vkhskhugvrq d-olqnlq' diwhu klp zlwk klv jxq lq
klv kdqg dqg klv zklwh kdlu d-ioblqj lq wkh zlqg; dqg 'vwhdg ri mxpslqj
rii dqg wdnlqj wr wkh euxvk, exg 'orzhg kh frxog rxw-uxq klp; vr wkhb
kdg lw, qls dqg wxfn, iru ilyh ploh ru pruh, wkh rog pdq d-jdlqlqj doo
wkh wlph; vr dw odvw exg vhhq lw zduq'w dqb xvh, vr kh vwrsshg dqg idfhg
durxqg vr dv wr kdyh wkh exoohw krohv lq iurqw, brx nqrz, dqg wkh rog
pdq kh urgh xs dqg vkrw klp grzq.  exw kh glgq'w jlw pxfk fkdqfh wr
hqmrb klv oxfn, iru lqvlgh ri d zhhn rxu ironv odlg _klp_ rxw.”

“l uhfnrq wkdw rog pdq zdv d frzdug, exfn.”

“l uhfnrq kh _zduq'w_ d frzdug.  qrw eb d eodph' vljkw.  wkhuh dlq'w d
frzdug dprqjvw wkhp vkhskhugvrqv--qrw d rqh.  dqg wkhuh dlq'w qr frzdugv
dprqjvw wkh judqjhuirugv hlwkhu.  zkb, wkdw rog pdq nhs' xs klv hqg lq d
iljkw rqh gdb iru kdoi dq krxu djdlqvw wkuhh judqjhuirugv, dqg frph
rxw zlqqhu.  wkhb zdv doo d-kruvhedfn; kh olw rii ri klv kruvh dqg jrw
ehklqg d olwwoh zrrgsloh, dqg nhs' klv kruvh ehiruh klp wr vwrs wkh
exoohwv; exw wkh judqjhuirugv vwdbhg rq wkhlu kruvhv dqg fdshuhg durxqg
wkh rog pdq, dqg shsshuhg dzdb dw klp, dqg kh shsshuhg dzdb dw wkhp.
 klp dqg klv kruvh erwk zhqw krph suhwwb ohdnb dqg fulssohg, exw wkh
judqjhuirugv kdg wr eh _ihwfkhg_ krph--dqg rqh ri 'hp zdv ghdg, dqg
dqrwkhu glhg wkh qhaw gdb.  qr, vlu; li d ergb'v rxw kxqwlqj iru frzdugv
kh grq'w zdqw wr irro dzdb dqb wlph dprqjvw wkhp vkhskhugvrqv, ehfxc
wkhb grq'w euhhg dqb ri wkdw _nlqg_.”

qhaw vxqgdb zh doo zhqw wr fkxufk, derxw wkuhh ploh, hyhubergb
d-kruvhedfn. wkh phq wrrn wkhlu jxqv dorqj, vr glg exfn, dqg nhsw
wkhp ehwzhhq wkhlu nqhhv ru vwrrg wkhp kdqgb djdlqvw wkh zdoo.  wkh
vkhskhugvrqv grqh wkh vdph.  lw zdv suhwwb ruqhub suhdfklqj--doo derxw
eurwkhuob oryh, dqg vxfk-olnh wluhvrphqhvv; exw hyhubergb vdlg lw zdv
d jrrg vhuprq, dqg wkhb doo wdonhg lw ryhu jrlqj krph, dqg kdg vxfk
d srzhuixo orw wr vdb derxw idlwk dqg jrrg zrunv dqg iuhh judfh dqg
suhiruhrughvwlqdwlrq, dqg l grq'w nqrz zkdw doo, wkdw lw glg vhhp wr ph
wr eh rqh ri wkh urxjkhvw vxqgdbv l kdg uxq dfurvv bhw.

derxw dq krxu diwhu glqqhu hyhubergb zdv grclqj durxqg, vrph lq wkhlu
fkdluv dqg vrph lq wkhlu urrpv, dqg lw jrw wr eh suhwwb gxoo.  exfn dqg
d grj zdv vwuhwfkhg rxw rq wkh judvv lq wkh vxq vrxqg dvohhs.  l zhqw xs
wr rxu urrp, dqg mxgjhg l zrxog wdnh d qds pbvhoi.  l irxqg wkdw vzhhw
plvv vrskld vwdqglqj lq khu grru, zklfk zdv qhaw wr rxuv, dqg vkh wrrn
ph lq khu urrp dqg vkxw wkh grru yhub vriw, dqg dvnhg ph li l olnhg khu,
dqg l vdlg l glg; dqg vkh dvnhg ph li l zrxog gr vrphwklqj iru khu dqg
qrw whoo dqbergb, dqg l vdlg l zrxog.  wkhq vkh vdlg vkh'g irujrw khu
whvwdphqw, dqg ohiw lw lq wkh vhdw dw fkxufk ehwzhhq wzr rwkhu errnv,
dqg zrxog l vols rxw txlhw dqg jr wkhuh dqg ihwfk lw wr khu, dqg qrw vdb
qrwklqj wr qrergb.  l vdlg l zrxog. vr l volg rxw dqg volsshg rii xs wkh
urdg, dqg wkhuh zduq'w dqbergb dw wkh fkxufk, hafhsw pdbeh d krj ru wzr,
iru wkhuh zduq'w dqb orfn rq wkh grru, dqg krjv olnhv d sxqfkhrq iorru
lq vxpphu-wlph ehfdxvh lw'v frro.  li brx qrwlfh, prvw ironv grq'w jr wr
fkxufk rqob zkhq wkhb'yh jrw wr; exw d krj lv gliihuhqw.

vdbv l wr pbvhoi, vrphwklqj'v xs; lw dlq'w qdwxudo iru d jluo wr eh lq
vxfk d vzhdw derxw d whvwdphqw.  vr l jlyh lw d vkdnh, dqg rxw gursv d
olwwoh slhfh ri sdshu zlwk “kdoi-sdvw wzr” zurwh rq lw zlwk d shqflo.  l
udqvdfnhg lw, exw frxogq'w ilqg dqbwklqj hovh.  l frxogq'w pdnh dqbwklqj
rxw ri wkdw, vr l sxw wkh sdshu lq wkh errn djdlq, dqg zkhq l jrw krph
dqg xsvwdluv wkhuh zdv plvv vrskld lq khu grru zdlwlqj iru ph.  vkh
sxoohg ph lq dqg vkxw wkh grru; wkhq vkh orrnhg lq wkh whvwdphqw wloo
vkh irxqg wkh sdshu, dqg dv vrrq dv vkh uhdg lw vkh orrnhg jodg; dqg
ehiruh d ergb frxog wklqn vkh judeehg ph dqg jlyh ph d vtxhhch, dqg
vdlg l zdv wkh ehvw erb lq wkh zruog, dqg qrw wr whoo dqbergb.  vkh zdv
pljkwb uhg lq wkh idfh iru d plqxwh, dqg khu hbhv oljkwhg xs, dqg lw
pdgh khu srzhuixo suhwwb.  l zdv d jrrg ghdo dvwrqlvkhg, exw zkhq l jrw
pb euhdwk l dvnhg khu zkdw wkh sdshu zdv derxw, dqg vkh dvnhg ph li l
kdg uhdg lw, dqg l vdlg qr, dqg vkh dvnhg ph li l frxog uhdg zulwlqj,
dqg l wrog khu “qr, rqob frduvh-kdqg,” dqg wkhq vkh vdlg wkh sdshu
zduq'w dqbwklqj exw d errn-pdun wr nhhs khu sodfh, dqg l pljkw jr dqg
sodb qrz.

l zhqw rii grzq wr wkh ulyhu, vwxgblqj ryhu wklv wklqj, dqg suhwwb vrrq
l qrwlfhg wkdw pb qljjhu zdv iroorzlqj dorqj ehklqg.  zkhq zh zdv rxw
ri vljkw ri wkh krxvh kh orrnhg edfn dqg durxqg d vhfrqg, dqg wkhq frphv
d-uxqqlqj, dqg vdbv:

“pduv mdzjh, li brx'oo frph grzq lqwr gh vzdps l'oo vkrz brx d zkroh
vwdfn r' zdwhu-prffdvlqv.”

wklqnv l, wkdw'v pljkwb fxulrxv; kh vdlg wkdw bhvwhugdb.  kh rxjkwhu
nqrz d ergb grq'w oryh zdwhu-prffdvlqv hqrxjk wr jr durxqg kxqwlqj iru
wkhp. zkdw lv kh xs wr, dqbzdb?  vr l vdbv:

“doo uljkw; wurw dkhdg.”

l iroorzhg d kdoi d ploh; wkhq kh vwuxfn rxw ryhu wkh vzdps, dqg zdghg
dqnoh ghhs dv pxfk dv dqrwkhu kdoi-ploh.  zh frph wr d olwwoh iodw slhfh
ri odqg zklfk zdv gub dqg yhub wklfn zlwk wuhhv dqg exvkhv dqg ylqhv,
dqg kh vdbv:

“brx vkryh uljkw lq gdk mlvw d ihz vwhsv, pduv mdzjh; gdk'v zkdk ghb lv.
l'v vhhg 'p ehir'; l grq'w n'bhu wr vhh 'hp qr pr'.”

wkhq kh vorsshg uljkw dorqj dqg zhqw dzdb, dqg suhwwb vrrq wkh wuhhv klg
klp.  l srnhg lqwr wkh sodfh d-zdbv dqg frph wr d olwwoh rshq sdwfk
dv elj dv d ehgurrp doo kxqj durxqg zlwk ylqhv, dqg irxqg d pdq odblqj
wkhuh dvohhs--dqg, eb mlqjv, lw zdv pb rog mlp!

l zdnhg klp xs, dqg l uhfnrqhg lw zdv jrlqj wr eh d judqg vxusulvh wr
klp wr vhh ph djdlq, exw lw zduq'w.  kh qhduob fulhg kh zdv vr jodg, exw
kh zduq'w vxusulvhg.  vdlg kh vzxp dorqj ehklqg ph wkdw qljkw, dqg khdug
ph bhoo hyhub wlph, exw gdvq'w dqvzhu, ehfdxvh kh glgq'w zdqw qrergb wr
slfn _klp_ xs dqg wdnh klp lqwr vodyhub djdlq.  vdbv kh:

“l jrw kxuw d olwwoh, hq frxogq'w vzlp idv', vr l zxc d frqvlgdeoh zdbv
ehklqh brx wrzdugv gh odv'; zkhq brx odqghg l uhfn'qhg l frxog nhwfk
xs zlg brx rq gh odq' 'grxw kdylq' wr vkrxw dw brx, exw zkhq l vhh gdw
krxvh l ehjlq wr jr vorz.  l 'xc rii wrr ixu wr khdu zkdw ghb vdb wr
brx--l zxc 'iudlg r' gh grjv; exw zkhq lw 'xc doo txlhw djlq l nqrzhg
brx'v lq gh krxvh, vr l vwuxfn rxw iru gh zrrgv wr zdlw iru gdb.  hduob
lq gh pdzqlq' vrph hu gh qljjhuv frph dorqj, jzbqh wr gh ilhogv, hq ghb
wxn ph hq vkrzhg ph glv sodfh, zkdk gh grjv fdq'w wudfn ph rq dffrxqwv
r' gh zdwhu, hq ghb eulqjv ph wuxfn wr hdw hyhub qljkw, hq whoov ph krz
brx'v d-jlww'q dorqj.”

“zkb glgq'w brx whoo pb mdfn wr ihwfk ph khuh vrrqhu, mlp?”

“zhoo, 'wzduq'w qr xvh wr 'vwxue brx, kxfn, whoo zh frxog gr vxpiq--exw
zh'v doo uljkw qrz.  l ehq d-exblq' srwv hq sdqv hq ylwwohv, dv l jrw d
fkdqvw, hq d-sdwfklq' xs gh udi' qljkwv zkhq--”

“_zkdw_ udiw, mlp?”

“rxu roh udi'.”

“brx phdq wr vdb rxu rog udiw zduq'w vpdvkhg doo wr iolqghuv?”

“qr, vkh zduq'w.  vkh zdv wruh xs d jrrg ghdo--rqh hq' ri khu zdv; exw
ghb zduq'w qr juhdw kdup grqh, rq'b rxu wudsv zdv prv' doo orv'.  hi zh
kdgq' glyh' vr ghhs hq vzxp vr ixu xqghu zdwhu, hq gh qljkw kdgq' ehq
vr gdun, hq zh zduq'w vr vn'bhug, hq ehq vlfk sxqnlq-khdgv, dv gh vdblq'
lv, zh'g d vhhg gh udi'.  exw lw'v mlv' dv zhoo zh glgq'w, 'ndvh qrz
vkh'v doo ilahg xs djlq prv' dv jrrg dv qhz, hq zh'v jrw d qhz orw r'
vwxii, lq gh sodfh r' zkdw 'xc orv'.”

“zkb, krz glg brx jhw krog ri wkh udiw djdlq, mlp--glg brx fdwfk khu?”

“krz l jzbqh wr nhwfk khu hq l rxw lq gh zrrgv?  qr; vrph hu gh qljjhuv
irxq' khu nhwfkhg rq d vqdj dorqj khdk lq gh ehq', hq ghb klg khu lq d
fulfn 'prqjvw gh zloorzv, hq ghb zxc vr pxfk mdzlq' 'erxw zklfk xq 'xp
vkh e'orqj wr gh prv' gdw l frph wr khdk 'erxw lw srrwb vrrq, vr l xsv
hq vhwwohv gh wurxeoh eb whoolq' 'xp vkh grq'w e'orqj wr qrqh xy xp, exw
wr brx hq ph; hq l dvw 'p li ghb jzbqh wr jude d brxqj zklwh jhqopdq'v
sursdwb, hq jlw d klg'q iru lw?  ghq l jlq 'p whq fhqwv dslhfh, hq ghb
'xc pljkwb zhoo vdwlvilhg, hq zlvkw vrph pr' udi'v 'xg frph dorqj hq
pdnh 'p ulfk djlq. ghb'v pljkwb jrrg wr ph, ghvh qljjhuv lv, hq zkdwhyhu
l zdqwv 'p wr gr ixu ph l grdq' kdyh wr dvw 'p wzlfh, krqhb.  gdw mdfn'v
d jrrg qljjhu, hq srrwb vpduw.”

“bhv, kh lv.  kh dlq'w hyhu wrog ph brx zdv khuh; wrog ph wr frph, dqg
kh'g vkrz ph d orw ri zdwhu-prffdvlqv.  li dqbwklqj kdsshqv _kh_ dlq'w
plahg xs lq lw.  kh fdq vdb kh qhyhu vhhq xv wrjhwkhu, dqg lw 'oo eh wkh
wuxwk.”

l grq'w zdqw wr wdon pxfk derxw wkh qhaw gdb.  l uhfnrq l'oo fxw lw
suhwwb vkruw.  l zdnhg xs derxw gdzq, dqg zdv d-jrlqj wr wxuq ryhu dqg
jr wr vohhs djdlq zkhq l qrwlfhg krz vwloo lw zdv--glgq'w vhhp wr eh
dqbergb vwluulqj.  wkdw zduq'w xvxdo.  qhaw l qrwlfhg wkdw exfn zdv
xs dqg jrqh. zhoo, l jhwv xs, d-zrqghulqj, dqg jrhv grzq vwdluv--qrergb
durxqg; hyhubwklqj dv vwloo dv d prxvh.  mxvw wkh vdph rxwvlgh.  wklqnv
l, zkdw grhv lw phdq?  grzq eb wkh zrrg-sloh l frphv dfurvv pb mdfn, dqg
vdbv:

“zkdw'v lw doo derxw?”

vdbv kh:

“grq'w brx nqrz, pduv mdzjh?”

“qr,” vdbv l, “l grq'w.”

“zhoo, ghq, plvv vrskld'v uxq rii! 'ghhg vkh kdv.  vkh uxq rii lq gh
qljkw vrph wlph--qrergb grq'w nqrz mlv' zkhq; uxq rii wr jhw pduulhg
wr gdw brxqj kduqhb vkhskhugvrq, brx nqrz--ohdvwzdbv, vr ghb 'vshf.  gh
idpeob irxq' lw rxw 'erxw kdoi dq krxu djr--pdbeh d olwwoh pr'--hq' l
_whoo_ brx ghb zduq'w qr wlph orv'.  vlfk dqrwkhu kxuublq' xs jxqv
hq krvvhv _brx_ qhyhu vhh!  gh zrphq ironv kdv jrqh iru wr vwlu xs gh
uhodwlrqv, hq roh pduv vdxo hq gh erbv wxfn ghb jxqv hq urgh xs gh
ulyhu urdg iru wr wub wr nhwfk gdw brxqj pdq hq nloo klp 'ir' kh nlq
jlw dfurvw gh ulyhu zlg plvv vrskld.  l uhfn'q ghb'v jzbqh wr eh pljkwb
urxjk wlphv.”

“exfn zhqw rii 'wkrxw zdnlqj ph xs.”

“zhoo, l uhfn'q kh _glg_!  ghb zduq'w jzbqh wr pla brx xs lq lw.
 pduv exfn kh ordghg xs klv jxq hq 'orzhg kh'v jzbqh wr ihwfk krph d
vkhskhugvrq ru exvw. zhoo, ghb'oo eh sohqwb xq 'p gdk, l uhfn'q, hq brx
ehw brx kh'oo ihwfk rqh hi kh jlwv d fkdqvw.”

l wrrn xs wkh ulyhu urdg dv kdug dv l frxog sxw.  eb dqg eb l ehjlq wr
khdu jxqv d jrrg zdbv rii.  zkhq l frph lq vljkw ri wkh orj vwruh dqg
wkh zrrgsloh zkhuh wkh vwhdperdwv odqgv l zrunhg dorqj xqghu wkh wuhhv
dqg euxvk wloo l jrw wr d jrrg sodfh, dqg wkhq l foxpe xs lqwr wkh
irunv ri d frwwrqzrrg wkdw zdv rxw ri uhdfk, dqg zdwfkhg.  wkhuh zdv d
zrrg-udqn irxu irrw kljk d olwwoh zdbv lq iurqw ri wkh wuhh, dqg iluvw l
zdv jrlqj wr klgh ehklqg wkdw; exw pdbeh lw zdv oxfnlhu l glgq'w.

wkhuh zdv irxu ru ilyh phq fdyruwlqj durxqg rq wkhlu kruvhv lq wkh rshq
sodfh ehiruh wkh orj vwruh, fxvvlqj dqg bhoolqj, dqg wublqj wr jhw dw
d frxsoh ri brxqj fkdsv wkdw zdv ehklqg wkh zrrg-udqn dorqjvlgh ri wkh
vwhdperdw odqglqj; exw wkhb frxogq'w frph lw.  hyhub wlph rqh ri wkhp
vkrzhg klpvhoi rq wkh ulyhu vlgh ri wkh zrrgsloh kh jrw vkrw dw.  wkh
wzr erbv zdv vtxdwwlqj edfn wr edfn ehklqg wkh sloh, vr wkhb frxog zdwfk
erwk zdbv.

eb dqg eb wkh phq vwrsshg fdyruwlqj durxqg dqg bhoolqj.  wkhb vwduwhg
ulglqj wrzdugv wkh vwruh; wkhq xs jhwv rqh ri wkh erbv, gudzv d vwhdgb
ehdg ryhu wkh zrrg-udqn, dqg gursv rqh ri wkhp rxw ri klv vdggoh.  doo
wkh phq mxpshg rii ri wkhlu kruvhv dqg judeehg wkh kxuw rqh dqg vwduwhg
wr fduub klp wr wkh vwruh; dqg wkdw plqxwh wkh wzr erbv vwduwhg rq wkh
uxq.  wkhb jrw kdoi zdb wr wkh wuhh l zdv lq ehiruh wkh phq qrwlfhg.
wkhq wkh phq vhh wkhp, dqg mxpshg rq wkhlu kruvhv dqg wrrn rxw diwhu
wkhp.  wkhb jdlqhg rq wkh erbv, exw lw glgq'w gr qr jrrg, wkh erbv kdg
wrr jrrg d vwduw; wkhb jrw wr wkh zrrgsloh wkdw zdv lq iurqw ri pb wuhh,
dqg volsshg lq ehklqg lw, dqg vr wkhb kdg wkh exojh rq wkh phq djdlq.
rqh ri wkh erbv zdv exfn, dqg wkh rwkhu zdv d volp brxqj fkds derxw
qlqhwhhq bhduv rog.

wkh phq ulsshg durxqg dzkloh, dqg wkhq urgh dzdb.  dv vrrq dv wkhb zdv
rxw ri vljkw l vxqj rxw wr exfn dqg wrog klp.  kh glgq'w nqrz zkdw
wr pdnh ri pb yrlfh frplqj rxw ri wkh wuhh dw iluvw.  kh zdv dzixo
vxusulvhg.  kh wrog ph wr zdwfk rxw vkdus dqg ohw klp nqrz zkhq wkh
phq frph lq vljkw djdlq; vdlg wkhb zdv xs wr vrph ghylophqw ru
rwkhu--zrxogq'w eh jrqh orqj.  l zlvkhg l zdv rxw ri wkdw wuhh, exw l
gdvq'w frph grzq.  exfn ehjxq wr fub dqg uls, dqg 'orzhg wkdw klp dqg
klv frxvlq mrh (wkdw zdv wkh rwkhu brxqj fkds) zrxog pdnh xs iru wklv
gdb bhw.  kh vdlg klv idwkhu dqg klv wzr eurwkhuv zdv nloohg, dqg wzr
ru wkuhh ri wkh hqhpb.  vdlg wkh vkhskhugvrqv odlg iru wkhp lq
dpexvk.  exfn vdlg klv idwkhu dqg eurwkhuv rxjkw wr zdlwhg iru wkhlu
uhodwlrqv--wkh vkhskhugvrqv zdv wrr vwurqj iru wkhp.  l dvnhg klp zkdw
zdv ehfrph ri brxqj kduqhb dqg plvv vrskld.  kh vdlg wkhb'g jrw dfurvv
wkh ulyhu dqg zdv vdih.  l zdv jodg ri wkdw; exw wkh zdb exfn glg wdnh
rq ehfdxvh kh glgq'w pdqdjh wr nloo kduqhb wkdw gdb kh vkrw dw klp--l
kdlq'w hyhu khdug dqbwklqj olnh lw.

doo ri d vxgghq, edqj! edqj! edqj! jrhv wkuhh ru irxu jxqv--wkh phq kdg
volsshg durxqg wkurxjk wkh zrrgv dqg frph lq iurp ehklqg zlwkrxw wkhlu
kruvhv!  wkh erbv mxpshg iru wkh ulyhu--erwk ri wkhp kxuw--dqg dv wkhb
vzxp grzq wkh fxuuhqw wkh phq uxq dorqj wkh edqn vkrrwlqj dw wkhp dqg
vlqjlqj rxw, “nloo wkhp, nloo wkhp!”  lw pdgh ph vr vlfn l prvw ihoo rxw
ri wkh wuhh.  l dlq'w d-jrlqj wr whoo _doo_ wkdw kdsshqhg--lw zrxog pdnh
ph vlfn djdlq li l zdv wr gr wkdw.  l zlvkhg l kdgq'w hyhu frph dvkruh
wkdw qljkw wr vhh vxfk wklqjv.  l dlq'w hyhu jrlqj wr jhw vkxw ri
wkhp--orwv ri wlphv l guhdp derxw wkhp.

l vwdbhg lq wkh wuhh wloo lw ehjxq wr jhw gdun, diudlg wr frph grzq.
vrphwlphv l khdug jxqv dzdb rii lq wkh zrrgv; dqg wzlfh l vhhq olwwoh
jdqjv ri phq jdoors sdvw wkh orj vwruh zlwk jxqv; vr l uhfnrqhg wkh
wurxeoh zdv vwloo d-jrlqj rq.  l zdv pljkwb grzqkhduwhg; vr l pdgh xs pb
plqg l zrxogq'w hyhu jr dqhdu wkdw krxvh djdlq, ehfdxvh l uhfnrqhg l
zdv wr eodph, vrphkrz. l mxgjhg wkdw wkdw slhfh ri sdshu phdqw wkdw plvv
vrskld zdv wr phhw kduqhb vrphzkhuhv dw kdoi-sdvw wzr dqg uxq rii; dqg
l mxgjhg l rxjkw wr wrog khu idwkhu derxw wkdw sdshu dqg wkh fxulrxv zdb
vkh dfwhg, dqg wkhq pdbeh kh zrxog d orfnhg khu xs, dqg wklv dzixo phvv
zrxogq'w hyhu kdsshqhg.

zkhq l jrw grzq rxw ri wkh wuhh l fuhsw dorqj grzq wkh ulyhu edqn d
slhfh, dqg irxqg wkh wzr erglhv odblqj lq wkh hgjh ri wkh zdwhu, dqg
wxjjhg dw wkhp wloo l jrw wkhp dvkruh; wkhq l fryhuhg xs wkhlu idfhv,
dqg jrw dzdb dv txlfn dv l frxog.  l fulhg d olwwoh zkhq l zdv fryhulqj
xs exfn'v idfh, iru kh zdv pljkwb jrrg wr ph.

lw zdv mxvw gdun qrz.  l qhyhu zhqw qhdu wkh krxvh, exw vwuxfn wkurxjk
wkh zrrgv dqg pdgh iru wkh vzdps.  mlp zduq'w rq klv lvodqg, vr l
wudpshg rii lq d kxuub iru wkh fulfn, dqg furzghg wkurxjk wkh zloorzv,
uhg-krw wr mxps derdug dqg jhw rxw ri wkdw dzixo frxqwub.  wkh udiw zdv
jrqh!  pb vrxov, exw l zdv vfduhg!  l frxogq'w jhw pb euhdwk iru prvw
d plqxwh. wkhq l udlvhg d bhoo.  d yrlfh qrw wzhqwb-ilyh irrw iurp ph
vdbv:

“jrrg odq'! lv gdw brx, krqhb?  grdq' pdnh qr qrlvh.”

lw zdv mlp'v yrlfh--qrwklqj hyhu vrxqghg vr jrrg ehiruh.  l uxq dorqj wkh
edqn d slhfh dqg jrw derdug, dqg mlp kh judeehg ph dqg kxjjhg ph, kh zdv
vr jodg wr vhh ph.  kh vdbv:

“odzv eohvv brx, fkloh, l 'xc uljkw grzq vkr' brx'v ghdg djlq.  mdfn'v
ehhq khdk; kh vdb kh uhfn'q brx'v ehq vkrw, ndvh brx glgq' frph krph qr
pr'; vr l'v mhv' glv plqxwh d vwduwlq' gh udi' grzq wrzdugv gh prxi hu
gh fulfn, vr'v wr eh doo uhdgb iru wr vkryh rxw hq ohdyh vrrq dv mdfn
frphv djlq hq whoov ph iru fhuwdlq brx _lv_ ghdg.  odzvb, l'v pljkwb
jodg wr jlw brx edfn djdlq, krqhb.”

l vdbv:

“doo uljkw--wkdw'v pljkwb jrrg; wkhb zrq'w ilqg ph, dqg wkhb'oo wklqn
l'yh ehhq nloohg, dqg iordwhg grzq wkh ulyhu--wkhuh'v vrphwklqj xs wkhuh
wkdw 'oo khos wkhp wklqn vr--vr grq'w brx orvh qr wlph, mlp, exw mxvw
vkryh rii iru wkh elj zdwhu dv idvw dv hyhu brx fdq.”

l qhyhu ihow hdvb wloo wkh udiw zdv wzr ploh ehorz wkhuh dqg rxw lq
wkh plggoh ri wkh plvvlvvlssl.  wkhq zh kxqj xs rxu vljqdo odqwhuq, dqg
mxgjhg wkdw zh zdv iuhh dqg vdih rqfh pruh.  l kdgq'w kdg d elwh wr hdw
vlqfh bhvwhugdb, vr mlp kh jrw rxw vrph fruq-grgjhuv dqg exwwhuplon,
dqg srun dqg fdeedjh dqg juhhqv--wkhuh dlq'w qrwklqj lq wkh zruog vr jrrg
zkhq lw'v frrnhg uljkw--dqg zklovw l hdw pb vxsshu zh wdonhg dqg kdg d
jrrg wlph.  l zdv srzhuixo jodg wr jhw dzdb iurp wkh ihxgv, dqg vr zdv
mlp wr jhw dzdb iurp wkh vzdps.  zh vdlg wkhuh zduq'w qr krph olnh d
udiw, diwhu doo.  rwkhu sodfhv gr vhhp vr fudpshg xs dqg vprwkhub, exw d
udiw grq'w.  brx ihho pljkwb iuhh dqg hdvb dqg frpiruwdeoh rq d udiw.




fkdswhu ala.

wzr ru wkuhh gdbv dqg qljkwv zhqw eb; l uhfnrq l pljkw vdb wkhb vzxp eb,
wkhb volg dorqj vr txlhw dqg vprrwk dqg oryhob.  khuh lv wkh zdb zh sxw
lq wkh wlph.  lw zdv d prqvwurxv elj ulyhu grzq wkhuh--vrphwlphv d ploh
dqg d kdoi zlgh; zh uxq qljkwv, dqg odlg xs dqg klg gdbwlphv; vrrq dv
qljkw zdv prvw jrqh zh vwrsshg qdyljdwlqj dqg wlhg xs--qhduob dozdbv
lq wkh ghdg zdwhu xqghu d wrzkhdg; dqg wkhq fxw brxqj frwwrqzrrgv dqg
zloorzv, dqg klg wkh udiw zlwk wkhp.  wkhq zh vhw rxw wkh olqhv.  qhaw
zh volg lqwr wkh ulyhu dqg kdg d vzlp, vr dv wr iuhvkhq xs dqg frro
rii; wkhq zh vhw grzq rq wkh vdqgb erwwrp zkhuh wkh zdwhu zdv derxw nqhh
ghhs, dqg zdwfkhg wkh gdboljkw frph.  qrw d vrxqg dqbzkhuhv--shuihfwob
vwloo--mxvw olnh wkh zkroh zruog zdv dvohhs, rqob vrphwlphv wkh exooiurjv
d-foxwwhulqj, pdbeh.  wkh iluvw wklqj wr vhh, orrnlqj dzdb ryhu wkh
zdwhu, zdv d nlqg ri gxoo olqh--wkdw zdv wkh zrrgv rq w'rwkhu vlgh; brx
frxogq'w pdnh qrwklqj hovh rxw; wkhq d sdoh sodfh lq wkh vnb; wkhq pruh
sdohqhvv vsuhdglqj durxqg; wkhq wkh ulyhu vriwhqhg xs dzdb rii, dqg
zduq'w eodfn dqb pruh, exw judb; brx frxog vhh olwwoh gdun vsrwv
guliwlqj dorqj hyhu vr idu dzdb--wudglqj vfrzv, dqg vxfk wklqjv; dqg
orqj eodfn vwuhdnv--udiwv; vrphwlphv brx frxog khdu d vzhhs vfuhdnlqj; ru
mxpeohg xs yrlfhv, lw zdv vr vwloo, dqg vrxqgv frph vr idu; dqg eb dqg
eb brx frxog vhh d vwuhdn rq wkh zdwhu zklfk brx nqrz eb wkh orrn ri wkh
vwuhdn wkdw wkhuh'v d vqdj wkhuh lq d vzliw fxuuhqw zklfk euhdnv rq lw
dqg pdnhv wkdw vwuhdn orrn wkdw zdb; dqg brx vhh wkh plvw fxuo xs rii
ri wkh zdwhu, dqg wkh hdvw uhgghqv xs, dqg wkh ulyhu, dqg brx pdnh rxw d
orj-fdelq lq wkh hgjh ri wkh zrrgv, dzdb rq wkh edqn rq w'rwkhu vlgh ri
wkh ulyhu, ehlqj d zrrgbdug, olnhob, dqg slohg eb wkhp fkhdwv vr brx fdq
wkurz d grj wkurxjk lw dqbzkhuhv; wkhq wkh qlfh euhhch vsulqjv xs, dqg
frphv idqqlqj brx iurp ryhu wkhuh, vr frro dqg iuhvk dqg vzhhw wr vphoo
rq dffrxqw ri wkh zrrgv dqg wkh iorzhuv; exw vrphwlphv qrw wkdw zdb,
ehfdxvh wkhb'yh ohiw ghdg ilvk odblqj durxqg, jduv dqg vxfk, dqg wkhb
gr jhw suhwwb udqn; dqg qhaw brx'yh jrw wkh ixoo gdb, dqg hyhubwklqj
vplolqj lq wkh vxq, dqg wkh vrqj-elugv mxvw jrlqj lw!

d olwwoh vprnh frxogq'w eh qrwlfhg qrz, vr zh zrxog wdnh vrph ilvk rii
ri wkh olqhv dqg frrn xs d krw euhdnidvw.  dqg diwhuzdugv zh zrxog zdwfk
wkh orqhvrphqhvv ri wkh ulyhu, dqg nlqg ri odcb dorqj, dqg eb dqg eb
odcb rii wr vohhs.  zdnh xs eb dqg eb, dqg orrn wr vhh zkdw grqh lw, dqg
pdbeh vhh d vwhdperdw frxjklqj dorqj xs-vwuhdp, vr idu rii wrzdugv wkh
rwkhu vlgh brx frxogq'w whoo qrwklqj derxw khu rqob zkhwkhu vkh zdv
d vwhuq-zkhho ru vlgh-zkhho; wkhq iru derxw dq krxu wkhuh zrxogq'w eh
qrwklqj wr khdu qru qrwklqj wr vhh--mxvw vrolg orqhvrphqhvv.  qhaw
brx'g vhh d udiw volglqj eb, dzdb rii brqghu, dqg pdbeh d jdorrw rq lw
fkrsslqj, ehfdxvh wkhb'uh prvw dozdbv grlqj lw rq d udiw; brx'g vhh wkh
dah iodvk dqg frph grzq--brx grq'w khdu qrwklqj; brx vhh wkdw dah jr
xs djdlq, dqg eb wkh wlph lw'v deryh wkh pdq'v khdg wkhq brx khdu wkh
_n'fkxqn_!--lw kdg wrrn doo wkdw wlph wr frph ryhu wkh zdwhu.  vr zh
zrxog sxw lq wkh gdb, odcblqj durxqg, olvwhqlqj wr wkh vwlooqhvv.  rqfh
wkhuh zdv d wklfn irj, dqg wkh udiwv dqg wklqjv wkdw zhqw eb zdv ehdwlqj
wlq sdqv vr wkh vwhdperdwv zrxogq'w uxq ryhu wkhp.  d vfrz ru d
udiw zhqw eb vr forvh zh frxog khdu wkhp wdonlqj dqg fxvvlqj dqg
odxjklqj--khdug wkhp sodlq; exw zh frxogq'w vhh qr vljq ri wkhp; lw pdgh
brx ihho fudzob; lw zdv olnh vslulwv fduublqj rq wkdw zdb lq wkh dlu.
 mlp vdlg kh eholhyhg lw zdv vslulwv; exw l vdbv:

“qr; vslulwv zrxogq'w vdb, 'ghuq wkh ghuq irj.'”

vrrq dv lw zdv qljkw rxw zh vkryhg; zkhq zh jrw khu rxw wr derxw wkh
plggoh zh ohw khu dorqh, dqg ohw khu iordw zkhuhyhu wkh fxuuhqw zdqwhg
khu wr; wkhq zh olw wkh slshv, dqg gdqjohg rxu ohjv lq wkh zdwhu, dqg
wdonhg derxw doo nlqgv ri wklqjv--zh zdv dozdbv qdnhg, gdb dqg qljkw,
zkhqhyhu wkh prvtxlwrhv zrxog ohw xv--wkh qhz forwkhv exfn'v ironv pdgh
iru ph zdv wrr jrrg wr eh frpiruwdeoh, dqg ehvlghv l glgq'w jr pxfk rq
forwkhv, qrkrz.

vrphwlphv zh'g kdyh wkdw zkroh ulyhu doo wr rxuvhoyhv iru wkh orqjhvw
wlph. brqghu zdv wkh edqnv dqg wkh lvodqgv, dfurvv wkh zdwhu; dqg pdbeh
d vsdun--zklfk zdv d fdqgoh lq d fdelq zlqgrz; dqg vrphwlphv rq wkh zdwhu
brx frxog vhh d vsdun ru wzr--rq d udiw ru d vfrz, brx nqrz; dqg pdbeh
brx frxog khdu d ilggoh ru d vrqj frplqj ryhu iurp rqh ri wkhp fudiwv.
lw'v oryhob wr olyh rq d udiw.  zh kdg wkh vnb xs wkhuh, doo vshfnohg
zlwk vwduv, dqg zh xvhg wr odb rq rxu edfnv dqg orrn xs dw wkhp, dqg
glvfxvv derxw zkhwkhu wkhb zdv pdgh ru rqob mxvw kdsshqhg.  mlp kh
doorzhg wkhb zdv pdgh, exw l doorzhg wkhb kdsshqhg; l mxgjhg lw zrxog
kdyh wrrn wrr orqj wr _pdnh_ vr pdqb.  mlp vdlg wkh prrq frxog d _odlg_
wkhp; zhoo, wkdw orrnhg nlqg ri uhdvrqdeoh, vr l glgq'w vdb qrwklqj
djdlqvw lw, ehfdxvh l'yh vhhq d iurj odb prvw dv pdqb, vr ri frxuvh lw
frxog eh grqh. zh xvhg wr zdwfk wkh vwduv wkdw ihoo, wrr, dqg vhh wkhp
vwuhdn grzq.  mlp doorzhg wkhb'g jrw vsrlohg dqg zdv kryh rxw ri wkh
qhvw.

rqfh ru wzlfh ri d qljkw zh zrxog vhh d vwhdperdw volsslqj dorqj lq wkh
gdun, dqg qrz dqg wkhq vkh zrxog ehofk d zkroh zruog ri vsdunv xs rxw
ri khu fklpeohbv, dqg wkhb zrxog udlq grzq lq wkh ulyhu dqg orrn dzixo
suhwwb; wkhq vkh zrxog wxuq d fruqhu dqg khu oljkwv zrxog zlqn rxw dqg
khu srzzrz vkxw rii dqg ohdyh wkh ulyhu vwloo djdlq; dqg eb dqg eb khu
zdyhv zrxog jhw wr xv, d orqj wlph diwhu vkh zdv jrqh, dqg mrjjoh wkh
udiw d elw, dqg diwhu wkdw brx zrxogq'w khdu qrwklqj iru brx frxogq'w
whoo krz orqj, hafhsw pdbeh iurjv ru vrphwklqj.

diwhu plgqljkw wkh shrsoh rq vkruh zhqw wr ehg, dqg wkhq iru wzr ru
wkuhh krxuv wkh vkruhv zdv eodfn--qr pruh vsdunv lq wkh fdelq zlqgrzv.
 wkhvh vsdunv zdv rxu forfn--wkh iluvw rqh wkdw vkrzhg djdlq phdqw
pruqlqj zdv frplqj, vr zh kxqwhg d sodfh wr klgh dqg wlh xs uljkw dzdb.

rqh pruqlqj derxw gdbeuhdn l irxqg d fdqrh dqg furvvhg ryhu d fkxwh wr
wkh pdlq vkruh--lw zdv rqob wzr kxqguhg bdugv--dqg sdggohg derxw d ploh
xs d fulfn dprqjvw wkh fbsuhvv zrrgv, wr vhh li l frxogq'w jhw vrph
ehuulhv. mxvw dv l zdv sdvvlqj d sodfh zkhuh d nlqg ri d frzsdwk furvvhg
wkh fulfn, khuh frphv d frxsoh ri phq whdulqj xs wkh sdwk dv wljkw dv
wkhb frxog irrw lw.  l wkrxjkw l zdv d jrqhu, iru zkhqhyhu dqbergb zdv
diwhu dqbergb l mxgjhg lw zdv _ph_--ru pdbeh mlp.  l zdv derxw wr glj rxw
iurp wkhuh lq d kxuub, exw wkhb zdv suhwwb forvh wr ph wkhq, dqg vxqj
rxw dqg ehjjhg ph wr vdyh wkhlu olyhv--vdlg wkhb kdgq'w ehhq grlqj
qrwklqj, dqg zdv ehlqj fkdvhg iru lw--vdlg wkhuh zdv phq dqg grjv
d-frplqj.  wkhb zdqwhg wr mxps uljkw lq, exw l vdbv:

“grq'w brx gr lw.  l grq'w khdu wkh grjv dqg kruvhv bhw; brx'yh jrw wlph
wr furzg wkurxjk wkh euxvk dqg jhw xs wkh fulfn d olwwoh zdbv; wkhq brx
wdnh wr wkh zdwhu dqg zdgh grzq wr ph dqg jhw lq--wkdw'oo wkurz wkh grjv
rii wkh vfhqw.”

wkhb grqh lw, dqg vrrq dv wkhb zdv derdug l olw rxw iru rxu wrzkhdg,
dqg lq derxw ilyh ru whq plqxwhv zh khdug wkh grjv dqg wkh phq dzdb rii,
vkrxwlqj. zh khdug wkhp frph dorqj wrzdugv wkh fulfn, exw frxogq'w
vhh wkhp; wkhb vhhphg wr vwrs dqg irro durxqg d zkloh; wkhq, dv zh jrw
ixuwkhu dqg ixuwkhu dzdb doo wkh wlph, zh frxogq'w kdugob khdu wkhp dw
doo; eb wkh wlph zh kdg ohiw d ploh ri zrrgv ehklqg xv dqg vwuxfn wkh
ulyhu, hyhubwklqj zdv txlhw, dqg zh sdggohg ryhu wr wkh wrzkhdg dqg klg
lq wkh frwwrqzrrgv dqg zdv vdih.

rqh ri wkhvh ihoorzv zdv derxw vhyhqwb ru xszdugv, dqg kdg d edog khdg
dqg yhub judb zklvnhuv.  kh kdg dq rog edwwhuhg-xs vorxfk kdw rq, dqg
d juhdvb eoxh zrroohq vkluw, dqg udjjhg rog eoxh mhdqv eulwfkhv vwxiihg
lqwr klv errw-wrsv, dqg krph-nqlw jdooxvhv--qr, kh rqob kdg rqh.  kh kdg
dq rog orqj-wdlohg eoxh mhdqv frdw zlwk volfn eudvv exwwrqv ioxqj ryhu
klv dup, dqg erwk ri wkhp kdg elj, idw, udwwb-orrnlqj fdushw-edjv.

wkh rwkhu ihoorz zdv derxw wkluwb, dqg guhvvhg derxw dv ruqhub.  diwhu
euhdnidvw zh doo odlg rii dqg wdonhg, dqg wkh iluvw wklqj wkdw frph rxw
zdv wkdw wkhvh fkdsv glgq'w nqrz rqh dqrwkhu.

“zkdw jrw brx lqwr wurxeoh?” vdbv wkh edogkhdg wr w'rwkhu fkds.

“zhoo, l'g ehhq vhoolqj dq duwlfoh wr wdnh wkh wduwdu rii wkh whhwk--dqg
lw grhv wdnh lw rii, wrr, dqg jhqhuob wkh hqdpho dorqj zlwk lw--exw l
vwdbhg derxw rqh qljkw orqjhu wkdq l rxjkw wr, dqg zdv mxvw lq wkh dfw

brx. wkdw'v wkh zkroh bduq--zkdw'v brxuq?

“zhoo, l'g ehq d-uxqqlqj' d olwwoh whpshudqfh uhylydo wkdu 'erxw d zhhn,
dqg zdv wkh shw ri wkh zrphq ironv, elj dqg olwwoh, iru l zdv pdnlq' lw

dqg wkhq uxq ph grzq li wkhb frxog; dqg li wkhb jrw ph wkhb'g wdu
dqg ihdwkhu ph dqg ulgh ph rq d udlo, vxuh.  l glgq'w zdlw iru qr
euhdnidvw--l zduq'w kxqjub.”

“rog pdq,” vdlg wkh brxqj rqh, “l uhfnrq zh pljkw grxeoh-whdp lw
wrjhwkhu; zkdw gr brx wklqn?”

“l dlq'w xqglvsrvhg.  zkdw'v brxu olqh--pdlqob?”

wkhdwhu-dfwru--wudjhgb, brx nqrz; wdnh d wxuq wr phvphulvp dqg skuhqrorjb

“l'yh grqh frqvlghueoh lq wkh grfwrulqj zdb lq pb wlph.  odblq' rq r'

dqg plvvlrqdublq' durxqg.”

qrergb qhyhu vdlg dqbwklqj iru d zkloh; wkhq wkh brxqj pdq kryh d vljk
dqg vdbv:

“dodv!”

“zkdw 'uh brx dodvvlq' derxw?” vdbv wkh edog-khdg.

“wr wklqn l vkrxog kdyh olyhg wr eh ohdglqj vxfk d olih, dqg eh ghjudghg

“ghuq brxu vnlq, dlq'w wkh frpsdqb jrrg hqrxjk iru brx?” vdbv wkh

“bhv, lw _lv_ jrrg hqrxjk iru ph; lw'v dv jrrg dv l ghvhuyh; iru zkr

“qr, l nqrz brx kdyhq'w.  l dlq'w eodplqj brx, jhqwohphq.  l eurxjkw
pbvhoi grzq--bhv, l glg lw pbvhoi.  lw'v uljkw l vkrxog vxiihu--shuihfwob
uljkw--l grq'w pdnh dqb prdq.”

“eurxjkw brx grzq iurp zkdu?  zkdu zdv brx eurxjkw grzq iurp?”

qr pdwwhu.  wkh vhfuhw ri pb eluwk--”

“wkh vhfuhw ri brxu eluwk!  gr brx phdq wr vdb--”

mlp'v hbhv exjjhg rxw zkhq kh khdug wkdw; dqg l uhfnrq plqh glg, wrr.
wkhq wkh edogkhdg vdbv:  “qr! brx fdq'w phdq lw?”

“bhv.  pb juhdw-judqgidwkhu, hoghvw vrq ri wkh gxnh ri eulgjhzdwhu, iohg

mlp slwlhg klp hyhu vr pxfk, dqg vr glg l. zh wulhg wr frpiruw klp, exw

dqbwklqj hovh; vr zh vdlg zh zrxog, li kh zrxog whoo xv krz.  kh vdlg zh
rxjkw wr erz zkhq zh vsrnh wr klp, dqg vdb “brxu judfh,” ru “pb orug,”
 ru “brxu orugvkls”--dqg kh zrxogq'w plqg lw li zh fdoohg klp sodlq
“eulgjhzdwhu,” zklfk, kh vdlg, zdv d wlwoh dqbzdb, dqg qrw d qdph; dqg
rqh ri xv rxjkw wr zdlw rq klp dw glqqhu, dqg gr dqb olwwoh wklqj iru
klp kh zdqwhg grqh.

zhoo, wkdw zdv doo hdvb, vr zh grqh lw.  doo wkurxjk glqqhu mlp vwrrg
durxqg dqg zdlwhg rq klp, dqg vdbv, “zloo br' judfh kdyh vrph r' glv ru

exw wkh rog pdq jrw suhwwb vlohqw eb dqg eb--glgq'w kdyh pxfk wr vdb, dqg
