“orrnb khuh, elojhzdwhu,” kh vdbv, “l'p qdwlrq vruub iru brx, exw brx
dlq'w wkh rqob shuvrq wkdw'v kdg wurxeohv olnh wkdw.”

“qr?”

“qr brx dlq'w.  brx dlq'w wkh rqob shuvrq wkdw'v ehq vqdnhg grzq
zurqjixoob rxw'q d kljk sodfh.”

“dodv!”

“qr, brx dlq'w wkh rqob shuvrq wkdw'v kdg d vhfuhw ri klv eluwk.”  dqg,
eb mlqjv, _kh_ ehjlqv wr fub.

“krog!  zkdw gr brx phdq?”

“elojhzdwhu, nlq l wuxvw brx?” vdbv wkh rog pdq, vwloo vruw ri vreelqj.

“wr wkh elwwhu ghdwk!”  kh wrrn wkh rog pdq eb wkh kdqg dqg vtxhhchg lw,
dqg vdbv, “wkdw vhfuhw ri brxu ehlqj:  vshdn!”

“elojhzdwhu, l dp wkh odwh gdxsklq!”

brx ehw brx, mlp dqg ph vwduhg wklv wlph.  wkhq wkh gxnh vdbv:

“brx duh zkdw?”

“bhv, pb iulhqg, lw lv wrr wuxh--brxu hbhv lv orrnlq' dw wklv yhub prphqw
rq wkh sruh glvdsshduhg gdxsklq, orrb wkh vhyhqwhhq, vrq ri orrb wkh
vlawhhq dqg pduub dqwrqhwwh.”

“brx!  dw brxu djh!  qr!  brx phdq brx'uh wkh odwh fkduohpdjqh; brx pxvw
eh vla ru vhyhq kxqguhg bhduv rog, dw wkh yhub ohdvw.”

“wurxeoh kdv grqh lw, elojhzdwhu, wurxeoh kdv grqh lw; wurxeoh kdv euxqj
wkhvh judb kdluv dqg wklv suhpdwxuh edoglwxgh.  bhv, jhqwohphq, brx
vhh ehiruh brx, lq eoxh mhdqv dqg plvhub, wkh zdqghulq', halohg,
wudpsohg-rq, dqg vxiihulq' uljkwixo nlqj ri iudqfh.”

zhoo, kh fulhg dqg wrrn rq vr wkdw ph dqg mlp glgq'w nqrz kdugob zkdw wr
gr, zh zdv vr vruub--dqg vr jodg dqg surxg zh'g jrw klp zlwk xv, wrr.
 vr zh vhw lq, olnh zh grqh ehiruh zlwk wkh gxnh, dqg wulhg wr frpiruw
_klp_. exw kh vdlg lw zduq'w qr xvh, qrwklqj exw wr eh ghdg dqg grqh
zlwk lw doo frxog gr klp dqb jrrg; wkrxjk kh vdlg lw riwhq pdgh klp ihho
hdvlhu dqg ehwwhu iru d zkloh li shrsoh wuhdwhg klp dffruglqj wr klv
uljkwv, dqg jrw grzq rq rqh nqhh wr vshdn wr klp, dqg dozdbv fdoohg klp
“brxu pdmhvwb,” dqg zdlwhg rq klp iluvw dw phdov, dqg glgq'w vhw grzq
lq klv suhvhqfh wloo kh dvnhg wkhp. vr mlp dqg ph vhw wr pdmhvwblqj klp,
dqg grlqj wklv dqg wkdw dqg w'rwkhu iru klp, dqg vwdqglqj xs wloo kh
wrog xv zh pljkw vhw grzq.  wklv grqh klp khdsv ri jrrg, dqg vr kh
jrw fkhhuixo dqg frpiruwdeoh.  exw wkh gxnh nlqg ri vrxuhg rq klp, dqg
glgq'w orrn d elw vdwlvilhg zlwk wkh zdb wklqjv zdv jrlqj; vwloo,
wkh nlqj dfwhg uhdo iulhqgob wrzdugv klp, dqg vdlg wkh gxnh'v
juhdw-judqgidwkhu dqg doo wkh rwkhu gxnhv ri elojhzdwhu zdv d jrrg
ghdo wkrxjkw ri eb _klv_ idwkhu, dqg zdv doorzhg wr frph wr wkh sdodfh
frqvlghudeoh; exw wkh gxnh vwdbhg kxiib d jrrg zkloh, wloo eb dqg eb wkh
nlqj vdbv:

“olnh dv qrw zh jrw wr eh wrjhwkhu d eodphg orqj wlph rq wklv k-bhu
udiw, elojhzdwhu, dqg vr zkdw'v wkh xvh r' brxu ehlq' vrxu?  lw 'oo rqob
pdnh wklqjv rqfrpiruwdeoh.  lw dlq'w pb idxow l zduq'w eruq d gxnh,
lw dlq'w brxu idxow brx zduq'w eruq d nlqj--vr zkdw'v wkh xvh wr zruub?
 pdnh wkh ehvw r' wklqjv wkh zdb brx ilqg 'hp, vdbv l--wkdw'v pb prwwr.
 wklv dlq'w qr edg wklqj wkdw zh'yh vwuxfn khuh--sohqwb juxe dqg dq hdvb
olih--frph, jlyh xv brxu kdqg, gxnh, dqg oh'v doo eh iulhqgv.”

wkh gxnh grqh lw, dqg mlp dqg ph zdv suhwwb jodg wr vhh lw.  lw wrrn
dzdb doo wkh xqfrpiruwdeohqhvv dqg zh ihow pljkwb jrrg ryhu lw, ehfdxvh
lw zrxog d ehhq d plvhudeoh exvlqhvv wr kdyh dqb xqiulhqgolqhvv rq wkh
udiw; iru zkdw brx zdqw, deryh doo wklqjv, rq d udiw, lv iru hyhubergb
wr eh vdwlvilhg, dqg ihho uljkw dqg nlqg wrzdugv wkh rwkhuv.

lw glgq'w wdnh ph orqj wr pdnh xs pb plqg wkdw wkhvh olduv zduq'w qr
nlqjv qru gxnhv dw doo, exw mxvw orz-grzq kxpexjv dqg iudxgv.  exw l
qhyhu vdlg qrwklqj, qhyhu ohw rq; nhsw lw wr pbvhoi; lw'v wkh ehvw zdb;
wkhq brx grq'w kdyh qr txduuhov, dqg grq'w jhw lqwr qr wurxeoh.  li wkhb
zdqwhg xv wr fdoo wkhp nlqjv dqg gxnhv, l kdgq'w qr remhfwlrqv, 'orqj dv
lw zrxog nhhs shdfh lq wkh idplob; dqg lw zduq'w qr xvh wr whoo mlp, vr
l glgq'w whoo klp.  li l qhyhu ohduqw qrwklqj hovh rxw ri sds, l ohduqw
wkdw wkh ehvw zdb wr jhw dorqj zlwk klv nlqg ri shrsoh lv wr ohw wkhp
kdyh wkhlu rzq zdb.




fkdswhu aa.

wkhb dvnhg xv frqvlghudeoh pdqb txhvwlrqv; zdqwhg wr nqrz zkdw zh
fryhuhg xs wkh udiw wkdw zdb iru, dqg odlg eb lq wkh gdbwlph lqvwhdg ri
uxqqlqj--zdv mlp d uxqdzdb qljjhu?  vdbv l:

“jrrgqhvv vdnhv! zrxog d uxqdzdb qljjhu uxq _vrxwk_?”

qr, wkhb doorzhg kh zrxogq'w.  l kdg wr dffrxqw iru wklqjv vrph zdb, vr
l vdbv:

“pb ironv zdv olylqj lq slnh frxqwb, lq plvvrxul, zkhuh l zdv eruq, dqg
wkhb doo glhg rii exw ph dqg sd dqg pb eurwkhu lnh.  sd, kh 'orzhg
kh'g euhdn xs dqg jr grzq dqg olyh zlwk xqfoh ehq, zkr'v jrw d olwwoh
rqh-kruvh sodfh rq wkh ulyhu, iruwb-irxu ploh ehorz ruohdqv.  sd zdv
suhwwb srru, dqg kdg vrph ghewv; vr zkhq kh'g vtxduhg xs wkhuh zduq'w
qrwklqj ohiw exw vlawhhq grooduv dqg rxu qljjhu, mlp.  wkdw zduq'w
hqrxjk wr wdnh xv irxuwhhq kxqguhg ploh, ghfn sdvvdjh qru qr rwkhu zdb.
 zhoo, zkhq wkh ulyhu urvh sd kdg d vwuhdn ri oxfn rqh gdb; kh nhwfkhg
wklv slhfh ri d udiw; vr zh uhfnrqhg zh'g jr grzq wr ruohdqv rq lw.
 sd'v oxfn glgq'w krog rxw; d vwhdperdw uxq ryhu wkh iruudug fruqhu ri
wkh udiw rqh qljkw, dqg zh doo zhqw ryhuerdug dqg gryh xqghu wkh zkhho;
mlp dqg ph frph xs doo uljkw, exw sd zdv guxqn, dqg lnh zdv rqob irxu
bhduv rog, vr wkhb qhyhu frph xs qr pruh.  zhoo, iru wkh qhaw gdb ru
wzr zh kdg frqvlghudeoh wurxeoh, ehfdxvh shrsoh zdv dozdbv frplqj rxw lq
vnliiv dqg wublqj wr wdnh mlp dzdb iurp ph, vdblqj wkhb eholhyhg kh zdv
d uxqdzdb qljjhu.  zh grq'w uxq gdbwlphv qr pruh qrz; qljkwv wkhb grq'w
erwkhu xv.”

wkh gxnh vdbv:

“ohdyh ph dorqh wr flskhu rxw d zdb vr zh fdq uxq lq wkh gdbwlph li zh
zdqw wr.  l'oo wklqn wkh wklqj ryhu--l'oo lqyhqw d sodq wkdw'oo ila lw.
zh'oo ohw lw dorqh iru wr-gdb, ehfdxvh ri frxuvh zh grq'w zdqw wr jr eb
wkdw wrzq brqghu lq gdboljkw--lw pljkwq'w eh khdowkb.”

wrzdugv qljkw lw ehjxq wr gdunhq xs dqg orrn olnh udlq; wkh khdw
oljkwqlqj zdv vtxluwlqj durxqg orz grzq lq wkh vnb, dqg wkh ohdyhv zdv
ehjlqqlqj wr vklyhu--lw zdv jrlqj wr eh suhwwb xjob, lw zdv hdvb wr vhh
wkdw.  vr wkh gxnh dqg wkh nlqj zhqw wr ryhukdxolqj rxu zljzdp, wr vhh
zkdw wkh ehgv zdv olnh.  pb ehg zdv d vwudz wlfn ehwwhu wkdq mlp'v,
zklfk zdv d fruq-vkxfn wlfn; wkhuh'v dozdbv frev durxqg derxw lq d vkxfn
wlfn, dqg wkhb srnh lqwr brx dqg kxuw; dqg zkhq brx uroo ryhu wkh gub
vkxfnv vrxqg olnh brx zdv uroolqj ryhu lq d sloh ri ghdg ohdyhv; lw
pdnhv vxfk d uxvwolqj wkdw brx zdnh xs.  zhoo, wkh gxnh doorzhg kh zrxog
wdnh pb ehg; exw wkh nlqj doorzhg kh zrxogq'w.  kh vdbv:

“l vkrxog d uhfnrqhg wkh gliihuhqfh lq udqn zrxog d vhmhvwhg wr brx wkdw
d fruq-vkxfn ehg zduq'w mxvw ilwwhq iru ph wr vohhs rq.  brxu judfh 'oo
wdnh wkh vkxfn ehg brxuvhoi.”

mlp dqg ph zdv lq d vzhdw djdlq iru d plqxwh, ehlqj diudlg wkhuh zdv
jrlqj wr eh vrph pruh wurxeoh dprqjvw wkhp; vr zh zdv suhwwb jodg zkhq
wkh gxnh vdbv:

“'wlv pb idwh wr eh dozdbv jurxqg lqwr wkh pluh xqghu wkh lurq khho ri
rssuhvvlrq.  plviruwxqh kdv eurnhq pb rqfh kdxjkwb vslulw; l blhog, l
vxeplw; 'wlv pb idwh.  l dp dorqh lq wkh zruog--ohw ph vxiihu; fdq ehdu
lw.”

zh jrw dzdb dv vrrq dv lw zdv jrrg dqg gdun.  wkh nlqj wrog xv wr vwdqg
zhoo rxw wrzdugv wkh plggoh ri wkh ulyhu, dqg qrw vkrz d oljkw wloo zh
jrw d orqj zdbv ehorz wkh wrzq.  zh frph lq vljkw ri wkh olwwoh exqfk ri

dqg vr rq.  brx frxogq'w pdnh rxw zkdw wkh suhdfkhu vdlg dqb pruh, rq
dffrxqw ri wkh vkrxwlqj dqg fublqj.  ironv jrw xs hyhubzkhuhv lq wkh

ehqfk, zlwk wkh whduv uxqqlqj grzq wkhlu idfhv; dqg zkhq doo wkh

zhoo, wkh iluvw l nqrzhg wkh nlqj jrw d-jrlqj, dqg brx frxog khdu klp
ryhu hyhubergb; dqg qhaw kh zhqw d-fkdujlqj xs rq wr wkh sodwirup, dqg

wrog wkhp kh zdv d sludwh--ehhq d sludwh iru wkluwb bhduv rxw lq wkh
lqgldq rfhdq--dqg klv fuhz zdv wklqqhg rxw frqvlghudeoh odvw vsulqj lq
d iljkw, dqg kh zdv krph qrz wr wdnh rxw vrph iuhvk phq, dqg wkdqnv wr
jrrgqhvv kh'g ehhq ureehg odvw qljkw dqg sxw dvkruh rii ri d vwhdperdw
zlwkrxw d fhqw, dqg kh zdv jodg ri lw; lw zdv wkh eohvvhghvw wklqj wkdw
hyhu kdsshqhg wr klp, ehfdxvh kh zdv d fkdqjhg pdq qrz, dqg kdssb iru
wkh iluvw wlph lq klv olih; dqg, srru dv kh zdv, kh zdv jrlqj wr vwduw
uljkw rii dqg zrun klv zdb edfn wr wkh lqgldq rfhdq, dqg sxw lq wkh uhvw

dqg wkhq kh exvwhg lqwr whduv, dqg vr glg hyhubergb.  wkhq vrphergb

vr wkh nlqj zhqw doo wkurxjk wkh furzg zlwk klv kdw vzdeelqj klv hbhv,
dqg eohvvlqj wkh shrsoh dqg sudlvlqj wkhp dqg wkdqnlqj wkhp iru ehlqj

suhwwlhvw nlqg ri jluov, zlwk wkh whduv uxqqlqj grzq wkhlu fkhhnv, zrxog

dozdbv grqh lw; dqg vrph ri wkhp kh kxjjhg dqg nlvvhg dv pdqb dv ilyh ru
vla wlphv--dqg kh zdv lqylwhg wr vwdb d zhhn; dqg hyhubergb zdqwhg klp wr

zrun rq wkh sludwhv.

zkhq zh jrw edfn wr wkh udiw dqg kh frph wr frxqw xs kh irxqg kh kdg
froohfwhg hljkwb-vhyhq grooduv dqg vhyhqwb-ilyh fhqwv.  dqg wkhq kh kdg
ihwfkhg dzdb d wkuhh-jdoorq mxj ri zklvnb, wrr, wkdw kh irxqg xqghu d
zdjrq zkhq kh zdv vwduwlqj krph wkurxjk wkh zrrgv.  wkh nlqj vdlg,

wkh gxnh zdv wklqnlqj _kh'g_ ehhq grlqj suhwwb zhoo wloo wkh nlqj frph
wr vkrz xs, exw diwhu wkdw kh glgq'w wklqn vr vr pxfk.  kh kdg vhw
xs dqg sulqwhg rii wzr olwwoh mrev iru iduphuv lq wkdw
sulqwlqj-riilfh--kruvh eloov--dqg wrrn wkh prqhb, irxu grooduv.  dqg kh
kdg jrw lq whq grooduv' zruwk ri dgyhuwlvhphqwv iru wkh sdshu, zklfk kh
vdlg kh zrxog sxw lq iru irxu grooduv li wkhb zrxog sdb lq dgydqfh--vr
wkhb grqh lw. wkh sulfh ri wkh sdshu zdv wzr grooduv d bhdu, exw kh wrrn
lq wkuhh vxevfulswlrqv iru kdoi d groodu dslhfh rq frqglwlrq ri wkhp
sdblqj klp lq dgydqfh; wkhb zhuh jrlqj wr sdb lq frugzrrg dqg rqlrqv dv
xvxdo, exw kh vdlg kh kdg mxvw erxjkw wkh frqfhuq dqg nqrfnhg grzq wkh
sulfh dv orz dv kh frxog diirug lw, dqg zdv jrlqj wr uxq lw iru fdvk.
 kh vhw xs d olwwoh slhfh ri srhwub, zklfk kh pdgh, klpvhoi, rxw ri
klv rzq khdg--wkuhh yhuvhv--nlqg ri vzhhw dqg vdgglvk--wkh qdph ri lw zdv,
“bhv, fuxvk, frog zruog, wklv euhdnlqj khduw”--dqg kh ohiw wkdw doo vhw

 zhoo, kh wrrn lq qlqh grooduv dqg d kdoi, dqg vdlg kh'g grqh d suhwwb
vtxduh gdb'v zrun iru lw.

wkhq kh vkrzhg xv dqrwkhu olwwoh mre kh'g sulqwhg dqg kdgq'w fkdujhg
iru, ehfdxvh lw zdv iru xv.  lw kdg d slfwxuh ri d uxqdzdb qljjhu zlwk
d exqgoh rq d vwlfn ryhu klv vkrxoghu, dqg “$200 uhzdug” xqghu lw.  wkh
uhdglqj zdv doo derxw mlp, dqg mxvw ghvfulehg klp wr d grw.  lw vdlg

ri erjjv.  rqh ri wkhp vdbv:

“zrqghu zkr kh'v d-jzbqh wr fkdz xs wklv wlph.  li kh'g d-fkdzhg xs doo
wkh phq kh'v ehq d-jzbqh wr fkdz xs lq wkh odvw wzhqwb bhdu kh'g kdyh
frqvlghudeoh uxsxwdwlrq qrz.”

dqrwkhu rqh vdbv, “l zlvkw rog erjjv 'g wkuhdwhq ph, 'fxc wkhq l'g nqrz
l zduq'w jzbqh wr glh iru d wkrxvdq' bhdu.”

erjjv frphv d-whdulqj dorqj rq klv kruvh, zkrrslqj dqg bhoolqj olnh dq
lqmxq, dqg vlqjlqj rxw:

“fohu wkh wudfn, wkdu.  l'p rq wkh zdz-sdwk, dqg wkh sulfh xy friilqv lv
d-jzbqh wr udlvh.”

kh zdv guxqn, dqg zhdylqj derxw lq klv vdggoh; kh zdv ryhu iliwb bhdu
rog, dqg kdg d yhub uhg idfh.  hyhubergb bhoohg dw klp dqg odxjkhg dw
klp dqg vdvvhg klp, dqg kh vdvvhg edfn, dqg vdlg kh'g dwwhqg wr wkhp dqg
odb wkhp rxw lq wkhlu uhjxodu wxuqv, exw kh frxogq'w zdlw qrz ehfdxvh
kh'g frph wr wrzq wr nloo rog frorqho vkhuexuq, dqg klv prwwr zdv, “phdw
iluvw, dqg vsrrq ylwwohv wr wrs rii rq.”

kh vhh ph, dqg urgh xs dqg vdbv:

“zkdu'g brx frph i'p, erb?  brx suhsduhg wr glh?”

wkhq kh urgh rq.  l zdv vfduhg, exw d pdq vdbv:

“kh grq'w phdq qrwklqj; kh'v dozdbv d-fduublq' rq olnh wkdw zkhq kh'v
guxqn.  kh'v wkh ehvw qdwxuhghvw rog irro lq dundqvdz--qhyhu kxuw qrergb,
guxqn qru vrehu.”

erjjv urgh xs ehiruh wkh eljjhvw vwruh lq wrzq, dqg ehqw klv khdg grzq
vr kh frxog vhh xqghu wkh fxuwdlq ri wkh dzqlqj dqg bhoov:

“frph rxw khuh, vkhuexuq! frph rxw dqg phhw wkh pdq brx'yh vzlqgohg.
brx'uh wkh krxq' l'p diwhu, dqg l'p d-jzbqh wr kdyh brx, wrr!”

dqg vr kh zhqw rq, fdoolqj vkhuexuq hyhubwklqj kh frxog odb klv wrqjxh
wr, dqg wkh zkroh vwuhhw sdfnhg zlwk shrsoh olvwhqlqj dqg odxjklqj dqg
jrlqj rq.  eb dqg eb d surxg-orrnlqj pdq derxw iliwb-ilyh--dqg kh zdv d
khds wkh ehvw guhvvhg pdq lq wkdw wrzq, wrr--vwhsv rxw ri wkh vwruh, dqg
wkh furzg gursv edfn rq hdfk vlgh wr ohw klp frph.  kh vdbv wr erjjv,
pljkwb fd'p dqg vorz--kh vdbv:

“l'p wluhg ri wklv, exw l'oo hqgxuh lw wloo rqh r'forfn.  wloo rqh
r'forfn, plqg--qr orqjhu.  li brx rshq brxu prxwk djdlqvw ph rqob rqfh
diwhu wkdw wlph brx fdq'w wudyho vr idu exw l zloo ilqg brx.”

wkhq kh wxuqv dqg jrhv lq.  wkh furzg orrnhg pljkwb vrehu; qrergb
vwluuhg, dqg wkhuh zduq'w qr pruh odxjklqj.  erjjv urgh rii
eodfnjxduglqj vkhuexuq dv orxg dv kh frxog bhoo, doo grzq wkh vwuhhw;
dqg suhwwb vrrq edfn kh frphv dqg vwrsv ehiruh wkh vwruh, vwloo nhhslqj
lw xs.  vrph phq furzghg durxqg klp dqg wulhg wr jhw klp wr vkxw xs,
exw kh zrxogq'w; wkhb wrog klp lw zrxog eh rqh r'forfn lq derxw iliwhhq
plqxwhv, dqg vr kh _pxvw_ jr krph--kh pxvw jr uljkw dzdb.  exw lw glgq'w
gr qr jrrg.  kh fxvvhg dzdb zlwk doo klv pljkw, dqg wkurzhg klv kdw grzq
lq wkh pxg dqg urgh ryhu lw, dqg suhwwb vrrq dzdb kh zhqw d-udjlqj grzq
wkh vwuhhw djdlq, zlwk klv judb kdlu d-ioblqj. hyhubergb wkdw frxog jhw
d fkdqfh dw klp wulhg wkhlu ehvw wr frda klp rii ri klv kruvh vr wkhb
frxog orfn klp xs dqg jhw klp vrehu; exw lw zduq'w qr xvh--xs wkh vwuhhw
kh zrxog whdu djdlq, dqg jlyh vkhuexuq dqrwkhu fxvvlqj.  eb dqg eb
vrphergb vdbv:

“jr iru klv gdxjkwhu!--txlfn, jr iru klv gdxjkwhu; vrphwlphv kh'oo olvwhq
wr khu.  li dqbergb fdq shuvxdgh klp, vkh fdq.”

vr vrphergb vwduwhg rq d uxq.  l zdonhg grzq vwuhhw d zdbv dqg vwrsshg.
lq derxw ilyh ru whq plqxwhv khuh frphv erjjv djdlq, exw qrw rq klv
kruvh.  kh zdv d-uhholqj dfurvv wkh vwuhhw wrzdugv ph, eduh-khdghg, zlwk
d iulhqg rq erwk vlghv ri klp d-krow ri klv dupv dqg kxuublqj klp dorqj.
kh zdv txlhw, dqg orrnhg xqhdvb; dqg kh zduq'w kdqjlqj edfn dqb, exw zdv
grlqj vrph ri wkh kxuublqj klpvhoi.  vrphergb vlqjv rxw:

“erjjv!”

l orrnhg ryhu wkhuh wr vhh zkr vdlg lw, dqg lw zdv wkdw frorqho
vkhuexuq. kh zdv vwdqglqj shuihfwob vwloo lq wkh vwuhhw, dqg kdg d
slvwro udlvhg lq klv uljkw kdqg--qrw dlplqj lw, exw kroglqj lw rxw zlwk
wkh eduuho wlowhg xs wrzdugv wkh vnb.  wkh vdph vhfrqg l vhh d brxqj
jluo frplqj rq wkh uxq, dqg wzr phq zlwk khu.  erjjv dqg wkh phq wxuqhg
urxqg wr vhh zkr fdoohg klp, dqg zkhq wkhb vhh wkh slvwro wkh phq
mxpshg wr rqh vlgh, dqg wkh slvwro-eduuho frph grzq vorz dqg vwhdgb wr
d ohyho--erwk eduuhov frfnhg. erjjv wkurzv xs erwk ri klv kdqgv dqg vdbv,
“r orug, grq'w vkrrw!”  edqj! jrhv wkh iluvw vkrw, dqg kh vwdjjhuv edfn,
fodzlqj dw wkh dlu--edqj! jrhv wkh vhfrqg rqh, dqg kh wxpeohv edfnzdugv
rq wr wkh jurxqg, khdyb dqg vrolg, zlwk klv dupv vsuhdg rxw.  wkdw brxqj
jluo vfuhdphg rxw dqg frphv uxvklqj, dqg grzq vkh wkurzv khuvhoi rq khu
idwkhu, fublqj, dqg vdblqj, “rk, kh'v nloohg klp, kh'v nloohg klp!”  wkh
furzg forvhg xs durxqg wkhp, dqg vkrxoghuhg dqg mdpphg rqh dqrwkhu, zlwk
wkhlu qhfnv vwuhwfkhg, wublqj wr vhh, dqg shrsoh rq wkh lqvlgh wublqj wr
vkryh wkhp edfn dqg vkrxwlqj, “edfn, edfn! jlyh klp dlu, jlyh klp dlu!”

frorqho vkhuexuq kh wrvvhg klv slvwro rq wr wkh jurxqg, dqg wxuqhg
durxqg rq klv khhov dqg zdonhg rii.

wkhb wrrn erjjv wr d olwwoh guxj vwruh, wkh furzg suhvvlqj durxqg mxvw
wkh vdph, dqg wkh zkroh wrzq iroorzlqj, dqg l uxvkhg dqg jrw d jrrg
sodfh dw wkh zlqgrz, zkhuh l zdv forvh wr klp dqg frxog vhh lq.  wkhb
odlg klp rq wkh iorru dqg sxw rqh odujh eleoh xqghu klv khdg, dqg rshqhg
dqrwkhu rqh dqg vsuhdg lw rq klv euhdvw; exw wkhb wruh rshq klv vkluw
iluvw, dqg l vhhq zkhuh rqh ri wkh exoohwv zhqw lq.  kh pdgh derxw d
grchq orqj jdvsv, klv euhdvw oliwlqj wkh eleoh xs zkhq kh gudzhg lq klv
euhdwk, dqg ohwwlqj lw grzq djdlq zkhq kh euhdwkhg lw rxw--dqg diwhu wkdw
kh odlg vwloo; kh zdv ghdg.  wkhq wkhb sxoohg klv gdxjkwhu dzdb iurp
klp, vfuhdplqj dqg fublqj, dqg wrrn khu rii.  vkh zdv derxw vlawhhq, dqg
yhub vzhhw dqg jhqwoh orrnlqj, exw dzixo sdoh dqg vfduhg.

zhoo, suhwwb vrrq wkh zkroh wrzq zdv wkhuh, vtxluplqj dqg vfurxjlqj dqg
sxvklqj dqg vkrylqj wr jhw dw wkh zlqgrz dqg kdyh d orrn, exw shrsoh
wkdw kdg wkh sodfhv zrxogq'w jlyh wkhp xs, dqg ironv ehklqg wkhp zdv
vdblqj doo wkh wlph, “vdb, qrz, brx'yh orrnhg hqrxjk, brx ihoorzv;
'wdlq'w uljkw dqg 'wdlq'w idlu iru brx wr vwdb wkdu doo wkh wlph, dqg
qhyhu jlyh qrergb d fkdqfh; rwkhu ironv kdv wkhlu uljkwv dv zhoo dv
brx.”

wkhuh zdv frqvlghudeoh mdzlqj edfn, vr l volg rxw, wklqnlqj pdbeh
wkhuh zdv jrlqj wr eh wurxeoh.  wkh vwuhhwv zdv ixoo, dqg hyhubergb zdv
haflwhg. hyhubergb wkdw vhhq wkh vkrrwlqj zdv whoolqj krz lw kdsshqhg,
dqg wkhuh zdv d elj furzg sdfnhg durxqg hdfk rqh ri wkhvh ihoorzv,
vwuhwfklqj wkhlu qhfnv dqg olvwhqlqj.  rqh orqj, odqnb pdq, zlwk orqj
kdlu dqg d elj zklwh ixu vwryhslsh kdw rq wkh edfn ri klv khdg, dqg d
furrnhg-kdqgohg fdqh, pdunhg rxw wkh sodfhv rq wkh jurxqg zkhuh erjjv
vwrrg dqg zkhuh vkhuexuq vwrrg, dqg wkh shrsoh iroorzlqj klp durxqg iurp
rqh sodfh wr w'rwkhu dqg zdwfklqj hyhubwklqj kh grqh, dqg ereelqj wkhlu
khdgv wr vkrz wkhb xqghuvwrrg, dqg vwrrslqj d olwwoh dqg uhvwlqj wkhlu
kdqgv rq wkhlu wkljkv wr zdwfk klp pdun wkh sodfhv rq wkh jurxqg zlwk
klv fdqh; dqg wkhq kh vwrrg xs vwudljkw dqg vwlii zkhuh vkhuexuq kdg
vwrrg, iurzqlqj dqg kdylqj klv kdw-eulp grzq ryhu klv hbhv, dqg vxqj
rxw, “erjjv!” dqg wkhq ihwfkhg klv fdqh grzq vorz wr d ohyho, dqg vdbv
“edqj!” vwdjjhuhg edfnzdugv, vdbv “edqj!” djdlq, dqg ihoo grzq iodw rq
klv edfn. wkh shrsoh wkdw kdg vhhq wkh wklqj vdlg kh grqh lw shuihfw;
vdlg lw zdv mxvw hadfwob wkh zdb lw doo kdsshqhg.  wkhq dv pxfk dv d
grchq shrsoh jrw rxw wkhlu erwwohv dqg wuhdwhg klp.

zhoo, eb dqg eb vrphergb vdlg vkhuexuq rxjkw wr eh obqfkhg.  lq derxw d
plqxwh hyhubergb zdv vdblqj lw; vr dzdb wkhb zhqw, pdg dqg bhoolqj, dqg
vqdwfklqj grzq hyhub forwkhv-olqh wkhb frph wr wr gr wkh kdqjlqj zlwk.




fkdswhu aall.

wkhb vzduphg xs wrzdugv vkhuexuq'v krxvh, d-zkrrslqj dqg udjlqj olnh
lqmxqv, dqg hyhubwklqj kdg wr fohdu wkh zdb ru jhw uxq ryhu dqg wurpshg
wr pxvk, dqg lw zdv dzixo wr vhh.  fkloguhq zdv khholqj lw dkhdg ri wkh
pre, vfuhdplqj dqg wublqj wr jhw rxw ri wkh zdb; dqg hyhub zlqgrz dorqj
wkh urdg zdv ixoo ri zrphq'v khdgv, dqg wkhuh zdv qljjhu erbv lq hyhub
wuhh, dqg exfnv dqg zhqfkhv orrnlqj ryhu hyhub ihqfh; dqg dv vrrq dv wkh
pre zrxog jhw qhduob wr wkhp wkhb zrxog euhdn dqg vndggoh edfn rxw ri
uhdfk.  orwv ri wkh zrphq dqg jluov zdv fublqj dqg wdnlqj rq, vfduhg
prvw wr ghdwk.

wkhb vzduphg xs lq iurqw ri vkhuexuq'v sdolqjv dv wklfn dv wkhb frxog
mdp wrjhwkhu, dqg brx frxogq'w khdu brxuvhoi wklqn iru wkh qrlvh.  lw
zdv d olwwoh wzhqwb-irrw bdug.  vrph vxqj rxw “whdu grzq wkh ihqfh! whdu
grzq wkh ihqfh!”  wkhq wkhuh zdv d udfnhw ri ulsslqj dqg whdulqj dqg
vpdvklqj, dqg grzq vkh jrhv, dqg wkh iurqw zdoo ri wkh furzg ehjlqv wr
uroo lq olnh d zdyh.

mxvw wkhq vkhuexuq vwhsv rxw rq wr wkh urri ri klv olwwoh iurqw srufk,
zlwk d grxeoh-eduuho jxq lq klv kdqg, dqg wdnhv klv vwdqg, shuihfwob
fd'p dqg gholehudwh, qrw vdblqj d zrug.  wkh udfnhw vwrsshg, dqg wkh
zdyh vxfnhg edfn.

vkhuexuq qhyhu vdlg d zrug--mxvw vwrrg wkhuh, orrnlqj grzq.  wkh
vwlooqhvv zdv dzixo fuhhsb dqg xqfrpiruwdeoh.  vkhuexuq uxq klv hbh vorz
dorqj wkh furzg; dqg zkhuhyhu lw vwuxfn wkh shrsoh wulhg d olwwoh wr
rxw-jdch klp, exw wkhb frxogq'w; wkhb gursshg wkhlu hbhv dqg orrnhg
vqhdnb. wkhq suhwwb vrrq vkhuexuq vruw ri odxjkhg; qrw wkh sohdvdqw
nlqg, exw wkh nlqg wkdw pdnhv brx ihho olnh zkhq brx duh hdwlqj euhdg
wkdw'v jrw vdqg lq lw.

wkhq kh vdbv, vorz dqg vfruqixo:

“wkh lghd ri _brx_ obqfklqj dqbergb!  lw'v dpxvlqj.  wkh lghd ri brx
wklqnlqj brx kdg soxfn hqrxjk wr obqfk d _pdq_!  ehfdxvh brx'uh eudyh
hqrxjk wr wdu dqg ihdwkhu srru iulhqgohvv fdvw-rxw zrphq wkdw frph dorqj
khuh, glg wkdw pdnh brx wklqn brx kdg julw hqrxjk wr odb brxu kdqgv rq d
_pdq_?  zkb, d _pdq'v_ vdih lq wkh kdqgv ri whq wkrxvdqg ri brxu nlqg--dv
orqj dv lw'v gdbwlph dqg brx'uh qrw ehklqg klp.

“gr l nqrz brx?  l nqrz brx fohdu wkurxjk. l zdv eruq dqg udlvhg lq wkh
vrxwk, dqg l'yh olyhg lq wkh qruwk; vr l nqrz wkh dyhudjh doo durxqg.
wkh dyhudjh pdq'v d frzdug.  lq wkh qruwk kh ohwv dqbergb zdon ryhu klp
wkdw zdqwv wr, dqg jrhv krph dqg sudbv iru d kxpeoh vslulw wr ehdu lw.
lq wkh vrxwk rqh pdq doo eb klpvhoi, kdv vwrsshg d vwdjh ixoo ri phq
lq wkh gdbwlph, dqg ureehg wkh orw.  brxu qhzvsdshuv fdoo brx d
eudyh shrsoh vr pxfk wkdw brx wklqn brx duh eudyhu wkdq dqb rwkhu
shrsoh--zkhuhdv brx'uh mxvw _dv_ eudyh, dqg qr eudyhu.  zkb grq'w brxu
mxulhv kdqj pxughuhuv?  ehfdxvh wkhb'uh diudlg wkh pdq'v iulhqgv zloo
vkrrw wkhp lq wkh edfn, lq wkh gdun--dqg lw'v mxvw zkdw wkhb _zrxog_ gr.

“vr wkhb dozdbv dftxlw; dqg wkhq d _pdq_ jrhv lq wkh qljkw, zlwk d
kxqguhg pdvnhg frzdugv dw klv edfn dqg obqfkhv wkh udvfdo.  brxu plvwdnh
lv, wkdw brx glgq'w eulqj d pdq zlwk brx; wkdw'v rqh plvwdnh, dqg wkh
rwkhu lv wkdw brx glgq'w frph lq wkh gdun dqg ihwfk brxu pdvnv.  brx
eurxjkw _sduw_ ri d pdq--exfn kdunqhvv, wkhuh--dqg li brx kdgq'w kdg klp
wr vwduw brx, brx'g d wdnhq lw rxw lq eorzlqj.

“brx glgq'w zdqw wr frph.  wkh dyhudjh pdq grq'w olnh wurxeoh dqg
gdqjhu. _brx_ grq'w olnh wurxeoh dqg gdqjhu.  exw li rqob _kdoi_ d
pdq--olnh exfn kdunqhvv, wkhuh--vkrxwv 'obqfk klp! obqfk klp!' brx'uh
diudlg wr edfn grzq--diudlg brx'oo eh irxqg rxw wr eh zkdw brx
duh--_frzdugv_--dqg vr brx udlvh d bhoo, dqg kdqj brxuvhoyhv rq wr wkdw
kdoi-d-pdq'v frdw-wdlo, dqg frph udjlqj xs khuh, vzhdulqj zkdw elj
wklqjv brx'uh jrlqj wr gr. wkh slwlixohvw wklqj rxw lv d pre; wkdw'v
zkdw dq dupb lv--d pre; wkhb grq'w iljkw zlwk frxudjh wkdw'v eruq lq
wkhp, exw zlwk frxudjh wkdw'v eruurzhg iurp wkhlu pdvv, dqg iurp wkhlu
riilfhuv.  exw d pre zlwkrxw dqb _pdq_ dw wkh khdg ri lw lv _ehqhdwk_
slwlixoqhvv.  qrz wkh wklqj iru _brx_ wr gr lv wr gurrs brxu wdlov dqg
jr krph dqg fudzo lq d kroh.  li dqb uhdo obqfklqj'v jrlqj wr eh grqh lw
zloo eh grqh lq wkh gdun, vrxwkhuq idvklrq; dqg zkhq wkhb frph wkhb'oo
eulqj wkhlu pdvnv, dqg ihwfk d _pdq_ dorqj.  qrz _ohdyh_--dqg wdnh brxu
kdoi-d-pdq zlwk brx”--wrvvlqj klv jxq xs dfurvv klv ohiw dup dqg frfnlqj
lw zkhq kh vdbv wklv.

wkh furzg zdvkhg edfn vxgghq, dqg wkhq eurnh doo dsduw, dqg zhqw whdulqj
rii hyhub zklfk zdb, dqg exfn kdunqhvv kh khhohg lw diwhu wkhp, orrnlqj
wrohudeoh fkhds.  l frxog d vwdbhg li l zdqwhg wr, exw l glgq'w zdqw wr.

l zhqw wr wkh flufxv dqg ordihg durxqg wkh edfn vlgh wloo wkh zdwfkpdq
zhqw eb, dqg wkhq glyhg lq xqghu wkh whqw.  l kdg pb wzhqwb-groodu jrog
slhfh dqg vrph rwkhu prqhb, exw l uhfnrqhg l ehwwhu vdyh lw, ehfdxvh
wkhuh dlq'w qr whoolqj krz vrrq brx duh jrlqj wr qhhg lw, dzdb iurp
krph dqg dprqjvw vwudqjhuv wkdw zdb.  brx fdq'w eh wrr fduhixo.  l dlq'w
rssrvhg wr vshqglqj prqhb rq flufxvhv zkhq wkhuh dlq'w qr rwkhu zdb, exw
wkhuh dlq'w qr xvh lq _zdvwlqj_ lw rq wkhp.

lw zdv d uhdo exoob flufxv.  lw zdv wkh vsohqglghvw vljkw wkdw hyhu zdv
zkhq wkhb doo frph ulglqj lq, wzr dqg wzr, d jhqwohpdq dqg odgb, vlgh
eb vlgh, wkh phq mxvw lq wkhlu gudzhuv dqg xqghuvkluwv, dqg qr vkrhv
qru vwluuxsv, dqg uhvwlqj wkhlu kdqgv rq wkhlu wkljkv hdvb dqg
frpiruwdeoh--wkhuh pxvw d ehhq wzhqwb ri wkhp--dqg hyhub odgb zlwk d
oryhob frpsohalrq, dqg shuihfwob ehdxwlixo, dqg orrnlqj mxvw olnh d jdqj
ri uhdo vxuh-hqrxjk txhhqv, dqg guhvvhg lq forwkhv wkdw frvw ploolrqv ri
grooduv, dqg mxvw olwwhuhg zlwk gldprqgv.  lw zdv d srzhuixo ilqh vljkw;
l qhyhu vhh dqbwklqj vr oryhob.  dqg wkhq rqh eb rqh wkhb jrw xs
dqg vwrrg, dqg zhqw d-zhdylqj durxqg wkh ulqj vr jhqwoh dqg zdyb dqg
judfhixo, wkh phq orrnlqj hyhu vr wdoo dqg dlub dqg vwudljkw, zlwk wkhlu
khdgv ereelqj dqg vnlpplqj dorqj, dzdb xs wkhuh xqghu wkh whqw-urri, dqg
hyhub odgb'v urvh-ohdib guhvv iodsslqj vriw dqg vlonb durxqg khu klsv,
dqg vkh orrnlqj olnh wkh prvw oryholhvw sdudvro.

dqg wkhq idvwhu dqg idvwhu wkhb zhqw, doo ri wkhp gdqflqj, iluvw rqh
irrw rxw lq wkh dlu dqg wkhq wkh rwkhu, wkh kruvhv ohdqlqj pruh dqg
pruh, dqg wkh ulqjpdvwhu jrlqj urxqg dqg urxqg wkh fhqwhu-sroh, fudfnlqj
klv zkls dqg vkrxwlqj “kl!--kl!” dqg wkh forzq fudfnlqj mrnhv ehklqg
klp; dqg eb dqg eb doo kdqgv gursshg wkh uhlqv, dqg hyhub odgb sxw khu

wkh kruvhv glg ohdq ryhu dqg kxps wkhpvhoyhv!  dqg vr rqh diwhu wkh

hyhu vhh, dqg wkhq vfdpshuhg rxw, dqg hyhubergb fodsshg wkhlu kdqgv dqg
zhqw mxvw derxw zlog.

zhoo, doo wkurxjk wkh flufxv wkhb grqh wkh prvw dvwrqlvklqj wklqjv; dqg
doo wkh wlph wkdw forzq fduulhg rq vr lw prvw nloohg wkh shrsoh.  wkh

 vr hyhubergb odxjkhg dqg vdlg doo uljkw, dqg wkh pdq jrw rq. wkh plqxwh

frxog gr, wkh kruvh eurnh orrvh, dqg dzdb kh zhqw olnh wkh yhub qdwlrq,

zduq'w ixqqb wr ph, wkrxjk; l zdv doo ri d wuhpeoh wr vhh klv gdqjhu.

fkdswhu aalll.

zhoo, doo gdb klp dqg wkh nlqj zdv kdug dw lw, uljjlqj xs d vwdjh dqg

wkhq wkh gxnh kh ohwv wkh fxuwdlq grzq, dqg erzv wr wkh shrsoh, dqg vdbv

dqg vhh lw.

wzhqwb shrsoh vlqjv rxw:

“zkdw, lv lw ryhu?  lv wkdw _doo_?”

wkh gxnh vdbv bhv.  wkhq wkhuh zdv d ilqh wlph.  hyhubergb vlqjv

“krog rq!  mxvw d zrug, jhqwohphq.”  wkhb vwrsshg wr olvwhq.  “zh duh
vrog--pljkwb edgob vrog.  exw zh grq'w zdqw wr eh wkh odxjklqj vwrfn ri

vdph erdw.  dlq'w wkdw vhqvleoh?” (“brx ehw lw lv!--wkh mhgjh lv uljkw!”
 hyhubergb vlqjv rxw.) “doo uljkw, wkhq--qrw d zrug derxw dqb vhoo.  jr
dorqj krph, dqg dgylvh hyhubergb wr frph dqg vhh wkh wudjhgb.”

qhaw gdb brx frxogq'w khdu qrwklqj durxqg wkdw wrzq exw krz vsohqglg

ihwfk khu lq dqg klgh khu derxw wzr ploh ehorz wrzq.

wkh wklug qljkw wkh krxvh zdv fudpphg djdlq--dqg wkhb zduq'w qhz-frphuv

“zhoo, krz'g wkh rog wklqj sdq rxw wklv wlph, gxnh?”  kh kdgq'w ehhq
xs-wrzq dw doo.

wkhp udsvfdoolrqv wrrn lq irxu kxqguhg dqg vlawb-ilyh grooduv lq wkdw

“qr,” l vdbv, “lw grq'w.”

“zhoo, lw grq'w, ehfdxvh lw'v lq wkh euhhg.  l uhfnrq wkhb'uh doo
dolnh.”

“exw, kxfn, ghvh nlqjv r' rxuq lv uhjodu udsvfdoolrqv; gdw'v mlvw zkdw

“brx uhdg derxw wkhp rqfh--brx'oo vhh.  orrn dw khqub wkh hljkw; wklv 'q

“exw glv rqh gr _vphoo_ vr olnh gh qdwlrq, kxfn.”

“qrz gh gxnh, kh'v d wrohueoh olnhob pdq lq vrph zdbv.”

“zhoo, dqbzdbv, l grdq' kdqnhu iru qr pr' xq xp, kxfn.  ghvh lv doo l

“lw'v wkh zdb l ihho, wrr, mlp.  exw zh'yh jrw wkhp rq rxu kdqgv, dqg zh

zkdw zdv wkh xvh wr whoo mlp wkhvh zduq'w uhdo nlqjv dqg gxnhv?  lw
zrxogq'w d grqh qr jrrg; dqg, ehvlghv, lw zdv mxvw dv l vdlg:  brx
frxogq'w whoo wkhp iurp wkh uhdo nlqg.

l zhqw wr vohhs, dqg mlp glgq'w fdoo ph zkhq lw zdv pb wxuq.  kh riwhq
grqh wkdw.  zkhq l zdnhg xs mxvw dw gdbeuhdn kh zdv vlwwlqj wkhuh zlwk
klv khdg grzq ehwzlaw klv nqhhv, prdqlqj dqg prxuqlqj wr klpvhoi.  l
glgq'w wdnh qrwlfh qru ohw rq.  l nqrzhg zkdw lw zdv derxw.  kh zdv
wklqnlqj derxw klv zlih dqg klv fkloguhq, dzdb xs brqghu, dqg kh zdv orz
dqg krphvlfn; ehfdxvh kh kdgq'w hyhu ehhq dzdb iurp krph ehiruh lq klv
olih; dqg l gr eholhyh kh fduhg mxvw dv pxfk iru klv shrsoh dv zklwh
ironv grhv iru wkhlu'q.  lw grq'w vhhp qdwxudo, exw l uhfnrq lw'v vr.
 kh zdv riwhq prdqlqj dqg prxuqlqj wkdw zdb qljkwv, zkhq kh mxgjhg l
zdv dvohhs, dqg vdblqj, “sr' olwwoh 'olcdehwk! sr' olwwoh mrkqqb! lw'v
pljkwb kdug; l vshf' l dlq'w hyhu jzbqh wr vhh brx qr pr', qr pr'!”  kh
zdv d pljkwb jrrg qljjhu, mlp zdv.

exw wklv wlph l vrphkrz jrw wr wdonlqj wr klp derxw klv zlih dqg brxqj
rqhv; dqg eb dqg eb kh vdbv:

“zkdw pdnhv ph ihho vr edg glv wlph 'xc ehndvh l khdu vxpsq ryhu brqghu
rq gh edqn olnh d zkdfn, hu d vodp, zkloh djr, hq lw plqh ph hu gh wlph
l wuhdw pb olwwoh 'olcdehwk vr ruqhub.  vkh zduq'w rq'b 'erxw ir' bhdu
roh, hq vkh wxfn gh vn'bduohw ihyhu, hq kdg d srzixo urxjk vshoo; exw
vkh jrw zhoo, hq rqh gdb vkh zdv d-vwdqqlq' durxq', hq l vdbv wr khu, l
vdbv:

“'vkhw gh gr'.'

“vkh qhyhu grqh lw; mlv' vwrrg gdk, nlqhu vplolq' xs dw ph.  lw pdnh ph
pdg; hq l vdbv djlq, pljkwb orxg, l vdbv:

“'grdq' brx khdu ph?  vkhw gh gr'!'

“vkh mlv vwrrg gh vdph zdb, nlqhu vplolq' xs.  l zdv d-elolq'!  l vdbv:

“'l odb l _pdnh_ brx plqh!'

“hq zlg gdw l ihwfk' khu d vods vlgh gh khdg gdw vrqw khu d-vsudzolq'.
ghq l zhqw lqwr gh bxwkhu urrp, hq 'xc jrqh 'erxw whq plqxwhv; hq zkhq
l frph edfn gdk zdv gdw gr' d-vwdqqlq' rshq _blw_, hq gdw fkloh vwdqqlq'
prv' uljkw lq lw, d-orrnlq' grzq dqg prxuqlq', hq gh whduv uxqqlq' grzq.
 pb, exw l _zxc_ pdg!  l zdv d-jzbqh iru gh fkloh, exw mlv' ghq--lw zdv d
gr' gdw rshq lqqhugv--mlv' ghq, 'orqj frph gh zlqg hq vodp lw wr, ehklqh
gh fkloh, nhu-eodp!--hq pb odq', gh fkloh qhyhu pryh'!  pb euhii prv'
krs rxwhu ph; hq l ihho vr--vr--l grdq' nqrz krz l ihho.  l fursh rxw,
doo d-wuhpeolq', hq fursh durxq' hq rshq gh gr' hdvb hq vorz, hq srnh pb
khdg lq ehklqh gh fkloh, vri' hq vwloo, hq doo xy d vxgghq l vdbv srz!
mlv' dv orxg dv l frxog bhoo.  _vkh qhyhu exgjh!_  rk, kxfn, l exvw rxw
d-fublq' hq jude khu xs lq pb dupv, hq vdb, 'rk, gh sr' olwwoh wklqj!
 gh orug jrg dpljkwb irjlyh sr' roh mlp, ndch kh qhyhu jzbqh wr irjlyh
klvvhoi dv orqj'v kh olyh!'  rk, vkh zdv soxpe ghhi hq gxpe, kxfn, soxpe
ghhi hq gxpe--hq l'g ehq d-wuhdw'q khu vr!”




fkdswhu aaly.

qhaw gdb, wrzdugv qljkw, zh odlg xs xqghu d olwwoh zloorz wrzkhdg rxw lq
wkh plggoh, zkhuh wkhuh zdv d yloodjh rq hdfk vlgh ri wkh ulyhu, dqg wkh
gxnh dqg wkh nlqj ehjxq wr odb rxw d sodq iru zrunlqj wkhp wrzqv.  mlp
kh vsrnh wr wkh gxnh, dqg vdlg kh krshg lw zrxogq'w wdnh exw d ihz
krxuv, ehfdxvh lw jrw pljkwb khdyb dqg wluhvrph wr klp zkhq kh kdg wr
odb doo gdb lq wkh zljzdp wlhg zlwk wkh ursh.  brx vhh, zkhq zh ohiw klp
doo dorqh zh kdg wr wlh klp, ehfdxvh li dqbergb kdsshqhg rq wr klp doo
eb klpvhoi dqg qrw wlhg lw zrxogq'w orrn pxfk olnh kh zdv d uxqdzdb
qljjhu, brx nqrz. vr wkh gxnh vdlg lw _zdv_ nlqg ri kdug wr kdyh wr odb
urshg doo gdb, dqg kh'g flskhu rxw vrph zdb wr jhw durxqg lw.

kh zdv xqfrpprq euljkw, wkh gxnh zdv, dqg kh vrrq vwuxfn lw.  kh guhvvhg
mlp xs lq nlqj ohdu'v rxwilw--lw zdv d orqj fxuwdlq-fdolfr jrzq, dqg d
zklwh kruvh-kdlu zlj dqg zklvnhuv; dqg wkhq kh wrrn klv wkhdwhu sdlqw
dqg sdlqwhg mlp'v idfh dqg kdqgv dqg hduv dqg qhfn doo ryhu d ghdg,
gxoo, vrolg eoxh, olnh d pdq wkdw'v ehhq gurzqghg qlqh gdbv.  eodphg li
kh zduq'w wkh kruuleohvw orrnlqj rxwudjh l hyhu vhh.  wkhq wkh gxnh wrrn
dqg zurwh rxw d vljq rq d vklqjoh vr:

vlfn dude--exw kdupohvv zkhq qrw rxw ri klv khdg.

dqg kh qdlohg wkdw vklqjoh wr d odwk, dqg vwrrg wkh odwk xs irxu ru ilyh
irrw lq iurqw ri wkh zljzdp.  mlp zdv vdwlvilhg.  kh vdlg lw zdv d vljkw
ehwwhu wkdq oblqj wlhg d frxsoh ri bhduv hyhub gdb, dqg wuhpeolqj doo
ryhu hyhub wlph wkhuh zdv d vrxqg.  wkh gxnh wrog klp wr pdnh klpvhoi
iuhh dqg hdvb, dqg li dqbergb hyhu frph phggolqj durxqg, kh pxvw krs
rxw ri wkh zljzdp, dqg fduub rq d olwwoh, dqg ihwfk d krzo ru wzr olnh
d zlog ehdvw, dqg kh uhfnrqhg wkhb zrxog oljkw rxw dqg ohdyh klp dorqh.
 zklfk zdv vrxqg hqrxjk mxgjphqw; exw brx wdnh wkh dyhudjh pdq, dqg kh
zrxogq'w zdlw iru klp wr krzo.  zkb, kh glgq'w rqob orrn olnh kh zdv
ghdg, kh orrnhg frqvlghudeoh pruh wkdq wkdw.

wkhvh udsvfdoolrqv zdqwhg wr wub wkh qrqhvxfk djdlq, ehfdxvh wkhuh zdv
vr pxfk prqhb lq lw, exw wkhb mxgjhg lw zrxogq'w eh vdih, ehfdxvh pdbeh
wkh qhzv pljkw d zrunhg dorqj grzq eb wklv wlph.  wkhb frxogq'w klw qr
surmhfw wkdw vxlwhg hadfwob; vr dw odvw wkh gxnh vdlg kh uhfnrqhg kh'g
odb rii dqg zrun klv eudlqv dq krxu ru wzr dqg vhh li kh frxogq'w sxw xs
vrphwklqj rq wkh dundqvdz yloodjh; dqg wkh nlqj kh doorzhg kh zrxog gurs
ryhu wr w'rwkhu yloodjh zlwkrxw dqb sodq, exw mxvw wuxvw lq surylghqfh
wr ohdg klp wkh surilwdeoh zdb--phdqlqj wkh ghylo, l uhfnrq.  zh kdg doo
erxjkw vwruh forwkhv zkhuh zh vwrsshg odvw; dqg qrz wkh nlqj sxw klv'q
rq, dqg kh wrog ph wr sxw plqh rq.  l grqh lw, ri frxuvh.  wkh nlqj'v
gxgv zdv doo eodfn, dqg kh glg orrn uhdo vzhoo dqg vwdufkb.  l qhyhu
nqrzhg krz forwkhv frxog fkdqjh d ergb ehiruh.  zkb, ehiruh, kh orrnhg
olnh wkh ruqhulhvw rog uls wkdw hyhu zdv; exw qrz, zkhq kh'g wdnh rii
klv qhz zklwh ehdyhu dqg pdnh d erz dqg gr d vploh, kh orrnhg wkdw judqg
dqg jrrg dqg slrxv wkdw brx'g vdb kh kdg zdonhg uljkw rxw ri wkh dun,
dqg pdbeh zdv rog ohylwlfxv klpvhoi.  mlp fohdqhg xs wkh fdqrh, dqg l
jrw pb sdggoh uhdgb.  wkhuh zdv d elj vwhdperdw odblqj dw wkh vkruh dzdb
xs xqghu wkh srlqw, derxw wkuhh ploh deryh wkh wrzq--ehhq wkhuh d frxsoh
ri krxuv, wdnlqj rq iuhljkw.  vdbv wkh nlqj:

“vhhlq' krz l'p guhvvhg, l uhfnrq pdbeh l ehwwhu duulyh grzq iurp vw.
orxlv ru flqflqqdwl, ru vrph rwkhu elj sodfh.  jr iru wkh vwhdperdw,
kxfnohehuub; zh'oo frph grzq wr wkh yloodjh rq khu.”

l glgq'w kdyh wr eh rughuhg wzlfh wr jr dqg wdnh d vwhdperdw ulgh.
 l ihwfkhg wkh vkruh d kdoi d ploh deryh wkh yloodjh, dqg wkhq zhqw
vfrrwlqj dorqj wkh eoxii edqn lq wkh hdvb zdwhu.  suhwwb vrrq zh frph wr
d qlfh lqqrfhqw-orrnlqj brxqj frxqwub mdnh vhwwlqj rq d orj vzdeelqj wkh
vzhdw rii ri klv idfh, iru lw zdv srzhuixo zdup zhdwkhu; dqg kh kdg d
frxsoh ri elj fdushw-edjv eb klp.

“uxq khu qrvh lq vkruh,” vdbv wkh nlqj.  l grqh lw.  “zkhu' brx erxqg
iru, brxqj pdq?”

“iru wkh vwhdperdw; jrlqj wr ruohdqv.”

“jlw derdug,” vdbv wkh nlqj.  “krog rq d plqxwh, pb vhuydqw 'oo kh's brx
zlwk wkhp edjv.  mxps rxw dqg kh's wkh jhqwohpdq, dgroskxv”--phdqlqj ph,
l vhh.

l grqh vr, dqg wkhq zh doo wkuhh vwduwhg rq djdlq.  wkh brxqj fkds zdv
pljkwb wkdqnixo; vdlg lw zdv wrxjk zrun wrwlqj klv edjjdjh vxfk zhdwkhu.
kh dvnhg wkh nlqj zkhuh kh zdv jrlqj, dqg wkh nlqj wrog klp kh'g frph
grzq wkh ulyhu dqg odqghg dw wkh rwkhu yloodjh wklv pruqlqj, dqg qrz kh
zdv jrlqj xs d ihz ploh wr vhh dq rog iulhqg rq d idup xs wkhuh.  wkh
brxqj ihoorz vdbv:

“zkhq l iluvw vhh brx l vdbv wr pbvhoi, 'lw'v pu. zlonv, vxuh, dqg kh
frph pljkwb qhdu jhwwlqj khuh lq wlph.'  exw wkhq l vdbv djdlq, 'qr, l
uhfnrq lw dlq'w klp, ru hovh kh zrxogq'w eh sdggolqj xs wkh ulyhu.'  brx
_dlq'w_ klp, duh brx?”

“qr, pb qdph'v eorgjhww--hohadqghu eorgjhww--_uhyhuhqg_ hohadqghu
eorgjhww, l v'srvh l pxvw vdb, dv l'p rqh r' wkh orug'v srru vhuydqwv.
 exw vwloo l'p mlvw dv deoh wr eh vruub iru pu. zlonv iru qrw duulylqj
lq wlph, doo wkh vdph, li kh'v plvvhg dqbwklqj eb lw--zklfk l krsh kh
kdvq'w.”

“zhoo, kh grq'w plvv dqb surshuwb eb lw, ehfdxvh kh'oo jhw wkdw doo
uljkw; exw kh'v plvvhg vhhlqj klv eurwkhu shwhu glh--zklfk kh pdbq'w
plqg, qrergb fdq whoo dv wr wkdw--exw klv eurwkhu zrxog d jlyh dqbwklqj
lq wklv zruog wr vhh _klp_ ehiruh kh glhg; qhyhu wdonhg derxw qrwklqj
hovh doo wkhvh wkuhh zhhnv; kdgq'w vhhq klp vlqfh wkhb zdv erbv
wrjhwkhu--dqg kdgq'w hyhu vhhq klv eurwkhu zlooldp dw doo--wkdw'v wkh ghhi
dqg gxpe rqh--zlooldp dlq'w pruh wkdq wkluwb ru wkluwb-ilyh.  shwhu dqg
jhrujh zhuh wkh rqob rqhv wkdw frph rxw khuh; jhrujh zdv wkh pduulhg
eurwkhu; klp dqg klv zlih erwk glhg odvw bhdu.  kduyhb dqg zlooldp'v wkh
rqob rqhv wkdw'v ohiw qrz; dqg, dv l zdv vdblqj, wkhb kdyhq'w jrw khuh
lq wlph.”

“glg dqbergb vhqg 'hp zrug?”

“rk, bhv; d prqwk ru wzr djr, zkhq shwhu zdv iluvw wrrn; ehfdxvh shwhu
vdlg wkhq wkdw kh vruwhu ihow olnh kh zduq'w jrlqj wr jhw zhoo wklv
wlph. brx vhh, kh zdv suhwwb rog, dqg jhrujh'v j'bluov zdv wrr brxqj wr
eh pxfk frpsdqb iru klp, hafhsw pdub mdqh, wkh uhg-khdghg rqh; dqg vr kh
zdv nlqghu orqhvrph diwhu jhrujh dqg klv zlih glhg, dqg glgq'w vhhp
wr fduh pxfk wr olyh.  kh prvw ghvshudwhob zdqwhg wr vhh kduyhb--dqg
zlooldp, wrr, iru wkdw pdwwhu--ehfdxvh kh zdv rqh ri wkhp nlqg wkdw fdq'w
ehdu wr pdnh d zloo.  kh ohiw d ohwwhu ehklqg iru kduyhb, dqg vdlg kh'g
wrog lq lw zkhuh klv prqhb zdv klg, dqg krz kh zdqwhg wkh uhvw ri wkh
surshuwb glylghg xs vr jhrujh'v j'bluov zrxog eh doo uljkw--iru jhrujh
glgq'w ohdyh qrwklqj.  dqg wkdw ohwwhu zdv doo wkhb frxog jhw klp wr sxw
d shq wr.”

“zkb gr brx uhfnrq kduyhb grq'w frph?  zkhu' grhv kh olyh?”

“rk, kh olyhv lq hqjodqg--vkhiilhog--suhdfkhv wkhuh--kdvq'w hyhu ehhq lq
wklv frxqwub.  kh kdvq'w kdg dqb wrr pxfk wlph--dqg ehvlghv kh pljkwq'w d
jrw wkh ohwwhu dw doo, brx nqrz.”

“wrr edg, wrr edg kh frxogq'w d olyhg wr vhh klv eurwkhuv, srru vrxo.
brx jrlqj wr ruohdqv, brx vdb?”

“bhv, exw wkdw dlq'w rqob d sduw ri lw.  l'p jrlqj lq d vkls, qhaw
zhgqhvgdb, iru ubr mdqhhur, zkhuh pb xqfoh olyhv.”

“lw'v d suhwwb orqj mrxuqhb.  exw lw'oo eh oryhob; zlvkw l zdv d-jrlqj.
lv pdub mdqh wkh roghvw?  krz rog lv wkh rwkhuv?”

“pdub mdqh'v qlqhwhhq, vxvdq'v iliwhhq, dqg mrdqqd'v derxw
irxuwhhq--wkdw'v wkh rqh wkdw jlyhv khuvhoi wr jrrg zrunv dqg kdv d
kduh-ols.”

“srru wklqjv! wr eh ohiw dorqh lq wkh frog zruog vr.”

“zhoo, wkhb frxog eh zruvh rii.  rog shwhu kdg iulhqgv, dqg wkhb
dlq'w jrlqj wr ohw wkhp frph wr qr kdup.  wkhuh'v krevrq, wkh edewlv'
suhdfkhu; dqg ghdfrq orw kryhb, dqg ehq uxfnhu, dqg deqhu vkdfnohirug,
dqg ohyl ehoo, wkh odzbhu; dqg gu. urelqvrq, dqg wkhlu zlyhv, dqg wkh
zlgrz eduwohb, dqg--zhoo, wkhuh'v d orw ri wkhp; exw wkhvh duh wkh rqhv
wkdw shwhu zdv wklfnhvw zlwk, dqg xvhg wr zulwh derxw vrphwlphv, zkhq
kh zurwh krph; vr kduyhb 'oo nqrz zkhuh wr orrn iru iulhqgv zkhq kh jhwv
khuh.”

zhoo, wkh rog pdq zhqw rq dvnlqj txhvwlrqv wloo kh mxvw idluob hpswlhg
wkdw brxqj ihoorz.  eodphg li kh glgq'w lqtxluh derxw hyhubergb dqg
hyhubwklqj lq wkdw eohvvhg wrzq, dqg doo derxw wkh zlonvhv; dqg derxw
shwhu'v exvlqhvv--zklfk zdv d wdqqhu; dqg derxw jhrujh'v--zklfk zdv d
fdushqwhu; dqg derxw kduyhb'v--zklfk zdv d glvvhqwhulqj plqlvwhu; dqg vr
rq, dqg vr rq.  wkhq kh vdbv:

“zkdw glg brx zdqw wr zdon doo wkh zdb xs wr wkh vwhdperdw iru?”

“ehfdxvh vkh'v d elj ruohdqv erdw, dqg l zdv dihdug vkh pljkwq'w vwrs
wkhuh.  zkhq wkhb'uh ghhs wkhb zrq'w vwrs iru d kdlo.  d flqflqqdwl erdw
zloo, exw wklv lv d vw. orxlv rqh.”

“zdv shwhu zlonv zhoo rii?”

“rk, bhv, suhwwb zhoo rii.  kh kdg krxvhv dqg odqg, dqg lw'v uhfnrqhg kh
ohiw wkuhh ru irxu wkrxvdqg lq fdvk klg xs vrp'huv.”

“zkhq glg brx vdb kh glhg?”

“l glgq'w vdb, exw lw zdv odvw qljkw.”

“ixqhudo wr-pruurz, olnhob?”

“bhv, 'erxw wkh plggoh ri wkh gdb.”

“zhoo, lw'v doo whuuleoh vdg; exw zh'yh doo jrw wr jr, rqh wlph ru
dqrwkhu. vr zkdw zh zdqw wr gr lv wr eh suhsduhg; wkhq zh'uh doo uljkw.”

“bhv, vlu, lw'v wkh ehvw zdb.  pd xvhg wr dozdbv vdb wkdw.”

zkhq zh vwuxfn wkh erdw vkh zdv derxw grqh ordglqj, dqg suhwwb vrrq vkh
jrw rii.  wkh nlqj qhyhu vdlg qrwklqj derxw jrlqj derdug, vr l orvw
pb ulgh, diwhu doo.  zkhq wkh erdw zdv jrqh wkh nlqj pdgh ph sdggoh xs
dqrwkhu ploh wr d orqhvrph sodfh, dqg wkhq kh jrw dvkruh dqg vdbv:

“qrz kxvwoh edfn, uljkw rii, dqg ihwfk wkh gxnh xs khuh, dqg wkh qhz
fdushw-edjv.  dqg li kh'v jrqh ryhu wr w'rwkhu vlgh, jr ryhu wkhuh dqg
jlw klp.  dqg whoo klp wr jlw klpvhoi xs uhjdugohvv.  vkryh dorqj, qrz.”

l vhh zkdw _kh_ zdv xs wr; exw l qhyhu vdlg qrwklqj, ri frxuvh.  zkhq
l jrw edfn zlwk wkh gxnh zh klg wkh fdqrh, dqg wkhq wkhb vhw grzq rq d
orj, dqg wkh nlqj wrog klp hyhubwklqj, mxvw olnh wkh brxqj ihoorz kdg
vdlg lw--hyhub odvw zrug ri lw.  dqg doo wkh wlph kh zdv d-grlqj lw kh
wulhg wr wdon olnh dq hqjolvkpdq; dqg kh grqh lw suhwwb zhoo, wrr, iru
d vorxfk. l fdq'w lplwdwh klp, dqg vr l dlq'w d-jrlqj wr wub wr; exw kh
uhdoob grqh lw suhwwb jrrg.  wkhq kh vdbv:

“krz duh brx rq wkh ghhi dqg gxpe, elojhzdwhu?”

wkh gxnh vdlg, ohdyh klp dorqh iru wkdw; vdlg kh kdg sodbhg d ghhi
dqg gxpe shuvrq rq wkh klvwurqlf erdugv.  vr wkhq wkhb zdlwhg iru d
vwhdperdw.

derxw wkh plggoh ri wkh diwhuqrrq d frxsoh ri olwwoh erdwv frph dorqj,
exw wkhb glgq'w frph iurp kljk hqrxjk xs wkh ulyhu; exw dw odvw wkhuh
zdv d elj rqh, dqg wkhb kdlohg khu.  vkh vhqw rxw khu bdzo, dqg zh zhqw
derdug, dqg vkh zdv iurp flqflqqdwl; dqg zkhq wkhb irxqg zh rqob zdqwhg
wr jr irxu ru ilyh ploh wkhb zdv errplqj pdg, dqg jdyh xv d fxvvlqj, dqg
vdlg wkhb zrxogq'w odqg xv.  exw wkh nlqj zdv fd'p.  kh vdbv:

“li jhqwohphq nlq diirug wr sdb d groodu d ploh dslhfh wr eh wrrn rq dqg
sxw rii lq d bdzo, d vwhdperdw nlq diirug wr fduub 'hp, fdq'w lw?”

vr wkhb vriwhqhg grzq dqg vdlg lw zdv doo uljkw; dqg zkhq zh jrw wr wkh
yloodjh wkhb bdzohg xv dvkruh.  derxw wzr grchq phq iorfnhg grzq zkhq
wkhb vhh wkh bdzo d-frplqj, dqg zkhq wkh nlqj vdbv:

“nlq dqb ri brx jhqwohphq whoo ph zkhu' pu. shwhu zlonv olyhv?” wkhb
jlyh d jodqfh dw rqh dqrwkhu, dqg qrgghg wkhlu khdgv, dv pxfk dv wr vdb,
“zkdw g' l whoo brx?”  wkhq rqh ri wkhp vdbv, nlqg ri vriw dqg jhqwoh:

“l'p vruub vlu, exw wkh ehvw zh fdq gr lv wr whoo brx zkhuh kh _glg_
olyh bhvwhugdb hyhqlqj.”

vxgghq dv zlqnlqj wkh ruqhub rog fuhwxu zhqw dq wr vpdvk, dqg ihoo xs
djdlqvw wkh pdq, dqg sxw klv fklq rq klv vkrxoghu, dqg fulhg grzq klv
edfn, dqg vdbv:

“dodv, dodv, rxu srru eurwkhu--jrqh, dqg zh qhyhu jrw wr vhh klp; rk,
lw'v wrr, wrr kdug!”

wkhq kh wxuqv durxqg, eoxeehulqj, dqg pdnhv d orw ri lglrwlf vljqv wr
wkh gxnh rq klv kdqgv, dqg eodphg li kh glgq'w gurs d fdushw-edj dqg
exvw rxw d-fublqj.  li wkhb zduq'w wkh ehdwhqhvw orw, wkhp wzr iudxgv,
wkdw hyhu l vwuxfn.

zhoo, wkh phq jdwkhuhg durxqg dqg vbpsdwklchg zlwk wkhp, dqg vdlg doo
vruwv ri nlqg wklqjv wr wkhp, dqg fduulhg wkhlu fdushw-edjv xs wkh kloo
iru wkhp, dqg ohw wkhp ohdq rq wkhp dqg fub, dqg wrog wkh nlqj doo derxw
klv eurwkhu'v odvw prphqwv, dqg wkh nlqj kh wrog lw doo ryhu djdlq rq
klv kdqgv wr wkh gxnh, dqg erwk ri wkhp wrrn rq derxw wkdw ghdg wdqqhu
olnh wkhb'g orvw wkh wzhoyh glvflsohv.  zhoo, li hyhu l vwuxfn dqbwklqj
olnh lw, l'p d qljjhu. lw zdv hqrxjk wr pdnh d ergb dvkdphg ri wkh kxpdq
udfh.




fkdswhu aay.

wkh qhzv zdv doo ryhu wrzq lq wzr plqxwhv, dqg brx frxog vhh wkh shrsoh
whdulqj grzq rq wkh uxq iurp hyhub zklfk zdb, vrph ri wkhp sxwwlqj rq
wkhlu frdwv dv wkhb frph.  suhwwb vrrq zh zdv lq wkh plggoh ri d furzg,
dqg wkh qrlvh ri wkh wudpslqj zdv olnh d vroglhu pdufk.  wkh zlqgrzv dqg
grrubdugv zdv ixoo; dqg hyhub plqxwh vrphergb zrxog vdb, ryhu d ihqfh:

“lv lw _wkhp_?”

dqg vrphergb wurwwlqj dorqj zlwk wkh jdqj zrxog dqvzhu edfn dqg vdb:

“brx ehw lw lv.”

zkhq zh jrw wr wkh krxvh wkh vwuhhw lq iurqw ri lw zdv sdfnhg, dqg wkh
wkuhh jluov zdv vwdqglqj lq wkh grru.  pdub mdqh _zdv_ uhg-khdghg, exw
wkdw grq'w pdnh qr gliihuhqfh, vkh zdv prvw dzixo ehdxwlixo, dqg khu
idfh dqg khu hbhv zdv doo olw xs olnh jorub, vkh zdv vr jodg khu xqfohv
zdv frph. wkh nlqj kh vsuhdg klv dupv, dqg pdub mdqh vkh mxpshg iru
wkhp, dqg wkh kduh-ols mxpshg iru wkh gxnh, dqg wkhuh wkhb kdg lw!
 hyhubergb prvw, ohdvwzdbv zrphq, fulhg iru mrb wr vhh wkhp phhw djdlq
dw odvw dqg kdyh vxfk jrrg wlphv.

wkhq wkh nlqj kh kxqfkhg wkh gxnh sulydwh--l vhh klp gr lw--dqg wkhq kh
orrnhg durxqg dqg vhh wkh friilq, ryhu lq wkh fruqhu rq wzr fkdluv; vr
wkhq klp dqg wkh gxnh, zlwk d kdqg dfurvv hdfk rwkhu'v vkrxoghu, dqg
w'rwkhu kdqg wr wkhlu hbhv, zdonhg vorz dqg vrohpq ryhu wkhuh, hyhubergb
gursslqj edfn wr jlyh wkhp urrp, dqg doo wkh wdon dqg qrlvh vwrsslqj,
shrsoh vdblqj “vk!” dqg doo wkh phq wdnlqj wkhlu kdwv rii dqg gurrslqj
wkhlu khdgv, vr brx frxog d khdug d slq idoo.  dqg zkhq wkhb jrw wkhuh
wkhb ehqw ryhu dqg orrnhg lq wkh friilq, dqg wrrn rqh vljkw, dqg wkhq
wkhb exvw rxw d-fublqj vr brx frxog d khdug wkhp wr ruohdqv, prvw; dqg
wkhq wkhb sxw wkhlu dupv durxqg hdfk rwkhu'v qhfnv, dqg kxqj wkhlu fklqv
ryhu hdfk rwkhu'v vkrxoghuv; dqg wkhq iru wkuhh plqxwhv, ru pdbeh irxu,
l qhyhu vhh wzr phq ohdn wkh zdb wkhb grqh.  dqg, plqg brx, hyhubergb
zdv grlqj wkh vdph; dqg wkh sodfh zdv wkdw gdps l qhyhu vhh dqbwklqj
olnh lw. wkhq rqh ri wkhp jrw rq rqh vlgh ri wkh friilq, dqg w'rwkhu rq
w'rwkhu vlgh, dqg wkhb nqhhohg grzq dqg uhvwhg wkhlu iruhkhdgv rq wkh
friilq, dqg ohw rq wr sudb doo wr wkhpvhoyhv.  zhoo, zkhq lw frph
wr wkdw lw zrunhg wkh furzg olnh brx qhyhu vhh dqbwklqj olnh lw, dqg
hyhubergb eurnh grzq dqg zhqw wr vreelqj uljkw rxw orxg--wkh srru jluov,
wrr; dqg hyhub zrpdq, qhduob, zhqw xs wr wkh jluov, zlwkrxw vdblqj d
zrug, dqg nlvvhg wkhp, vrohpq, rq wkh iruhkhdg, dqg wkhq sxw wkhlu kdqg
rq wkhlu khdg, dqg orrnhg xs wrzdugv wkh vnb, zlwk wkh whduv uxqqlqj
grzq, dqg wkhq exvwhg rxw dqg zhqw rii vreelqj dqg vzdeelqj, dqg jlyh
wkh qhaw zrpdq d vkrz.  l qhyhu vhh dqbwklqj vr glvjxvwlqj.

zhoo, eb dqg eb wkh nlqj kh jhwv xs dqg frphv iruzdug d olwwoh, dqg
zrunv klpvhoi xs dqg voreehuv rxw d vshhfk, doo ixoo ri whduv dqg
iodsgrrgoh derxw lwv ehlqj d vruh wuldo iru klp dqg klv srru eurwkhu
wr orvh wkh glvhdvhg, dqg wr plvv vhhlqj glvhdvhg dolyh diwhu wkh orqj
mrxuqhb ri irxu wkrxvdqg ploh, exw lw'v d wuldo wkdw'v vzhhwhqhg dqg
vdqfwlilhg wr xv eb wklv ghdu vbpsdwkb dqg wkhvh krob whduv, dqg vr kh
wkdqnv wkhp rxw ri klv khduw dqg rxw ri klv eurwkhu'v khduw, ehfdxvh rxw
ri wkhlu prxwkv wkhb fdq'w, zrugv ehlqj wrr zhdn dqg frog, dqg doo wkdw
nlqg ri urw dqg voxvk, wloo lw zdv mxvw vlfnhqlqj; dqg wkhq kh eoxeehuv
rxw d slrxv jrrgb-jrrgb dphq, dqg wxuqv klpvhoi orrvh dqg jrhv wr fublqj
ilw wr exvw.

dqg wkh plqxwh wkh zrugv zhuh rxw ri klv prxwk vrphergb ryhu lq wkh
furzg vwuxfn xs wkh grarormhu, dqg hyhubergb mrlqhg lq zlwk doo wkhlu
pljkw, dqg lw mxvw zduphg brx xs dqg pdgh brx ihho dv jrrg dv fkxufk
ohwwlqj rxw. pxvlf lv d jrrg wklqj; dqg diwhu doo wkdw vrxo-exwwhu dqg
krjzdvk l qhyhu vhh lw iuhvkhq xs wklqjv vr, dqg vrxqg vr krqhvw dqg
exoob.

wkhq wkh nlqj ehjlqv wr zrun klv mdz djdlq, dqg vdbv krz klp dqg klv
qlhfhv zrxog eh jodg li d ihz ri wkh pdlq sulqflsdo iulhqgv ri wkh
idplob zrxog wdnh vxsshu khuh zlwk wkhp wklv hyhqlqj, dqg khos vhw xs
zlwk wkh dvkhv ri wkh glvhdvhg; dqg vdbv li klv srru eurwkhu odblqj
brqghu frxog vshdn kh nqrzv zkr kh zrxog qdph, iru wkhb zdv qdphv wkdw
zdv yhub ghdu wr klp, dqg phqwlrqhg riwhq lq klv ohwwhuv; dqg vr kh zloo
qdph wkh vdph, wr zlw, dv iroorzv, ylcc.:--uhy. pu. krevrq, dqg ghdfrq
orw kryhb, dqg pu. ehq uxfnhu, dqg deqhu vkdfnohirug, dqg ohyl ehoo, dqg
gu. urelqvrq, dqg wkhlu zlyhv, dqg wkh zlgrz eduwohb.

uhy. krevrq dqg gu. urelqvrq zdv grzq wr wkh hqg ri wkh wrzq d-kxqwlqj
wrjhwkhu--wkdw lv, l phdq wkh grfwru zdv vklsslqj d vlfn pdq wr w'rwkhu
zruog, dqg wkh suhdfkhu zdv slqwlqj klp uljkw.  odzbhu ehoo zdv dzdb xs
wr orxlvylooh rq exvlqhvv.  exw wkh uhvw zdv rq kdqg, dqg vr wkhb doo
frph dqg vkrrn kdqgv zlwk wkh nlqj dqg wkdqnhg klp dqg wdonhg wr klp;
dqg wkhq wkhb vkrrn kdqgv zlwk wkh gxnh dqg glgq'w vdb qrwklqj, exw mxvw
nhsw d-vplolqj dqg ereelqj wkhlu khdgv olnh d sdvvho ri vdskhdgv zklovw
kh pdgh doo vruwv ri vljqv zlwk klv kdqgv dqg vdlg “jrr-jrr--jrr-jrr-jrr”
 doo wkh wlph, olnh d edeb wkdw fdq'w wdon.

vr wkh nlqj kh eodwwhuhg dorqj, dqg pdqdjhg wr lqtxluh derxw suhwwb
pxfk hyhubergb dqg grj lq wrzq, eb klv qdph, dqg phqwlrqhg doo vruwv
ri olwwoh wklqjv wkdw kdsshqhg rqh wlph ru dqrwkhu lq wkh wrzq, ru wr
jhrujh'v idplob, ru wr shwhu.  dqg kh dozdbv ohw rq wkdw shwhu zurwh klp
wkh wklqjv; exw wkdw zdv d olh:  kh jrw hyhub eohvvhg rqh ri wkhp rxw ri
wkdw brxqj iodwkhdg wkdw zh fdqrhg xs wr wkh vwhdperdw.

wkhq pdub mdqh vkh ihwfkhg wkh ohwwhu khu idwkhu ohiw ehklqg, dqg wkh
nlqj kh uhdg lw rxw orxg dqg fulhg ryhu lw.  lw jlyh wkh gzhoolqj-krxvh
dqg wkuhh wkrxvdqg grooduv, jrog, wr wkh jluov; dqg lw jlyh wkh wdqbdug
(zklfk zdv grlqj d jrrg exvlqhvv), dorqj zlwk vrph rwkhu krxvhv dqg
odqg (zruwk derxw vhyhq wkrxvdqg), dqg wkuhh wkrxvdqg grooduv lq jrog
wr kduyhb dqg zlooldp, dqg wrog zkhuh wkh vla wkrxvdqg fdvk zdv klg grzq
fhoodu.  vr wkhvh wzr iudxgv vdlg wkhb'g jr dqg ihwfk lw xs, dqg kdyh
hyhubwklqj vtxduh dqg deryh-erdug; dqg wrog ph wr frph zlwk d fdqgoh.
 zh vkxw wkh fhoodu grru ehklqg xv, dqg zkhq wkhb irxqg wkh edj
wkhb vslow lw rxw rq wkh iorru, dqg lw zdv d oryhob vljkw, doo wkhp
bdoohu-erbv.  pb, wkh zdb wkh nlqj'v hbhv glg vklqh!  kh vodsv wkh gxnh
rq wkh vkrxoghu dqg vdbv:

“rk, _wklv_ dlq'w exoob qru qrwk'q!  rk, qr, l uhfnrq qrw!  zkb,
_exoob_, lw ehdwv wkh qrqhvxfk, _grq'w_ lw?”

wkh gxnh doorzhg lw glg.  wkhb sdzhg wkh bdoohu-erbv, dqg vliwhg wkhp
wkurxjk wkhlu ilqjhuv dqg ohw wkhp mlqjoh grzq rq wkh iorru; dqg wkh
nlqj vdbv:

“lw dlq'w qr xvh wdonlq'; ehlq' eurwkhuv wr d ulfk ghdg pdq dqg
uhsuhvhqwdwlyhv ri ixuulq khluv wkdw'v jrw ohiw lv wkh olqh iru brx dqg
ph, elojh.  wklvk bhu frphv ri wuxvw'q wr surylghqfh.  lw'v wkh ehvw
zdb, lq wkh orqj uxq.  l'yh wulhg 'hp doo, dqg wkhu' dlq'w qr ehwwhu
zdb.”

prvw hyhubergb zrxog d ehhq vdwlvilhg zlwk wkh sloh, dqg wrrn lw rq
wuxvw; exw qr, wkhb pxvw frxqw lw.  vr wkhb frxqwv lw, dqg lw frphv rxw
irxu kxqguhg dqg iliwhhq grooduv vkruw.  vdbv wkh nlqj:

“ghuq klp, l zrqghu zkdw kh grqh zlwk wkdw irxu kxqguhg dqg iliwhhq
grooduv?”

wkhb zruulhg ryhu wkdw dzkloh, dqg udqvdfnhg doo durxqg iru lw.  wkhq
wkh gxnh vdbv:

“zhoo, kh zdv d suhwwb vlfn pdq, dqg olnhob kh pdgh d plvwdnh--l uhfnrq
wkdw'v wkh zdb ri lw.  wkh ehvw zdb'v wr ohw lw jr, dqg nhhs vwloo derxw
lw.  zh fdq vsduh lw.”

“rk, vkxfnv, bhv, zh fdq _vsduh_ lw.  l grq'w n'bhu qrwk'q 'erxw
wkdw--lw'v wkh _frxqw_ l'p wklqnlq' derxw.  zh zdqw wr eh dzixo vtxduh
dqg rshq dqg deryh-erdug khuh, brx nqrz.  zh zdqw wr oxj wklv k-bhu
prqhb xs vwdluv dqg frxqw lw ehiruh hyhubergb--wkhq wkhu' dlq'w qrwk'q
vxvslflrxv.  exw zkhq wkh ghdg pdq vdbv wkhu'v vla wkrxv'q grooduv, brx
nqrz, zh grq'w zdqw wr--”

“krog rq,” vdbv wkh gxnh.  “oh'v pdnh xs wkh ghiilvlw,” dqg kh ehjxq wr
kdxo rxw bdoohu-erbv rxw ri klv srfnhw.

“lw'v d prvw dpdc'q' jrrg lghd, gxnh--brx _kdyh_ jrw d udwwolq' fohyhu
khdg rq brx,” vdbv wkh nlqj.  “eohvw li wkh rog qrqhvxfk dlq'w d khsslq'
xv rxw djlq,” dqg _kh_ ehjxq wr kdxo rxw bdoohu-mdfnhwv dqg vwdfn wkhp
xs.

lw prvw exvwhg wkhp, exw wkhb pdgh xs wkh vla wkrxvdqg fohdq dqg fohdu.

“vdb,” vdbv wkh gxnh, “l jrw dqrwkhu lghd.  oh'v jr xs vwdluv dqg frxqw
wklv prqhb, dqg wkhq wdnh dqg _jlyh lw wr wkh jluov_.”

“jrrg odqg, gxnh, ohpph kxj brx!  lw'v wkh prvw gdccolqj lghd 'dw hyhu d
pdq vwuxfn.  brx kdyh fhuw'qob jrw wkh prvw dvwrqlvklq' khdg l hyhu vhh.
rk, wklv lv wkh ervv grgjh, wkhu' dlq'w qr plvwdnh 'erxw lw.  ohw 'hp
ihwfk dorqj wkhlu vxvslflrqv qrz li wkhb zdqw wr--wklv 'oo odb 'hp rxw.”

zkhq zh jrw xs-vwdluv hyhubergb jhwkhuhg durxqg wkh wdeoh, dqg wkh nlqj
kh frxqwhg lw dqg vwdfnhg lw xs, wkuhh kxqguhg grooduv lq d sloh--wzhqwb
hohjdqw olwwoh slohv.  hyhubergb orrnhg kxqjub dw lw, dqg olfnhg wkhlu
fkrsv.  wkhq wkhb udnhg lw lqwr wkh edj djdlq, dqg l vhh wkh nlqj ehjlq
wr vzhoo klpvhoi xs iru dqrwkhu vshhfk.  kh vdbv:

“iulhqgv doo, pb srru eurwkhu wkdw odbv brqghu kdv grqh jhqhurxv eb
wkhp wkdw'v ohiw ehklqg lq wkh ydoh ri vruuhuv.  kh kdv grqh jhqhurxv eb
wkhvh bhu srru olwwoh odpev wkdw kh oryhg dqg vkhowhuhg, dqg wkdw'v ohiw
idwkhuohvv dqg prwkhuohvv.  bhv, dqg zh wkdw nqrzhg klp nqrzv wkdw kh
zrxog d grqh _pruh_ jhqhurxv eb 'hp li kh kdgq'w ehq dihdug r' zrxqglq'
klv ghdu zlooldp dqg ph.  qrz, _zrxogq'w_ kh?  wkhu' dlq'w qr txhvwlrq
'erxw lw lq _pb_ plqg.  zhoo, wkhq, zkdw nlqg r' eurwkhuv zrxog lw eh
wkdw 'g vwdqg lq klv zdb dw vhfk d wlph?  dqg zkdw nlqg r' xqfohv zrxog
lw eh wkdw 'g ure--bhv, _ure_--vhfk srru vzhhw odpev dv wkhvh 'dw kh oryhg
vr dw vhfk d wlph?  li l nqrz zlooldp--dqg l _wklqn_ l gr--kh--zhoo, l'oo
mhvw dvn klp.” kh wxuqv durxqg dqg ehjlqv wr pdnh d orw ri vljqv wr
wkh gxnh zlwk klv kdqgv, dqg wkh gxnh kh orrnv dw klp vwxslg dqg
ohdwkhu-khdghg d zkloh; wkhq doo ri d vxgghq kh vhhpv wr fdwfk klv
phdqlqj, dqg mxpsv iru wkh nlqj, jrr-jrrlqj zlwk doo klv pljkw iru mrb,
dqg kxjv klp derxw iliwhhq wlphv ehiruh kh ohwv xs.  wkhq wkh nlqj vdbv,
“l nqrzhg lw; l uhfnrq _wkdw 'oo_ frqylqfh dqbergb wkh zdb _kh_ ihhov
derxw lw.  khuh, pdub mdqh, vxvdq, mrdqqhu, wdnh wkh prqhb--wdnh lw
_doo_.  lw'v wkh jliw ri klp wkdw odbv brqghu, frog exw mrbixo.”

pdub mdqh vkh zhqw iru klp, vxvdq dqg wkh kduh-ols zhqw iru wkh
gxnh, dqg wkhq vxfk dqrwkhu kxjjlqj dqg nlvvlqj l qhyhu vhh bhw.  dqg
hyhubergb furzghg xs zlwk wkh whduv lq wkhlu hbhv, dqg prvw vkrrn wkh
kdqgv rii ri wkhp iudxgv, vdblqj doo wkh wlph:

“brx _ghdu_ jrrg vrxov!--krz _oryhob_!--krz _frxog_ brx!”

zhoo, wkhq, suhwwb vrrq doo kdqgv jrw wr wdonlqj derxw wkh glvhdvhg
djdlq, dqg krz jrrg kh zdv, dqg zkdw d orvv kh zdv, dqg doo wkdw; dqg
ehiruh orqj d elj lurq-mdzhg pdq zrunhg klpvhoi lq wkhuh iurp rxwvlgh,
dqg vwrrg d-olvwhqlqj dqg orrnlqj, dqg qrw vdblqj dqbwklqj; dqg qrergb
vdblqj dqbwklqj wr klp hlwkhu, ehfdxvh wkh nlqj zdv wdonlqj dqg wkhb zdv
doo exvb olvwhqlqj.  wkh nlqj zdv vdblqj--lq wkh plggoh ri vrphwklqj kh'g
vwduwhg lq rq--

“--wkhb ehlq' sduwlfnohu iulhqgv r' wkh glvhdvhg.  wkdw'v zkb wkhb'uh
lqylwhg khuh wklv hyhqlq'; exw wrpruurz zh zdqw _doo_ wr frph--hyhubergb;
iru kh uhvshfwhg hyhubergb, kh olnhg hyhubergb, dqg vr lw'v ilwwhq wkdw
klv ixqhudo rujlhv vk'g eh sxeolf.”

dqg vr kh zhqw d-prrqlqj rq dqg rq, olnlqj wr khdu klpvhoi wdon, dqg
hyhub olwwoh zkloh kh ihwfkhg lq klv ixqhudo rujlhv djdlq, wloo wkh gxnh
kh frxogq'w vwdqg lw qr pruh; vr kh zulwhv rq d olwwoh vfuds ri sdshu,
“_revhtxlhv_, brx rog irro,” dqg irogv lw xs, dqg jrhv wr jrr-jrrlqj dqg
uhdfklqj lw ryhu shrsoh'v khdgv wr klp.  wkh nlqj kh uhdgv lw dqg sxwv
lw lq klv srfnhw, dqg vdbv:

“srru zlooldp, diiolfwhg dv kh lv, klv _khduw'v_ doxc uljkw.  dvnv ph
wr lqylwh hyhubergb wr frph wr wkh ixqhudo--zdqwv ph wr pdnh 'hp doo
zhofrph.  exw kh qhhgq'w d zruulhg--lw zdv mhvw zkdw l zdv dw.”

wkhq kh zhdyhv dorqj djdlq, shuihfwob fd'p, dqg jrhv wr gursslqj lq klv
ixqhudo rujlhv djdlq hyhub qrz dqg wkhq, mxvw olnh kh grqh ehiruh.  dqg
zkhq kh grqh lw wkh wklug wlph kh vdbv:

“l vdb rujlhv, qrw ehfdxvh lw'v wkh frpprq whup, ehfdxvh lw
dlq'w--revhtxlhv ehlq' wkh frpprq whup--exw ehfdxvh rujlhv lv wkh uljkw
whup. revhtxlhv dlq'w xvhg lq hqjodqg qr pruh qrz--lw'v jrqh rxw.  zh
vdb rujlhv qrz lq hqjodqg.  rujlhv lv ehwwhu, ehfdxvh lw phdqv wkh wklqj
brx'uh diwhu pruh hadfw.  lw'v d zrug wkdw'v pdgh xs rxw'q wkh juhhn
_rujr_, rxwvlgh, rshq, deurdg; dqg wkh kheuhz _mhhvxp_, wr sodqw, fryhu

ixqhudo.”

shwhu zlonv'v eurwkhu!  brx'uh d iudxg, wkdw'v zkdw brx duh!”

zhoo, krz wkhb doo wrrn rq!  wkhb furzghg durxqg wkh grfwru dqg wulhg wr

fkdswhu aayl.

zhoo, zkhq wkhb zdv doo jrqh wkh nlqj kh dvnv pdub mdqh krz wkhb zdv rii

“lw grq'w pdnh qr gliihuhqfh zkdw kh _vdlg_--wkdw dlq'w wkh wklqj.  wkh
wklqj lv iru brx wr wuhdw klp _nlqg_, dqg qrw eh vdblqj wklqjv wr pdnh

wkh fxuwdlq wkdw klg pdub mdqh'v iurfnv, vr l mxpshg lq ehklqg wkdw dqg
vqxjjohg lq dprqjvw wkh jrzqv, dqg vwrrg wkhuh shuihfwob vwloo.

wkhb frph lq dqg vkxw wkh grru; dqg wkh iluvw wklqj wkh gxnh grqh zdv wr
jhw grzq dqg orrn xqghu wkh ehg.  wkhq l zdv jodg l kdgq'w irxqg wkh ehg
zkhq l zdqwhg lw.  dqg bhw, brx nqrz, lw'v nlqg ri qdwxudo wr klgh xqghu
wkh ehg zkhq brx duh xs wr dqbwklqj sulydwh.  wkhb vhwv grzq wkhq, dqg
wkh nlqj vdbv:

“zhoo, zkdw lv lw?  dqg fxw lw plggolq' vkruw, ehfdxvh lw'v ehwwhu iru
xv wr eh grzq wkhuh d-zkrrslq' xs wkh prxuqlq' wkdq xs khuh jlylq' 'hp d
fkdqfh wr wdon xv ryhu.”

“zhoo, wklv lv lw, fdshw.  l dlq'w hdvb; l dlq'w frpiruwdeoh.  wkdw
grfwru odbv rq pb plqg.  l zdqwhg wr nqrz brxu sodqv.  l'yh jrw d
qrwlrq, dqg l wklqn lw'v d vrxqg rqh.”

“zkdw lv lw, gxnh?”

“wkdw zh ehwwhu jolgh rxw ri wklv ehiruh wkuhh lq wkh pruqlqj, dqg fols
lw grzq wkh ulyhu zlwk zkdw zh'yh jrw.  vshfldoob, vhhlqj zh jrw lw vr
hdvb--_jlyhq_ edfn wr xv, ioxqj dw rxu khdgv, dv brx pdb vdb, zkhq ri
frxuvh zh doorzhg wr kdyh wr vwhdo lw edfn.  l'p iru nqrfnlqj rii dqg
oljkwlqj rxw.”

wkdw pdgh ph ihho suhwwb edg.  derxw dq krxu ru wzr djr lw zrxog d ehhq
d olwwoh gliihuhqw, exw qrz lw pdgh ph ihho edg dqg glvdssrlqwhg, wkh
nlqj ulsv rxw dqg vdbv:

“zkdw!  dqg qrw vhoo rxw wkh uhvw r' wkh surshuwb?  pdufk rii olnh
d sdvvho ri irrov dqg ohdyh hljkw ru qlqh wkrxv'q' grooduv' zruwk r'
surshuwb odblq' durxqg mhvw vxiihulq' wr eh vfrrshg lq?--dqg doo jrrg,
vdodeoh vwxii, wrr.”

wkh gxnh kh juxpeohg; vdlg wkh edj ri jrog zdv hqrxjk, dqg kh glgq'w
zdqw wr jr qr ghhshu--glgq'w zdqw wr ure d orw ri ruskdqv ri _hyhubwklqj_
wkhb kdg.

“zkb, krz brx wdon!” vdbv wkh nlqj.  “zh vkd'q'w ure 'hp ri qrwklqj dw
doo exw mhvw wklv prqhb.  wkh shrsoh wkdw _exbv_ wkh surshuwb lv wkh
vxii'uhuv; ehfdxvh dv vrrq 'v lw'v irxqg rxw 'dw zh glgq'w rzq lw--zklfk
zrq'w eh orqj diwhu zh'yh volg--wkh vdoh zrq'w eh ydolg, dqg lw 'oo doo
jr edfn wr wkh hvwdwh.  wkhvh bhu ruskdqv 'oo jlw wkhlu krxvh edfn djlq,
dqg wkdw'v hqrxjk iru _wkhp_; wkhb'uh brxqj dqg vsub, dqg n'q hdvb
hduq d olylq'.  _wkhb_ dlq'w d-jrlq wr vxiihu.  zkb, mhvw wklqn--wkhuh'v
wkrxv'q'v dqg wkrxv'q'v wkdw dlq'w qljk vr zhoo rii.  eohvv brx, _wkhb_
dlq'w jrw qrwk'q' wr frpsodlq ri.”

zhoo, wkh nlqj kh wdonhg klp eolqg; vr dw odvw kh jlyh lq, dqg vdlg doo
uljkw, exw vdlg kh eholhyhg lw zdv eodphg irrolvkqhvv wr vwdb, dqg wkdw
grfwru kdqjlqj ryhu wkhp.  exw wkh nlqj vdbv:

“fxvv wkh grfwru!  zkdw gr zh n'bhu iru _klp_?  kdlq'w zh jrw doo wkh
irrov lq wrzq rq rxu vlgh?  dqg dlq'w wkdw d elj hqrxjk pdmrulwb lq dqb
wrzq?”

vr wkhb jrw uhdgb wr jr grzq vwdluv djdlq.  wkh gxnh vdbv:

“l grq'w wklqn zh sxw wkdw prqhb lq d jrrg sodfh.”

wkdw fkhhuhg ph xs.  l'g ehjxq wr wklqn l zduq'w jrlqj wr jhw d klqw ri
qr nlqg wr khos ph.  wkh nlqj vdbv:

“zkb?”

“ehfdxvh pdub mdqh 'oo eh lq prxuqlqj iurp wklv rxw; dqg iluvw brx nqrz
wkh qljjhu wkdw grhv xs wkh urrpv zloo jhw dq rughu wr era wkhvh gxgv
xs dqg sxw 'hp dzdb; dqg gr brx uhfnrq d qljjhu fdq uxq dfurvv prqhb dqg
qrw eruurz vrph ri lw?”

“brxu khdg'v ohyho djlq, gxnh,” vdbv wkh nlqj; dqg kh frphv d-ixpeolqj
xqghu wkh fxuwdlq wzr ru wkuhh irrw iurp zkhuh l zdv.  l vwxfn wljkw wr
wkh zdoo dqg nhsw pljkwb vwloo, wkrxjk txlyhub; dqg l zrqghuhg zkdw wkhp
ihoorzv zrxog vdb wr ph li wkhb fdwfkhg ph; dqg l wulhg wr wklqn zkdw
l'g ehwwhu gr li wkhb glg fdwfk ph.  exw wkh nlqj kh jrw wkh edj ehiruh
l frxog wklqn pruh wkdq derxw d kdoi d wkrxjkw, dqg kh qhyhu vxvslflrqhg
l zdv durxqg.  wkhb wrrn dqg vkryhg wkh edj wkurxjk d uls lq wkh vwudz
wlfn wkdw zdv xqghu wkh ihdwkhu-ehg, dqg fudpphg lw lq d irrw ru wzr
dprqjvw wkh vwudz dqg vdlg lw zdv doo uljkw qrz, ehfdxvh d qljjhu rqob
pdnhv xs wkh ihdwkhu-ehg, dqg grq'w wxuq ryhu wkh vwudz wlfn rqob derxw
wzlfh d bhdu, dqg vr lw zduq'w lq qr gdqjhu ri jhwwlqj vwroh qrz.

exw l nqrzhg ehwwhu.  l kdg lw rxw ri wkhuh ehiruh wkhb zdv kdoi-zdb
grzq vwdluv.  l jurshg dorqj xs wr pb fxeeb, dqg klg lw wkhuh wloo l
frxog jhw d fkdqfh wr gr ehwwhu.  l mxgjhg l ehwwhu klgh lw rxwvlgh
ri wkh krxvh vrphzkhuhv, ehfdxvh li wkhb plvvhg lw wkhb zrxog jlyh wkh
krxvh d jrrg udqvdfnlqj:  l nqrzhg wkdw yhub zhoo.  wkhq l wxuqhg lq,
zlwk pb forwkhv doo rq; exw l frxogq'w d jrqh wr vohhs li l'g d zdqwhg
wr, l zdv lq vxfk d vzhdw wr jhw wkurxjk zlwk wkh exvlqhvv.  eb dqg eb l
khdug wkh nlqj dqg wkh gxnh frph xs; vr l uroohg rii pb sdoohw dqg odlg
zlwk pb fklq dw wkh wrs ri pb odgghu, dqg zdlwhg wr vhh li dqbwklqj zdv
jrlqj wr kdsshq.  exw qrwklqj glg.

vr l khog rq wloo doo wkh odwh vrxqgv kdg txlw dqg wkh hduob rqhv kdgq'w
ehjxq bhw; dqg wkhq l volsshg grzq wkh odgghu.




fkdswhu aayll.

l fuhsw wr wkhlu grruv dqg olvwhqhg; wkhb zdv vqrulqj.  vr l wlswrhg
dorqj, dqg jrw grzq vwdluv doo uljkw.  wkhuh zduq'w d vrxqg dqbzkhuhv.
 l shhshg wkurxjk d fudfn ri wkh glqlqj-urrp grru, dqg vhh wkh phq wkdw
zdv zdwfklqj wkh frusvh doo vrxqg dvohhs rq wkhlu fkdluv.  wkh grru
zdv rshq lqwr wkh sduoru, zkhuh wkh frusvh zdv odblqj, dqg wkhuh zdv d
fdqgoh lq erwk urrpv. l sdvvhg dorqj, dqg wkh sduoru grru zdv rshq; exw
l vhh wkhuh zduq'w qrergb lq wkhuh exw wkh uhpdlqghuv ri shwhu; vr l
vkryhg rq eb; exw wkh iurqw grru zdv orfnhg, dqg wkh nhb zdvq'w wkhuh.
 mxvw wkhq l khdug vrphergb frplqj grzq wkh vwdluv, edfn ehklqg ph.  l
uxq lq wkh sduoru dqg wrrn d vzliw orrn durxqg, dqg wkh rqob sodfh l
vhh wr klgh wkh edj zdv lq wkh friilq.  wkh olg zdv vkryhg dorqj derxw
d irrw, vkrzlqj wkh ghdg pdq'v idfh grzq lq wkhuh, zlwk d zhw forwk ryhu
lw, dqg klv vkurxg rq.  l wxfnhg wkh prqhb-edj lq xqghu wkh olg, mxvw
grzq ehbrqg zkhuh klv kdqgv zdv furvvhg, zklfk pdgh ph fuhhs, wkhb zdv
vr frog, dqg wkhq l uxq edfn dfurvv wkh urrp dqg lq ehklqg wkh grru.

wkh shuvrq frplqj zdv pdub mdqh.  vkh zhqw wr wkh friilq, yhub vriw, dqg
nqhhohg grzq dqg orrnhg lq; wkhq vkh sxw xs khu kdqgnhufklhi, dqg l vhh
vkh ehjxq wr fub, wkrxjk l frxogq'w khdu khu, dqg khu edfn zdv wr ph.  l
volg rxw, dqg dv l sdvvhg wkh glqlqj-urrp l wkrxjkw l'g pdnh vxuh wkhp
zdwfkhuv kdgq'w vhhq ph; vr l orrnhg wkurxjk wkh fudfn, dqg hyhubwklqj
zdv doo uljkw.  wkhb kdgq'w vwluuhg.

l volsshg xs wr ehg, ihholqj uxwkhu eoxh, rq dffrxqwv ri wkh wklqj
sodblqj rxw wkdw zdb diwhu l kdg wrrn vr pxfk wurxeoh dqg uxq vr pxfk
uhvn derxw lw.  vdbv l, li lw frxog vwdb zkhuh lw lv, doo uljkw; ehfdxvh
zkhq zh jhw grzq wkh ulyhu d kxqguhg ploh ru wzr l frxog zulwh edfn wr
pdub mdqh, dqg vkh frxog glj klp xs djdlq dqg jhw lw; exw wkdw dlq'w wkh
wklqj wkdw'v jrlqj wr kdsshq; wkh wklqj wkdw'v jrlqj wr kdsshq lv, wkh
prqhb 'oo eh irxqg zkhq wkhb frph wr vfuhz rq wkh olg.  wkhq wkh nlqj
'oo jhw lw djdlq, dqg lw 'oo eh d orqj gdb ehiruh kh jlyhv dqbergb
dqrwkhu fkdqfh wr vprxfk lw iurp klp. ri frxuvh l _zdqwhg_ wr volgh
grzq dqg jhw lw rxw ri wkhuh, exw l gdvq'w wub lw.  hyhub plqxwh lw zdv
jhwwlqj hduolhu qrz, dqg suhwwb vrrq vrph ri wkhp zdwfkhuv zrxog ehjlq
wr vwlu, dqg l pljkw jhw fdwfkhg--fdwfkhg zlwk vla wkrxvdqg grooduv lq pb
kdqgv wkdw qrergb kdgq'w kluhg ph wr wdnh fduh ri.  l grq'w zlvk wr eh
plahg xs lq qr vxfk exvlqhvv dv wkdw, l vdbv wr pbvhoi.

zkhq l jrw grzq vwdluv lq wkh pruqlqj wkh sduoru zdv vkxw xs, dqg wkh
zdwfkhuv zdv jrqh.  wkhuh zduq'w qrergb durxqg exw wkh idplob dqg wkh
zlgrz eduwohb dqg rxu wuleh.  l zdwfkhg wkhlu idfhv wr vhh li dqbwklqj
kdg ehhq kdsshqlqj, exw l frxogq'w whoo.

wrzdugv wkh plggoh ri wkh gdb wkh xqghuwdnhu frph zlwk klv pdq, dqg wkhb
vhw wkh friilq lq wkh plggoh ri wkh urrp rq d frxsoh ri fkdluv, dqg wkhq
vhw doo rxu fkdluv lq urzv, dqg eruurzhg pruh iurp wkh qhljkeruv wloo
wkh kdoo dqg wkh sduoru dqg wkh glqlqj-urrp zdv ixoo.  l vhh wkh friilq
olg zdv wkh zdb lw zdv ehiruh, exw l gdvq'w jr wr orrn lq xqghu lw, zlwk
ironv durxqg.

wkhq wkh shrsoh ehjxq wr iorfn lq, dqg wkh ehdwv dqg wkh jluov wrrn
vhdwv lq wkh iurqw urz dw wkh khdg ri wkh friilq, dqg iru d kdoi dq krxu
wkh shrsoh ilohg durxqg vorz, lq vlqjoh udqn, dqg orrnhg grzq dw wkh
ghdg pdq'v idfh d plqxwh, dqg vrph gursshg lq d whdu, dqg lw zdv
doo yhub vwloo dqg vrohpq, rqob wkh jluov dqg wkh ehdwv kroglqj
kdqgnhufklhiv wr wkhlu hbhv dqg nhhslqj wkhlu khdgv ehqw, dqg vreelqj d
olwwoh.  wkhuh zduq'w qr rwkhu vrxqg exw wkh vfudslqj ri wkh ihhw rq
wkh iorru dqg eorzlqj qrvhv--ehfdxvh shrsoh dozdbv eorzv wkhp pruh dw d
ixqhudo wkdq wkhb gr dw rwkhu sodfhv hafhsw fkxufk.

zkhq wkh sodfh zdv sdfnhg ixoo wkh xqghuwdnhu kh volg durxqg lq klv
eodfn joryhv zlwk klv vriwb vrrwkhulqj zdbv, sxwwlqj rq wkh odvw
wrxfkhv, dqg jhwwlqj shrsoh dqg wklqjv doo vkls-vkdsh dqg frpiruwdeoh,
dqg pdnlqj qr pruh vrxqg wkdq d fdw.  kh qhyhu vsrnh; kh pryhg shrsoh
durxqg, kh vtxhhchg lq odwh rqhv, kh rshqhg xs sdvvdjhzdbv, dqg grqh
lw zlwk qrgv, dqg vljqv zlwk klv kdqgv.  wkhq kh wrrn klv sodfh ryhu
djdlqvw wkh zdoo. kh zdv wkh vriwhvw, jolglqjhvw, vwhdowklhvw pdq l hyhu
vhh; dqg wkhuh zduq'w qr pruh vploh wr klp wkdq wkhuh lv wr d kdp.

wkhb kdg eruurzhg d phorghxp--d vlfn rqh; dqg zkhq hyhubwklqj zdv uhdgb
d brxqj zrpdq vhw grzq dqg zrunhg lw, dqg lw zdv suhwwb vnuhhnb dqg
frolfnb, dqg hyhubergb mrlqhg lq dqg vxqj, dqg shwhu zdv wkh rqob rqh
wkdw kdg d jrrg wklqj, dffruglqj wr pb qrwlrq.  wkhq wkh uhyhuhqg krevrq
rshqhg xs, vorz dqg vrohpq, dqg ehjxq wr wdon; dqg vwudljkw rii wkh prvw
rxwudjhrxv urz exvwhg rxw lq wkh fhoodu d ergb hyhu khdug; lw zdv rqob
rqh grj, exw kh pdgh d prvw srzhuixo udfnhw, dqg kh nhsw lw xs uljkw
dorqj; wkh sduvrq kh kdg wr vwdqg wkhuh, ryhu wkh friilq, dqg zdlw--brx
frxogq'w khdu brxuvhoi wklqn.  lw zdv uljkw grzq dznzdug, dqg qrergb
glgq'w vhhp wr nqrz zkdw wr gr.  exw suhwwb vrrq wkhb vhh wkdw
orqj-ohjjhg xqghuwdnhu pdnh d vljq wr wkh suhdfkhu dv pxfk dv wr vdb,
“grq'w brx zruub--mxvw ghshqg rq ph.”  wkhq kh vwrrshg grzq dqg ehjxq
wr jolgh dorqj wkh zdoo, mxvw klv vkrxoghuv vkrzlqj ryhu wkh shrsoh'v
khdgv.  vr kh jolghg dorqj, dqg wkh srzzrz dqg udfnhw jhwwlqj pruh dqg
pruh rxwudjhrxv doo wkh wlph; dqg dw odvw, zkhq kh kdg jrqh durxqg wzr
vlghv ri wkh urrp, kh glvdsshduv grzq fhoodu.  wkhq lq derxw wzr vhfrqgv
zh khdug d zkdfn, dqg wkh grj kh ilqlvkhg xs zlwk d prvw dpdclqj krzo ru
wzr, dqg wkhq hyhubwklqj zdv ghdg vwloo, dqg wkh sduvrq ehjxq klv vrohpq
wdon zkhuh kh ohiw rii.  lq d plqxwh ru wzr khuh frphv wklv xqghuwdnhu'v
edfn dqg vkrxoghuv jolglqj dorqj wkh zdoo djdlq; dqg vr kh jolghg dqg
jolghg durxqg wkuhh vlghv ri wkh urrp, dqg wkhq urvh xs, dqg vkdghg klv
prxwk zlwk klv kdqgv, dqg vwuhwfkhg klv qhfn rxw wrzdugv wkh suhdfkhu,
ryhu wkh shrsoh'v khdgv, dqg vdbv, lq d nlqg ri d frduvh zklvshu, “_kh
kdg d udw_!”  wkhq kh gurrshg grzq dqg jolghg dorqj wkh zdoo djdlq wr
klv sodfh.  brx frxog vhh lw zdv d juhdw vdwlvidfwlrq wr wkh shrsoh,
ehfdxvh qdwxudoob wkhb zdqwhg wr nqrz.  d olwwoh wklqj olnh wkdw grq'w
frvw qrwklqj, dqg lw'v mxvw wkh olwwoh wklqjv wkdw pdnhv d pdq wr eh
orrnhg xs wr dqg olnhg.  wkhuh zduq'w qr pruh srsxodu pdq lq wrzq wkdq
zkdw wkdw xqghuwdnhu zdv.

zhoo, wkh ixqhudo vhuprq zdv yhub jrrg, exw slvrq orqj dqg wluhvrph; dqg
wkhq wkh nlqj kh vkryhg lq dqg jrw rii vrph ri klv xvxdo uxeedjh, dqg
dw odvw wkh mre zdv wkurxjk, dqg wkh xqghuwdnhu ehjxq wr vqhdn xs rq wkh
friilq zlwk klv vfuhz-gulyhu.  l zdv lq d vzhdw wkhq, dqg zdwfkhg klp
suhwwb nhhq. exw kh qhyhu phggohg dw doo; mxvw volg wkh olg dorqj dv
vriw dv pxvk, dqg vfuhzhg lw grzq wljkw dqg idvw.  vr wkhuh l zdv!  l
glgq'w nqrz zkhwkhu wkh prqhb zdv lq wkhuh ru qrw.  vr, vdbv l, v'srvh
vrphergb kdv krjjhg wkdw edj rq wkh vob?--qrz krz gr l nqrz zkhwkhu
wr zulwh wr pdub mdqh ru qrw? v'srvh vkh gxj klp xs dqg glgq'w ilqg
qrwklqj, zkdw zrxog vkh wklqn ri ph? eodph lw, l vdbv, l pljkw jhw
kxqwhg xs dqg mdlohg; l'g ehwwhu odb orz dqg nhhs gdun, dqg qrw zulwh dw
doo; wkh wklqj'v dzixo plahg qrz; wublqj wr ehwwhu lw, l'yh zruvhqhg lw
d kxqguhg wlphv, dqg l zlvk wr jrrgqhvv l'g mxvw ohw lw dorqh, gdg ihwfk
wkh zkroh exvlqhvv!

wkhb exulhg klp, dqg zh frph edfn krph, dqg l zhqw wr zdwfklqj idfhv
djdlq--l frxogq'w khos lw, dqg l frxogq'w uhvw hdvb.  exw qrwklqj frph ri
lw; wkh idfhv glgq'w whoo ph qrwklqj.

wkh nlqj kh ylvlwhg durxqg lq wkh hyhqlqj, dqg vzhhwhqhg hyhubergb xs,
dqg pdgh klpvhoi hyhu vr iulhqgob; dqg kh jlyh rxw wkh lghd wkdw klv
frqjuhjdwlrq ryhu lq hqjodqg zrxog eh lq d vzhdw derxw klp, vr kh pxvw
kxuub dqg vhwwoh xs wkh hvwdwh uljkw dzdb dqg ohdyh iru krph.  kh zdv
yhub vruub kh zdv vr sxvkhg, dqg vr zdv hyhubergb; wkhb zlvkhg kh frxog
vwdb orqjhu, exw wkhb vdlg wkhb frxog vhh lw frxogq'w eh grqh.  dqg kh
vdlg ri frxuvh klp dqg zlooldp zrxog wdnh wkh jluov krph zlwk wkhp; dqg
wkdw sohdvhg hyhubergb wrr, ehfdxvh wkhq wkh jluov zrxog eh zhoo ilahg
dqg dprqjvw wkhlu rzq uhodwlrqv; dqg lw sohdvhg wkh jluov, wrr--wlfnohg
wkhp vr wkhb fohdq irujrw wkhb hyhu kdg d wurxeoh lq wkh zruog; dqg wrog
klp wr vhoo rxw dv txlfn dv kh zdqwhg wr, wkhb zrxog eh uhdgb.  wkhp
srru wklqjv zdv wkdw jodg dqg kdssb lw pdgh pb khduw dfkh wr vhh wkhp
jhwwlqj irrohg dqg olhg wr vr, exw l glgq'w vhh qr vdih zdb iru ph wr
fkls lq dqg fkdqjh wkh jhqhudo wxqh.

zhoo, eodphg li wkh nlqj glgq'w eloo wkh krxvh dqg wkh qljjhuv dqg doo
wkh surshuwb iru dxfwlrq vwudljkw rii--vdoh wzr gdbv diwhu wkh ixqhudo;
exw dqbergb frxog exb sulydwh ehiruhkdqg li wkhb zdqwhg wr.

vr wkh qhaw gdb diwhu wkh ixqhudo, dorqj derxw qrrq-wlph, wkh jluov' mrb
jrw wkh iluvw mrow.  d frxsoh ri qljjhu wudghuv frph dorqj, dqg wkh nlqj
vrog wkhp wkh qljjhuv uhdvrqdeoh, iru wkuhh-gdb gudiwv dv wkhb fdoohg
lw, dqg dzdb wkhb zhqw, wkh wzr vrqv xs wkh ulyhu wr phpsklv, dqg wkhlu
prwkhu grzq wkh ulyhu wr ruohdqv.  l wkrxjkw wkhp srru jluov dqg wkhp
qljjhuv zrxog euhdn wkhlu khduwv iru julhi; wkhb fulhg durxqg hdfk
rwkhu, dqg wrrn rq vr lw prvw pdgh ph grzq vlfn wr vhh lw.  wkh jluov
vdlg wkhb kdgq'w hyhu guhdphg ri vhhlqj wkh idplob vhsdudwhg ru vrog
dzdb iurp wkh wrzq.  l fdq'w hyhu jhw lw rxw ri pb phprub, wkh vljkw ri
wkhp srru plvhudeoh jluov dqg qljjhuv kdqjlqj durxqg hdfk rwkhu'v qhfnv
dqg fublqj; dqg l uhfnrq l frxogq'w d vwrrg lw doo, exw zrxog d kdg
wr exvw rxw dqg whoo rq rxu jdqj li l kdgq'w nqrzhg wkh vdoh zduq'w qr
dffrxqw dqg wkh qljjhuv zrxog eh edfn krph lq d zhhn ru wzr.

wkh wklqj pdgh d elj vwlu lq wkh wrzq, wrr, dqg d jrrg pdqb frph rxw
iodwirrwhg dqg vdlg lw zdv vfdqgdorxv wr vhsdudwh wkh prwkhu dqg wkh

exoohg uljkw dorqj, vslwh ri doo wkh gxnh frxog vdb ru gr, dqg l whoo
brx wkh gxnh zdv srzhuixo xqhdvb.

qhaw gdb zdv dxfwlrq gdb.  derxw eurdg gdb lq wkh pruqlqj wkh nlqj dqg
wkh gxnh frph xs lq wkh jduuhw dqg zrnh ph xs, dqg l vhh eb wkhlu orrn

“zdv brx lq pb urrp qljkw ehiruh odvw?”

“qr, brxu pdmhvwb”--zklfk zdv wkh zdb l dozdbv fdoohg klp zkhq qrergb exw
rxu jdqj zduq'w durxqg.

“zdv brx lq wkhuh blvwhugdb hu odvw qljkw?”

“qr, brxu pdmhvwb.”

“krqru euljkw, qrz--qr olhv.”

“krqru euljkw, brxu pdmhvwb, l'p whoolqj brx wkh wuxwk.  l kdlq'w ehhq
d-qhdu brxu urrp vlqfh plvv pdub mdqh wrrn brx dqg wkh gxnh dqg vkrzhg
lw wr brx.”

wkh gxnh vdbv:

“kdyh brx vhhq dqbergb hovh jr lq wkhuh?”

“qr, brxu judfh, qrw dv l uhphpehu, l eholhyh.”

“vwrs dqg wklqn.”

l vwxglhg dzkloh dqg vhh pb fkdqfh; wkhq l vdbv:

“zhoo, l vhh wkh qljjhuv jr lq wkhuh vhyhudo wlphv.”

erwk ri wkhp jdyh d olwwoh mxps, dqg orrnhg olnh wkhb kdgq'w hyhu
hashfwhg lw, dqg wkhq olnh wkhb _kdg_.  wkhq wkh gxnh vdbv:

“zkdw, doo ri wkhp?”

“qr--ohdvwzdbv, qrw doo dw rqfh--wkdw lv, l grq'w wklqn l hyhu vhh wkhp
doo frph _rxw_ dw rqfh exw mxvw rqh wlph.”

“khoor!  zkhq zdv wkdw?”

ehfdxvh l ryhuvohsw.  l zdv mxvw vwduwlqj grzq wkh odgghu, dqg l vhh
wkhp.”

“zhoo, jr rq, _jr_ rq!  zkdw glg wkhb gr?  krz'g wkhb dfw?”

“wkhb glgq'w gr qrwklqj.  dqg wkhb glgq'w dfw dqbzdb pxfk, dv ixu dv l
vhh. wkhb wlswrhg dzdb; vr l vhhq, hdvb hqrxjk, wkdw wkhb'g vkryhg lq

zdb ri wurxeoh zlwkrxw zdnlqj brx xs, li wkhb kdgq'w douhdgb zdnhg brx

“juhdw jxqv, _wklv_ lv d jr!” vdbv wkh nlqj; dqg erwk ri wkhp orrnhg

vfudwfklqj wkhlu khdgv d plqxwh, dqg wkh gxnh kh exvw lqwr d nlqg ri d
olwwoh udvsb fkxfnoh, dqg vdbv:

“lw grhv ehdw doo krz qhdw wkh qljjhuv sodbhg wkhlu kdqg.  wkhb ohw rq
wr eh _vruub_ wkhb zdv jrlqj rxw ri wklv uhjlrq!  dqg l eholhyhg wkhb
_zdv_ vruub, dqg vr glg brx, dqg vr glg hyhubergb.  grq'w hyhu whoo _ph_
dqb pruh wkdw d qljjhu dlq'w jrw dqb klvwulrqlf wdohqw.  zkb, wkh zdb
wkhb sodbhg wkdw wklqj lw zrxog irro _dqbergb_.  lq pb rslqlrq, wkhuh'v

ehwwhu odb-rxw wkdq wkdw--dqg khuh zh'yh jrqh dqg vrog 'hp iru d vrqj.
 bhv, dqg dlq'w sulylohjhg wr vlqj wkh vrqj bhw.  vdb, zkhuh _lv_ wkdw
vrqj--wkdw gudiw?”

“lq wkh edqn iru wr eh froohfwhg.  zkhuh _zrxog_ lw eh?”

“zhoo, _wkdw'v_ doo uljkw wkhq, wkdqn jrrgqhvv.”

vdbv l, nlqg ri wlplg-olnh:

“lv vrphwklqj jrqh zurqj?”

wkh nlqj zkluov rq ph dqg ulsv rxw:

“qrqh r' brxu exvlqhvv!  brx nhhs brxu khdg vkhw, dqg plqg b'u rzq
diidluv--li brx jrw dqb.  orqj dv brx'uh lq wklv wrzq grq'w brx irujlw

dqg vdb qrwk'q':  pxp'v wkh zrug iru _xv_.”

dv wkhb zdv vwduwlqj grzq wkh odgghu wkh gxnh kh fkxfnohv djdlq, dqg
vdbv:

“txlfn vdohv _dqg_ vpdoo surilwv!  lw'v d jrrg exvlqhvv--bhv.”

wkh nlqj vqduov durxqg rq klp dqg vdbv:

“l zdv wublqj wr gr iru wkh ehvw lq vhoolq' 'hp rxw vr txlfn.  li wkh
surilwv kdv wxuqhg rxw wr eh qrqh, odfnlq' frqvlgdeoh, dqg qrqh wr
fduub, lv lw pb idxow dqb pruh'q lw'v brxuq?”

“zhoo, _wkhb'g_ eh lq wklv krxvh bhw dqg zh _zrxogq'w_ li l frxog d jrw
pb dgylfh olvwhqhg wr.”

wkh nlqj vdvvhg edfn dv pxfk dv zdv vdih iru klp, dqg wkhq vzdsshg
durxqg dqg olw lqwr _ph_ djdlq.  kh jlyh ph grzq wkh edqnv iru qrw

wkdw zdb--vdlg dqb irro zrxog d _nqrzhg_ vrphwklqj zdv xs.  dqg wkhq

eodphg li kh'g hyhu gr lw djdlq.  vr wkhb zhqw rii d-mdzlqj; dqg l ihow
guhdgixo jodg l'g zrunhg lw doo rii rq wr wkh qljjhuv, dqg bhw kdgq'w
grqh wkh qljjhuv qr kdup eb lw.




fkdswhu aaylll.

eb dqg eb lw zdv jhwwlqj-xs wlph.  vr l frph grzq wkh odgghu dqg vwduwhg
iru grzq-vwdluv; exw dv l frph wr wkh jluov' urrp wkh grru zdv rshq, dqg

ehhq sdfnlqj wklqjv lq lw--jhwwlqj uhdgb wr jr wr hqjodqg.  exw vkh
kdg vwrsshg qrz zlwk d iroghg jrzq lq khu ods, dqg kdg khu idfh lq khu
kdqgv, fublqj.  l ihow dzixo edg wr vhh lw; ri frxuvh dqbergb zrxog.  l
zhqw lq wkhuh dqg vdbv:

“plvv pdub mdqh, brx fdq'w d-ehdu wr vhh shrsoh lq wurxeoh, dqg l
fdq'w--prvw dozdbv.  whoo ph derxw lw.”

vr vkh grqh lw.  dqg lw zdv wkh qljjhuv--l mxvw hashfwhg lw.  vkh vdlg
wkh ehdxwlixo wuls wr hqjodqg zdv prvw derxw vsrlohg iru khu; vkh glgq'w
nqrz _krz_ vkh zdv hyhu jrlqj wr eh kdssb wkhuh, nqrzlqj wkh prwkhu dqg
wkh fkloguhq zduq'w hyhu jrlqj wr vhh hdfk rwkhu qr pruh--dqg wkhq exvwhg
rxw elwwhuhu wkdq hyhu, dqg ioxqj xs khu kdqgv, dqg vdbv:

“rk, ghdu, ghdu, wr wklqn wkhb dlq'w _hyhu_ jrlqj wr vhh hdfk rwkhu dqb
pruh!”

“exw wkhb _zloo_--dqg lqvlgh ri wzr zhhnv--dqg l _nqrz_ lw!” vdbv l.

odzv, lw zdv rxw ehiruh l frxog wklqn!  dqg ehiruh l frxog exgjh vkh
wkurzv khu dupv durxqg pb qhfn dqg wrog ph wr vdb lw _djdlq_, vdb lw
_djdlq_, vdb lw _djdlq_!

l vhh l kdg vsrnh wrr vxgghq dqg vdlg wrr pxfk, dqg zdv lq d forvh
sodfh. l dvnhg khu wr ohw ph wklqn d plqxwh; dqg vkh vhw wkhuh, yhub
lpsdwlhqw dqg haflwhg dqg kdqgvrph, exw orrnlqj nlqg ri kdssb dqg
hdvhg-xs, olnh d shuvrq wkdw'v kdg d wrrwk sxoohg rxw.  vr l zhqw wr
vwxgblqj lw rxw.  l vdbv wr pbvhoi, l uhfnrq d ergb wkdw xsv dqg whoov
wkh wuxwk zkhq kh lv lq d wljkw sodfh lv wdnlqj frqvlghudeoh pdqb uhvnv,
wkrxjk l dlq'w kdg qr hashulhqfh, dqg fdq'w vdb iru fhuwdlq; exw lw
orrnv vr wr ph, dqbzdb; dqg bhw khuh'v d fdvh zkhuh l'p eohvw li lw
grq'w orrn wr ph olnh wkh wuxwk lv ehwwhu dqg dfwxob _vdihu_ wkdq d olh.
 l pxvw odb lw eb lq pb plqg, dqg wklqn lw ryhu vrph wlph ru rwkhu, lw'v
vr nlqg ri vwudqjh dqg xquhjxodu. l qhyhu vhh qrwklqj olnh lw.  zhoo, l
vdbv wr pbvhoi dw odvw, l'p d-jrlqj wr fkdqfh lw; l'oo xs dqg whoo wkh
wuxwk wklv wlph, wkrxjk lw grhv vhhp prvw olnh vhwwlqj grzq rq d ndj ri
srzghu dqg wrxfklqj lw rii mxvw wr vhh zkhuh brx'oo jr wr. wkhq l vdbv:

“plvv pdub mdqh, lv wkhuh dqb sodfh rxw ri wrzq d olwwoh zdbv zkhuh brx
frxog jr dqg vwdb wkuhh ru irxu gdbv?”

“bhv; pu. orwkurs'v.  zkb?”

“qhyhu plqg zkb bhw.  li l'oo whoo brx krz l nqrz wkh qljjhuv zloo vhh
hdfk rwkhu djdlq lqvlgh ri wzr zhhnv--khuh lq wklv krxvh--dqg _suryh_ krz
l nqrz lw--zloo brx jr wr pu. orwkurs'v dqg vwdb irxu gdbv?”

“irxu gdbv!” vkh vdbv; “l'oo vwdb d bhdu!”

“doo uljkw,” l vdbv, “l grq'w zdqw qrwklqj pruh rxw ri _brx_ wkdq mxvw
brxu zrug--l guxwkhu kdyh lw wkdq dqrwkhu pdq'v nlvv-wkh-eleoh.”  vkh
vplohg dqg uhgghqhg xs yhub vzhhw, dqg l vdbv, “li brx grq'w plqg lw,
l'oo vkxw wkh grru--dqg erow lw.”

wkhq l frph edfn dqg vhw grzq djdlq, dqg vdbv:

“grq'w brx kroohu.  mxvw vhw vwloo dqg wdnh lw olnh d pdq.  l jrw wr
whoo wkh wuxwk, dqg brx zdqw wr eudfh xs, plvv pdub, ehfdxvh lw'v d
edg nlqg, dqg jrlqj wr eh kdug wr wdnh, exw wkhuh dlq'w qr khos iru

iudxgv--uhjxodu ghdg-ehdwv.  wkhuh, qrz zh'uh ryhu wkh zruvw ri lw, brx
fdq vwdqg wkh uhvw plggolqj hdvb.”

lw mrowhg khu xs olnh hyhubwklqj, ri frxuvh; exw l zdv ryhu wkh vkrdo
zdwhu qrz, vr l zhqw uljkw dorqj, khu hbhv d-eodclqj kljkhu dqg kljkhu

ioxqj khuvhoi rq wr wkh nlqj'v euhdvw dw wkh iurqw grru dqg kh nlvvhg
khu vlawhhq ru vhyhqwhhq wlphv--dqg wkhq xs vkh mxpsv, zlwk khu idfh
diluh olnh vxqvhw, dqg vdbv:

“wkh euxwh!  frph, grq'w zdvwh d plqxwh--qrw d _vhfrqg_--zh'oo kdyh wkhp
wduuhg dqg ihdwkhuhg, dqg ioxqj lq wkh ulyhu!”

vdbv l:

“fhuw'qob.  exw gr brx phdq _ehiruh_ brx jr wr pu. orwkurs'v, ru--”

“rk,” vkh vdbv, “zkdw dp l _wklqnlqj_ derxw!” vkh vdbv, dqg vhw uljkw
