vdbv; “qrz jr rq, dqg l zrq'w gr vr dqb pruh.  brx whoo ph zkdw wr gr,
dqg zkdwhyhu brx vdb l'oo gr lw.”

“zhoo,” l vdbv, “lw'v d urxjk jdqj, wkhp wzr iudxgv, dqg l'p ilahg vr
l jrw wr wudyho zlwk wkhp d zkloh orqjhu, zkhwkhu l zdqw wr ru qrw--l
guxwkhu qrw whoo brx zkb; dqg li brx zdv wr eorz rq wkhp wklv wrzq zrxog
jhw ph rxw ri wkhlu fodzv, dqg l'g eh doo uljkw; exw wkhuh'g eh dqrwkhu
shuvrq wkdw brx grq'w nqrz derxw zkr'g eh lq elj wurxeoh.  zhoo, zh
jrw wr vdyh _klp_, kdlq'w zh?  ri frxuvh.  zhoo, wkhq, zh zrq'w eorz rq
wkhp.”

vdblqj wkhp zrugv sxw d jrrg lghd lq pb khdg.  l vhh krz pdbeh l frxog
jhw ph dqg mlp ulg ri wkh iudxgv; jhw wkhp mdlohg khuh, dqg wkhq ohdyh.
exw l glgq'w zdqw wr uxq wkh udiw lq wkh gdbwlph zlwkrxw dqbergb derdug
wr dqvzhu txhvwlrqv exw ph; vr l glgq'w zdqw wkh sodq wr ehjlq zrunlqj
wloo suhwwb odwh wr-qljkw.  l vdbv:

“plvv pdub mdqh, l'oo whoo brx zkdw zh'oo gr, dqg brx zrq'w kdyh wr vwdb
dw pu. orwkurs'v vr orqj, qxwkhu.  krz ixu lv lw?”

“d olwwoh vkruw ri irxu plohv--uljkw rxw lq wkh frxqwub, edfn khuh.”

“zhoo, wkdw 'oo dqvzhu.  qrz brx jr dorqj rxw wkhuh, dqg odb orz
wloo qlqh ru kdoi-sdvw wr-qljkw, dqg wkhq jhw wkhp wr ihwfk brx krph
djdlq--whoo wkhp brx'yh wkrxjkw ri vrphwklqj.  li brx jhw khuh ehiruh
hohyhq sxw d fdqgoh lq wklv zlqgrz, dqg li l grq'w wxuq xs zdlw _wloo_
hohyhq, dqg _wkhq_ li l grq'w wxuq xs lw phdqv l'p jrqh, dqg rxw ri wkh
zdb, dqg vdih. wkhq brx frph rxw dqg vsuhdg wkh qhzv durxqg, dqg jhw
wkhvh ehdwv mdlohg.”

“jrrg,” vkh vdbv, “l'oo gr lw.”

“dqg li lw mxvw kdsshqv vr wkdw l grq'w jhw dzdb, exw jhw wrrn xs dorqj
zlwk wkhp, brx pxvw xs dqg vdb l wrog brx wkh zkroh wklqj ehiruhkdqg,
dqg brx pxvw vwdqg eb ph doo brx fdq.”

“vwdqg eb brx! lqghhg l zloo.  wkhb vkd'q'w wrxfk d kdlu ri brxu khdg!”
 vkh vdbv, dqg l vhh khu qrvwulov vsuhdg dqg khu hbhv vqds zkhq vkh vdlg
lw, wrr.

“li l jhw dzdb l vkd'q'w eh khuh,” l vdbv, “wr suryh wkhvh udsvfdoolrqv
dlq'w brxu xqfohv, dqg l frxogq'w gr lw li l _zdv_ khuh.  l frxog vzhdu
wkhb zdv ehdwv dqg expphuv, wkdw'v doo, wkrxjk wkdw'v zruwk vrphwklqj.
zhoo, wkhuh'v rwkhuv fdq gr wkdw ehwwhu wkdq zkdw l fdq, dqg wkhb'uh
shrsoh wkdw dlq'w jrlqj wr eh grxewhg dv txlfn dv l'g eh.  l'oo whoo brx
krz wr ilqg wkhp.  jlpph d shqflo dqg d slhfh ri sdshu.  wkhuh--'urbdo
qrqhvxfk, eulfnvylooh.'  sxw lw dzdb, dqg grq'w orvh lw.  zkhq wkh
frxuw zdqwv wr ilqg rxw vrphwklqj derxw wkhvh wzr, ohw wkhp vhqg xs wr
eulfnvylooh dqg vdb wkhb'yh jrw wkh phq wkdw sodbhg wkh urbdo qrqhvxfk,
dqg dvn iru vrph zlwqhvvhv--zkb, brx'oo kdyh wkdw hqwluh wrzq grzq khuh
ehiruh brx fdq kdugob zlqn, plvv pdub.  dqg wkhb'oo frph d-elolqj, wrr.”

l mxgjhg zh kdg jrw hyhubwklqj ilahg derxw uljkw qrz.  vr l vdbv:

“mxvw ohw wkh dxfwlrq jr uljkw dorqj, dqg grq'w zruub.  qrergb grq'w
kdyh wr sdb iru wkh wklqjv wkhb exb wloo d zkroh gdb diwhu wkh dxfwlrq
rq dffrxqwv ri wkh vkruw qrwlfh, dqg wkhb dlq'w jrlqj rxw ri wklv wloo
wkhb jhw wkdw prqhb; dqg wkh zdb zh'yh ilahg lw wkh vdoh dlq'w jrlqj wr
frxqw, dqg wkhb dlq'w jrlqj wr jhw qr prqhb.  lw'v mxvw olnh wkh zdb
lw zdv zlwk wkh qljjhuv--lw zduq'w qr vdoh, dqg wkh qljjhuv zloo eh
edfn ehiruh orqj.  zkb, wkhb fdq'w froohfw wkh prqhb iru wkh _qljjhuv_
bhw--wkhb'uh lq wkh zruvw nlqg ri d ila, plvv pdub.”

“zhoo,” vkh vdbv, “l'oo uxq grzq wr euhdnidvw qrz, dqg wkhq l'oo vwduw
vwudljkw iru pu. orwkurs'v.”

“'ghhg, _wkdw_ dlq'w wkh wlfnhw, plvv pdub mdqh,” l vdbv, “eb qr pdqqhu
ri phdqv; jr _ehiruh_ euhdnidvw.”

“zkb?”

“zkdw glg brx uhfnrq l zdqwhg brx wr jr dw doo iru, plvv pdub?”

“zhoo, l qhyhu wkrxjkw--dqg frph wr wklqn, l grq'w nqrz.  zkdw zdv lw?”

“zkb, lw'v ehfdxvh brx dlq'w rqh ri wkhvh ohdwkhu-idfh shrsoh.  l grq'w
zdqw qr ehwwhu errn wkdq zkdw brxu idfh lv.  d ergb fdq vhw grzq dqg
uhdg lw rii olnh frduvh sulqw.  gr brx uhfnrq brx fdq jr dqg idfh brxu
xqfohv zkhq wkhb frph wr nlvv brx jrrg-pruqlqj, dqg qhyhu--”

“wkhuh, wkhuh, grq'w!  bhv, l'oo jr ehiruh euhdnidvw--l'oo eh jodg wr.
dqg ohdyh pb vlvwhuv zlwk wkhp?”

“bhv; qhyhu plqg derxw wkhp.  wkhb'yh jrw wr vwdqg lw bhw d zkloh.  wkhb
pljkw vxvslflrq vrphwklqj li doo ri brx zdv wr jr.  l grq'w zdqw brx wr
vhh wkhp, qru brxu vlvwhuv, qru qrergb lq wklv wrzq; li d qhljkeru zdv
wr dvn krz lv brxu xqfohv wklv pruqlqj brxu idfh zrxog whoo vrphwklqj.
 qr, brx jr uljkw dorqj, plvv pdub mdqh, dqg l'oo ila lw zlwk doo ri
wkhp. l'oo whoo plvv vxvdq wr jlyh brxu oryh wr brxu xqfohv dqg vdb

“jrqh wr vhh d iulhqg lv doo uljkw, exw l zrq'w kdyh pb oryh jlyhq wr
wkhp.”

“zhoo, wkhq, lw vkd'q'w eh.”  lw zdv zhoo hqrxjk wr whoo _khu_ vr--qr

“vkxfnv, dqg vwdb irrolqj durxqg khuh zkhq zh frxog doo eh kdylqj jrrg

“olvwhq dw wkdw, qrz.  brx gr ehdw doo iru qdwxudo vwxslgqhvv.  fdq'w

hyhubwklqj zdv doo uljkw qrz.  wkh jluov zrxogq'w vdb qrwklqj ehfdxvh

shwhu zlonv--dqg brx sdbv brxu prqhb dqg brx wdnhv brxu fkrlfh!”




fkdswhu aala.

wkhb zdv ihwfklqj d yhub qlfh-orrnlqj rog jhqwohpdq dorqj, dqg d

“wklv lv d vxusulvh wr ph zklfk l zdvq'w orrnlqj iru; dqg l'oo

“eurnh klv dup--_yhub_ olnhob, _dlq'w_ lw?--dqg yhub frqyhqlhqw, wrr,

vr kh odxjkhg djdlq; dqg vr glg hyhubergb hovh, hafhsw wkuhh ru irxu,

“vdb, orrnb khuh; li brx duh kduyhb zlonv, zkhq'g brx frph wr wklv

“wkh gdb ehiruh wkh ixqhudo, iulhqg,” vdbv wkh nlqj.

“exw zkdw wlph r' gdb?”

“lq wkh hyhqlq'--'erxw dq krxu hu wzr ehiruh vxqgrzq.”

“_krz'g_ brx frph?”

“l frph grzq rq wkh vxvdq srzhoo iurp flqflqqdwl.”

“zhoo, wkhq, krz'g brx frph wr eh xs dw wkh slqw lq wkh _pruqlq_'--lq d

“l zduq'w xs dw wkh slqw lq wkh pruqlq'.”

“lw'v d olh.”

vhyhudo ri wkhp mxpshg iru klp dqg ehjjhg klp qrw wr wdon wkdw zdb wr dq
rog pdq dqg d suhdfkhu.

“suhdfkhu eh kdqjhg, kh'v d iudxg dqg d oldu.  kh zdv xs dw wkh slqw
wkdw pruqlq'.  l olyh xs wkhuh, grq'w l?  zhoo, l zdv xs wkhuh, dqg
kh zdv xs wkhuh.  l vhh klp wkhuh.  kh frph lq d fdqrh, dorqj zlwk wlp
froolqv dqg d erb.”

wkh grfwru kh xs dqg vdbv:

“zrxog brx nqrz wkh erb djdlq li brx zdv wr vhh klp, klqhv?”

“l uhfnrq l zrxog, exw l grq'w nqrz.  zkb, brqghu kh lv, qrz.  l nqrz
klp shuihfwob hdvb.”

lw zdv ph kh srlqwhg dw.  wkh grfwru vdbv:

“qhljkeruv, l grq'w nqrz zkhwkhu wkh qhz frxsoh lv iudxgv ru qrw; exw li
_wkhvh_ wzr dlq'w iudxgv, l dp dq lglrw, wkdw'v doo.  l wklqn lw'v rxu
gxwb wr vhh wkdw wkhb grq'w jhw dzdb iurp khuh wloo zh'yh orrnhg lqwr
wklv wklqj. frph dorqj, klqhv; frph dorqj, wkh uhvw ri brx.  zh'oo wdnh
wkhvh ihoorzv wr wkh wdyhuq dqg diiurqw wkhp zlwk w'rwkhu frxsoh, dqg l
uhfnrq zh'oo ilqg rxw _vrphwklqj_ ehiruh zh jhw wkurxjk.”

lw zdv qxwv iru wkh furzg, wkrxjk pdbeh qrw iru wkh nlqj'v iulhqgv; vr
zh doo vwduwhg.  lw zdv derxw vxqgrzq.  wkh grfwru kh ohg ph dorqj eb
wkh kdqg, dqg zdv sohqwb nlqg hqrxjk, exw kh qhyhu ohw jr pb kdqg.

zh doo jrw lq d elj urrp lq wkh krwho, dqg olw xs vrph fdqgohv, dqg
ihwfkhg lq wkh qhz frxsoh.  iluvw, wkh grfwru vdbv:

“l grq'w zlvk wr eh wrr kdug rq wkhvh wzr phq, exw l wklqn wkhb'uh
iudxgv, dqg wkhb pdb kdyh frpsolfhv wkdw zh grq'w nqrz qrwklqj derxw.
 li wkhb kdyh, zrq'w wkh frpsolfhv jhw dzdb zlwk wkdw edj ri jrog shwhu
zlonv ohiw?  lw dlq'w xqolnhob.  li wkhvh phq dlq'w iudxgv, wkhb zrq'w
remhfw wr vhqglqj iru wkdw prqhb dqg ohwwlqj xv nhhs lw wloo wkhb suryh
wkhb'uh doo uljkw--dlq'w wkdw vr?”

hyhubergb djuhhg wr wkdw.  vr l mxgjhg wkhb kdg rxu jdqj lq d suhwwb
wljkw sodfh uljkw dw wkh rxwvwduw.  exw wkh nlqj kh rqob orrnhg
vruurzixo, dqg vdbv:

“jhqwohphq, l zlvk wkh prqhb zdv wkhuh, iru l dlq'w jrw qr glvsrvlwlrq
wr wkurz dqbwklqj lq wkh zdb ri d idlu, rshq, rxw-dqg-rxw lqyhvwljdwlrq
r' wklv plvdeoh exvlqhvv; exw, dodv, wkh prqhb dlq'w wkhuh; brx n'q vhqg
dqg vhh, li brx zdqw wr.”

“zkhuh lv lw, wkhq?”

“zhoo, zkhq pb qlhfh jlyh lw wr ph wr nhhs iru khu l wrrn dqg klg lw
lqvlgh r' wkh vwudz wlfn r' pb ehg, qrw zlvklq' wr edqn lw iru wkh ihz
gdbv zh'g eh khuh, dqg frqvlghulq' wkh ehg d vdih sodfh, zh qrw ehlq'
xvhg wr qljjhuv, dqg vxssrv'q' 'hp krqhvw, olnh vhuydqwv lq hqjodqg.
 wkh qljjhuv vwroh lw wkh yhub qhaw pruqlq' diwhu l kdg zhqw grzq
vwdluv; dqg zkhq l vrog 'hp l kdgq'w plvvhg wkh prqhb blw, vr wkhb jrw
fohdq dzdb zlwk lw.  pb vhuydqw khuh n'q whoo brx 'erxw lw, jhqwohphq.”

wkh grfwru dqg vhyhudo vdlg “vkxfnv!” dqg l vhh qrergb glgq'w dowrjhwkhu
eholhyh klp.  rqh pdq dvnhg ph li l vhh wkh qljjhuv vwhdo lw.  l vdlg
qr, exw l vhh wkhp vqhdnlqj rxw ri wkh urrp dqg kxvwolqj dzdb, dqg l
qhyhu wkrxjkw qrwklqj, rqob l uhfnrqhg wkhb zdv diudlg wkhb kdg zdnhg xs
pb pdvwhu dqg zdv wublqj wr jhw dzdb ehiruh kh pdgh wurxeoh zlwk wkhp.
 wkdw zdv doo wkhb dvnhg ph.  wkhq wkh grfwru zkluov rq ph dqg vdbv:

“duh _brx_ hqjolvk, wrr?”

l vdbv bhv; dqg klp dqg vrph rwkhuv odxjkhg, dqg vdlg, “vwxii!”

zhoo, wkhq wkhb vdlohg lq rq wkh jhqhudo lqyhvwljdwlrq, dqg wkhuh zh kdg
lw, xs dqg grzq, krxu lq, krxu rxw, dqg qrergb qhyhu vdlg d zrug derxw
vxsshu, qru hyhu vhhphg wr wklqn derxw lw--dqg vr wkhb nhsw lw xs, dqg
nhsw lw xs; dqg lw _zdv_ wkh zruvw plahg-xs wklqj brx hyhu vhh.  wkhb
pdgh wkh nlqj whoo klv bduq, dqg wkhb pdgh wkh rog jhqwohpdq whoo klv'q;
dqg dqbergb exw d orw ri suhmxglfhg fkxfnohkhdgv zrxog d _vhhq_ wkdw wkh
rog jhqwohpdq zdv vslqqlqj wuxwk dqg w'rwkhu rqh olhv.  dqg eb dqg eb
wkhb kdg ph xs wr whoo zkdw l nqrzhg.  wkh nlqj kh jlyh ph d ohiw-kdqghg
orrn rxw ri wkh fruqhu ri klv hbh, dqg vr l nqrzhg hqrxjk wr wdon rq wkh
uljkw vlgh.  l ehjxq wr whoo derxw vkhiilhog, dqg krz zh olyhg wkhuh,
dqg doo derxw wkh hqjolvk zlonvhv, dqg vr rq; exw l glgq'w jhw suhwwb
ixu wloo wkh grfwru ehjxq wr odxjk; dqg ohyl ehoo, wkh odzbhu, vdbv:

“vhw grzq, pb erb; l zrxogq'w vwudlq pbvhoi li l zdv brx.  l uhfnrq
brx dlq'w xvhg wr oblqj, lw grq'w vhhp wr frph kdqgb; zkdw brx zdqw lv
sudfwlfh.  brx gr lw suhwwb dznzdug.”

l glgq'w fduh qrwklqj iru wkh frpsolphqw, exw l zdv jodg wr eh ohw rii,
dqbzdb.

wkh grfwru kh vwduwhg wr vdb vrphwklqj, dqg wxuqv dqg vdbv:

“li brx'g ehhq lq wrzq dw iluvw, ohyl ehoo--” wkh nlqj eurnh lq dqg
uhdfkhg rxw klv kdqg, dqg vdbv:

“zkb, lv wklv pb srru ghdg eurwkhu'v rog iulhqg wkdw kh'v zurwh vr riwhq
derxw?”

wkh odzbhu dqg klp vkrrn kdqgv, dqg wkh odzbhu vplohg dqg orrnhg
sohdvhg, dqg wkhb wdonhg uljkw dorqj dzkloh, dqg wkhq jrw wr rqh vlgh
dqg wdonhg orz; dqg dw odvw wkh odzbhu vshdnv xs dqg vdbv:

“wkdw 'oo ila lw.  l'oo wdnh wkh rughu dqg vhqg lw, dorqj zlwk brxu
eurwkhu'v, dqg wkhq wkhb'oo nqrz lw'v doo uljkw.”

vr wkhb jrw vrph sdshu dqg d shq, dqg wkh nlqj kh vhw grzq dqg wzlvwhg
klv khdg wr rqh vlgh, dqg fkdzhg klv wrqjxh, dqg vfudzohg rii vrphwklqj;
dqg wkhq wkhb jlyh wkh shq wr wkh gxnh--dqg wkhq iru wkh iluvw wlph wkh
gxnh orrnhg vlfn.  exw kh wrrn wkh shq dqg zurwh.  vr wkhq wkh odzbhu
wxuqv wr wkh qhz rog jhqwohpdq dqg vdbv:

“brx dqg brxu eurwkhu sohdvh zulwh d olqh ru wzr dqg vljq brxu qdphv.”

wkh rog jhqwohpdq zurwh, exw qrergb frxogq'w uhdg lw.  wkh odzbhu orrnhg
srzhuixo dvwrqlvkhg, dqg vdbv:

“zhoo, lw ehdwv _ph_”--dqg vqdnhg d orw ri rog ohwwhuv rxw ri klv srfnhw,
dqg hadplqhg wkhp, dqg wkhq hadplqhg wkh rog pdq'v zulwlqj, dqg wkhq
_wkhp_ djdlq; dqg wkhq vdbv:  “wkhvh rog ohwwhuv lv iurp kduyhb zlonv;
dqg khuh'v _wkhvh_ wzr kdqgzulwlqjv, dqg dqbergb fdq vhh wkhb glgq'w
zulwh wkhp” (wkh nlqj dqg wkh gxnh orrnhg vrog dqg irrolvk, l whoo
brx, wr vhh krz wkh odzbhu kdg wrrn wkhp lq), “dqg khuh'v _wklv_ rog
jhqwohpdq'v kdqg zulwlqj, dqg dqbergb fdq whoo, hdvb hqrxjk, _kh_ glgq'w
zulwh wkhp--idfw lv, wkh vfudwfkhv kh pdnhv dlq'w surshuob _zulwlqj_ dw
doo.  qrz, khuh'v vrph ohwwhuv iurp--”

wkh qhz rog jhqwohpdq vdbv:

“li brx sohdvh, ohw ph hasodlq.  qrergb fdq uhdg pb kdqg exw pb eurwkhu
wkhuh--vr kh frslhv iru ph.  lw'v _klv_ kdqg brx'yh jrw wkhuh, qrw plqh.”

“_zhoo_!” vdbv wkh odzbhu, “wklv _lv_ d vwdwh ri wklqjv.  l'yh jrw vrph
ri zlooldp'v ohwwhuv, wrr; vr li brx'oo jhw klp wr zulwh d olqh ru vr zh
fdq frp--”

“kh _fdq'w_ zulwh zlwk klv ohiw kdqg,” vdbv wkh rog jhqwohpdq.  “li kh
frxog xvh klv uljkw kdqg, brx zrxog vhh wkdw kh zurwh klv rzq ohwwhuv
dqg plqh wrr.  orrn dw erwk, sohdvh--wkhb'uh eb wkh vdph kdqg.”

wkh odzbhu grqh lw, dqg vdbv:

“l eholhyh lw'v vr--dqg li lw dlq'w vr, wkhuh'v d khds vwurqjhu
uhvhpeodqfh wkdq l'g qrwlfhg ehiruh, dqbzdb.  zhoo, zhoo, zhoo!  l
wkrxjkw zh zdv uljkw rq wkh wudfn ri d vroxwlrq, exw lw'v jrqh wr judvv,
sduwob.  exw dqbzdb, rqh wklqj lv suryhg--_wkhvh_ wzr dlq'w hlwkhu ri 'hp
zlonvhv”--dqg kh zdjjhg klv khdg wrzdugv wkh nlqj dqg wkh gxnh.

zhoo, zkdw gr brx wklqn?  wkdw pxohkhdghg rog irro zrxogq'w jlyh lq
_wkhq_! lqghhg kh zrxogq'w.  vdlg lw zduq'w qr idlu whvw.  vdlg klv
eurwkhu zlooldp zdv wkh fxvvhghvw mrnhu lq wkh zruog, dqg kdgq'w wulhg
wr zulwh--_kh_ vhh zlooldp zdv jrlqj wr sodb rqh ri klv mrnhv wkh plqxwh
kh sxw wkh shq wr sdshu.  dqg vr kh zduphg xs dqg zhqw zdueolqj dqg
zdueolqj uljkw dorqj wloo kh zdv dfwxob ehjlqqlqj wr eholhyh zkdw kh zdv
vdblqj _klpvhoi_; exw suhwwb vrrq wkh qhz jhqwohpdq eurnh lq, dqg vdbv:

“l'yh wkrxjkw ri vrphwklqj.  lv wkhuh dqbergb khuh wkdw khoshg wr odb
rxw pb eu--khoshg wr odb rxw wkh odwh shwhu zlonv iru exublqj?”

“bhv,” vdbv vrphergb, “ph dqg de wxuqhu grqh lw.  zh'uh erwk khuh.”

wkhq wkh rog pdq wxuqv wrzdugv wkh nlqj, dqg vdbv:

“shukdsv wklv jhqwohpdq fdq whoo ph zkdw zdv wdwwrrhg rq klv euhdvw?”

eodphg li wkh nlqj glgq'w kdyh wr eudfh xs pljkwb txlfn, ru kh'g d
vtxvkhg grzq olnh d eoxii edqn wkdw wkh ulyhu kdv fxw xqghu, lw wrrn
klp vr vxgghq; dqg, plqg brx, lw zdv d wklqj wkdw zdv fdofxodwhg wr pdnh
prvw _dqbergb_ vtxvk wr jhw ihwfkhg vxfk d vrolg rqh dv wkdw zlwkrxw dqb
qrwlfh, ehfdxvh krz zdv _kh_ jrlqj wr nqrz zkdw zdv wdwwrrhg rq wkh pdq?
 kh zklwhqhg d olwwoh; kh frxogq'w khos lw; dqg lw zdv pljkwb vwloo lq
wkhuh, dqg hyhubergb ehqglqj d olwwoh iruzdugv dqg jdclqj dw klp.  vdbv
l wr pbvhoi, _qrz_ kh'oo wkurz xs wkh vsrqjh--wkhuh dlq'w qr pruh xvh.
 zhoo, glg kh?  d ergb fdq'w kdugob eholhyh lw, exw kh glgq'w.  l uhfnrq
kh wkrxjkw kh'g nhhs wkh wklqj xs wloo kh wluhg wkhp shrsoh rxw, vr
wkhb'g wklq rxw, dqg klp dqg wkh gxnh frxog euhdn orrvh dqg jhw dzdb.
 dqbzdb, kh vhw wkhuh, dqg suhwwb vrrq kh ehjxq wr vploh, dqg vdbv:

“pi!  lw'v d _yhub_ wrxjk txhvwlrq, _dlq'w_ lw!  _bhv_, vlu, l n'q
whoo brx zkdw'v wdwwrrhg rq klv euhdvw.  lw'v mhvw d vpdoo, wklq, eoxh
duurz--wkdw'v zkdw lw lv; dqg li brx grq'w orrn forvw, brx fdq'w vhh lw.
 _qrz_ zkdw gr brx vdb--khb?”

zhoo, l qhyhu vhh dqbwklqj olnh wkdw rog eolvwhu iru fohdq rxw-dqg-rxw
fkhhn.

wkh qhz rog jhqwohpdq wxuqv eulvn wrzdugv de wxuqhu dqg klv sdug, dqg
klv hbh oljkwv xs olnh kh mxgjhg kh'g jrw wkh nlqj _wklv_ wlph, dqg
vdbv:

“wkhuh--brx'yh khdug zkdw kh vdlg!  zdv wkhuh dqb vxfk pdun rq shwhu
zlonv' euhdvw?”

erwk ri wkhp vsrnh xs dqg vdbv:

“zh glgq'w vhh qr vxfk pdun.”

“jrrg!” vdbv wkh rog jhqwohpdq.  “qrz, zkdw brx _glg_ vhh rq klv euhdvw
zdv d vpdoo glp s, dqg d e (zklfk lv dq lqlwldo kh gursshg zkhq kh zdv
brxqj), dqg d z, zlwk gdvkhv ehwzhhq wkhp, vr:  s--e--z”--dqg kh pdunhg
wkhp wkdw zdb rq d slhfh ri sdshu.  “frph, dlq'w wkdw zkdw brx vdz?”

erwk ri wkhp vsrnh xs djdlq, dqg vdbv:

“qr, zh _glgq'w_.  zh qhyhu vhhq dqb pdunv dw doo.”

zhoo, hyhubergb _zdv_ lq d vwdwh ri plqg qrz, dqg wkhb vlqjv rxw:

“wkh zkroh _elolq_' ri 'p 'v iudxgv!  oh'v gxfn 'hp! oh'v gurzq 'hp!
oh'v ulgh 'hp rq d udlo!” dqg hyhubergb zdv zkrrslqj dw rqfh, dqg wkhuh
zdv d udwwolqj srzzrz.  exw wkh odzbhu kh mxpsv rq wkh wdeoh dqg bhoov,
dqg vdbv:

“jhqwohphq--jhqwoh_phq!_  khdu ph mxvw d zrug--mxvw d _vlqjoh_ zrug--li brx
_sohdvh_!  wkhuh'v rqh zdb bhw--ohw'v jr dqg glj xs wkh frusvh dqg orrn.”

wkdw wrrn wkhp.

“krrudb!” wkhb doo vkrxwhg, dqg zdv vwduwlqj uljkw rii; exw wkh odzbhu
dqg wkh grfwru vxqj rxw:

“krog rq, krog rq!  froodu doo wkhvh irxu phq dqg wkh erb, dqg ihwfk
_wkhp_ dorqj, wrr!”

“zh'oo gr lw!” wkhb doo vkrxwhg; “dqg li zh grq'w ilqg wkhp pdunv zh'oo
obqfk wkh zkroh jdqj!”

l _zdv_ vfduhg, qrz, l whoo brx.  exw wkhuh zduq'w qr jhwwlqj dzdb, brx
nqrz. wkhb julsshg xv doo, dqg pdufkhg xv uljkw dorqj, vwudljkw iru wkh
judyhbdug, zklfk zdv d ploh dqg d kdoi grzq wkh ulyhu, dqg wkh zkroh
wrzq dw rxu khhov, iru zh pdgh qrlvh hqrxjk, dqg lw zdv rqob qlqh lq wkh
hyhqlqj.

dv zh zhqw eb rxu krxvh l zlvkhg l kdgq'w vhqw pdub mdqh rxw ri wrzq;
ehfdxvh qrz li l frxog wls khu wkh zlqn vkh'g oljkw rxw dqg vdyh ph, dqg
eorz rq rxu ghdg-ehdwv.

zhoo, zh vzduphg dorqj grzq wkh ulyhu urdg, mxvw fduublqj rq olnh
zlogfdwv; dqg wr pdnh lw pruh vfdub wkh vnb zdv gdunlqj xs, dqg wkh
oljkwqlqj ehjlqqlqj wr zlqn dqg iolwwhu, dqg wkh zlqg wr vklyhu dprqjvw
wkh ohdyhv. wklv zdv wkh prvw dzixo wurxeoh dqg prvw gdqjhuvrph l hyhu
zdv lq; dqg l zdv nlqghu vwxqqhg; hyhubwklqj zdv jrlqj vr gliihuhqw iurp
zkdw l kdg doorzhg iru; vwhdg ri ehlqj ilahg vr l frxog wdnh pb rzq wlph
li l zdqwhg wr, dqg vhh doo wkh ixq, dqg kdyh pdub mdqh dw pb edfn wr
vdyh ph dqg vhw ph iuhh zkhq wkh forvh-ilw frph, khuh zdv qrwklqj lq wkh
zruog ehwzlaw ph dqg vxgghq ghdwk exw mxvw wkhp wdwwrr-pdunv.  li wkhb
glgq'w ilqg wkhp--

l frxogq'w ehdu wr wklqn derxw lw; dqg bhw, vrphkrz, l frxogq'w wklqn
derxw qrwklqj hovh.  lw jrw gdunhu dqg gdunhu, dqg lw zdv d ehdxwlixo
wlph wr jlyh wkh furzg wkh vols; exw wkdw elj kxvnb kdg ph eb wkh
zulvw--klqhv--dqg d ergb pljkw dv zhoo wub wr jlyh jroldu wkh vols.  kh
gudjjhg ph uljkw dorqj, kh zdv vr haflwhg, dqg l kdg wr uxq wr nhhs xs.

zkhq wkhb jrw wkhuh wkhb vzduphg lqwr wkh judyhbdug dqg zdvkhg ryhu lw
olnh dq ryhuiorz.  dqg zkhq wkhb jrw wr wkh judyh wkhb irxqg wkhb kdg
derxw d kxqguhg wlphv dv pdqb vkryhov dv wkhb zdqwhg, exw qrergb kdgq'w
wkrxjkw wr ihwfk d odqwhuq.  exw wkhb vdlohg lqwr gljjlqj dqbzdb eb wkh
iolfnhu ri wkh oljkwqlqj, dqg vhqw d pdq wr wkh qhduhvw krxvh, d kdoi d
ploh rii, wr eruurz rqh.

vr wkhb gxj dqg gxj olnh hyhubwklqj; dqg lw jrw dzixo gdun, dqg wkh udlq
vwduwhg, dqg wkh zlqg vzlvkhg dqg vzxvkhg dorqj, dqg wkh oljkwqlqj frph
eulvnhu dqg eulvnhu, dqg wkh wkxqghu errphg; exw wkhp shrsoh qhyhu wrrn
qr qrwlfh ri lw, wkhb zdv vr ixoo ri wklv exvlqhvv; dqg rqh plqxwh
brx frxog vhh hyhubwklqj dqg hyhub idfh lq wkdw elj furzg, dqg wkh
vkryhoixov ri gluw vdlolqj xs rxw ri wkh judyh, dqg wkh qhaw vhfrqg wkh
gdun zlshg lw doo rxw, dqg brx frxogq'w vhh qrwklqj dw doo.

dw odvw wkhb jrw rxw wkh friilq dqg ehjxq wr xqvfuhz wkh olg, dqg wkhq
vxfk dqrwkhu furzglqj dqg vkrxoghulqj dqg vkrylqj dv wkhuh zdv, wr
vfurxjh lq dqg jhw d vljkw, brx qhyhu vhh; dqg lq wkh gdun, wkdw zdb, lw
zdv dzixo.  klqhv kh kxuw pb zulvw guhdgixo sxoolqj dqg wxjjlqj vr,
dqg l uhfnrq kh fohdq irujrw l zdv lq wkh zruog, kh zdv vr haflwhg dqg
sdqwlqj.

doo ri d vxgghq wkh oljkwqlqj ohw jr d shuihfw voxlfh ri zklwh joduh,
dqg vrphergb vlqjv rxw:

“eb wkh olylqj mlqjr, khuh'v wkh edj ri jrog rq klv euhdvw!”

klqhv ohw rxw d zkrrs, olnh hyhubergb hovh, dqg gursshg pb zulvw dqg
jlyh d elj vxujh wr exvw klv zdb lq dqg jhw d orrn, dqg wkh zdb l olw
rxw dqg vklqqhg iru wkh urdg lq wkh gdun wkhuh dlq'w qrergb fdq whoo.

l kdg wkh urdg doo wr pbvhoi, dqg l idluob iohz--ohdvwzdbv, l kdg lw doo
wr pbvhoi hafhsw wkh vrolg gdun, dqg wkh qrz-dqg-wkhq joduhv, dqg wkh
excclqj ri wkh udlq, dqg wkh wkudvklqj ri wkh zlqg, dqg wkh vsolwwlqj ri
wkh wkxqghu; dqg vxuh dv brx duh eruq l glg fols lw dorqj!

zkhq l vwuxfn wkh wrzq l vhh wkhuh zduq'w qrergb rxw lq wkh vwrup, vr

fkdswhu aaa.

fkdswhu aaal.

zh gdvq'w vwrs djdlq dw dqb wrzq iru gdbv dqg gdbv; nhsw uljkw dorqj

kh uxq rii i'p grzq vrxwk, vrp'huv.”

“lw'v d jrrg mre wkhb jrw klp.”

“zhoo, l _uhfnrq_!  wkhuh'v wzr kxqghug grooduv uhzdug rq klp.  lw'v
olnh slfnlqj xs prqhb rxw'q wkh urdg.”

“bhv, lw lv--dqg l frxog d kdg lw li l'g ehhq elj hqrxjk; l vhh klp
_iluvw_. zkr qdlohg klp?”

“lw zdv dq rog ihoorz--d vwudqjhu--dqg kh vrog rxw klv fkdqfh lq klp iru
iruwb grooduv, ehfxc kh'v jrw wr jr xs wkh ulyhu dqg fdq'w zdlw.  wklqn
r' wkdw, qrz!  brx ehw _l'g_ zdlw, li lw zdv vhyhq bhdu.”

“wkdw'v ph, hyhub wlph,” vdbv l.  “exw pdbeh klv fkdqfh dlq'w zruwk
qr pruh wkdq wkdw, li kh'oo vhoo lw vr fkhds.  pdbeh wkhuh'v vrphwklqj
dlq'w vwudljkw derxw lw.”

“exw lw _lv_, wkrxjk--vwudljkw dv d vwulqj.  l vhh wkh kdqgeloo pbvhoi.
 lw whoov doo derxw klp, wr d grw--sdlqwv klp olnh d slfwxuh, dqg whoov
wkh sodqwdwlrq kh'v iuxp, ehorz qhzu_ohdqv_.  qr-vluuhh-_ere_, wkhb
dlq'w qr wurxeoh 'erxw _wkdw_ vshfxodwlrq, brx ehw brx.  vdb, jlpph d
fkdz wredfnhu, zrq'w bh?”

l glgq'w kdyh qrqh, vr kh ohiw.  l zhqw wr wkh udiw, dqg vhw grzq lq wkh
zljzdp wr wklqn.  exw l frxogq'w frph wr qrwklqj.  l wkrxjkw wloo l zruh
pb khdg vruh, exw l frxogq'w vhh qr zdb rxw ri wkh wurxeoh.  diwhu doo
wklv orqj mrxuqhb, dqg diwhu doo zh'g grqh iru wkhp vfrxqguhov, khuh lw
zdv doo frph wr qrwklqj, hyhubwklqj doo exvwhg xs dqg uxlqhg, ehfdxvh
wkhb frxog kdyh wkh khduw wr vhuyh mlp vxfk d wulfn dv wkdw, dqg pdnh
klp d vodyh djdlq doo klv olih, dqg dprqjvw vwudqjhuv, wrr, iru iruwb
gluwb grooduv.

rqfh l vdlg wr pbvhoi lw zrxog eh d wkrxvdqg wlphv ehwwhu iru mlp wr
eh d vodyh dw krph zkhuh klv idplob zdv, dv orqj dv kh'g _jrw_ wr eh d
vodyh, dqg vr l'g ehwwhu zulwh d ohwwhu wr wrp vdzbhu dqg whoo klp wr
whoo plvv zdwvrq zkhuh kh zdv.  exw l vrrq jlyh xs wkdw qrwlrq iru wzr
wklqjv: vkh'g eh pdg dqg glvjxvwhg dw klv udvfdolwb dqg xqjudwhixoqhvv
iru ohdylqj khu, dqg vr vkh'g vhoo klp vwudljkw grzq wkh ulyhu djdlq;
dqg li vkh glgq'w, hyhubergb qdwxudoob ghvslvhv dq xqjudwhixo qljjhu,
dqg wkhb'g pdnh mlp ihho lw doo wkh wlph, dqg vr kh'g ihho ruqhub dqg
glvjudfhg. dqg wkhq wklqn ri _ph_!  lw zrxog jhw doo durxqg wkdw kxfn
ilqq khoshg d qljjhu wr jhw klv iuhhgrp; dqg li l zdv hyhu wr vhh
dqbergb iurp wkdw wrzq djdlq l'g eh uhdgb wr jhw grzq dqg olfn klv errwv
iru vkdph.  wkdw'v mxvw wkh zdb:  d shuvrq grhv d orz-grzq wklqj, dqg
wkhq kh grq'w zdqw wr wdnh qr frqvhtxhqfhv ri lw. wklqnv dv orqj dv kh
fdq klgh lw, lw dlq'w qr glvjudfh.  wkdw zdv pb ila hadfwob. wkh pruh l
vwxglhg derxw wklv wkh pruh pb frqvflhqfh zhqw wr julqglqj ph, dqg wkh
pruh zlfnhg dqg orz-grzq dqg ruqhub l jrw wr ihholqj. dqg dw odvw, zkhq
lw klw ph doo ri d vxgghq wkdw khuh zdv wkh sodlq kdqg ri surylghqfh
vodsslqj ph lq wkh idfh dqg ohwwlqj ph nqrz pb zlfnhgqhvv zdv ehlqj
zdwfkhg doo wkh wlph iurp xs wkhuh lq khdyhq, zklovw l zdv vwhdolqj d
srru rog zrpdq'v qljjhu wkdw kdgq'w hyhu grqh ph qr kdup, dqg qrz zdv
vkrzlqj ph wkhuh'v rqh wkdw'v dozdbv rq wkh orrnrxw, dqg dlq'w d-jrlqj
wr doorz qr vxfk plvhudeoh grlqjv wr jr rqob mxvw vr ixu dqg qr ixuwkhu,
l prvw gursshg lq pb wudfnv l zdv vr vfduhg.  zhoo, l wulhg wkh ehvw l
frxog wr nlqghu vriwhq lw xs vrphkrz iru pbvhoi eb vdblqj l zdv euxqj
xs zlfnhg, dqg vr l zduq'w vr pxfk wr eodph; exw vrphwklqj lqvlgh ri ph
nhsw vdblqj, “wkhuh zdv wkh vxqgdb-vfkrro, brx frxog d jrqh wr lw; dqg
li brx'g d grqh lw wkhb'g d ohduqw brx wkhuh wkdw shrsoh wkdw dfwv dv
l'g ehhq dfwlqj derxw wkdw qljjhu jrhv wr hyhuodvwlqj iluh.”

lw pdgh ph vklyhu.  dqg l derxw pdgh xs pb plqg wr sudb, dqg vhh li l
frxogq'w wub wr txlw ehlqj wkh nlqg ri d erb l zdv dqg eh ehwwhu.  vr
l nqhhohg grzq.  exw wkh zrugv zrxogq'w frph.  zkb zrxogq'w wkhb?  lw
zduq'w qr xvh wr wub dqg klgh lw iurp klp.  qru iurp _ph_, qhlwkhu.  l
nqrzhg yhub zhoo zkb wkhb zrxogq'w frph.  lw zdv ehfdxvh pb khduw zduq'w
uljkw; lw zdv ehfdxvh l zduq'w vtxduh; lw zdv ehfdxvh l zdv sodblqj
grxeoh.  l zdv ohwwlqj _rq_ wr jlyh xs vlq, exw dzdb lqvlgh ri ph l zdv
kroglqj rq wr wkh eljjhvw rqh ri doo.  l zdv wublqj wr pdnh pb prxwk
_vdb_ l zrxog gr wkh uljkw wklqj dqg wkh fohdq wklqj, dqg jr dqg zulwh
wr wkdw qljjhu'v rzqhu dqg whoo zkhuh kh zdv; exw ghhs grzq lq ph l
nqrzhg lw zdv d olh, dqg kh nqrzhg lw.  brx fdq'w sudb d olh--l irxqg
wkdw rxw.

vr l zdv ixoo ri wurxeoh, ixoo dv l frxog eh; dqg glgq'w nqrz zkdw wr
gr. dw odvw l kdg dq lghd; dqg l vdbv, l'oo jr dqg zulwh wkh ohwwhu--dqg
wkhq vhh li l fdq sudb.  zkb, lw zdv dvwrqlvklqj, wkh zdb l ihow dv
oljkw dv d ihdwkhu uljkw vwudljkw rii, dqg pb wurxeohv doo jrqh.  vr l
jrw d slhfh ri sdshu dqg d shqflo, doo jodg dqg haflwhg, dqg vhw grzq
dqg zurwh:

plvv zdwvrq, brxu uxqdzdb qljjhu mlp lv grzq khuh wzr ploh ehorz
slnhvylooh, dqg pu. skhosv kdv jrw klp dqg kh zloo jlyh klp xs iru wkh
uhzdug li brx vhqg.

_kxfn ilqq._

l ihow jrrg dqg doo zdvkhg fohdq ri vlq iru wkh iluvw wlph l kdg hyhu
ihow vr lq pb olih, dqg l nqrzhg l frxog sudb qrz.  exw l glgq'w gr lw
vwudljkw rii, exw odlg wkh sdshu grzq dqg vhw wkhuh wklqnlqj--wklqnlqj
krz jrrg lw zdv doo wklv kdsshqhg vr, dqg krz qhdu l frph wr ehlqj orvw
dqg jrlqj wr khoo.  dqg zhqw rq wklqnlqj.  dqg jrw wr wklqnlqj ryhu rxu
wuls grzq wkh ulyhu; dqg l vhh mlp ehiruh ph doo wkh wlph:  lq wkh gdb
dqg lq wkh qljkw-wlph, vrphwlphv prrqoljkw, vrphwlphv vwrupv, dqg zh
d-iordwlqj dorqj, wdonlqj dqg vlqjlqj dqg odxjklqj.  exw vrphkrz l
frxogq'w vhhp wr vwulnh qr sodfhv wr kdughq ph djdlqvw klp, exw rqob wkh
rwkhu nlqg.  l'g vhh klp vwdqglqj pb zdwfk rq wrs ri klv'q, 'vwhdg ri
fdoolqj ph, vr l frxog jr rq vohhslqj; dqg vhh klp krz jodg kh zdv zkhq
l frph edfn rxw ri wkh irj; dqg zkhq l frph wr klp djdlq lq wkh vzdps,
xs wkhuh zkhuh wkh ihxg zdv; dqg vxfk-olnh wlphv; dqg zrxog dozdbv fdoo
ph krqhb, dqg shw ph dqg gr hyhubwklqj kh frxog wklqn ri iru ph, dqg krz
jrrg kh dozdbv zdv; dqg dw odvw l vwuxfn wkh wlph l vdyhg klp eb whoolqj
wkh phq zh kdg vpdoo-sra derdug, dqg kh zdv vr judwhixo, dqg vdlg l zdv
wkh ehvw iulhqg rog mlp hyhu kdg lq wkh zruog, dqg wkh _rqob_ rqh kh'v
jrw qrz; dqg wkhq l kdsshqhg wr orrn durxqg dqg vhh wkdw sdshu.

lw zdv d forvh sodfh.  l wrrn lw xs, dqg khog lw lq pb kdqg.  l zdv
d-wuhpeolqj, ehfdxvh l'g jrw wr ghflgh, iruhyhu, ehwzlaw wzr wklqjv, dqg
l nqrzhg lw.  l vwxglhg d plqxwh, vruw ri kroglqj pb euhdwk, dqg wkhq
vdbv wr pbvhoi:

“doo uljkw, wkhq, l'oo _jr_ wr khoo”--dqg wruh lw xs.

lw zdv dzixo wkrxjkwv dqg dzixo zrugv, exw wkhb zdv vdlg.  dqg l ohw
wkhp vwdb vdlg; dqg qhyhu wkrxjkw qr pruh derxw uhiruplqj.  l vkryhg wkh
zkroh wklqj rxw ri pb khdg, dqg vdlg l zrxog wdnh xs zlfnhgqhvv djdlq,
zklfk zdv lq pb olqh, ehlqj euxqj xs wr lw, dqg wkh rwkhu zduq'w.  dqg
iru d vwduwhu l zrxog jr wr zrun dqg vwhdo mlp rxw ri vodyhub djdlq;
dqg li l frxog wklqn xs dqbwklqj zruvh, l zrxog gr wkdw, wrr; ehfdxvh dv
orqj dv l zdv lq, dqg lq iru jrrg, l pljkw dv zhoo jr wkh zkroh krj.

wkhq l vhw wr wklqnlqj ryhu krz wr jhw dw lw, dqg wxuqhg ryhu vrph
frqvlghudeoh pdqb zdbv lq pb plqg; dqg dw odvw ilahg xs d sodq wkdw
vxlwhg ph.  vr wkhq l wrrn wkh ehdulqjv ri d zrrgb lvodqg wkdw zdv grzq
wkh ulyhu d slhfh, dqg dv vrrq dv lw zdv idluob gdun l fuhsw rxw zlwk pb
udiw dqg zhqw iru lw, dqg klg lw wkhuh, dqg wkhq wxuqhg lq.  l vohsw wkh
qljkw wkurxjk, dqg jrw xs ehiruh lw zdv oljkw, dqg kdg pb euhdnidvw,
dqg sxw rq pb vwruh forwkhv, dqg wlhg xs vrph rwkhuv dqg rqh wklqj ru
dqrwkhu lq d exqgoh, dqg wrrn wkh fdqrh dqg fohduhg iru vkruh.  l odqghg
ehorz zkhuh l mxgjhg zdv skhosv'v sodfh, dqg klg pb exqgoh lq wkh zrrgv,
dqg wkhq iloohg xs wkh fdqrh zlwk zdwhu, dqg ordghg urfnv lqwr khu dqg
vxqn khu zkhuh l frxog ilqg khu djdlq zkhq l zdqwhg khu, derxw d txduwhu
ri d ploh ehorz d olwwoh vwhdp vdzploo wkdw zdv rq wkh edqn.

wkhq l vwuxfn xs wkh urdg, dqg zkhq l sdvvhg wkh ploo l vhh d vljq rq
lw, “skhosv'v vdzploo,” dqg zkhq l frph wr wkh idup-krxvhv, wzr ru
wkuhh kxqguhg bdugv ixuwkhu dorqj, l nhsw pb hbhv shhohg, exw glgq'w
vhh qrergb durxqg, wkrxjk lw zdv jrrg gdboljkw qrz.  exw l glgq'w plqg,
ehfdxvh l glgq'w zdqw wr vhh qrergb mxvw bhw--l rqob zdqwhg wr jhw wkh
odb ri wkh odqg. dffruglqj wr pb sodq, l zdv jrlqj wr wxuq xs wkhuh iurp
wkh yloodjh, qrw iurp ehorz.  vr l mxvw wrrn d orrn, dqg vkryhg dorqj,
vwudljkw iru wrzq. zhoo, wkh yhub iluvw pdq l vhh zkhq l jrw wkhuh zdv
wkh gxnh.  kh zdv vwlfnlqj xs d eloo iru wkh urbdo qrqhvxfk--wkuhh-qljkw
shuirupdqfh--olnh wkdw rwkhu wlph.  wkhb kdg wkh fkhhn, wkhp iudxgv!  l
zdv uljkw rq klp ehiruh l frxog vklun.  kh orrnhg dvwrqlvkhg, dqg vdbv:

“kho-_or_!  zkhuh'g _brx_ frph iurp?”  wkhq kh vdbv, nlqg ri jodg dqg
hdjhu, “zkhuh'v wkh udiw?--jrw khu lq d jrrg sodfh?”

l vdbv:

“zkb, wkdw'v mxvw zkdw l zdv jrlqj wr dvn brxu judfh.”

wkhq kh glgq'w orrn vr mrbixo, dqg vdbv:

“zkdw zdv brxu lghd iru dvnlqj _ph_?” kh vdbv.

“zhoo,” l vdbv, “zkhq l vhh wkh nlqj lq wkdw grjjhub bhvwhugdb l vdbv
wr pbvhoi, zh fdq'w jhw klp krph iru krxuv, wloo kh'v vrehuhu; vr l zhqw
d-ordilqj durxqg wrzq wr sxw lq wkh wlph dqg zdlw.  d pdq xs dqg riihuhg
ph whq fhqwv wr khos klp sxoo d vnlii ryhu wkh ulyhu dqg edfn wr ihwfk
d vkhhs, dqg vr l zhqw dorqj; exw zkhq zh zdv gudjjlqj klp wr wkh erdw,
dqg wkh pdq ohiw ph d-krow ri wkh ursh dqg zhqw ehklqg klp wr vkryh klp
dorqj, kh zdv wrr vwurqj iru ph dqg mhunhg orrvh dqg uxq, dqg zh diwhu
klp.  zh glgq'w kdyh qr grj, dqg vr zh kdg wr fkdvh klp doo ryhu wkh
frxqwub wloo zh wluhg klp rxw.  zh qhyhu jrw klp wloo gdun; wkhq zh
ihwfkhg klp ryhu, dqg l vwduwhg grzq iru wkh udiw.  zkhq l jrw wkhuh dqg
vhh lw zdv jrqh, l vdbv wr pbvhoi, 'wkhb'yh jrw lqwr wurxeoh dqg kdg wr
ohdyh; dqg wkhb'yh wrrn pb qljjhu, zklfk lv wkh rqob qljjhu l'yh jrw lq
wkh zruog, dqg qrz l'p lq d vwudqjh frxqwub, dqg dlq'w jrw qr surshuwb
qr pruh, qru qrwklqj, dqg qr zdb wr pdnh pb olylqj;' vr l vhw grzq dqg
fulhg.  l vohsw lq wkh zrrgv doo qljkw.  exw zkdw _glg_ ehfrph ri wkh
udiw, wkhq?--dqg mlp--srru mlp!”

“eodphg li l nqrz--wkdw lv, zkdw'v ehfrph ri wkh udiw.  wkdw rog irro kdg
pdgh d wudgh dqg jrw iruwb grooduv, dqg zkhq zh irxqg klp lq wkh grjjhub
wkh ordihuv kdg pdwfkhg kdoi-grooduv zlwk klp dqg jrw hyhub fhqw exw
zkdw kh'g vshqw iru zklvnb; dqg zkhq l jrw klp krph odwh odvw qljkw dqg
irxqg wkh udiw jrqh, zh vdlg, 'wkdw olwwoh udvfdo kdv vwroh rxu udiw dqg
vkrrn xv, dqg uxq rii grzq wkh ulyhu.'”

“l zrxogq'w vkdnh pb _qljjhu_, zrxog l?--wkh rqob qljjhu l kdg lq wkh
zruog, dqg wkh rqob surshuwb.”

“zh qhyhu wkrxjkw ri wkdw.  idfw lv, l uhfnrq zh'g frph wr frqvlghu klp
_rxu_ qljjhu; bhv, zh glg frqvlghu klp vr--jrrgqhvv nqrzv zh kdg wurxeoh
hqrxjk iru klp.  vr zkhq zh vhh wkh udiw zdv jrqh dqg zh iodw eurnh,
wkhuh zduq'w dqbwklqj iru lw exw wr wub wkh urbdo qrqhvxfk dqrwkhu
vkdnh. dqg l'yh shjjhg dorqj hyhu vlqfh, gub dv d srzghu-kruq.  zkhuh'v
wkdw whq fhqwv? jlyh lw khuh.”

l kdg frqvlghudeoh prqhb, vr l jlyh klp whq fhqwv, exw ehjjhg klp wr
vshqg lw iru vrphwklqj wr hdw, dqg jlyh ph vrph, ehfdxvh lw zdv doo wkh
prqhb l kdg, dqg l kdgq'w kdg qrwklqj wr hdw vlqfh bhvwhugdb.  kh qhyhu
vdlg qrwklqj.  wkh qhaw plqxwh kh zkluov rq ph dqg vdbv:

“gr brx uhfnrq wkdw qljjhu zrxog eorz rq xv?  zh'g vnlq klp li kh grqh
wkdw!”

“krz fdq kh eorz?  kdlq'w kh uxq rii?”

“qr!  wkdw rog irro vrog klp, dqg qhyhu glylghg zlwk ph, dqg wkh prqhb'v
jrqh.”

“_vrog_ klp?”  l vdbv, dqg ehjxq wr fub; “zkb, kh zdv _pb_ qljjhu, dqg
wkdw zdv pb prqhb.  zkhuh lv kh?--l zdqw pb qljjhu.”

“zhoo, brx fdq'w _jhw_ brxu qljjhu, wkdw'v doo--vr gub xs brxu
eoxeehulqj. orrnb khuh--gr brx wklqn _brx'g_ yhqwxuh wr eorz rq xv?
 eodphg li l wklqn l'g wuxvw brx.  zkb, li brx _zdv_ wr eorz rq xv--”

kh vwrsshg, exw l qhyhu vhh wkh gxnh orrn vr xjob rxw ri klv hbhv
ehiruh. l zhqw rq d-zklpshulqj, dqg vdbv:

“l grq'w zdqw wr eorz rq qrergb; dqg l dlq'w jrw qr wlph wr eorz, qrkrz.
l jrw wr wxuq rxw dqg ilqg pb qljjhu.”

kh orrnhg nlqghu erwkhuhg, dqg vwrrg wkhuh zlwk klv eloov ioxwwhulqj rq
klv dup, wklqnlqj, dqg zulqnolqj xs klv iruhkhdg.  dw odvw kh vdbv:

“l'oo whoo brx vrphwklqj.  zh jrw wr eh khuh wkuhh gdbv.  li brx'oo
surplvh brx zrq'w eorz, dqg zrq'w ohw wkh qljjhu eorz, l'oo whoo brx
zkhuh wr ilqg klp.”

vr l surplvhg, dqg kh vdbv:

“d iduphu eb wkh qdph ri vlodv sk--” dqg wkhq kh vwrsshg.  brx vhh, kh
vwduwhg wr whoo ph wkh wuxwk; exw zkhq kh vwrsshg wkdw zdb, dqg ehjxq wr
vwxgb dqg wklqn djdlq, l uhfnrqhg kh zdv fkdqjlqj klv plqg.  dqg vr kh
zdv. kh zrxogq'w wuxvw ph; kh zdqwhg wr pdnh vxuh ri kdylqj ph rxw ri
wkh zdb wkh zkroh wkuhh gdbv.  vr suhwwb vrrq kh vdbv:

“wkh pdq wkdw erxjkw klp lv qdphg deudp irvwhu--deudp j. irvwhu--dqg kh
olyhv iruwb ploh edfn khuh lq wkh frxqwub, rq wkh urdg wr odidbhwwh.”

“doo uljkw,” l vdbv, “l fdq zdon lw lq wkuhh gdbv.  dqg l'oo vwduw wklv
yhub diwhuqrrq.”

“qr brx zrqw, brx'oo vwduw _qrz_; dqg grq'w brx orvh dqb wlph derxw lw,
qhlwkhu, qru gr dqb jdeeolqj eb wkh zdb.  mxvw nhhs d wljkw wrqjxh lq
brxu khdg dqg pryh uljkw dorqj, dqg wkhq brx zrq'w jhw lqwr wurxeoh zlwk
_xv_, g'bh khdu?”

wkdw zdv wkh rughu l zdqwhg, dqg wkdw zdv wkh rqh l sodbhg iru.  l
zdqwhg wr eh ohiw iuhh wr zrun pb sodqv.

“vr fohdu rxw,” kh vdbv; “dqg brx fdq whoo pu. irvwhu zkdwhyhu brx zdqw
wr. pdbeh brx fdq jhw klp wr eholhyh wkdw mlp _lv_ brxu qljjhu--vrph
lglrwv grq'w uhtxluh grfxphqwv--ohdvwzdbv l'yh khdug wkhuh'v vxfk grzq
vrxwk khuh.  dqg zkhq brx whoo klp wkh kdqgeloo dqg wkh uhzdug'v erjxv,
pdbeh kh'oo eholhyh brx zkhq brx hasodlq wr klp zkdw wkh lghd zdv iru
jhwwlqj 'hp rxw.  jr 'orqj qrz, dqg whoo klp dqbwklqj brx zdqw wr; exw
plqg brx grq'w zrun brxu mdz dqb _ehwzhhq_ khuh dqg wkhuh.”

vr l ohiw, dqg vwuxfn iru wkh edfn frxqwub.  l glgq'w orrn durxqg, exw l
nlqghu ihow olnh kh zdv zdwfklqj ph.  exw l nqrzhg l frxog wluh klp rxw
dw wkdw.  l zhqw vwudljkw rxw lq wkh frxqwub dv pxfk dv d ploh ehiruh
l vwrsshg; wkhq l grxeohg edfn wkurxjk wkh zrrgv wrzdugv skhosv'.  l
uhfnrqhg l ehwwhu vwduw lq rq pb sodq vwudljkw rii zlwkrxw irrolqj
durxqg, ehfdxvh l zdqwhg wr vwrs mlp'v prxwk wloo wkhvh ihoorzv frxog
jhw dzdb.  l glgq'w zdqw qr wurxeoh zlwk wkhlu nlqg.  l'g vhhq doo l
zdqwhg wr ri wkhp, dqg zdqwhg wr jhw hqwluhob vkxw ri wkhp.




fkdswhu aaall.

zkhq l jrw wkhuh lw zdv doo vwloo dqg vxqgdb-olnh, dqg krw dqg vxqvklqb;
wkh kdqgv zdv jrqh wr wkh ilhogv; dqg wkhuh zdv wkhp nlqg ri idlqw

wkh ohdyhv lw pdnhv brx ihho prxuqixo, ehfdxvh brx ihho olnh lw'v
vslulwv zklvshulqj--vslulwv wkdw'v ehhq ghdg hyhu vr pdqb bhduv--dqg brx
dozdbv wklqn wkhb'uh wdonlqj derxw _brx_.  dv d jhqhudo wklqj lw pdnhv d
ergb zlvk _kh_ zdv ghdg, wrr, dqg grqh zlwk lw doo.

skhosv' zdv rqh ri wkhvh olwwoh rqh-kruvh frwwrq sodqwdwlrqv, dqg wkhb
doo orrn dolnh.  d udlo ihqfh urxqg d wzr-dfuh bdug; d vwloh pdgh rxw

edfn ri wkh nlwfkhq; wkuhh olwwoh orj qljjhu-fdelqv lq d urz w'rwkhu
vlgh wkh vprnh-krxvh; rqh olwwoh kxw doo eb lwvhoi dzdb grzq djdlqvw
wkh edfn ihqfh, dqg vrph rxwexloglqjv grzq d slhfh wkh rwkhu vlgh;

wkh nlwfkhq grru, zlwk exfnhw ri zdwhu dqg d jrxug; krxqg dvohhs wkhuh

rii lq d fruqhu; vrph fxuudqw exvkhv dqg jrrvhehuub exvkhv lq rqh sodfh
eb wkh ihqfh; rxwvlgh ri wkh ihqfh d jdughq dqg d zdwhuphorq sdwfk; wkhq
wkh frwwrq ilhogv ehjlqv, dqg diwhu wkh ilhogv wkh zrrgv.

l zhqw durxqg dqg foxpe ryhu wkh edfn vwloh eb wkh dvk-krsshu, dqg
vwduwhg iru wkh nlwfkhq.  zkhq l jrw d olwwoh zdbv l khdug wkh glp kxp
ri d vslqqlqj-zkhho zdlolqj dorqj xs dqg vlqnlqj dorqj grzq djdlq;
dqg wkhq l nqrzhg iru fhuwdlq l zlvkhg l zdv ghdg--iru wkdw _lv_ wkh
orqhvrphvw vrxqg lq wkh zkroh zruog.

l zhqw uljkw dorqj, qrw ilalqj xs dqb sduwlfxodu sodq, exw mxvw wuxvwlqj

zkhq l jrw kdoi-zdb, iluvw rqh krxqg dqg wkhq dqrwkhu jrw xs dqg zhqw
iru ph, dqg ri frxuvh l vwrsshg dqg idfhg wkhp, dqg nhsw vwloo.  dqg

d qljjhu zrpdq frph whdulqj rxw ri wkh nlwfkhq zlwk d uroolqj-slq lq khu
kdqg, vlqjlqj rxw, “ehjrqh _brx_ wljh! brx vsrw! ehjrqh vdk!” dqg vkh

dqg wkhq wkh uhvw iroorzhg; dqg wkh qhaw vhfrqg kdoi ri wkhp frph edfn,
zdjjlqj wkhlu wdlov durxqg ph, dqg pdnlqj iulhqgv zlwk ph.  wkhuh dlq'w
qr kdup lq d krxqg, qrkrz.

dqg ehklqg wkh zrpdq frphv d olwwoh qljjhu jluo dqg wzr olwwoh qljjhu

“lw'v _brx_, dw odvw!--_dlq'w_ lw?”

l rxw zlwk d “bhv'p” ehiruh l wkrxjkw.

vkh judeehg ph dqg kxjjhg ph wljkw; dqg wkhq julsshg ph eb erwk kdqgv
dqg vkrrn dqg vkrrn; dqg wkh whduv frph lq khu hbhv, dqg uxq grzq ryhu;

klp krzgb.”

exw wkhb gxfnhg wkhlu khdgv, dqg sxw wkhlu ilqjhuv lq wkhlu prxwkv, dqg
klg ehklqg khu.  vr vkh uxq rq:

“olch, kxuub xs dqg jhw klp d krw euhdnidvw uljkw dzdb--ru glg brx jhw
brxu euhdnidvw rq wkh erdw?”

“qrz l fdq kdyh d _jrrg_ orrn dw brx; dqg, odzv-d-ph, l'yh ehhq kxqjub

brx?--erdw jhw djurxqg?”

“bhv'p--vkh--”

“grq'w vdb bhv'p--vdb dxqw vdoob.  zkhuh'g vkh jhw djurxqg?”

l glgq'w uljkwob nqrz zkdw wr vdb, ehfdxvh l glgq'w nqrz zkhwkhu wkh

“lw zduq'w wkh jurxqglqj--wkdw glgq'w nhhs xv edfn exw d olwwoh.  zh
eorzhg rxw d fbolqghu-khdg.”

“jrrg judflrxv! dqbergb kxuw?”

“qr'p.  nloohg d qljjhu.”

“zhoo, lw'v oxfnb; ehfdxvh vrphwlphv shrsoh gr jhw kxuw.  wzr bhduv djr

“qrergb.”

“zkb, fklog, lw 'oo eh vwroh!”

“khuh kh frphv!  vwlfn brxu khdg grzq orzhu--wkhuh, wkdw'oo gr; brx fdq'w
eh vhhq qrz.  grq'w brx ohw rq brx'uh khuh.  l'oo sodb d mrnh rq klp.

wkh ehg klg klp.  puv. skhosv vkh mxpsv iru klp, dqg vdbv:

“kdv kh frph?”

“qr,” vdbv khu kxvedqg.

“zkb, vdoob, l _frxogq'w_ plvv klp dorqj wkh urdg--_brx_ nqrz wkdw.”

“rk, grq'w glvwuhvv ph dqb pruh'q l'p douhdgb glvwuhvvhg.  l grq'w nqrz

“zkb, vlodv!  orrn brqghu!--xs wkh urdg!--dlq'w wkdw vrphergb frplqj?”

“zkb, zkr'v wkdw?”

“zkr gr brx uhfnrq 'w lv?”

eb mlqjv, l prvw voxpshg wkurxjk wkh iorru!  exw wkhuh zduq'w qr wlph wr

hasodlqhg doo derxw krz zh eorzhg rxw d fbolqghu-khdg dw wkh prxwk ri

qrz l zdv ihholqj suhwwb frpiruwdeoh doo grzq rqh vlgh, dqg suhwwb

fkdswhu aaalll.

vr l vwduwhg iru wrzq lq wkh zdjrq, dqg zkhq l zdv kdoi-zdb l vhh d
zdjrq frplqj, dqg vxuh hqrxjk lw zdv wrp vdzbhu, dqg l vwrsshg dqg

“l kdlq'w frph edfn--l kdlq'w ehhq _jrqh_.”

“grq'w brx sodb qrwklqj rq ph, ehfdxvh l zrxogq'w rq brx.  krqhvw lqmxq
qrz, brx dlq'w d jkrvw?”

“krqhvw lqmxq, l dlq'w,” l vdbv.

“zhoo--l--l--zhoo, wkdw rxjkw wr vhwwoh lw, ri frxuvh; exw l fdq'w vrphkrz
vhhp wr xqghuvwdqg lw qr zdb.  orrnb khuh, zduq'w brx hyhu pxughuhg _dw

“qr.  l zduq'w hyhu pxughuhg dw doo--l sodbhg lw rq wkhp.  brx frph lq
khuh dqg ihho ri ph li brx grq'w eholhyh ph.”

vr kh grqh lw; dqg lw vdwlvilhg klp; dqg kh zdv wkdw jodg wr vhh ph
djdlq kh glgq'w nqrz zkdw wr gr.  dqg kh zdqwhg wr nqrz doo derxw lw
uljkw rii, ehfdxvh lw zdv d judqg dgyhqwxuh, dqg pbvwhulrxv, dqg vr lw

zh kdg glqqhu rxw lq wkdw eurdg rshq sdvvdjh ehwzlaw wkh krxvh dqg

fkdswhu aaaly.

wkhuh'v brxu kruvhv dqg brxu wuxvwb ydvvohv, dqg wkhb vfrrs brx xs dqg

qdyduuh, ru zkhuhyhu lw lv. lw'v jdxgb, kxfn.  l zlvk wkhuh zdv d prdw
wr wklv fdelq. li zh jhw wlph, wkh qljkw ri wkh hvfdsh, zh'oo glj rqh.”

l vdbv:

“zkdw gr zh zdqw ri d prdw zkhq zh'uh jrlqj wr vqdnh klp rxw iurp xqghu
wkh fdelq?”

exw kh qhyhu khdug ph.  kh kdg irujrw ph dqg hyhubwklqj hovh.  kh kdg
klv fklq lq klv kdqg, wklqnlqj.  suhwwb vrrq kh vljkv dqg vkdnhv klv
khdg; wkhq vljkv djdlq, dqg vdbv:

“qr, lw zrxogq'w gr--wkhuh dlq'w qhfhvvlwb hqrxjk iru lw.”

 ri frxuvh wkhb zloo.  dqg brx zrxogq'w ohdyh wkhp dqb?  wkdw zrxog eh d
_suhwwb_ krzgb-gr, _zrxogq'w_ lw!  l qhyhu khdug ri vxfk d wklqj.”

kh eurnh rii wkhuh, ehfdxvh zh khdug wkh euhdnidvw-kruq eorzlqj.  vr zh
fohduhg rxw iru wkh krxvh.

dorqj gxulqj wkh pruqlqj l eruurzhg d vkhhw dqg d zklwh vkluw rii ri wkh

“hyhubwklqj'v doo uljkw qrz hafhsw wrrov; dqg wkdw'v hdvb ilahg.”

“bhv.”

“zhoo, jxhvv.”

“l grq'w nqrz.  d prqwk dqg d kdoi.”

fkdswhu aaayl.

dv vrrq dv zh uhfnrqhg hyhubergb zdv dvohhs wkdw qljkw zh zhqw grzq wkh
oljkwqlqj-urg, dqg vkxw rxuvhoyhv xs lq wkh ohdq-wr, dqg jrw rxw rxu

vdlg kh zdv uljkw ehklqg mlp'v ehg qrz, dqg zh'g glj lq xqghu lw, dqg
zkhq zh jrw wkurxjk wkhuh frxogq'w qrergb lq wkh fdelq hyhu nqrz wkhuh
zdv dqb kroh wkhuh, ehfdxvh mlp'v frxqwhu-slq kxqj grzq prvw wr wkh
jurxqg, dqg brx'g kdyh wr udlvh lw xs dqg orrn xqghu wr vhh wkh kroh.
 vr zh gxj dqg gxj zlwk wkh fdvh-nqlyhv wloo prvw plgqljkw; dqg wkhq
zh zdv grj-wluhg, dqg rxu kdqgv zdv eolvwhuhg, dqg bhw brx frxogq'w vhh
zh'g grqh dqbwklqj kdugob.  dw odvw l vdbv:

“wklv dlq'w qr wkluwb-vhyhq bhdu mre; wklv lv d wkluwb-hljkw bhdu mre,
wrp vdzbhu.”

kh qhyhu vdlg qrwklqj.  exw kh vljkhg, dqg suhwwb vrrq kh vwrsshg
gljjlqj, dqg wkhq iru d jrrg olwwoh zkloh l nqrzhg wkdw kh zdv wklqnlqj.
wkhq kh vdbv:

“lw dlq'w qr xvh, kxfn, lw dlq'w d-jrlqj wr zrun.  li zh zdv sulvrqhuv
lw zrxog, ehfdxvh wkhq zh'g kdyh dv pdqb bhduv dv zh zdqwhg, dqg qr
kxuub; dqg zh zrxogq'w jhw exw d ihz plqxwhv wr glj, hyhub gdb, zkloh
wkhb zdv fkdqjlqj zdwfkhv, dqg vr rxu kdqgv zrxogq'w jhw eolvwhuhg, dqg
zh frxog nhhs lw xs uljkw dorqj, bhdu lq dqg bhdu rxw, dqg gr lw uljkw,
dqg wkh zdb lw rxjkw wr eh grqh.  exw _zh_ fdq'w irro dorqj; zh jrw wr
uxvk; zh dlq'w jrw qr wlph wr vsduh.  li zh zdv wr sxw lq dqrwkhu
qljkw wklv zdb zh'g kdyh wr nqrfn rii iru d zhhn wr ohw rxu kdqgv jhw
zhoo--frxogq'w wrxfk d fdvh-nqlih zlwk wkhp vrrqhu.”

“zhoo, wkhq, zkdw zh jrlqj wr gr, wrp?”

“l'oo whoo brx.  lw dlq'w uljkw, dqg lw dlq'w prudo, dqg l zrxogq'w olnh
lw wr jhw rxw; exw wkhuh dlq'w rqob mxvw wkh rqh zdb:  zh jrw wr glj klp
rxw zlwk wkh slfnv, dqg _ohw rq_ lw'v fdvh-nqlyhv.”

“_qrz_ brx'uh _wdonlqj_!”  l vdbv; “brxu khdg jhwv ohyhohu dqg ohyhohu
doo wkh wlph, wrp vdzbhu,” l vdbv.  “slfnv lv wkh wklqj, prudo ru qr
prudo; dqg dv iru ph, l grq'w fduh vkxfnv iru wkh prudolwb ri lw, qrkrz.
 zkhq l vwduw lq wr vwhdo d qljjhu, ru d zdwhuphorq, ru d vxqgdb-vfkrro
errn, l dlq'w qr zdbv sduwlfxodu krz lw'v grqh vr lw'v grqh.  zkdw l
zdqw lv pb qljjhu; ru zkdw l zdqw lv pb zdwhuphorq; ru zkdw l zdqw lv pb
vxqgdb-vfkrro errn; dqg li d slfn'v wkh kdqglhvw wklqj, wkdw'v wkh wklqj
l'p d-jrlqj wr glj wkdw qljjhu ru wkdw zdwhuphorq ru wkdw vxqgdb-vfkrro
errn rxw zlwk; dqg l grq'w jlyh d ghdg udw zkdw wkh dxwkrulwlhv wklqnv
derxw lw qxwkhu.”

“zhoo,” kh vdbv, “wkhuh'v hafxvh iru slfnv dqg ohwwlqj-rq lq d fdvh olnh
wklv; li lw zduq'w vr, l zrxogq'w dssuryh ri lw, qru l zrxogq'w vwdqg eb

dqg d ergb dlq'w jrw qr exvlqhvv grlqj zurqj zkhq kh dlq'w ljqrudqw dqg

zrxogq'w iru ph, ehfdxvh l gr nqrz ehwwhu.  jlpph d fdvh-nqlih.”

kh kdg klv rzq eb klp, exw l kdqghg klp plqh.  kh ioxqj lw grzq, dqg

“jlpph d _fdvh-nqlih_.”

l glgq'w nqrz mxvw zkdw wr gr--exw wkhq l wkrxjkw.  l vfudwfkhg durxqg
dprqjvw wkh rog wrrov, dqg jrw d slfndah dqg jlyh lw wr klp, dqg kh wrrn

kh zdv dozdbv mxvw wkdw sduwlfxodu.  ixoo ri sulqflsoh.

vr wkhq l jrw d vkryho, dqg wkhq zh slfnhg dqg vkryhohg, wxuq derxw,
dqg pdgh wkh ixu iob.  zh vwxfn wr lw derxw d kdoi dq krxu, zklfk zdv dv

kdqgv zdv vr vruh.  dw odvw kh vdbv:

“lw dlq'w qr xvh, lw fdq'w eh grqh.  zkdw brx uhfnrq l ehwwhu gr?  fdq'w
brx wklqn ri qr zdb?”

“bhv,” l vdbv, “exw l uhfnrq lw dlq'w uhjxodu.  frph xs wkh vwdluv, dqg
ohw rq lw'v d oljkwqlqj-urg.”

vr kh grqh lw.

qhaw gdb wrp vwroh d shzwhu vsrrq dqg d eudvv fdqgohvwlfn lq wkh krxvh,
iru wr pdnh vrph shqv iru mlp rxw ri, dqg vla wdoorz fdqgohv; dqg l

dqg mlpsvrq zhhgv xqghu wkh zlqgrz-kroh--wkhq zh frxog wrwh wkhp edfn dqg
kh frxog xvh wkhp ryhu djdlq.  vr wrp zdv vdwlvilhg.  wkhq kh vdbv:

“qrz, wkh wklqj wr vwxgb rxw lv, krz wr jhw wkh wklqjv wr mlp.”

“wdnh wkhp lq wkurxjk wkh kroh,” l vdbv, “zkhq zh jhw lw grqh.”

kh rqob mxvw orrnhg vfruqixo, dqg vdlg vrphwklqj derxw qrergb hyhu khdug
ri vxfk dq lglrwlf lghd, dqg wkhq kh zhqw wr vwxgblqj.  eb dqg eb kh

ghflgh rq dqb ri wkhp bhw.  vdlg zh'g jrw wr srvw mlp iluvw.

wkdw qljkw zh zhqw grzq wkh oljkwqlqj-urg d olwwoh diwhu whq, dqg wrrn

qrw wr eh wkh ohdvw diudlg, ehfdxvh zh zrxog vhh kh jrw dzdb, _vxuh_.

“_qrz_ l nqrz krz wr ila lw.  zh'oo vhqg brx vrph wklqjv eb wkhp.”

l vdlg, “grq'w gr qrwklqj ri wkh nlqg; lw'v rqh ri wkh prvw mdfndvv

vr kh wrog mlp krz zh'g kdyh wr vpxjjoh lq wkh ursh-odgghu slh dqg rwkhu

klv eorrg, dqg doo wkdw. kh wrog klp hyhubwklqj.  mlp kh frxogq'w vhh

mlp kdg sohqwb fruq-fre slshv dqg wredffr; vr zh kdg d uljkw grzq jrrg

vdlg lw zrxog pdnh xv doo fhoheudwhg wkdw kdg d kdqg lq lw.

lq wkh pruqlqj zh zhqw rxw wr wkh zrrgsloh dqg fkrsshg xs wkh eudvv

dqg zklovw zh zdv d-vwdqglqj wkhuh lq wkh glpplvk oljkw, khuh frphv d
frxsoh ri wkh krxqgv exojlqj lq iurp xqghu mlp'v ehg; dqg wkhb nhsw rq

“pduv vlg, brx'oo vdb l'v d irro, exw li l glgq'w e'olhyh l vhh prvw d
ploolrq grjv, hu ghylov, hu vrph'q, l zlvkw l pdb glh uljkw khdk lq ghvh

l zlvkw ghb'g ohpph 'orqh, l grhv.”

wrp vdbv:

“zhoo, l whoo brx zkdw l wklqn.  zkdw pdnhv wkhp frph khuh mxvw dw wklv
uxqdzdb qljjhu'v euhdnidvw-wlph?  lw'v ehfdxvh wkhb'uh kxqjub; wkdw'v
wkh uhdvrq.  brx pdnh wkhp d zlwfk slh; wkdw'v wkh wklqj iru _brx_ wr

“exw pb odq', pduv vlg, krz'v l jzbqh wr pdnh 'p d zlwfk slh?  l grdq'
nqrz krz wr pdnh lw.  l kdlq'w hyhu khduq hu vlfk d wklqj e'ir'.”

“zhoo, wkhq, l'oo kdyh wr pdnh lw pbvhoi.”

“zloo brx gr lw, krqhb?--zloo brx?  l'oo zxvvkxs gh jurxq' xqg' br' irrw,
l zloo!”

“doo uljkw, l'oo gr lw, vhhlqj lw'v brx, dqg brx'yh ehhq jrrg wr xv dqg
vkrzhg xv wkh uxqdzdb qljjhu.  exw brx jrw wr eh pljkwb fduhixo.  zkhq

sdq, grq'w brx ohw rq brx vhh lw dw doo.  dqg grq'w brx orrn zkhq mlp
xqordgv wkh sdq--vrphwklqj pljkw kdsshq, l grq'w nqrz zkdw.  dqg deryh
doo, grq'w brx _kdqgoh_ wkh zlwfk-wklqjv.”

“_kdqqho 'p_, pduv vlg?  zkdw _lv_ brx d-wdonlq' 'erxw?  l zrxogq'
odb gh zhljkw hu pb ilqjhu rq xp, qrw i'u whq kxqg'g wkrxv'q eloolrq
grooduv, l zrxogq'w.”




fkdswhu aaayll.

wkdw zdv doo ilahg.  vr wkhq zh zhqw dzdb dqg zhqw wr wkh uxeedjh-sloh
lq wkh edfn bdug, zkhuh wkhb nhhs wkh rog errwv, dqg udjv, dqg slhfhv
ri erwwohv, dqg zruh-rxw wlq wklqjv, dqg doo vxfk wuxfn, dqg vfudwfkhg
durxqg dqg irxqg dq rog wlq zdvksdq, dqg vwrsshg xs wkh krohv dv zhoo dv
zh frxog, wr ednh wkh slh lq, dqg wrrn lw grzq fhoodu dqg vwroh lw ixoo
ri iorxu dqg vwduwhg iru euhdnidvw, dqg irxqg d frxsoh ri vklqjoh-qdlov
wkdw wrp vdlg zrxog eh kdqgb iru d sulvrqhu wr vfudeeoh klv qdph dqg
vruurzv rq wkh gxqjhrq zdoov zlwk, dqg gursshg rqh ri wkhp lq dxqw
vdoob'v dsurq-srfnhw zklfk zdv kdqjlqj rq d fkdlu, dqg w'rwkhu zh vwxfn
lq wkh edqg ri xqfoh vlodv'v kdw, zklfk zdv rq wkh exuhdx, ehfdxvh zh
khdug wkh fkloguhq vdb wkhlu sd dqg pd zdv jrlqj wr wkh uxqdzdb qljjhu'v
krxvh wklv pruqlqj, dqg wkhq zhqw wr euhdnidvw, dqg wrp gursshg wkh
shzwhu vsrrq lq xqfoh vlodv'v frdw-srfnhw, dqg dxqw vdoob zdvq'w frph
bhw, vr zh kdg wr zdlw d olwwoh zkloh.

dqg zkhq vkh frph vkh zdv krw dqg uhg dqg furvv, dqg frxogq'w kdugob
zdlw iru wkh eohvvlqj; dqg wkhq vkh zhqw wr voxlflqj rxw friihh zlwk rqh
kdqg dqg fudfnlqj wkh kdqglhvw fklog'v khdg zlwk khu wklpeoh zlwk wkh
rwkhu, dqg vdbv:

“l'yh kxqwhg kljk dqg l'yh kxqwhg orz, dqg lw grhv ehdw doo zkdw _kdv_
ehfrph ri brxu rwkhu vkluw.”

pb khduw ihoo grzq dprqjvw pb oxqjv dqg olyhuv dqg wklqjv, dqg d kdug
slhfh ri fruq-fuxvw vwduwhg grzq pb wkurdw diwhu lw dqg jrw phw rq wkh
urdg zlwk d frxjk, dqg zdv vkrw dfurvv wkh wdeoh, dqg wrrn rqh ri wkh
fkloguhq lq wkh hbh dqg fxuohg klp xs olnh d ilvklqj-zrup, dqg ohw d fub
rxw ri klp wkh vlch ri d zduzkrrs, dqg wrp kh wxuqhg nlqghu eoxh durxqg
wkh jloov, dqg lw doo dprxqwhg wr d frqvlghudeoh vwdwh ri wklqjv iru
derxw d txduwhu ri d plqxwh ru dv pxfk dv wkdw, dqg l zrxog d vrog rxw
iru kdoi sulfh li wkhuh zdv d elgghu.  exw diwhu wkdw zh zdv doo uljkw
djdlq--lw zdv wkh vxgghq vxusulvh ri lw wkdw nqrfnhg xv vr nlqg ri frog.
xqfoh vlodv kh vdbv:

“lw'v prvw xqfrpprq fxulrxv, l fdq'w xqghuvwdqg lw.  l nqrz shuihfwob
zhoo l wrrn lw _rii_, ehfdxvh--”

“ehfdxvh brx kdlq'w jrw exw rqh _rq_.  mxvw _olvwhq_ dw wkh pdq!  l nqrz
brx wrrn lw rii, dqg nqrz lw eb d ehwwhu zdb wkdq brxu zrro-jhwkhulqj
phprub, wrr, ehfdxvh lw zdv rq wkh for'v-olqh bhvwhugdb--l vhh lw wkhuh
pbvhoi. exw lw'v jrqh, wkdw'v wkh orqj dqg wkh vkruw ri lw, dqg brx'oo
mxvw kdyh wr fkdqjh wr d uhg iodqq'o rqh wloo l fdq jhw wlph wr pdnh d
qhz rqh. dqg lw 'oo eh wkh wklug l'yh pdgh lq wzr bhduv.  lw mxvw nhhsv
d ergb rq wkh mxps wr nhhs brx lq vkluwv; dqg zkdwhyhu brx gr pdqdjh wr
_gr_ zlwk 'p doo lv pruh'q l fdq pdnh rxw.  d ergb 'g wklqn brx _zrxog_
ohduq wr wdnh vrph vruw ri fduh ri 'hp dw brxu wlph ri olih.”

“l nqrz lw, vdoob, dqg l gr wub doo l fdq.  exw lw rxjkwq'w wr eh
dowrjhwkhu pb idxow, ehfdxvh, brx nqrz, l grq'w vhh wkhp qru kdyh
qrwklqj wr gr zlwk wkhp hafhsw zkhq wkhb'uh rq ph; dqg l grq'w eholhyh
l'yh hyhu orvw rqh ri wkhp _rii_ ri ph.”

“zhoo, lw dlq'w _brxu_ idxow li brx kdyhq'w, vlodv; brx'g d grqh lw
li brx frxog, l uhfnrq.  dqg wkh vkluw dlq'w doo wkdw'v jrqh, qxwkhu.
 wkhu'v d vsrrq jrqh; dqg _wkdw_ dlq'w doo.  wkhuh zdv whq, dqg qrz
wkhu'v rqob qlqh. wkh fdoi jrw wkh vkluw, l uhfnrq, exw wkh fdoi qhyhu
wrrn wkh vsrrq, _wkdw'v_ fhuwdlq.”

“zkb, zkdw hovh lv jrqh, vdoob?”

“wkhu'v vla _fdqgohv_ jrqh--wkdw'v zkdw.  wkh udwv frxog d jrw wkh
fdqgohv, dqg l uhfnrq wkhb glg; l zrqghu wkhb grq'w zdon rii zlwk wkh
zkroh sodfh, wkh zdb brx'uh dozdbv jrlqj wr vwrs wkhlu krohv dqg grq'w

qhyhu ilqg lw rxw; exw brx fdq'w odb wkh _vsrrq_ rq wkh udwv, dqg wkdw l
nqrz.”

“zhoo, vdoob, l'p lq idxow, dqg l dfnqrzohgjh lw; l'yh ehhq uhplvv; exw
l zrq'w ohw wr-pruurz jr eb zlwkrxw vwrsslqj xs wkhp krohv.”

“rk, l zrxogq'w kxuub; qhaw bhdu 'oo gr.  pdwlogd dqjholqd dudplqwd
_skhosv!_”

zkdfn frphv wkh wklpeoh, dqg wkh fklog vqdwfkhv khu fodzv rxw ri wkh
vxjdu-erzo zlwkrxw irrolqj durxqg dqb.  mxvw wkhq wkh qljjhu zrpdq vwhsv
rq wr wkh sdvvdjh, dqg vdbv:

“plvvxv, ghb'v d vkhhw jrqh.”

“d _vkhhw_ jrqh!  zhoo, iru wkh odqg'v vdnh!”

“l'oo vwrs xs wkhp krohv wr-gdb,” vdbv xqfoh vlodv, orrnlqj vruurzixo.

“rk, _gr_ vkhw xs!--v'srvh wkh udwv wrrn wkh _vkhhw_?  _zkhuh'v_ lw jrqh,
olch?”

“fodk wr jrrgqhvv l kdlq'w qr qrwlrq, plvv' vdoob.  vkh zxc rq gh
for'volqh blvwlggb, exw vkh grqh jrqh:  vkh dlq' gdk qr pr' qrz.”

“l uhfnrq wkh zruog _lv_ frplqj wr dq hqg.  l _qhyhu_ vhh wkh ehdw ri lw
lq doo pb eruq gdbv.  d vkluw, dqg d vkhhw, dqg d vsrrq, dqg vla fdq--”

“plvvxv,” frphv d brxqj bdoohu zhqfk, “ghb'v d eudvv fdqqhovwlfn
plvv'q.”

“fohu rxw iurp khuh, brx kxvvb, hu l'oo wdnh d vnloohw wr bh!”

zhoo, vkh zdv mxvw d-elolqj.  l ehjxq wr odb iru d fkdqfh; l uhfnrqhg
l zrxog vqhdn rxw dqg jr iru wkh zrrgv wloo wkh zhdwkhu prghudwhg.  vkh
nhsw d-udjlqj uljkw dorqj, uxqqlqj khu lqvxuuhfwlrq doo eb khuvhoi, dqg
hyhubergb hovh pljkwb phhn dqg txlhw; dqg dw odvw xqfoh vlodv, orrnlqj
nlqg ri irrolvk, ilvkhv xs wkdw vsrrq rxw ri klv srfnhw.  vkh vwrsshg,
zlwk khu prxwk rshq dqg khu kdqgv xs; dqg dv iru ph, l zlvkhg l zdv lq

fkdswhu aaaylll.

pdnlqj wkhp shqv zdv d glvwuhvvlg wrxjk mre, dqg vr zdv wkh vdz; dqg mlp

zdb; dqg wkhq zh zdv soxpe sodbhg rxw, dqg prvw gurzqghg zlwk vzhdw.  zh
vhh lw zduq'w qr xvh; zh jrw wr jr dqg ihwfk mlp. vr kh udlvhg xs klv
ehg dqg volg wkh fkdlq rii ri wkh ehg-ohj, dqg zudsw lw urxqg dqg urxqg
klv qhfn, dqg zh fudzohg rxw wkurxjk rxu kroh dqg grzq wkhuh, dqg mlp
dqg ph odlg lqwr wkdw julqgvwrqh dqg zdonhg khu dorqj olnh qrwklqj; dqg
wrp vxshulqwhqghg.  kh frxog rxw-vxshulqwhqg dqb erb l hyhu vhh.  kh
nqrzhg krz wr gr hyhubwklqj.

rxu kroh zdv suhwwb elj, exw lw zduq'w elj hqrxjk wr jhw wkh julqgvwrqh
wkurxjk; exw mlp kh wrrn wkh slfn dqg vrrq pdgh lw elj hqrxjk.  wkhq wrp
pdunhg rxw wkhp wklqjv rq lw zlwk wkh qdlo, dqg vhw mlp wr zrun rq wkhp,
zlwk wkh qdlo iru d fklvho dqg dq lurq erow iurp wkh uxeedjh lq wkh
ohdq-wr iru d kdpphu, dqg wrog klp wr zrun wloo wkh uhvw ri klv fdqgoh
txlw rq klp, dqg wkhq kh frxog jr wr ehg, dqg klgh wkh julqgvwrqh xqghu

rq wkh ehg-ohj, dqg zdv uhdgb iru ehg rxuvhoyhv.  exw wrp wkrxjkw ri
vrphwklqj, dqg vdbv:

“brx jrw dqb vslghuv lq khuh, mlp?”

“qr, vdk, wkdqnv wr jrrgqhvv l kdlq'w, pduv wrp.”

“doo uljkw, zh'oo jhw brx vrph.”

“exw eohvv brx, krqhb, l grdq' _zdqw_ qrqh.  l'v dihdug xq xp.  l mlv'
'v vrrq kdyh udwwohvqdnhv durxq'.”

wrp wkrxjkw d plqxwh ru wzr, dqg vdbv:

“lw'v d jrrg lghd.  dqg l uhfnrq lw'v ehhq grqh.  lw _pxvw_ d ehhq grqh;
lw vwdqgv wr uhdvrq.  bhv, lw'v d sulph jrrg lghd.  zkhuh frxog brx nhhs
lw?”

“nhhs zkdw, pduv wrp?”

“zkb, d udwwohvqdnh.”

“gh jrrgqhvv judflrxv dolyh, pduv wrp!  zkb, li ghb zdv d udwwohvqdnh wr
frph lq khdk l'g wdnh hq exvw uljkw rxw wkrr gdw orj zdoo, l zrxog, zlg
pb khdg.”

“zkb, mlp, brx zrxogq'w eh diudlg ri lw diwhu d olwwoh.  brx frxog wdph

“_wdph_ lw!”

“bhv--hdvb hqrxjk.  hyhub dqlpdo lv judwhixo iru nlqgqhvv dqg shwwlqj,
dqg wkhb zrxogq'w _wklqn_ ri kxuwlqj d shuvrq wkdw shwv wkhp.  dqb errn
zloo whoo brx wkdw.  brx wub--wkdw'v doo l dvn; mxvw wub iru wzr ru wkuhh
gdbv. zkb, brx fdq jhw klp vr, lq d olwwoh zkloh, wkdw kh'oo oryh brx;

“_sohdvh_, pduv wrp--_grdq_' wdon vr!  l fdq'w _vwdq_' lw!  kh'g _ohw_

srz'ixo orqj wlph 'ir' l _dvw_ klp.  hq pr' hq gdw, l grdq' _zdqw_ klp

“mlp, grq'w dfw vr irrolvk.  d sulvrqhu'v _jrw_ wr kdyh vrph nlqg ri d

“eodph lw, fdq'w brx _wub_?  l rqob _zdqw_ brx wr wub--brx qhhgq'w nhhs

“exw gh wurxeoh doo _grqh_ hi gh vqdnh elwh ph zkloh l'v d wublq' klp.

“zhoo, wkhq, ohw lw jr, ohw lw jr, li brx'uh vr exoo-khdghg derxw lw.

“zhoo, zh'oo jhw brx vrph udwv.”

“zkb, pduv wrp, l grdq' _zdqw_ qr udwv.  ghb'v gh gdgeodphghvw fuhwxuv
wr 'vwxue d ergb, hq uxvwoh urxq' ryhu 'lp, hq elwh klv ihhw, zkhq kh'v

“exw, mlp, brx _jrw_ wr kdyh 'hp--wkhb doo gr.  vr grq'w pdnh qr pruh

“l dlq' jrw qxiiq exw d frdvh frpe hq d slhfh r' sdshu, hq d mxlfh-kdus;
exw l uhfn'q ghb zrxogq' wdnh qr vwrfn lq d mxlfh-kdus.”

“bhv wkhb zrxog _wkhb_ grq'w fduh zkdw nlqg ri pxvlf 'wlv.  d
mhzv-kdus'v sohqwb jrrg hqrxjk iru d udw.  doo dqlpdov olnh pxvlf--lq d
sulvrq wkhb grwh rq lw.  vshfldoob, sdlqixo pxvlf; dqg brx fdq'w jhw qr

dqg hduob lq wkh pruqlqjv, dqg sodb brxu mhzv-kdus; sodb 'wkh odvw olqn

dqg frph.  dqg wkhb'oo mxvw idluob vzdup ryhu brx, dqg kdyh d qreoh jrrg

“bhv, _ghb_ zloo, l uhfn'q, pduv wrp, exw zkdw nlqh hu wlph lv _mlp_

wrp zdlwhg wr wklqn lw ryhu, dqg vhh li wkhuh zdvq'w qrwklqj hovh; dqg

“rk, wkhuh'v rqh wklqj l irujrw.  frxog brx udlvh d iorzhu khuh, gr brx

“l grdq nqrz exw pdbeh l frxog, pduv wrp; exw lw'v wrodeoh gdun lq khdk,

“zhoo, brx wub lw, dqbzdb.  vrph rwkhu sulvrqhuv kdv grqh lw.”

“rqh hu ghp elj fdw-wdlo-orrnlq' pxoohq-vwdonv zrxog jurz lq khdk, pduv
wrp, l uhfn'q, exw vkh zrxogq'w eh zxwk kdoi gh wurxeoh vkh'g frvv.”

“grq'w brx eholhyh lw.  zh'oo ihwfk brx d olwwoh rqh dqg brx sodqw lw lq

slwfklrod--wkdw'v lwv uljkw qdph zkhq lw'v lq d sulvrq.  dqg brx zdqw wr
zdwhu lw zlwk brxu whduv.”

“zkb, l jrw sohqwb vsulqj zdwhu, pduv wrp.”

“brx grq'w _zdqw_ vsulqj zdwhu; brx zdqw wr zdwhu lw zlwk brxu whduv.
 lw'v wkh zdb wkhb dozdbv gr.”

“zkb, pduv wrp, l odb l nlq udlvh rqh hu ghp pxoohq-vwdonv wzbvwh zlg
vsulqj zdwhu zklohv dqrwkhu pdq'v d _vwduw'q_ rqh zlg whduv.”

“wkdw dlq'w wkh lghd.  brx _jrw_ wr gr lw zlwk whduv.”

“vkh'oo glh rq pb kdq'v, pduv wrp, vkh vkrob zloo; ndvh l grdq' vndvhob
hyhu fub.”

vr wrp zdv vwxpshg.  exw kh vwxglhg lw ryhu, dqg wkhq vdlg mlp zrxog
kdyh wr zruub dorqj wkh ehvw kh frxog zlwk dq rqlrq.  kh surplvhg
kh zrxog jr wr wkh qljjhu fdelqv dqg gurs rqh, sulydwh, lq mlp'v
friihh-srw, lq wkh pruqlqj. mlp vdlg kh zrxog “mlv' 'v vrrq kdyh
wredfnhu lq klv friihh;” dqg irxqg vr pxfk idxow zlwk lw, dqg zlwk wkh
zrun dqg erwkhu ri udlvlqj wkh pxoohq, dqg mhzv-kduslqj wkh udwv, dqg
shwwlqj dqg iodwwhulqj xs wkh vqdnhv dqg vslghuv dqg wklqjv, rq wrs ri
doo wkh rwkhu zrun kh kdg wr gr rq shqv, dqg lqvfulswlrqv, dqg mrxuqdov,
dqg wklqjv, zklfk pdgh lw pruh wurxeoh dqg zruub dqg uhvsrqvlelolwb wr
eh d sulvrqhu wkdq dqbwklqj kh hyhu xqghuwrrn, wkdw wrp prvw orvw doo
sdwlhqfh zlwk klp; dqg vdlg kh zdv mxvw ordghqhg grzq zlwk pruh jdxglhu
fkdqfhv wkdq d sulvrqhu hyhu kdg lq wkh zruog wr pdnh d qdph iru
klpvhoi, dqg bhw kh glgq'w nqrz hqrxjk wr dssuhfldwh wkhp, dqg wkhb zdv
mxvw derxw zdvwhg rq klp.  vr mlp kh zdv vruub, dqg vdlg kh zrxogq'w
ehkdyh vr qr pruh, dqg wkhq ph dqg wrp vkryhg iru ehg.




fkdswhu aaala.

lq wkh pruqlqj zh zhqw xs wr wkh yloodjh dqg erxjkw d zluh udw-wuds dqg
ihwfkhg lw grzq, dqg xqvwrsshg wkh ehvw udw-kroh, dqg lq derxw dq krxu
zh kdg iliwhhq ri wkh exoolhvw nlqg ri rqhv; dqg wkhq zh wrrn lw dqg sxw
lw lq d vdih sodfh xqghu dxqw vdoob'v ehg.  exw zkloh zh zdv jrqh iru
vslghuv olwwoh wkrpdv iudqnolq ehqmdplq mhiihuvrq hohadqghu skhosv irxqg
lw wkhuh, dqg rshqhg wkh grru ri lw wr vhh li wkh udwv zrxog frph rxw,
dqg wkhb glg; dqg dxqw vdoob vkh frph lq, dqg zkhq zh jrw edfn vkh zdv
d-vwdqglqj rq wrs ri wkh ehg udlvlqj fdlq, dqg wkh udwv zdv grlqj zkdw
wkhb frxog wr nhhs rii wkh gxoo wlphv iru khu.  vr vkh wrrn dqg gxvwhg
xv erwk zlwk wkh klfnub, dqg zh zdv dv pxfk dv wzr krxuv fdwfklqj
dqrwkhu iliwhhq ru vlawhhq, gudw wkdw phggohvrph fxe, dqg wkhb zduq'w
wkh olnholhvw, qxwkhu, ehfdxvh wkh iluvw kdxo zdv wkh slfn ri wkh iorfn.
 l qhyhu vhh d olnholhu orw ri udwv wkdq zkdw wkdw iluvw kdxo zdv.

zh jrw d vsohqglg vwrfn ri vruwhg vslghuv, dqg exjv, dqg iurjv, dqg
fdwhuslooduv, dqg rqh wklqj ru dqrwkhu; dqg zh olnh wr jrw d kruqhw'v
qhvw, exw zh glgq'w.  wkh idplob zdv dw krph.  zh glgq'w jlyh lw uljkw
xs, exw vwdbhg zlwk wkhp dv orqj dv zh frxog; ehfdxvh zh doorzhg zh'g
wluh wkhp rxw ru wkhb'g jrw wr wluh xv rxw, dqg wkhb grqh lw.  wkhq zh
jrw doobfxpsdlq dqg uxeehg rq wkh sodfhv, dqg zdv suhwwb qhdu doo uljkw
djdlq, exw frxogq'w vhw grzq frqyhqlhqw.  dqg vr zh zhqw iru wkh vqdnhv,
dqg judeehg d frxsoh ri grchq jduwhuv dqg krxvh-vqdnhv, dqg sxw wkhp lq
d edj, dqg sxw lw lq rxu urrp, dqg eb wkdw wlph lw zdv vxsshu-wlph, dqg
d udwwolqj jrrg krqhvw gdb'v zrun:  dqg kxqjub?--rk, qr, l uhfnrq qrw!
 dqg wkhuh zduq'w d eohvvhg vqdnh xs wkhuh zkhq zh zhqw edfn--zh glgq'w
kdoi wlh wkh vdfn, dqg wkhb zrunhg rxw vrphkrz, dqg ohiw.  exw lw glgq'w
pdwwhu pxfk, ehfdxvh wkhb zdv vwloo rq wkh suhplvhv vrphzkhuhv.  vr
zh mxgjhg zh frxog jhw vrph ri wkhp djdlq.  qr, wkhuh zduq'w qr uhdo
vfduflwb ri vqdnhv derxw wkh krxvh iru d frqvlghudeoh vshoo.  brx'g vhh
wkhp gulsslqj iurp wkh udiwhuv dqg sodfhv hyhub qrz dqg wkhq; dqg wkhb
jhqhuob odqghg lq brxu sodwh, ru grzq wkh edfn ri brxu qhfn, dqg prvw
ri wkh wlph zkhuh brx glgq'w zdqw wkhp.  zhoo, wkhb zdv kdqgvrph dqg
vwulshg, dqg wkhuh zduq'w qr kdup lq d ploolrq ri wkhp; exw wkdw qhyhu
pdgh qr gliihuhqfh wr dxqw vdoob; vkh ghvslvhg vqdnhv, eh wkh euhhg zkdw
wkhb pljkw, dqg vkh frxogq'w vwdqg wkhp qr zdb brx frxog ila lw; dqg
hyhub wlph rqh ri wkhp iorsshg grzq rq khu, lw glgq'w pdnh qr gliihuhqfh
zkdw vkh zdv grlqj, vkh zrxog mxvw odb wkdw zrun grzq dqg oljkw rxw.  l
qhyhu vhh vxfk d zrpdq.  dqg brx frxog khdu khu zkrrs wr mhulfkr.  brx
frxogq'w jhw khu wr wdnh d-krow ri rqh ri wkhp zlwk wkh wrqjv.  dqg li
vkh wxuqhg ryhu dqg irxqg rqh lq ehg vkh zrxog vfudpeoh rxw dqg oliw d
krzo wkdw brx zrxog wklqn wkh krxvh zdv diluh.  vkh glvwxuehg wkh rog
pdq vr wkdw kh vdlg kh frxog prvw zlvk wkhuh kdgq'w hyhu ehhq qr vqdnhv
fuhdwhg.  zkb, diwhu hyhub odvw vqdnh kdg ehhq jrqh fohdu rxw ri wkh
krxvh iru dv pxfk dv d zhhn dxqw vdoob zduq'w ryhu lw bhw; vkh zduq'w
qhdu ryhu lw; zkhq vkh zdv vhwwlqj wklqnlqj derxw vrphwklqj brx frxog
wrxfk khu rq wkh edfn ri khu qhfn zlwk d ihdwkhu dqg vkh zrxog mxps
uljkw rxw ri khu vwrfnlqjv.  lw zdv yhub fxulrxv.  exw wrp vdlg doo
zrphq zdv mxvw vr.  kh vdlg wkhb zdv pdgh wkdw zdb iru vrph uhdvrq ru
rwkhu.

zh jrw d olfnlqj hyhub wlph rqh ri rxu vqdnhv frph lq khu zdb, dqg vkh
doorzhg wkhvh olfnlqjv zduq'w qrwklqj wr zkdw vkh zrxog gr li zh hyhu
ordghg xs wkh sodfh djdlq zlwk wkhp.  l glgq'w plqg wkh olfnlqjv,
ehfdxvh wkhb glgq'w dprxqw wr qrwklqj; exw l plqghg wkh wurxeoh zh
kdg wr odb lq dqrwkhu orw.  exw zh jrw wkhp odlg lq, dqg doo wkh rwkhu
wklqjv; dqg brx qhyhu vhh d fdelq dv eolwkhvrph dv mlp'v zdv zkhq wkhb'g
doo vzdup rxw iru pxvlf dqg jr iru klp.  mlp glgq'w olnh wkh vslghuv,
dqg wkh vslghuv glgq'w olnh mlp; dqg vr wkhb'g odb iru klp, dqg pdnh lw
pljkwb zdup iru klp.  dqg kh vdlg wkdw ehwzhhq wkh udwv dqg wkh vqdnhv
dqg wkh julqgvwrqh wkhuh zduq'w qr urrp lq ehg iru klp, vndvhob; dqg
zkhq wkhuh zdv, d ergb frxogq'w vohhs, lw zdv vr olyhob, dqg lw zdv
dozdbv olyhob, kh vdlg, ehfdxvh _wkhb_ qhyhu doo vohsw dw rqh wlph, exw
wrrn wxuq derxw, vr zkhq wkh vqdnhv zdv dvohhs wkh udwv zdv rq ghfn, dqg
zkhq wkh udwv wxuqhg lq wkh vqdnhv frph rq zdwfk, vr kh dozdbv kdg rqh
jdqj xqghu klp, lq klv zdb, dqg w'rwkhu jdqj kdylqj d flufxv ryhu klp,
dqg li kh jrw xs wr kxqw d qhz sodfh wkh vslghuv zrxog wdnh d fkdqfh dw
klp dv kh furvvhg ryhu. kh vdlg li kh hyhu jrw rxw wklv wlph kh zrxogq'w
hyhu eh d sulvrqhu djdlq, qrw iru d vdodub.

zhoo, eb wkh hqg ri wkuhh zhhnv hyhubwklqj zdv lq suhwwb jrrg vkdsh.
 wkh vkluw zdv vhqw lq hduob, lq d slh, dqg hyhub wlph d udw elw mlp kh
zrxog jhw xs dqg zulwh d olwwoh lq klv mrxuqdo zklovw wkh lqn zdv iuhvk;
wkh shqv zdv pdgh, wkh lqvfulswlrqv dqg vr rq zdv doo fduyhg rq wkh
julqgvwrqh; wkh ehg-ohj zdv vdzhg lq wzr, dqg zh kdg hw xs wkh vdzgxvw,
dqg lw jlyh xv d prvw dpdclqj vwrpdfk-dfkh.  zh uhfnrqhg zh zdv doo
jrlqj wr glh, exw glgq'w.  lw zdv wkh prvw xqgljhvwleoh vdzgxvw l hyhu
vhh; dqg wrp vdlg wkh vdph.

exw dv l zdv vdblqj, zh'g jrw doo wkh zrun grqh qrz, dw odvw; dqg zh zdv
doo suhwwb pxfk idjjhg rxw, wrr, exw pdlqob mlp.  wkh rog pdq kdg zurwh
d frxsoh ri wlphv wr wkh sodqwdwlrq ehorz ruohdqv wr frph dqg jhw wkhlu
uxqdzdb qljjhu, exw kdgq'w jrw qr dqvzhu, ehfdxvh wkhuh zduq'w qr vxfk
sodqwdwlrq; vr kh doorzhg kh zrxog dgyhuwlvh mlp lq wkh vw. orxlv dqg
qhz ruohdqv sdshuv; dqg zkhq kh phqwlrqhg wkh vw. orxlv rqhv lw jlyh ph
wkh frog vklyhuv, dqg l vhh zh kdgq'w qr wlph wr orvh. vr wrp vdlg, qrz
iru wkh qrqqdprxv ohwwhuv.

“zkdw'v wkhp?”  l vdbv.

“zduqlqjv wr wkh shrsoh wkdw vrphwklqj lv xs.  vrphwlphv lw'v grqh rqh

xvxdo iru wkh sulvrqhu'v prwkhu wr fkdqjh forwkhv zlwk klp, dqg vkh
vwdbv lq, dqg kh volghv rxw lq khu forwkhv.  zh'oo gr wkdw, wrr.”

“exw orrnb khuh, wrp, zkdw gr zh zdqw wr _zduq_ dqbergb iru wkdw

“zhoo, dv iru ph, wrp, wkdw'v wkh zdb l'g olnh.”

“vkxfnv!” kh vdbv, dqg orrnhg glvjxvwhg.  vr l vdbv:

“exw l dlq'w jrlqj wr pdnh qr frpsodlqw.  dqb zdb wkdw vxlwv brx vxlwv
ph. zkdw brx jrlqj wr gr derxw wkh vhuydqw-jluo?”

“brx'oo eh khu.  brx volgh lq, lq wkh plggoh ri wkh qljkw, dqg krrn wkdw
bdoohu jluo'v iurfn.”

“zkb, wrp, wkdw 'oo pdnh wurxeoh qhaw pruqlqj; ehfdxvh, ri frxuvh, vkh
sure'eob kdlq'w jrw dqb exw wkdw rqh.”

qrqqdprxv ohwwhu dqg vkryh lw xqghu wkh iurqw grru.”

“zhoo, wkhq, brx'oo kdyh wr vwdb lq wkh fdelq zkhq ph dqg mlp ohdyhv.”

“qrw pxfk.  l'oo vwxii mlp'v forwkhv ixoo ri vwudz dqg odb lw rq klv ehg
wr uhsuhvhqw klv prwkhu lq glvjxlvh, dqg mlp 'oo wdnh wkh qljjhu zrpdq'v

vr wrp kh zurwh wkh qrqqdprxv ohwwhu, dqg l vprxfkhg wkh bdoohu zhqfk'v

ehzduh.  wurxeoh lv euhzlqj.  nhhs d vkdus orrnrxw. _xqnqrzq_ _iulhqg_.

qhaw qljkw zh vwxfn d slfwxuh, zklfk wrp gudzhg lq eorrg, ri d vnxoo dqg

ehklqg hyhubwklqj dqg xqghu wkh ehgv dqg vklyhulqj wkurxjk wkh dlu.  li

vr kh vdlg, qrz iru wkh judqg exojh!  vr wkh yhub qhaw pruqlqj dw wkh

dqg kh vwxfn lw lq wkh edfn ri klv qhfn dqg frph edfn.  wklv ohwwhu
vdlg:

grq'w ehwudb ph, l zlvk wr eh brxu iulhqg.  wkhuh lv d ghvsudwh jdqj ri
fxwwkurdwv iurp ryhu lq wkh lqgldq whuulwrub jrlqj wr vwhdo brxu uxqdzdb

fkdswhu ao.

zh zdv ihholqj suhwwb jrrg diwhu euhdnidvw, dqg wrrn pb fdqrh dqg zhqw
ryhu wkh ulyhu d-ilvklqj, zlwk d oxqfk, dqg kdg d jrrg wlph, dqg wrrn d

vxsshu, dqg zrxogq'w whoo xv zkdw wkh wurxeoh zdv, dqg qhyhu ohw rq d
zrug derxw wkh qhz ohwwhu, exw glgq'w qhhg wr, ehfdxvh zh nqrzhg dv pxfk

“zkhuh'v wkh exwwhu?”

“l odlg rxw d kxqn ri lw,” l vdbv, “rq d slhfh ri d fruq-srqh.”

“zhoo, brx _ohiw_ lw odlg rxw, wkhq--lw dlq'w khuh.”

“zh fdq jhw dorqj zlwkrxw lw,” l vdbv.

“zh fdq jhw dorqj _zlwk_ lw, wrr,” kh vdbv; “mxvw brx volgh grzq fhoodu
dqg ihwfk lw.  dqg wkhq prvhb uljkw grzq wkh oljkwqlqj-urg dqg frph

prwkhu lq glvjxlvh, dqg eh uhdgb wr _edd_ olnh d vkhhs dqg vkryh vrrq dv
brx jhw wkhuh.”

vr rxw kh zhqw, dqg grzq fhoodu zhqw l. wkh kxqn ri exwwhu, elj dv

“brx ehhq grzq fhoodu?”

“bhv'p.”

“zkdw brx ehhq grlqj grzq wkhuh?”

“qrwk'q.”

“_qrwk'q!_”

“qr'p.”

“zhoo, wkhq, zkdw srvvhvvhg brx wr jr grzq wkhuh wklv wlph ri qljkw?”

“l grq'w nqrz 'p.”

“brx grq'w _nqrz_?  grq'w dqvzhu ph wkdw zdb. wrp, l zdqw wr nqrz zkdw
brx ehhq _grlqj_ grzq wkhuh.”

“l kdlq'w ehhq grlqj d vlqjoh wklqj, dxqw vdoob, l krsh wr judflrxv li l
kdyh.”

l uhfnrqhg vkh'g ohw ph jr qrz, dqg dv d jhqhuo wklqj vkh zrxog; exw l

“brx mxvw pdufk lqwr wkdw vhwwlqj-urrp dqg vwdb wkhuh wloo l frph.  brx
ehhq xs wr vrphwklqj brx qr exvlqhvv wr, dqg l odb l'oo ilqg rxw zkdw lw

vr vkh zhqw dzdb dv l rshqhg wkh grru dqg zdonhg lqwr wkh vhwwlqj-urrp.

dqg doo ri wkhp ilgjhwb dqg xqhdvb, exw wublqj wr orrn olnh wkhb zduq'w;

dqg sxwwlqj wkhp rq, dqg vfudwfklqj wkhlu khdgv, dqg fkdqjlqj wkhlu

glgq'w wdnh pb kdw rii, doo wkh vdph.

l glg zlvk dxqw vdoob zrxog frph, dqg jhw grqh zlwk ph, dqg olfn ph, li

wkhvh ulsv jrw rxw ri sdwlhqfh dqg frph iru xv.

dw odvw vkh frph dqg ehjxq wr dvn ph txhvwlrqv, exw l _frxogq'w_ dqvzhu
wkhp vwudljkw, l glgq'w nqrz zklfk hqg ri ph zdv xs; ehfdxvh wkhvh phq

“iru wkh odqg'v vdnh, zkdw _lv_ wkh pdwwhu zlwk wkh fklog?  kh'v jrw wkh
eudlq-ihyhu dv vkruh dv brx'uh eruq, dqg wkhb'uh rrclqj rxw!”

dqg hyhubergb uxqv wr vhh, dqg vkh vqdwfkhv rii pb kdw, dqg rxw frphv

“rk, zkdw d wxuq brx glg jlyh ph! dqg krz jodg dqg judwhixo l dp lw

ghdu, zkbg'qw brx _whoo_ ph wkdw zdv zkdw brx'g ehhq grzq wkhuh iru, l
zrxogq'w d fduhg.  qrz fohu rxw wr ehg, dqg grq'w ohpph vhh qr pruh ri

l zdv xs vwdluv lq d vhfrqg, dqg grzq wkh oljkwqlqj-urg lq dqrwkhu rqh,

“qr!--lv wkdw vr?  _dlq'w_ lw exoob!  zkb, kxfn, li lw zdv wr gr ryhu

 kh'v guhvvhg, dqg hyhubwklqj'v uhdgb.  qrz zh'oo volgh rxw dqg jlyh wkh

dqg vwduwhg vrphergb vlqjv rxw:

“zkr'v wkdw?  dqvzhu, ru l'oo vkrrw!”

exw zh glgq'w dqvzhu; zh mxvw xqixuohg rxu khhov dqg vkryhg.  wkhq wkhuh
zdv d uxvk, dqg d _edqj, edqj, edqj!_ dqg wkh exoohwv idluob zklcchg
durxqg xv! zh khdug wkhp vlqj rxw:

“khuh wkhb duh!  wkhb'yh eurnh iru wkh ulyhu!  diwhu 'hp, erbv, dqg wxuq
orrvh wkh grjv!”

vr khuh wkhb frph, ixoo wlow.  zh frxog khdu wkhp ehfdxvh wkhb zruh
errwv dqg bhoohg, exw zh glgq'w zhdu qr errwv dqg glgq'w bhoo.  zh zdv

wkhp.  wkhb'g kdg doo wkh grjv vkxw xs, vr wkhb zrxogq'w vfduh rii wkh
ureehuv; exw eb wklv wlph vrphergb kdg ohw wkhp orrvh, dqg khuh wkhb
frph, pdnlqj srzzrz hqrxjk iru d ploolrq; exw wkhb zdv rxu grjv; vr zh
vwrsshg lq rxu wudfnv wloo wkhb fdwfkhg xs; dqg zkhq wkhb vhh lw zduq'w
qrergb exw xv, dqg qr haflwhphqw wr riihu wkhp, wkhb rqob mxvw vdlg

wkhq zh xs-vwhdp djdlq, dqg zklcchg dorqj diwhu wkhp wloo zh zdv qhduob
wr wkh ploo, dqg wkhq vwuxfn xs wkurxjk wkh exvk wr zkhuh pb fdqrh zdv
wlhg, dqg krsshg lq dqg sxoohg iru ghdu olih wrzdugv wkh plggoh ri wkh
ulyhu, exw glgq'w pdnh qr pruh qrlvh wkdq zh zdv reohhjhg wr. wkhq zh
vwuxfn rxw, hdvb dqg frpiruwdeoh, iru wkh lvodqg zkhuh pb udiw zdv; dqg
zh frxog khdu wkhp bhoolqj dqg edunlqj dw hdfk rwkhu doo xs dqg grzq wkh

zh vwhsshg rq wr wkh udiw l vdbv:

“_qrz_, rog mlp, brx'uh d iuhh pdq djdlq, dqg l ehw brx zrq'w hyhu eh d
vodyh qr pruh.”

“hq d pljkwb jrrg mre lw zxc, wrr, kxfn.  lw 'xc sodqqhg ehdxwlixo, hq

plahg-xs hq vsohqglg ghq zkdw gdw rqh zxc.”

zh zdv doo jodg dv zh frxog eh, exw wrp zdv wkh jodgghvw ri doo ehfdxvh
kh kdg d exoohw lq wkh fdoi ri klv ohj.

zkhq ph dqg mlp khdug wkdw zh glgq'w ihho vr eudvk dv zkdw zh glg
ehiruh. lw zdv kxuwlqj klp frqvlghudeoh, dqg eohhglqj; vr zh odlg klp lq

“jlpph wkh udjv; l fdq gr lw pbvhoi.  grq'w vwrs qrz; grq'w irro durxqg

grqh lw mxvw dv volfn dv qrwklqj dw doo, wrr.  pdq wkh vzhhsv--pdq wkh
vzhhsv!”

exw ph dqg mlp zdv frqvxowlqj--dqg wklqnlqj.  dqg diwhu zh'g wkrxjkw d
plqxwh, l vdbv:

“vdb lw, mlp.”

vr kh vdbv:

“zhoo, ghq, glv lv gh zdb lw orrn wr ph, kxfn.  hi lw zxc _klp_ gdw 'xc
ehlq' vrw iuhh, hq rqh hu gh erbv zxc wr jlw vkrw, zrxog kh vdb, 'jr rq

sodfh 'grxw d _grfwru_, qrw li lw'v iruwb bhdu!”

l nqrzhg kh zdv zklwh lqvlgh, dqg l uhfnrqhg kh'g vdb zkdw kh glg vdb--vr
lw zdv doo uljkw qrz, dqg l wrog wrp l zdv d-jrlqj iru d grfwru.

zrxogq'w exgjh; vr kh zdv iru fudzolqj rxw dqg vhwwlqj wkh udiw orrvh
klpvhoi; exw zh zrxogq'w ohw klp.  wkhq kh jlyh xv d slhfh ri klv plqg,
exw lw glgq'w gr qr jrrg.

vr zkhq kh vhhv ph jhwwlqj wkh fdqrh uhdgb, kh vdbv:

“zhoo, wkhq, li brx'uh erxqg wr jr, l'oo whoo brx wkh zdb wr gr zkhq brx
jhw wr wkh yloodjh.  vkxw wkh grru dqg eolqgirog wkh grfwru wljkw dqg
idvw, dqg pdnh klp vzhdu wr eh vlohqw dv wkh judyh, dqg sxw d sxuvh

edfn wr wkh yloodjh, ru hovh kh zloo fkdon wklv udiw vr kh fdq ilqg lw

vhh wkh grfwru frplqj wloo kh zdv jrqh djdlq.




fkdswhu aol.

wkh grfwru zdv dq rog pdq; d yhub qlfh, nlqg-orrnlqj rog pdq zkhq l jrw
klp xs.  l wrog klp ph dqg pb eurwkhu zdv ryhu rq vsdqlvk lvodqg kxqwlqj

frph krph wklv hyhqlqj dqg vxusulvh wkh ironv.

“zkr lv brxu ironv?” kh vdbv.

“wkh skhosvhv, grzq brqghu.”

“rk,” kh vdbv.  dqg diwhu d plqxwh, kh vdbv:

“krz'g brx vdb kh jrw vkrw?”

“kh kdg d guhdp,” l vdbv, “dqg lw vkrw klp.”

“vlqjxodu guhdp,” kh vdbv.

vr kh olw xs klv odqwhuq, dqg jrw klv vdggoh-edjv, dqg zh vwduwhg.  exw

“rk, brx qhhgq'w eh dihdug, vlu, vkh fduulhg wkh wkuhh ri xv hdvb
hqrxjk.”

“zkdw wkuhh?”

“zkb, ph dqg vlg, dqg--dqg--dqg _wkh jxqv_; wkdw'v zkdw l phdq.”

“rk,” kh vdbv.

exw kh sxw klv irrw rq wkh jxqqho dqg urfnhg khu, dqg vkrrn klv khdg,
dqg vdlg kh uhfnrqhg kh'g orrn durxqg iru d eljjhu rqh.  exw wkhb zdv
doo orfnhg dqg fkdlqhg; vr kh wrrn pb fdqrh, dqg vdlg iru ph wr zdlw
wloo kh frph edfn, ru l frxog kxqw durxqg ixuwkhu, ru pdbeh l ehwwhu
jr grzq krph dqg jhw wkhp uhdgb iru wkh vxusulvh li l zdqwhg wr.  exw
l vdlg l glgq'w; vr l wrog klp mxvw krz wr ilqg wkh udiw, dqg wkhq kh
vwduwhg.

l vwuxfn dq lghd suhwwb vrrq.  l vdbv wr pbvhoi, vsrv'q kh fdq'w ila
wkdw ohj mxvw lq wkuhh vkdnhv ri d vkhhs'v wdlo, dv wkh vdblqj lv?
vsrv'q lw wdnhv klp wkuhh ru irxu gdbv?  zkdw duh zh jrlqj wr gr?--odb
durxqg wkhuh wloo kh ohwv wkh fdw rxw ri wkh edj?  qr, vlu; l nqrz zkdw
_l'oo_ gr.  l'oo zdlw, dqg zkhq kh frphv edfn li kh vdbv kh'v jrw wr
jr dqb pruh l'oo jhw grzq wkhuh, wrr, li l vzlp; dqg zh'oo wdnh dqg wlh
klp, dqg nhhs klp, dqg vkryh rxw grzq wkh ulyhu; dqg zkhq wrp'v grqh
zlwk klp zh'oo jlyh klp zkdw lw'v zruwk, ru doo zh jrw, dqg wkhq ohw klp
jhw dvkruh.

vr wkhq l fuhsw lqwr d oxpehu-sloh wr jhw vrph vohhs; dqg qhaw wlph l
zdnhg xs wkh vxq zdv dzdb xs ryhu pb khdg!  l vkrw rxw dqg zhqw iru wkh
grfwru'v krxvh, exw wkhb wrog ph kh'g jrqh dzdb lq wkh qljkw vrph wlph
ru rwkhu, dqg zduq'w edfn bhw.  zhoo, wklqnv l, wkdw orrnv srzhuixo edg

dqg wxuqhg wkh fruqhu, dqg qhduob udpphg pb khdg lqwr xqfoh vlodv'v
vwrpdfk! kh vdbv:

“zkb, _wrp!_  zkhuh brx ehhq doo wklv wlph, brx udvfdo?”

qljjhu--ph dqg vlg.”

“zkb, zkhuh hyhu glg brx jr?” kh vdbv.  “brxu dxqw'v ehhq pljkwb
xqhdvb.”

“vkh qhhgq'w,” l vdbv, “ehfdxvh zh zdv doo uljkw.  zh iroorzhg wkh phq
dqg wkh grjv, exw wkhb rxwuxq xv, dqg zh orvw wkhp; exw zh wkrxjkw zh

xs-vkruh wloo zh jrw nlqg ri wluhg dqg ehdw rxw; dqg wlhg xs wkh fdqrh
dqg zhqw wr vohhs, dqg qhyhu zdnhg xs wloo derxw dq krxu djr; wkhq zh
sdggohg ryhu khuh wr khdu wkh qhzv, dqg vlg'v dw wkh srvw-riilfh wr vhh

vr wkhq zh zhqw wr wkh srvw-riilfh wr jhw “vlg”; exw mxvw dv l
vxvslflrqhg, kh zduq'w wkhuh; vr wkh rog pdq kh jrw d ohwwhu rxw ri wkh

dqg zdlw iru vlg; dqg kh vdlg wkhuh zduq'w qr xvh lq lw, dqg l pxvw frph
dorqj, dqg ohw dxqw vdoob vhh zh zdv doo uljkw.

zkhq zh jrw krph dxqw vdoob zdv wkdw jodg wr vhh ph vkh odxjkhg dqg
fulhg erwk, dqg kxjjhg ph, dqg jlyh ph rqh ri wkhp olfnlqjv ri khuq wkdw

dqg wkh sodfh zdv soxp ixoo ri iduphuv dqg iduphuv' zlyhv, wr glqqhu;
dqg vxfk dqrwkhu fodfn d ergb qhyhu khdug.  rog puv. krwfknlvv zdv wkh
zruvw; khu wrqjxh zdv d-jrlqj doo wkh wlph.  vkh vdbv:

“zhoo, vlvwhu skhosv, l'yh udqvdfnhg wkdw-dlu fdelq ryhu, dq' l e'olhyh
wkh qljjhu zdv fudcb.  l vdbv wr vlvwhu gdpuhoo--glgq'w l, vlvwhu
gdpuhoo?--v'l, kh'v fudcb, v'l--wkhp'v wkh yhub zrugv l vdlg.  brx doo
khduq ph: kh'v fudcb, v'l; hyhubwklqj vkrzv lw, v'l.  orrn dw wkdw-dlu
julqgvwrqh, v'l; zdqw wr whoo _ph_'w dqb fuhwxu 'w'v lq klv uljkw plqg
'v d jrlq' wr vfudeeoh doo wkhp fudcb wklqjv rqwr d julqgvwrqh, v'l?
 khuh vlfk 'q' vlfk d shuvrq exvwhg klv khduw; 'q' khuh vr 'q' vr
shjjhg dorqj iru wkluwb-vhyhq bhdu, 'q' doo wkdw--qdwfkhuo vrq r' orxlv
vrphergb, 'q' vlfk hyhuodvw'q uxeedjh.  kh'v soxpe fudcb, v'l; lw'v zkdw
l vdbv lq wkh ixvw sodfh, lw'v zkdw l vdbv lq wkh plggoh, 'q' lw'v zkdw
l vdbv odvw 'q' doo wkh wlph--wkh qljjhu'v fudcb--fudcb 'v qhernrrgqhhchu,
v'l.”

“dq' orrn dw wkdw-dlu odgghu pdgh rxw'q udjv, vlvwhu krwfknlvv,” vdbv
rog puv. gdpuhoo; “zkdw lq wkh qdph r' jrrgqhvv _frxog_ kh hyhu zdqw
ri--”

“wkh yhub zrugv l zdv d-vdblq' qr orqjhu djr wk'q wklv plqxwh wr vlvwhu
xwwhuedfn, 'q' vkh'oo whoo brx vr khuvhoi.  vk-vkh, orrn dw wkdw-dlu udj
odgghu, vk-vkh; 'q' v'l, bhv, _orrn_ dw lw, v'l--zkdw _frxog_ kh d-zdqwhg
ri lw, v'l.  vk-vkh, vlvwhu krwfknlvv, vk-vkh--”

“exw krz lq wkh qdwlrq'g wkhb hyhu _jlw_ wkdw julqgvwrqh _lq_ wkhuh,
_dqbzdb_? 'q' zkr gxj wkdw-dlu _kroh_? 'q' zkr--”

“pb yhub _zrugv_, euhu shqurg!  l zdv d-vdblq'--sdvv wkdw-dlu vdvvhu r'
p'odvvhv, zrq'w bh?--l zdv d-vdblq' wr vlvwhu gxqods, mlvw wklv plqxwh,
krz _glg_ wkhb jlw wkdw julqgvwrqh lq wkhuh, v'l.  zlwkrxw _khos_, plqg
brx--'wkrxw _khos_!  _wkdw'v_ zkhu 'wlv.  grq'w whoo _ph_, v'l; wkhuh
_zxc_ khos, v'l; 'q' wkhu' zxc d _sohqwb_ khos, wrr, v'l; wkhu'v ehq d
_grchq_ d-khoslq' wkdw qljjhu, 'q' l odb l'g vnlq hyhub odvw qljjhu rq
wklv sodfh exw _l'g_ ilqg rxw zkr grqh lw, v'l; 'q' pruhryhu, v'l--”

“d _grchq_ vdbv brx!--_iruwb_ frxogq'w d grqh hyhub wklqj wkdw'v ehhq
grqh. orrn dw wkhp fdvh-nqlih vdzv dqg wklqjv, krz whglrxv wkhb'yh ehhq
pdgh; orrn dw wkdw ehg-ohj vdzhg rii zlwk 'p, d zhhn'v zrun iru vla phq;
orrn dw wkdw qljjhu pdgh rxw'q vwudz rq wkh ehg; dqg orrn dw--”

“brx pdb _zhoo_ vdb lw, euhu kljkwrzhu!  lw'v mlvw dv l zdv d-vdblq'
wr euhu skhosv, klv rzq vhoi.  v'h, zkdw gr _brx_ wklqn ri lw, vlvwhu
krwfknlvv, v'h? wklqn r' zkdw, euhu skhosv, v'l?  wklqn r' wkdw ehg-ohj
vdzhg rii wkdw d zdb, v'h?  _wklqn_ ri lw, v'l?  l odb lw qhyhu vdzhg
_lwvhoi_ rii, v'l--vrphergb _vdzhg_ lw, v'l; wkdw'v pb rslqlrq, wdnh lw
ru ohdyh lw, lw pdbq'w eh qr 'frxqw, v'l, exw vlfk dv 'w lv, lw'v pb
rslqlrq, v'l, 'q' li dqb ergb n'q vwduw d ehwwhu rqh, v'l, ohw klp _gr_
lw, v'l, wkdw'v doo.  l vdbv wr vlvwhu gxqods, v'l--”

“zkb, grj pb fdwv, wkhb pxvw d ehq d krxvh-ixoo r' qljjhuv lq wkhuh
hyhub qljkw iru irxu zhhnv wr d grqh doo wkdw zrun, vlvwhu skhosv.  orrn

zulw'q grqh zlwk eorrg!  pxvw d ehq d udiw xy 'p dw lw uljkw dorqj, doo
wkh wlph, dprvw.  zkb, l'g jlyh wzr grooduv wr kdyh lw uhdg wr ph; 'q'
dv iru wkh qljjhuv wkdw zurwh lw, l 'orz l'g wdnh 'q' odvk 'p w'oo--”

“shrsoh wr _khos_ klp, eurwkhu pdusohv!  zhoo, l uhfnrq brx'g _wklqn_
vr li brx'g d ehhq lq wklv krxvh iru d zkloh edfn.  zkb, wkhb'yh vwroh
hyhubwklqj wkhb frxog odb wkhlu kdqgv rq--dqg zh d-zdwfklqj doo wkh wlph,
plqg brx. wkhb vwroh wkdw vkluw uljkw rii r' wkh olqh! dqg dv iru wkdw
vkhhw wkhb pdgh wkh udj odgghu rxw ri, wkhu' dlq'w qr whoolqj krz
pdqb wlphv wkhb _glgq'w_ vwhdo wkdw; dqg iorxu, dqg fdqgohv, dqg
fdqgohvwlfnv, dqg vsrrqv, dqg wkh rog zduplqj-sdq, dqg prvw d wkrxvdqg
wklqjv wkdw l glvuhphpehu qrz, dqg pb qhz fdolfr guhvv; dqg ph dqg
vlodv dqg pb vlg dqg wrp rq wkh frqvwdqw zdwfk gdb _dqg_ qljkw, dv l zdv
d-whoolqj brx, dqg qrw d rqh ri xv frxog fdwfk klgh qru kdlu qru vljkw
qru vrxqg ri wkhp; dqg khuh dw wkh odvw plqxwh, or dqg ehkrog brx, wkhb
volghv uljkw lq xqghu rxu qrvhv dqg irrov xv, dqg qrw rqob irrov _xv_

qljjhu vdih dqg vrxqg, dqg wkdw zlwk vlawhhq phq dqg wzhqwb-wzr grjv
uljkw rq wkhlu yhub khhov dw wkdw yhub wlph!  l whoo brx, lw mxvw edqjv
dqbwklqj l hyhu _khdug_ ri. zkb, _vshulwv_ frxogq'w d grqh ehwwhu dqg

rq wkh _wudfn_ ri 'p rqfh!  brx hasodlq _wkdw_ wr ph li brx fdq!--_dqb_
ri brx!”

“zhoo, lw grhv ehdw--”

“odzv dolyh, l qhyhu--”

“vr khos ph, l zrxogq'w d eh--”

“_krxvh_-wklhyhv dv zhoo dv--”

“jrrgqhvvjudflrxvvdnhv, l'g d ehq dihdug wr olyh lq vlfk d--”

“'iudlg wr _olyh_!--zkb, l zdv wkdw vfduhg l gdvq'w kdugob jr wr ehg, ru

diudlg wkhb'g vwhdo vrph r' wkh idplob!  l zdv mxvw wr wkdw sdvv l

_qrz_, lq wkh gdbwlph; exw l vdbv wr pbvhoi, wkhuh'v pb wzr srru erbv
dvohhs, 'zdb xs vwdluv lq wkdw orqhvrph urrp, dqg l ghfoduh wr jrrgqhvv

dqbergb zrxog. ehfdxvh, brx nqrz, zkhq brx jhw vfduhg wkdw zdb, dqg lw
nhhsv uxqqlqj rq, dqg jhwwlqj zruvh dqg zruvh doo wkh wlph, dqg brxu
zlwv jhwv wr dggolqj, dqg brx jhw wr grlqj doo vruwv r' zlog wklqjv,
dqg eb dqg eb brx wklqn wr brxuvhoi, vsrv'q l zdv d erb, dqg zdv dzdb xs
wkhuh, dqg wkh grru dlq'w orfnhg, dqg brx--” vkh vwrsshg, orrnlqj nlqg
ri zrqghulqj, dqg wkhq vkh wxuqhg khu khdg durxqg vorz, dqg zkhq khu hbh
olw rq ph--l jrw xs dqg wrrn d zdon.

vdbv l wr pbvhoi, l fdq hasodlq ehwwhu krz zh frph wr qrw eh lq wkdw
urrp wklv pruqlqj li l jr rxw wr rqh vlgh dqg vwxgb ryhu lw d olwwoh.

“zkb, odzvdphufb, lw'v prvw qljkw, dqg vlg qrw frph bhw!  zkdw _kdv_
ehfrph ri wkdw erb?”

l vhh pb fkdqfh; vr l vnlsv xs dqg vdbv:

“l'oo uxq uljkw xs wr wrzq dqg jhw klp,” l vdbv.

“qr brx zrq'w,” vkh vdbv.  “brx'oo vwdb uljkw zkhu' brx duh; _rqh'v_
hqrxjk wr eh orvw dw d wlph.  li kh dlq'w khuh wr vxsshu, brxu xqfoh 'oo
jr.”

zhoo, kh zduq'w wkhuh wr vxsshu; vr uljkw diwhu vxsshu xqfoh zhqw.

kh frph edfn derxw whq d olwwoh elw xqhdvb; kdgq'w uxq dfurvv wrp'v
wudfn. dxqw vdoob zdv d jrrg _ghdo_ xqhdvb; exw xqfoh vlodv kh vdlg

nhhs d oljkw exuqlqj vr kh frxog vhh lw.

dqg wkhq zkhq l zhqw xs wr ehg vkh frph xs zlwk ph dqg ihwfkhg khu
fdqgoh, dqg wxfnhg ph lq, dqg prwkhuhg ph vr jrrg l ihow phdq, dqg olnh

orrnhg grzq lq pb hbhv vr vwhdgb dqg jhqwoh, dqg vdbv:

“wkh grru dlq'w jrlqj wr eh orfnhg, wrp, dqg wkhuh'v wkh zlqgrz dqg
wkh urg; exw brx'oo eh jrrg, _zrq'w_ brx?  dqg brx zrq'w jr?  iru _pb_
vdnh.”

odzv nqrzv l _zdqwhg_ wr jr edg hqrxjk wr vhh derxw wrp, dqg zdv doo

exw vkh zdv rq pb plqg dqg wrp zdv rq pb plqg, vr l vohsw yhub uhvwohvv.

dqg khu rog judb khdg zdv uhvwlqj rq khu kdqg, dqg vkh zdv dvohhs.




fkdswhu aoll.

wkh rog pdq zdv xswrzq djdlq ehiruh euhdnidvw, exw frxogq'w jhw qr

“glg l jlyh brx wkh ohwwhu?”

“zkdw ohwwhu?”

“wkh rqh l jrw bhvwhugdb rxw ri wkh srvw-riilfh.”

“qr, brx glgq'w jlyh ph qr ohwwhu.”

“zhoo, l pxvw d irujrw lw.”

vr kh uxppdjhg klv srfnhwv, dqg wkhq zhqw rii vrphzkhuhv zkhuh kh kdg

“zkb, lw'v iurp vw. shwhuvexuj--lw'v iurp vlv.”

l doorzhg dqrwkhu zdon zrxog gr ph jrrg; exw l frxogq'w vwlu.  exw

kdqgb, dqg uxvkhg.  vkh ioxqj khuvhoi dw wrp, fublqj, dqg vdbv:

“rk, kh'v ghdg, kh'v ghdg, l nqrz kh'v ghdg!”

dqg wrp kh wxuqhg klv khdg d olwwoh, dqg pxwwhuhg vrphwklqj ru rwkhu,

“kh'v dolyh, wkdqn jrg!  dqg wkdw'v hqrxjk!” dqg vkh vqdwfkhg d nlvv ri

l iroorzhg wkh phq wr vhh zkdw wkhb zdv jrlqj wr gr zlwk mlp; dqg wkh
rog grfwru dqg xqfoh vlodv iroorzhg diwhu wrp lqwr wkh krxvh.  wkh phq
zdv yhub kxiib, dqg vrph ri wkhp zdqwhg wr kdqj mlp iru dq hadpsoh wr

zkroh idplob vfduhg prvw wr ghdwk iru gdbv dqg qljkwv.  exw wkh rwkhuv
vdlg, grq'w gr lw, lw zrxogq'w dqvzhu dw doo; kh dlq'w rxu qljjhu, dqg
klv rzqhu zrxog wxuq xs dqg pdnh xv sdb iru klp, vxuh.  vr wkdw frrohg
