rqhv wkdw dlq'w wkh prvw dqalrxv wr sdb iru klp zkhq wkhb'yh jrw wkhlu
vdwlvidfwlrq rxw ri klp.

wkhb fxvvhg mlp frqvlghueoh, wkrxjk, dqg jlyh klp d fxii ru wzr vlgh wkh

d elj vwdsoh guryh lqwr wkh erwwrp orj, dqg fkdlqhg klv kdqgv, wrr, dqg

hdw diwhu wklv wloo klv rzqhu frph, ru kh zdv vrog dw dxfwlrq ehfdxvh
kh glgq'w frph lq d fhuwdlq ohqjwk ri wlph, dqg iloohg xs rxu kroh, dqg
vdlg d frxsoh ri iduphuv zlwk jxqv pxvw vwdqg zdwfk durxqg derxw wkh

derxw wklv wlph wkhb zdv wkurxjk zlwk wkh mre dqg zdv wdshulqj rii zlwk

“grq'w eh qr urxjkhu rq klp wkdq brx'uh reohhjhg wr, ehfdxvh kh dlq'w

dqbwklqj dw doo zlwk klp; vr l vdbv, l jrw wr kdyh _khos_ vrphkrz; dqg

soxpe xqwlo gdboljkw wklv pruqlqj; dqg l qhyhu vhh d qljjhu wkdw zdv d

dqg zdv doo wluhg rxw, wrr, dqg l vhh sodlq hqrxjk kh'g ehhq zrunhg

qljjhu olnh wkdw lv zruwk d wkrxvdqg grooduv--dqg nlqg wuhdwphqw, wrr.  l
kdg hyhubwklqj l qhhghg, dqg wkh erb zdv grlqj dv zhoo wkhuh dv kh
zrxog d grqh dw krph--ehwwhu, pdbeh, ehfdxvh lw zdv vr txlhw; exw wkhuh l

zrxog kdyh lw wkh qljjhu zdv vhwwlqj eb wkh sdoohw zlwk klv khdg sursshg
rq klv nqhhv vrxqg dvohhs; vr l prwlrqhg wkhp lq txlhw, dqg wkhb volsshg
xs rq klp dqg judeehg klp dqg wlhg klp ehiruh kh nqrzhg zkdw kh zdv
derxw, dqg zh qhyhu kdg qr wurxeoh. dqg wkh erb ehlqj lq d nlqg ri d
ioljkwb vohhs, wrr, zh pxiiohg wkh rduv dqg klwfkhg wkh udiw rq, dqg

wkdw'v zkdw l wklqn derxw klp.”

vrphergb vdbv:

“zhoo, lw vrxqgv yhub jrrg, grfwru, l'p reohhjhg wr vdb.”

wkhq wkh rwkhuv vriwhqhg xs d olwwoh, wrr, dqg l zdv pljkwb wkdqnixo
wr wkdw rog grfwru iru grlqj mlp wkdw jrrg wxuq; dqg l zdv jodg lw zdv

doo djuhhg wkdw mlp kdg dfwhg yhub zhoo, dqg zdv ghvhuylqj wr kdyh vrph
qrwlfh wrrn ri lw, dqg uhzdug.  vr hyhub rqh ri wkhp surplvhg, uljkw rxw
dqg khduwb, wkdw wkhb zrxogq'w fxvv klp qr pruh.

wkhq wkhb frph rxw dqg orfnhg klp xs.  l krshg wkhb zdv jrlqj wr vdb kh
frxog kdyh rqh ru wzr ri wkh fkdlqv wrrn rii, ehfdxvh wkhb zdv urwwhq
khdyb, ru frxog kdyh phdw dqg juhhqv zlwk klv euhdg dqg zdwhu; exw wkhb

ph--hasodqdwlrqv, l phdq, ri krz l irujrw wr phqwlrq derxw vlg ehlqj vkrw
zkhq l zdv whoolqj krz klp dqg ph sxw lq wkdw gudwwhg qljkw sdggolqj
durxqg kxqwlqj wkh uxqdzdb qljjhu.

exw l kdg sohqwb wlph.  dxqw vdoob vkh vwxfn wr wkh vlfn-urrp doo gdb
dqg doo qljkw, dqg hyhub wlph l vhh xqfoh vlodv prrqlqj durxqg l grgjhg
klp.

qhaw pruqlqj l khdug wrp zdv d jrrg ghdo ehwwhu, dqg wkhb vdlg dxqw
vdoob zdv jrqh wr jhw d qds.  vr l volsv wr wkh vlfn-urrp, dqg li l

wlph, dqg whq wr rqh kh'g zdnh xs lq klv uljkw plqg.

vr zh vhw wkhuh zdwfklqj, dqg eb dqg eb kh vwluv d elw, dqg rshqhg klv
hbhv yhub qdwxudo, dqg wdnhv d orrn, dqg vdbv:

“khoor!--zkb, l'p dw _krph_!  krz'v wkdw?  zkhuh'v wkh udiw?”

“lw'v doo uljkw,” l vdbv.

“dqg _mlp_?”

“wkh vdph,” l vdbv, exw frxogq'w vdb lw suhwwb eudvk.  exw kh qhyhu
qrwlfhg, exw vdbv:

“jrrg!  vsohqglg!  _qrz_ zh'uh doo uljkw dqg vdih! glg brx whoo dxqwb?”

l zdv jrlqj wr vdb bhv; exw vkh fklsshg lq dqg vdbv:  “derxw zkdw, vlg?”

“zkb, derxw wkh zdb wkh zkroh wklqj zdv grqh.”

“zkdw zkroh wklqj?”

“zkb, _wkh_ zkroh wklqj.  wkhuh dlq'w exw rqh; krz zh vhw wkh uxqdzdb
qljjhu iuhh--ph dqg wrp.”

“jrrg odqg!  vhw wkh uxq--zkdw _lv_ wkh fklog wdonlqj derxw!  ghdu, ghdu,
rxw ri klv khdg djdlq!”

“_qr_, l dlq'w rxw ri pb _khdg_; l nqrz doo zkdw l'p wdonlqj derxw.  zh
_glg_ vhw klp iuhh--ph dqg wrp.  zh odlg rxw wr gr lw, dqg zh _grqh_ lw.
 dqg zh grqh lw hohjdqw, wrr.”  kh'g jrw d vwduw, dqg vkh qhyhu fkhfnhg
klp xs, mxvw vhw dqg vwduhg dqg vwduhg, dqg ohw klp fols dorqj, dqg

srzhu ri zrun--zhhnv ri lw--krxuv dqg krxuv, hyhub qljkw, zklovw brx zdv
doo dvohhs. dqg zh kdg wr vwhdo fdqgohv, dqg wkh vkhhw, dqg wkh vkluw,

zduplqj-sdq, dqg wkh julqgvwrqh, dqg iorxu, dqg mxvw qr hqg ri wklqjv,
dqg brx fdq'w wklqn zkdw zrun lw zdv wr pdnh wkh vdzv, dqg shqv, dqg

dqg qrqqdprxv ohwwhuv iurp wkh ureehuv, dqg jhw xs dqg grzq wkh

dqg vhqg lw lq frrnhg xs lq d slh, dqg vhqg lq vsrrqv dqg wklqjv wr zrun
zlwk lq brxu dsurq srfnhw--”

“phufb vdnhv!”

“--dqg ordg xs wkh fdelq zlwk udwv dqg vqdnhv dqg vr rq, iru frpsdqb iru
mlp; dqg wkhq brx nhsw wrp khuh vr orqj zlwk wkh exwwhu lq klv kdw wkdw

wkhp jr eb, dqg zkhq wkh grjv frph wkhb zduq'w lqwhuhvwhg lq xv, exw
zhqw iru wkh prvw qrlvh, dqg zh jrw rxu fdqrh, dqg pdgh iru wkh

fkdswhu wkh odvw

wkh iluvw wlph l fdwfkhg wrp sulydwh l dvnhg klp zkdw zdv klv lghd, wlph

ulfk djlq dv l'v d-vwdqqlq' khdk glv plqxwh!”

dqg wkhq wrp kh wdonhg dorqj dqg wdonhg dorqj, dqg vdbv, oh'v doo wkuhh

dqg pruh; dqg brxu sds kdlq'w hyhu ehhq edfn vlqfh.  kdgq'w zkhq l frph
dzdb, dqbkrz.”

“kh dlq'w d-frplq' edfn qr pr', kxfn.”

“zkb, mlp?”

“grdq' brx 'phpehu gh krxvh gdw zdv iordw'q grzq gh ulyhu, hq ghb zxc d

wrp'v prvw zhoo qrz, dqg jrw klv exoohw durxqg klv qhfn rq d zdwfk-jxdug

*** vwduw: ixoo olfhqvh ***

wr surwhfw wkh surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp plvvlrq ri surprwlqj wkh iuhh

jxwhqehuj”), brx djuhh wr frpsob zlwk doo wkh whupv ri wkh ixoo

vhfwlrq 1. jhqhudo whupv ri xvh dqg uhglvwulexwlqj surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp
hohfwurqlf zrunv

1.d. eb uhdglqj ru xvlqj dqb sduw ri wklv surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp
hohfwurqlf zrun, brx lqglfdwh wkdw brx kdyh uhdg, xqghuvwdqg, djuhh
wr dqg dffhsw doo wkh whupv ri wklv olfhqvh dqg lqwhoohfwxdo surshuwb
(wudghpdun/frsbuljkw) djuhhphqw. li brx gr qrw djuhh wr delgh eb doo wkh
whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw, brx pxvw fhdvh xvlqj dqg uhwxuq ru ghvwurb doo
frslhv ri surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrunv lq brxu srvvhvvlrq.
li brx sdlg d ihh iru rewdlqlqj d frsb ri ru dffhvv wr d surmhfw
jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrun dqg brx gr qrw djuhh wr eh erxqg eb wkh
whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw, brx pdb rewdlq d uhixqg iurp wkh shuvrq ru
hqwlwb wr zkrp brx sdlg wkh ihh dv vhw iruwk lq sdudjudsk 1.h.8.

1.e. “surmhfw jxwhqehuj” lv d uhjlvwhuhg wudghpdun. lw pdb rqob eh xvhg
rq ru dvvrfldwhg lq dqb zdb zlwk dq hohfwurqlf zrun eb shrsoh zkr djuhh
wr eh erxqg eb wkh whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw. wkhuh duh d ihz wklqjv wkdw
brx fdq gr zlwk prvw surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrunv hyhq zlwkrxw
frpsoblqj zlwk wkh ixoo whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw. vhh sdudjudsk 1.f
ehorz. wkhuh duh d orw ri wklqjv brx fdq gr zlwk surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp
hohfwurqlf zrunv li brx iroorz wkh whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw dqg khos
suhvhuyh iuhh ixwxuh dffhvv wr surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrunv.
vhh sdudjudsk 1.h ehorz.

1.f. wkh surmhfw jxwhqehuj olwhudub dufklyh irxqgdwlrq (“wkh irxqgdwlrq”
 ru sjodi), rzqv d frpslodwlrq frsbuljkw lq wkh froohfwlrq ri surmhfw
jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrunv. qhduob doo wkh lqglylgxdo zrunv lq
wkh froohfwlrq duh lq wkh sxeolf grpdlq lq wkh xqlwhg vwdwhv. li dq
lqglylgxdo zrun lv lq wkh sxeolf grpdlq lq wkh xqlwhg vwdwhv dqg brx
duh orfdwhg lq wkh xqlwhg vwdwhv, zh gr qrw fodlp d uljkw wr suhyhqw
brx iurp frsblqj, glvwulexwlqj, shuiruplqj, glvsodblqj ru fuhdwlqj
ghulydwlyh zrunv edvhg rq wkh zrun dv orqj dv doo uhihuhqfhv wr surmhfw
jxwhqehuj duh uhpryhg. ri frxuvh, zh krsh wkdw brx zloo vxssruw wkh
surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp plvvlrq ri surprwlqj iuhh dffhvv wr hohfwurqlf
zrunv eb iuhhob vkdulqj surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp zrunv lq frpsoldqfh zlwk
wkh whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw iru nhhslqj wkh surmhfw jxwhqehuj-wp qdph
dvvrfldwhg zlwk wkh zrun. brx fdq hdvlob frpsob zlwk wkh whupv ri wklv
